ye triṣaptāḥ pariyanti viśvā rūpāṇi bibhrataḥ   vācaḥ patiḥ balā teṣām tanvaḥ adya dadhātu me  
punar ehi vacaḥ pate devena manasā saha   vasoḥ pate ni ramaya mayi eva astu mayi śrutam  
iha eva abhi vi tanūbhe ārtnī iva jyayā   vācaḥ patiḥ ni yacchatu mayi eva astu mayi śrutam  
upahūtaḥ vācaḥ patiḥ upa asmān vācaspatiḥ hvayatām   sam śrutena gamemahi mā śrutena vi rādhiṣi  
vidma śarasya pitaram parjanyam bhūri dhāyasam   vidma u su asya mātaram pṛthivīm bhūri varpasam  
jyāke pari naḥ nama aśmānam tanvam kṛdhi   vīḍuḥ varīyaḥ arātīḥ apa dveṣāṃsi ā kṛdhi  
vṛkṣam yat gāvaḥ pariṣasvajānāḥ anusphuram śaram arcanti ṛbhum   śarum asmat yāvaya didyum indra  
yathā dyām ca pṛthivīm ca antar tiṣṭhati tejanam   eva rogam ca āsrāvam ca antar tiṣṭhatu muñjaḥ id  
vidma śarasya pitaram parjanyam śata vṛṣṇyam   tena te tanve śam karam pṛthivyām te niṣecanam bahis te astu bāl iti  
vidma śarasya pitaram mitram śata vṛṣṇyam   tena te tanve śam karam pṛthivyām te niṣecanam bahis te astu bāl iti  
vidma śarasya pitaram varuṇam śata vṛṣṇyam   tena te tanve śam karam pṛthivyām te niṣecanam bahis te astu bāl iti  
vidma śarasya pitaram candram śata vṛṣṇyam   tena te tanve śam karam pṛthivyām te niṣecanam bahis te astu bāl iti  
vidma śarasya pitaram sūryam śata vṛṣṇyam   tena te tanve śam karam pṛthivyām te niṣecanam bahis te astu bāl iti  
yat āntreṣu gavīnyoḥ yat vastau adhi saṃśritam   eva te mūtram mucyatām bahis bāl iti sarvakam  
pra te bhinadmi mehanam vartram veśantyāḥ iva   eva te mūtram mucyatām bahis bāl iti sarvakam  
viṣitam te vasti bilam samudrasya udadheḥ iva   eva te mūtram mucyatām bahis bāl iti sarvakam  
yathā iṣukā parāpatat avasṛṣṭā adhi dhanvanaḥ   eva te mūtram mucyatām bahis bāl iti sarvakam  
ambayaḥ yanti adhvabhiḥ jāmayaḥ adhvarīyatām   pṛñcatīḥ madhunā payaḥ  
amūḥ yāḥ upa sūrye yābhiḥ vā sūryaḥ saha   tāḥ naḥ hinvantu adhvaram  
apaḥ devīḥ upa hvaye yatra gāvaḥ pibanti naḥ   sindhubhyaḥ kartvam haviḥ  
apsu antar amṛtam apsu bheṣajam   apām uta praśastibhiḥ aśvāḥ bhavatha vājinaḥ gāvaḥ bhavatha vājinīḥ  
āpaḥ hi stha mayobhuvaḥ tāḥ naḥ ūrje dadhātana   mahe raṇāya cakṣase  
yaḥ vaḥ śivatamaḥ rasaḥ tasya bhājayata iha naḥ   uśatīḥ iva mātaraḥ  
tasmai aram gamāma vaḥ yasya kṣayāya jinvatha   āpaḥ janayatha ca naḥ  
īśānāḥ vāryāṇām kṣayantīḥ carṣaṇīnām   apaḥ yācāmi bheṣajam  
śam naḥ devīḥ abhiṣṭaye āpaḥ bhavantu pītaye   śam yos abhi sravantu naḥ  
apsu me somaḥ abravīt antar viśvāni bheṣajā   agnim ca viśva śaṃbhuvam  
āpaḥ pṛṇīta bheṣajam varūtham tanve mama  jyok ca sūryam dṛśe 
śam naḥ āpaḥ dhanvanyāḥ śam u santu anūpyāḥ   śam naḥ khanitrimāḥ āpaḥ śam u yāḥ kumbhe ābhṛtāḥ   śivāḥ naḥ santu vārṣikīḥ  
stuvānam agne ā vaha yātudhānam kimīdinam   tvam hi deva vanditaḥ hantā dasyoḥ babhūvitha  
ājyasya parameṣṭhin jātavedaḥ tanū vaśin   agne taulasya prāśāna yātudhānān vi lāpaya  
vi lapantu yātudhānāḥ attriṇaḥ ye kimīdinaḥ   atha idam agne naḥ haviḥ indraḥ ca prati haryatam  
agniḥ pūrvaḥ ā rabhatām pra indraḥ nudatu bāhumān   bravītu sarvaḥ yātumān ayam asmi iti etya  
paśyāma te vīryam jātavedaḥ pra naḥ brūhi yātudhānāt nṛ cakṣaḥ   tvayā sarve paritaptāḥ purastāt te ā yantu prabruvāṇāḥ upa idam  
ā rabhasva jātavedaḥ asmāka arthāya jajñiṣe   dūtaḥ naḥ agne bhūtvā yātudhānān vi lāpaya  
tvam agne yātudhānān upabaddhām iha ā vaha   atha eṣām indraḥ vajreṇa api śīrṣāṇi vṛścatu  
idam haviḥ yātudhānāt nādī phenam iva ā vahat   yaḥ idam strī pumān akaḥ iha saḥ stuvatām janaḥ  
ayam stuvānaḥ āgamat imam sma prati haryata   bṛhaspate vaśe labdhvā agnīṣomā vi vidhyatam  
yātudhānasya soma pa jahi prajām nayasva ca   ni stuvānasya pātaya param akṣi uta avaram  
yatra eṣām agne janimāni vettha guhā satām attriṇām jātavedaḥ   tān tvam brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānaḥ jahi eṣām śatatarham agne  
asmin vasu vasavaḥ dhārayantu indraḥ pūṣā varuṇaḥ mitraḥ agniḥ   imam ādityāḥ uta viśve ca devāḥ uttarasmin jyotiṣi dhārayantu  
asya devāḥ pradiśi jyotiḥ astu sūryaḥ agniḥ uta vā hiraṇyam   sapatnāḥ asmat adhare bhavantu uttamam nākam adhi rohaya imam  
yena indrāya samabharaḥ payāṃsi uttamena brahmaṇā jātavedaḥ   tena tvam agne iha vardhaya imam sajātānām śraiṣṭhye ā dhehi enam  
ā eṣām yajñam uta varcaḥ dade aham rāyaḥ poṣam uta cittāni agne   sapatnāḥ asmat adhare bhavantu uttamam nākam adhi rohaya imam  
ayam devānām asuraḥ vi rājati vaśā hi satyā varuṇasya rājñaḥ   tatas pari brahmaṇā śāśadānaḥ ugrasya manyoḥ ud imam nayāmi  
namaḥ te rajan varuṇa astu manyave viśvam hi ugra nicikeṣi drugdham   sahasram anyān pra suvāmi sākam śatam jīvāti śaradaḥ tava ayam  
yat uvaktha anṛtam jihvayā vṛjinam bahu   rājñaḥ tvā satya dharmaṇaḥ muñcāmi varuṇāt aham  
muñcāmi tvā vaiśvānarāt arṇavāt mahataḥ pari   sajātān ugra iha ā vada brahma ca apa cikīhi naḥ  
vaṣaṭ te pūṣan asmin sūtau aryamā hotā kṛṇotu vedhāḥ   sisratām nārī ṛta prajātā vi parvāṇi jihatām sūtavai u 
catasraḥ divaḥ pradiśaḥ catasraḥ bhūmyāḥ uta   devāḥ garbham sam airayan tam vi ūrṇuvantu sūtave  
sūṣā vi ūrṇotu vi yonim hāpayāmasi   śrathaya sūṣaṇe tvam ava tvam biṣkale sṛja  
na iva māṃse na pīvasi nā iva majjasu āhatam   avaitu pṛśni śevalam śune jarāyu attave ava jarāyu padyatām  
vi te bhinadmi mehanam vi yonim vi gavīnike   vi mātaram ca putram ca vi kumāram jarāyuṇā ava jarāyu padyatām  
yathā vātaḥ yathā manaḥ yathā patanti pakṣiṇaḥ   eva tvam daśamāsya sākam jarāyuṇā pata ava jarāyu padyatām  
jarāyu jaḥ prathamaḥ usriyaḥ vṛṣā vāta abhra jā stanayan eti vṛṣṭyā   sa naḥ mṛḍāti tanvaḥ ṛju gaḥ rujan yaḥ ekam ojaḥ tredhā vicakrame  
aṅge aṅge śociṣā śiśriyāṇam namasyantaḥ tvā haviṣā vidhema   aṅkān samaṅkān haviṣā vidhema yaḥ agrabhīt parvā asyāḥ grabhītā  
muñca śīrṣaktyai uta kāsaḥ enam paruḥ paruḥ āviveśa yaḥ asya   yaḥ abhra jāḥ vāta jāḥ yaḥ ca śuṣmaḥ vanaspatīn sacatām parvatān ca  
śam me parasmai gātrāya śam astu avarāya me   śam me caturbhyaḥ aṅgebhyaḥ śam astu tanve mama  
namaḥ te astu vidyute namaḥ te stanayitnave   namaḥ te astu aśmane yena dūḍāśe asyasi  
namaḥ te pravataḥ napāt yatas tapaḥ samūhasi   mṛḍaya naḥ tanūbhyaḥ mayaḥ tokebhyaḥ kṛdhi  
pravataḥ napāt namaḥ eva astu tubhyam namaḥ te hetaye tapuṣe ca kṛṇmaḥ   vidma te dhāma paramam guhā yat samudre antar nihitā asi nābhiḥ  
yām tvā devāḥ asṛjanta viśve iṣum kṛṇvānāḥ asanāya dhṛṣṇum   sā naḥ mṛḍa vidathe gṛṇānā tasyai te namaḥ astu devi  
bhagam asyāḥ varcaḥ ādiṣi adhi vṛkṣāt iva srajam   mahā budhnaḥ iva parvataḥ jyok pitṛṣu āstām  
eṣā te rājan kanyā vadhūḥ ni dhūyatām yama   sā mātuḥ badhyatām gṛhe atha u bhrātuḥ atha u pituḥ  
eṣā te kulapā rājan tām u te pari dadmasi   jyok pitṛṣu āsātai ā śīrṣṇaḥ śamopyāt  
asitasya te brahmaṇā kaśyapasya gayasya ca   antaḥkośam iva jāmayaḥ api nahyāmi te bhagam   
sam sam sravantu sindhavaḥ sam vātāḥ sam patatriṇaḥ   imam yajñam pradivaḥ me juṣantām saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi  
iha eva havam ā yāta me iha saṃsrāvaṇāḥ uta imam vardhayata giraḥ   iha etu sarvaḥ yaḥ paśuḥ asmin tiṣṭhatu yā rayiḥ  
ye nadīnām saṃsravanti utsāsaḥ sadam akṣitāḥ   tebhiḥ me sarvaiḥ saṃsrāvaiḥ dhanam sam srāvayāmasi  
ye sarpiṣaḥ saṃsravanti kṣīrasya ca udakasya ca
tebhiḥ me sarvaiḥ saṃsrāvaiḥ dhanam sam srāvayāmasi 
ye amāvāsyām rātrim udasthuḥ vrājam attriṇaḥ   agniḥ turīyaḥ yātu hā saḥ asmabhyam adhi bravat  
sīsāya adhi āha varuṇaḥ sīsāya agniḥ upāvati   sīsam me indraḥ prāyacchat tat aṅga yātu cātanam  
idam viṣkandham sahate idam bādhate attriṇaḥ   anena viśvā sasahe yā jātāni piśācyāḥ  
yadi naḥ gām haṃsi yadi aśvam yadi pūruṣam   tam tvā sīsena vidhyāmaḥ yathā naḥ asaḥ avīra hā  
amūḥ yāḥ yanti yoṣitaḥ hirāḥ lohita vāsasaḥ   abhrātaraḥ iva jāmayaḥ tiṣṭhantu hata varcasaḥ  
tiṣṭha avare tiṣṭha paras uta tvam tiṣṭha madhyame   kaniṣṭhikā ca tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhāt id dhamaniḥ mahī  
śatasya dhamanīnām sahasrasya hirāṇām   asthuḥ id madhyamāḥ imāḥ sākam antāḥ araṃsata  
pari vaḥ sikatāvatī dhanūḥ bṛhatī akramīt  tiṣṭhatā ilayatā su kam 
niḥ lakṣmyam lalāmyam niḥ arātim suvāmasi   atha yā bhadrā tāni naḥ prajāyāḥ arātim nayāmasi  
niḥ araṇim savitā sāviṣak padoḥ niḥ hastayoḥ varuṇaḥ mitraḥ aryamā   niḥ asmabhyam anumatiḥ rarāṇā pra imām devāḥ asāviṣuḥ saubhagāya  
yat te ātmani tanvām ghoram asti yat vā keśeṣu praticakṣaṇe vā   sarvam tat vācā apa hanmaḥ vayam devaḥ tvā savitā sūdayatu  
riśyapadīm vṛṣadatīm goṣedhām vidhamām uta   vilīḍhyam lalāmyam tāḥ asmat nāśayāmasi  
mā naḥ vidan vivyādhinaḥ mā u abhivyādhinaḥ vidan   ārāt śaravyāḥ asmat viṣūcīḥ indra pātaya  
viṣvañcaḥ asmat śaravaḥ patantu ye astāḥ ye ca asyāḥ   daivīḥ manuṣyesavaḥ mama amitrān vi vidhyata  
yaḥ naḥ svaḥ yaḥ araṇaḥ sajātaḥ uta niṣṭyaḥ yaḥ asmān abhidāsati   rudraḥ śaravyayā etān mama amitrān vi vidhyatu  
yaḥ sapatnaḥ yaḥ asapatnaḥ yaḥ ca dviṣan śapāti naḥ   devāḥ tam sarve dhūrvantu brahma varma mama antaram  
adāra sṛt bhavatu deva soma asmin yajñe marutaḥ mṛḍata naḥ   mā naḥ vidat abhibhā mā u aśastiḥ mā naḥ vidat vṛjinā dveṣyā yā  
yaḥ adya senyaḥ vadhaḥ aghāyūnām udīrate   yuvam tam mitrāvaruṇau asmat yāvayatam pari  
itas ca yat amutas ca yat vadham varuṇa yāvaya   vi mahat śarma yaccha varīyaḥ yāvaya vadham  
śāsaḥ itthā mahān asi amitra sāhaḥ a stṛtaḥ   na yasya hanyate sakhā na jīyate kadā cana  
svasti dāḥ viśām patiḥ vṛtra hā vimṛdhaḥ vaśī   vṛṣā indraḥ puras etu naḥ soma pāḥ abhayaṃkaraḥ  
vi naḥ indra mṛdhaḥ jahi nīcā yaccha pṛtanyataḥ   adhamam gamaya tamaḥ yaḥ asmām abhidāsati  
vi rakṣaḥ vi mṛdhaḥ jahi vi vṛtrasya hanū ruja   vi manyum indra vṛtrahan amitrasya abhidāsataḥ  
apa indra dviṣataḥ manaḥ apa jijyāsataḥ vadham   vi mahat śarma yaccha varīyaḥ yāvaya vadham  
anu sūryam ud ayatām hṛd dyotaḥ harimā ca te   goḥ rohitasya varṇena tena tvā pari dadhmasi  
pari tvā rohitaiḥ varṇaiḥ dīrgha āyu tvāya dadhmasi   yathā ayam arapāḥ asat atha u a haritaḥ bhuvat  
yāḥ rohiṇīḥ devatyāḥ gāvaḥ yāḥ uta rohiṇīḥ   rūpam rūpam vayaḥ vayaḥ tābhiḥ tvā pari dadhmasi  
śukeṣu te harimāṇam ropaṇākāsu dadhmasi   atha u hāridraveṣu te harimāṇam ni dadhmasi  
naktaṃjātā asi oṣadhe rāme kṛṣṇe asikni ca   idam rajani rajaya kilāsam palitam ca yat  
kilāsam ca palitam ca niḥ itas nāśaya pṛṣat   ā tvā svaḥ viśatām varṇaḥ parā śuklāni pātaya  
asitam te pralayanam āsthānam asitam tava   asiknī asi oṣadhe niḥ itas nāśaya pṛṣat  
asthi jasya kilāsasya tanū jasya ca yat tvaci   dūṣyā kṛtasya brahmaṇā lakṣma śvetam anīnaśam  
suparṇaḥ jātaḥ prathamaḥ tasya tvam pittam āsitha   tat āsurī yudhā jitā rūpam cakre vanaspatīn  
āsurī cakre prathamā idam kilāsa bheṣajam idam kilāsa nāśanam   anīnaśat kilāsam sarūpām akarat tvacam  
sarūpā nāma te mātā sarūpaḥ nāma te pitā   sarūpa kṛt tvam oṣadhe sā sarūpam idam kṛdhi  
śyāmā sarūpaṃkaraṇī pṛthivyāḥ adhi udbhṛtā   idam u su pra sādhaya punā rūpāṇi kalpaya  
yat agniḥ āpaḥ adahat praviśya yatra akṛṇvan dharma dhṛtaḥ namāṃsi   tatra te āhuḥ paramam janitram sa naḥ saṃvidvān pari vṛṅgdhi takman  
yadi arciḥ yadi vā asi śociḥ śakalyeṣi yadi vā te janitram   hrūḍuḥ nāma asi haritasya deva sa naḥ saṃvidvān pari vṛṅgdhi takman  
yadi śokaḥ yadi vā abhiśokaḥ yadi vā rājñaḥ varuṇasya asi putraḥ   hrūḍuḥ nāma asi haritasya deva sa naḥ saṃvidvān pari vṛṅgdhi takman  
namaḥ śītāya takmane namaḥ rūrāya śociṣe kṛṇomi   yaḥ anyedyus ubhayadyus abhyeti tṛtīyakāya namaḥ astu takmane  
āre asau asmat astu hetiḥ devāsaḥ asat   āre aśmā yam asyatha   āre aśmā yam asyatha  
sakhā asau asmabhyam astu rātiḥ sakhā indraḥ bhagaḥ   savitā citra rādhāḥ  
yūyam naḥ pravataḥ napāt marutaḥ sūrya tvacasaḥ   śarma yacchatha saprathāḥ  
suṣūdata mṛḍata mṛḍayā naḥ tanūbhyaḥ   mayaḥ tokebhyaḥ kṛdhi  
amūḥ pāre pṛdākvaḥ triṣaptāḥ nirjarāyavaḥ   tāsām jarāyubhiḥ vayam akṣyau api vyayāmasi aghāyoḥ paripanthinaḥ  
viṣūcī etu kṛntatī pinākam iva bibhratī   viṣvak punarbhuvā manaḥ asamṛddhāḥ aghāyavaḥ  
na bahavaḥ sam aśakat na arbhakāḥ abhi dādhṛṣuḥ   veṇoḥ adgāḥ iva abhitas asamṛddhāḥ aghāyavaḥ  
pretam pādau pra sphuratam vahatam pṛṇataḥ gṛhān   indrāni etu prathamā ajīta a muṣitā puras  
upa prāgāt devaḥ agniḥ rakṣaḥ hā amīva cātanaḥ   dahan apa dvayāvinaḥ yātudhānān kimīdinaḥ  
prati daha yātudhānān prati deva kimīdinaḥ   pratīcīḥ kṛṣṇavartane sam daha yātudhānyaḥ  
yā śaśāpa śapanena yā agham mūram ādadhe   yā rasasya haraṇāya jātam ārebhe tokam attu sā  
putram attu yātudhānīḥ svasāram uta naptyam   adhā mithas vikeśyaḥ vi ghnatām yātudhānyaḥ vi tṛhyantām arāyyaḥ  
abhīvartena maṇinā yena indraḥ abhivavṛdhe   tena asmān brahmaṇas pate abhi rāṣṭrāya vardhaya  
abhivṛtya sapatnān abhi yāḥ naḥ arātayaḥ   abhi pṛtanyantam tiṣṭha abhi yaḥ naḥ durasyati  
abhi tvā devaḥ savitā abhi ṣomaḥ avīvṛdhat   abhi tvā viśvā bhūtāni abhīvartaḥ yathā asasi  
abhīvartaḥ abhibhavaḥ sapatna kṣayaṇaḥ maṇiḥ   rāṣṭrāya mahyam badhyatām sapatnebhyaḥ parābhuve  
ud asau sūryaḥ agāt ud idam māmakam vacaḥ   yathā aham śatru haḥ asāni a sapatnaḥ sapatna hā  
sapatna kṣayaṇaḥ vṛṣā abhiraṣṭraḥ viṣāsahiḥ   yathā aham eṣām vīrāṇām virājāni janasya ca  
viśve devāḥ vasavaḥ rakṣata imam uta ādityāḥ jāgṛta yūyam asmin   mā imam sanābhiḥ uta vā anyanābhiḥ mā imam prāpat pauruṣeyaḥ vadhaḥ yaḥ  
ye vaḥ devāḥ pitaraḥ ye ca putrāḥ sacetasaḥ me śṛṇuta idam uktam   sarvebhyaḥ vaḥ pari dadāmi etam svasti enam jarase vahātha  
ye devāḥ divi ṣṭha ye pṛthivyām ye antarikṣe oṣadhīṣu paśuṣu apsu antar   te kṛṇuta jarasam āyuḥ asmai śatam anyān pari vṛṇaktu mṛtyūn  
yeṣām prayājāḥ uta vā anuyājāḥ huta bhāgāḥ a huta adaḥ ca devāḥ   yeṣām vaḥ pañca pradiśaḥ vibhaktāḥ tān vaḥ asmai satra sadaḥ kṛṇomi  
āśānām āśā pālebhyaḥ caturbhyaḥ amṛtebhyaḥ   idam bhūtasya adhyakṣebhyaḥ vidhema haviṣā vayam  
yaḥ āśānām āśā pālāḥ catvāraḥ sthana devāḥ   te naḥ nirṛtyāḥ pāśebhyaḥ muñcata aṃhasaḥ aṃhasaḥ  
a srāmaḥ tvā haviṣā yajāmi a śloṇaḥ tvā ghṛtena juhomi   yaḥ āśānām āśā pālaḥ turīyaḥ devaḥ sa naḥ su bhūtam ā iha vakṣat  
svasti mātre uta pitre naḥ astu svasti gobhyaḥ jagate puruṣebhyaḥ   viśvam su bhūtam suvidatram naḥ astu jyok eva dṛśema sūryam  
idam janāsaḥ vidatha mahat brahma vadiṣyati   na tat pṛthivyām naḥ divi yena prāṇanti vīrudhaḥ  
antarikṣe āsām sthāma śrānta sadām iva   āsthānam asya bhūtasya viduḥ tat vedhasaḥ na vā  
yat rodasī rejamāne bhūmiḥ ca niratakṣatam   ārdram tat adya sarvadā samudrasya iva śrotyāḥ  
viśvam anyām abhīvāra tat anyasyām adhi śritam   dive ca viśva vedase pṛthivyai ca akaram namaḥ  
hiraṇya varṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ yāsu jātaḥ savitā yāsu agniḥ   yāḥ agnim garbham dadhire suvarṇāḥ tāḥ naḥ āpaḥ śam syonāḥ bhavantu  
yāsām rājā varuṇaḥ yāti madhye satya anṛte avapaśyan janānām   yāḥ agnim garbham dadhire suvarṇāḥ tāḥ naḥ āpaḥ śam syonāḥ bhavantu  
yāsām devāḥ divi kṛṇvanti bhakṣam yāḥ antarikṣe bahudhā bhavanti   yāḥ agnim garbham dadhire suvarṇāḥ tāḥ naḥ āpaḥ śam syonāḥ bhavantu  
śivena mā cakṣuṣā paśyata apaḥ śivayā tanvā upa spṛśata tvacam me   ghṛtaścutaḥ śucayaḥ yāḥ pāvakāḥ tāḥ naḥ āpaḥ śam syonāḥ bhavantu  
iyam vīrudh madhu jātā madhunā tvā khanāmasi   madhoḥ adhi prajātā asi sā naḥ madhumataḥ kṛdhi  
jihvāyāḥ agre madhu me jihvā mūle madhūlakam   mama id aha kratau asaḥ mama cittam upāyasi  
madhumat me nikramaṇam madhumat me parāyaṇam   vācā vadāmi madhumat bhūyāsam madhu saṃdṛśaḥ  
madhoḥ asmi madhutaraḥ madughāt madhumattaraḥ   mām id kila tvam vanāḥ śākhām madhumatīm iva  
pari tvā paritatnunā ikṣuṇā āgām a vidviṣe   yathā mām kaminī asaḥ yathā mat na āpagāḥ asaḥ  
yat ābadhnan dākṣāyaṇāḥ hiraṇyam śatānīkāya sumanasyamānāḥ   tat te badnāmi āyuṣe varcase balāya dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya  
na enam rakṣāṃsi na piśācāḥ sahante devānām ojaḥ prathama jam hi etat   yaḥ bibharti dākṣāyaṇam hiraṇyam sa jīveṣu kṛṇute dīrgham āyuḥ  
apām tejaḥ jyotiḥ ojaḥ balam ca vanaspatīnām uta vīryāṇi   indraḥ iva indriyāṇi adhi dhārayāmaḥ asmin tat dakṣamāṇaḥ bibharat hiraṇyam  
samānām māsām ṛtubhiḥ tvā vayam saṃvatsarasya payasā piparmi   indra agnī viśve devāḥ te anu manyantām a hṛṇīyamānāḥ  
venaḥ tat paśyat paramam guhā yat yatra viśvam bhavati eka rūpam   idam pṛśniḥ aduhat jāyamānāḥ svarvidaḥ abhi anūṣata vrāḥ  
pra tat vocet amṛtasya vidvān gandharvaḥ dhāma paramam guhā yat   trīṇi padāni nihitā guhā asya yaḥ tāni veda sa pituḥ pitā asat  
sa naḥ pitā janitā saḥ uta bandhuḥ dhāmāni veda bhuvanāni viśvā   yaḥ devānām nāmadhe ekaḥ eva tam saṃpraśnam bhuvanā yanti sarvā  
pari dyāvāpṛthivī sadyas āyam upātiṣṭhe prathama jām ṛtasya   vācam iva vaktari bhuvaneṣṭhāḥ dhāsyuḥ eṣa nanu eṣaḥ agniḥ  
pari viśvā bhuvanāni āyam ṛtasya tantum vitatam dṛśe kam   yatra devāḥ amṛtam ānaśānāḥ samāne yonau adhi airayanta  
divyaḥ gandharvaḥ bhuvanasya yaḥ patiḥ ekaḥ eva namasyaḥ vikṣu īḍyaḥ   tam tvā yaumi brahmaṇā divya deva namaḥ te astu divi te sadhastham  
divi spṛṣṭaḥ yajataḥ sūrya tvac avayātā harasaḥ daivyasya   mṛḍāt gandharvaḥ bhuvanasya yaḥ patiḥ ekaḥ eva namasyaḥ su śevāḥ  
anavadyābhiḥ sam u jagme ābhiḥ apsarāsu api gandharvaḥ āsīt   samudraḥ āsām sadanam me āhuḥ yatas sadyas ā ca parā ca yanti  
abhriye didyut nakṣatriye yā viśvāvasum gandharvam sacadhve   tābhyaḥ vaḥ devīḥ namaḥ id kṛṇomi  
yāḥ klandāḥ tamiṣīcayaḥ akṣa kāmāḥ manomuhaḥ   tābhyaḥ gandharvabhyaḥ apsarābhyaḥ akaram namaḥ  
adaḥ yat avadhāvati avatkam adhi parvatāt   tat te kṛṇomi bheṣajam su bheṣajam yathā asasi  
āt aṅgā kuvid aṅga śatam yā bheṣajāni te   teṣām asi tvam uttamam anāsrāvam arogaṇam  
nīcais khananti asurāḥ arusrāṇam idam mahat   tat āsrāvasya bheṣajam tat u rogam anīnaśat  
upajīkāḥ ud bharanti samudrāt adhi bheṣajam   tat āsrāvasya bheṣajam tat u rogam aśīśamat  
arusrāṇam idam mahat pṛthivyāḥ adhi udbhṛtam   tat āsrāvasya bheṣajam tat u rogam anīnaśat  
śam naḥ bhavantu apaḥ oṣadhayaḥ śivāḥ   indrasya vajraḥ apa hantu rakṣasaḥ ārāt visṛṣṭāḥ iṣavaḥ patantu rakṣasām  
dīrgha āyu tvāya bṛhate raṇāya ariṣyantaḥ dakṣamāṇāḥ sadā eva   maṇim viṣkandha dūṣaṇam jaṅgiḍam bibhṛmaḥ vayam  
jaṅgiḍaḥ jambhāt viśarāt viṣkandhāt abhiśocanāt   maṇiḥ sahasra vīryaḥ pari naḥ pātu viśvatas  
ayam viṣkandham sahate ayam bādhate attriṇaḥ   ayam naḥ viśva bheṣajaḥ jaṅgiḍaḥ pātu aṃhasaḥ  
devaiḥ dattena maṇinā jaṅgiḍena mayobhuvā   viṣkandham sarvāḥ rakṣāṃsi vyāyāme sahāmahe  
śaṇaḥ ca mā jaṅgiḍaḥ ca viṣkandhāt abhi rakṣatām   araṇyāt anyaḥ ābhṛtaḥ kṛṣyāḥ anyaḥ rasebhyaḥ  
kṛtyā dūṣiḥ ayam maṇiḥ atha u arāti dūṣiḥ   atha u sahasvān jaṅgiḍaḥ pra naḥ āyuṃṣi tāriṣat  
indra juṣasva pra vaha yāhi śūra haribhyām   pibā sutasya mateḥ iha madhoḥ cakānaḥ cāruḥ madāya  
indra jaṭharam navyaḥ na pṛṇasva madhoḥ divaḥ na   asya sutasya svar na upa tvā madāḥ su vācaḥ aguḥ  
indraḥ turāṣāh mitraḥ vṛtram yaḥ jaghāna yatīḥ na   bibheda valam bhṛguḥ na sasahe śatrūn made somasya  
ā tvā viśantu sutāsaḥ indra pṛṇasva kukṣī viḍḍhi śakra dhiyā ihi ā naḥ   śrudhi havam giraḥ me juṣasva indra sva yugbhiḥ matsva iha mahe raṇāya  
indrasya nu pra vocam vīryāṇi yāni cakāra prathamāni vajrī   ahan ahim anu apaḥ tatarda pra vakṣaṇāḥ abhinat parvatānām  
ahan ahim parvate śiśriyāṇam tvaṣṭā asmai vajram svaryam tatakṣa   vāśrāḥ iva dhenavaḥ syandamānāḥ añjaḥ samudram ava jagmuḥ āpaḥ  
vṛṣāyamāṇaḥ avṛṇīta somam trikadrukeṣu apibat sutasya   ā sāyakam maghavā adatta vajram ahan enam prathama jām ahīnām  
samāḥ tvā agne ṛtavaḥ vardhayantu saṃvatsarāḥ ṛṣayaḥ yāni satyā   sam divyena dīdihi rocanena viśvāḥ ā māhi pradiśaḥ catasraḥ  
sam ca idhyasva agne pra ca vardhaya imam ud ca tiṣṭha mahate saubhagāya   mā te riṣan upasattāraḥ agne brahmāṇaḥ te yaśasaḥ santu mānye  
tvām agne vṛṇate brāhmaṇāḥ ime śivaḥ agne saṃvaraṇe bhava naḥ   sapatna hā agne abhimāti jit bhava sve gaye jāgṛhi aprayuchan  
kṣatreṇa agne svena sam rabhasva mitreṇa agne mitradhā yatasva   sajātānām madhyameṣṭhāḥ rājñām agne vihavyaḥ dīdihi iha  
ati nihaḥ ati sṛdhaḥ ati acittīḥ ati dviṣaḥ   viśvā hi agne duritā tara tvam atha asmabhyam saha vīram rayim dāḥ  
agha dviṣṭā deva jātā vīrudh śapatha yopanī   āpaḥ malam iva prāṇaikṣīt sarvān mat śapathām adhi  
yaḥ ca sāpatnaḥ śapathaḥ jāmyāḥ śapathaḥ ca yaḥ   brahmā yat manyutaḥ śapāt sarvam tat naḥ adhaspadam  
divaḥ mūlam avatatam pṛthivyāḥ adhi uttatam   tena sahasra kāṇḍena pari naḥ pāhi viśvatas  
pari mām pari me prajām pari naḥ pāhi yat dhanam   arātiḥ naḥ mā tārīt mā naḥ tāriśuḥ abhimātayaḥ  
śaptāram etu śapathaḥ yaḥ su hārd tena naḥ saha   cakṣuḥ mantrasya durhārdaḥ pṛṣṭīḥ api śṛṇīmasi  
ud agātām bhagavatī vicṛtau nāma tārake   vi kṣetriyasya muñcatām adhamam pāśam uttamam  
apa iyam rātriḥ uchatu apochantu abhikṛtvarīḥ   vīrudh kṣetriya nāśanī apa kṣetriyam uchatu  
babhroḥ arjuna kāṇḍasya yavasya te palālyā tilasya tila piñjyā   vīrudh kṣetriya nāśanī apa kṣetriyam uchatu  
namaḥ te lāṅgalebhyaḥ namaḥ īṣā yugebhyaḥ   vīrudh kṣetriya nāśanī apa kṣetriyam uchatu  
namaḥ sanisrasa akṣebhyaḥ namaḥ saṃdeśyebhyaḥ   namaḥ kṣetrasya pataye vīrudh kṣetriya nāśanī apa kṣetriyam uchatu  
daśa vṛkṣa muñca imam rakṣasaḥ grāhyāḥ adhi yā enam jagrāha parvasu   atha u enam vanaspate jīvānām lokam ud naya  
āgāt ud agāt ayam jīvānām vrātam api agāt   abhūt u putrāṇām pitā nṛṇām ca bhagavattamaḥ  
adhītīḥ adhi agāt ayam adhi jīva purāḥ agān   śatam hi asya bhiṣajaḥ sahasram uta vīrudhaḥ  
devāḥ te cītim avidan brahmāṇaḥ uta vīrudhaḥ   cītim te viśve devāḥ avidan bhūmyām adhi  
yaḥ cakāra sa niḥ karat saḥ eva subhiṣaktamaḥ   saḥ eva tubhyam bheṣajāni kṛṇavat bhiṣajā śuciḥ  
kṣetriyāt tvā nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
śam te agniḥ saha adbhiḥ astu śam somaḥ saha oṣadhībhiḥ   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
śam te vātaḥ antarikṣe vayaḥ dhāt śam te bhavantu pradiśaḥ catasraḥ   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
imāḥ yāḥ devīḥ pradiśaḥ catasraḥ vāta patnīḥ abhi sūryaḥ vicaṣṭe   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛnomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
tāsu tvā antar jarasi ā dadhāmi pra yakṣmaḥ etu nirṛtiḥ parācais   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
amukthāḥ yakṣmāt duritāt avadyāt druhaḥ pāśāt grāhyāḥ ca ud amukthāḥ   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
ahar arātim avidaḥ syonam api abhūḥ bhadre su kṛtasya loke   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
sūryam ṛtam tamasaḥ grāhyāḥ adhi devāḥ muñcantaḥ asṛjan niḥ enasaḥ   eva aham tvām kṣetriyāt nirṛtyāḥ jāmi śaṃsāt druhaḥ muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt   anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
dūṣyāḥ dūṣiḥ asi hetyāḥ hetiḥ asi menyāḥ meniḥ asi   āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samam krāma  
sraktyaḥ asi pratisaraḥ asi pratyabhicaraṇaḥ asi   āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samam krāma  
prati tam abhi cara yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samam krāma  
sūriḥ asi varcaḥ dhāḥ asi tanū pānaḥ asi   āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samam krāma  
śukraḥ asi bhrājaḥ asi svar asi jyotiḥ asi   āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samam krāma  
dyāvāpṛthivī uru antarikṣam kṣetrasya patnī uru gāyaḥ adbhutaḥ   uta antarikṣam uru vāta gopam te iha tapyantām mayi tapyamāne  
idam devāḥ śṛṇuta ye yajñiyāḥ stha bharadvājaḥ mahyam ukthāni śaṃsati   pāśe sa baddhaḥ durite ni yujyatām yaḥ asmākam manaḥ idam hinasti  
idam indra śṛṇuhi somapa yat tvā hṛdā śocatā johavīmi   vṛścāmi tam kuliśena iva vṛkṣam yaḥ asmākam manaḥ idam hinasti  
aśītibhiḥ tisṛbhiḥ sāmagebhiḥ ādityebhiḥ vasubhiḥ aṅgirobhiḥ   iṣṭāpūrtam avatu naḥ pitṝṇām ā amum dade harasā daivyena  
dyāvāpṛthivī anu mā dīdhīthām viśve devāsaḥ anu mā rabhadhvam   aṅgirasaḥ pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ pāpam ā ṛchatu apakāmasya kartā  
atīva yaḥ marutaḥ manyate naḥ brahma vā yaḥ nindiṣat kriyamāṇam   tapūṃṣi tasmai vṛjināni santu brahma dviṣam dyauḥ abhisaṃtapāti  
sapta prāṇān aṣṭau manyaḥ tān te vṛścāmi brahmaṇā   ayāḥ yamasya sādanam agni dūtaḥ araṃkṛtaḥ  
ā dadhāmi te padam samiddhe jātavedasi   agniḥ śarīram veveṣṭu asum vāc api gacchatu  
āyuḥ dāḥ agne jarasam vṛṇānaḥ ghṛta pratīkaḥ ghṛta pṛṣṭhaḥ agne   ghṛtam pītvā madhu cāru gavyam pitā iva putrān abhi rakṣatāt imam  
pari dhatta dhatta naḥ varcasā imam jarā mṛtyum kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ   bṛhaspatiḥ prāyacchat vāsaḥ etat somāya rājñe paridhātavai u 
pari idam vāsaḥ adhithāḥ svastaye abhūḥ gṛṣṭīnām abhiśasti pāḥ u  śatam ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcī rāyaḥ ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva  
ehi aśmānam ā tiṣṭha aśmā bhavatu te tanūḥ   kṛṇvantu viśve devāḥ āyuḥ te śaradaḥ śatam  
yasya te vāsaḥ prathama vāsyam harāmaḥ tam tvā viśve avantu devāḥ   tam tvā bhrātaraḥ suvṛdhāḥ vardhamānam anu jāyantām bahavaḥ su jātam  
niḥsālām dhṛṣṇum dhiṣaṇam ekavādyām jighatsvam   sarvāḥ caṇḍasya naptyaḥ nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ  
niḥ vaḥ goṣṭhāt ajāmasi niḥ akṣāt niḥ upānaśāt   niḥ vaḥ magundyāḥ duhitaraḥ gṛhebhyaḥ cātayāmahe  
asau yaḥ adharāt gṛhaḥ tatra santu arāyyaḥ   tatra sediḥ ni ucyatu sarvāḥ ca yātudhānyaḥ  
bhūta patiḥ niḥ ajatu indraḥ ca itas sadānvāḥ   gṛhasya budhne āsīnāḥ tāḥ indraḥ vajreṇa adhi tiṣṭhatu  
yadi stha kṣetriyāṇām yadi vā puruṣa iṣitāḥ   yadi stha dasyubhyaḥ jātāḥ naśyata itas sadānvāḥ  
pari dhāmāni āsām āśuḥ gāṣṭhām iva asaram   ajaiṣam sarvān ājīn vaḥ naśyata itas sadānvāḥ  
yathā dyauḥ ca pṛthivī ca na bibhītaḥ na riṣyataḥ   eva me prāṇa mā bibheḥ  
yathā ahar ca rātrī ca na bibhītaḥ na riṣyataḥ   eva me prāṇa mā bibheḥ  
yathā sūryaḥ ca candraḥ ca na bibhītaḥ na riṣyataḥ   eva me prāṇa mā bibheḥ  
yathā brahma ca kṣatram ca na bibhītaḥ na riṣyataḥ   eva me prāṇa mā bibheḥ  
yathā satyam ca anṛtam ca na bibhītaḥ na riṣyataḥ   eva me prāṇa mā bibheḥ  
yathā bhūtam ca bhavyam ca na bibhītaḥ na riṣyataḥ   eva me prāṇa mā bibheḥ  
prāṇa apānau mṛtyoḥ mā pātam svāhā 
dyāvāpṛthivī upaśrutya mā pātam svāhā 
sūrya cakṣuṣā mā pāhi svāhā 
agne vaiśvānara viśvaiḥ mā devaiḥ pāhi svāhā 
viśvambhara viśvena mā bharasā pāhi svāhā 
ojaḥ asi ojaḥ me dāḥ svāhā 
sahaḥ asi sahaḥ me dāḥ svāhā 
balam asi balam dāḥ svāhā 
āyuḥ asi āyuḥ me dāḥ svāha 
śrotram asi śrotram me dāḥ svāha  
cakṣuḥ asi cakṣuḥ me dāḥ svāha  
paripāṇam asi paripāṇam me dāḥ svāha  
bhrātṛvya kṣayaṇam asi bhrātṛvya cātanam me dāḥ svāha  
sapatna kṣayaṇam asi sapatna cātanam me dāḥ svāha  
arāya kṣayaṇam asi arāya cātanam me dāḥ svāha  
piśāca kṣayaṇam asi piśāca cātanam me dāḥ svāha  
sadānvā kṣayaṇam asi sadānvā cātanam me dāḥ svāha  
agne yat te tapaḥ tena tam prati tapa yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
agne yat te haraḥ tena tam prati hara yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
agne yat te arciḥ tena tam prati arca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
agne yat te śociḥ tena tam prati śoca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
agne yat te tejaḥ tena tam atejasam kṛṇu yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
vāyo yat te tapaḥ tena tam prati tapa yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
vāyo yat te haraḥ tena tam prati hara yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
vāyo yat te arciḥ tena tam prati arca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
vāyo yat te śociḥ tena tam prati śoca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
vāyo yat te tejaḥ tena tam atejasam kṛṇu yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ  
sūrya yat te tapaḥ tena tam prati tapa yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
sūrya yat te haraḥ tena tam prati hara yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
sūrya yat te arciḥ tena tam prati arca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
sūrya yat te śociḥ tena tam prati śoca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
sūrya yat te tejaḥ tena tam atejasam kṛṇu yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ  
candra yat te tapaḥ tena tam prati tapa yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
candra yat te haraḥ tena tam prati hara yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
candra yat te arciḥ tena tam prati arca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
candra yat te śociḥ tena tam prati śoca yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
candra yat te tejaḥ tena tam atejasam kṛṇu yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
āpaḥ yat vaḥ tapaḥ tena tam prati tapata yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
āpaḥ yat vaḥ haraḥ tena tam prati harata yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
āpaḥ yat vaḥ arciḥ tena tam prati arcata yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
āpaḥ yat vaḥ śociḥ tena tam prati śocata yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ 
āpaḥ yat vaḥ tejaḥ tena tam atejasam kṛṇuta yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ  
śerabhaka śerabha punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
śevṛdhaka śevṛdha punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
mroka anumroka punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
sarpa anusarpa punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
jūrṇi punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
upabde punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
arjuni punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
bharūji punar vaḥ yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ   yasya stha tam atta yaḥ vaḥ prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāni atta  
śam naḥ devī pṛśniparṇī aśam nirṛtyāḥ akaḥ   ugrā hi kaṇva jambhanī tām abhakṣi sahasvatīm  
sahamānā iyam prathamā pṛśniparṇī ajāyata   tayā aham durṇāmnām śiraḥ vṛścāmi śakuneḥ iva  
arāyam asṛk pāvānam yaḥ ca sphātim jihīrṣati   garbha adam kaṇvam nāśaya pṛśniparṇi sahasva ca  
girim enām ā veśaya kaṇvān jīvita yopanān   tān tvam devi pṛśniparṇī agniḥ iva anudahan ihi  
parācaḥ enān pra nuda kaṇvān jīvita yopanān   tamāṃsi yatra gacchanti tat kravya adaḥ ajīgamam  
ā iha yantu paśavaḥ ye pareyuḥ vāyuḥ yeṣām sahacāram jujoṣa   tvaṣṭā yeṣām rūpadheyāni veda asmin tān goṣṭhe savitā ni yacchatu  
imam goṣṭham paśavaḥ sam sravantu bṛhaspatiḥ ā nayatu prajānan   sinīvālī nayatu ā agram eṣām ājagmuṣaḥ anumate ni yaccha  
sam sam sravantu paśavaḥ sam aśvāḥ sam u pūruṣāḥ   sam dhānyasya yā sphātiḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi  
sam siñcāmi gavām kṣīram sam ājyena balam rasam   saṃsiktāḥ asmākam vīrāḥ dhruvāḥ gāvaḥ mayi gopatau  
ā harāmi gavām kṣīram āhārṣam dhānyam rasam   āhṛtāḥ asmākam vīrāḥ ā patnīḥ idam astakam  
na id śatruḥ prāśam jayāti sahamānā abhibhūḥ asi   prāśam pratiprāśaḥ jahi arasān kṛṇu oṣadhe  
suparṇaḥ tvā anu avindat sūkaraḥ tvā akhanat nasā   prāśam pratiprāśaḥ jahi arasān kṛṇu oṣadhe  
indraḥ ha cakre tvā bāhau asurebhyaḥ starītave   prāśam pratiprāśaḥ jahi arasān kṛṇu oṣadhe  
pāṭām indraḥ vi āśnāt asurebhyaḥ starītave   prāśam pratiprāśaḥ jahi arasān kṛṇu oṣadhe  
tayā aham śatrūn sa akṣaḥ indraḥ sa alāvṛkān iva   prāśam pratiprāśaḥ jahi arasān kṛṇu oṣadhe  
rudra jalāṣa bheṣaja nīlaśikhaṇḍa karma kṛt   prāśam pratiprāśaḥ jahi arasān kṛṇu oṣadhe  
tasya prāśam tvam jahi yaḥ naḥ indra abhidāsati   adhi naḥ brūhi śaktibhiḥ prāśi mām uttaram kṛdhi  
tubhyam eva jariman vardhatām ayam mā imam anye mṛtyavaḥ hiṃsiṣuḥ śatam ye   mātā iva putram pramanāḥ upasthe mitraḥ enam mitriyāt pātu aṃhasaḥ  
mitraḥ enam varuṇaḥ vā riśādāḥ jarā mṛtyum kṛṇutām saṃvidānau   tat agniḥ hotā vayunāni vidvān viśvā devānām janimā vivakti  
tvam īśiṣe paśūnām pārthivānām ye jātāḥ uta vā ye janitrāḥ   mā imam prāṇaḥ ha āsīt mā u apānaḥ mā imam mitrāḥ vadhiṣuḥ mā u amitrāḥ  
dyauḥ tvā pitā pṛthivī mātā jarā mṛtyum kṛṇutām saṃvidāne   yathā jīvāḥ aditeḥ upasthe prāṇa apānābhyām gupitaḥ śatam himāḥ  
imam agne āyuṣe varcase naya priyam retaḥ varuṇa mitra rājan   mātā iva asmai adite śarma yaccha viśve devāḥ jaradaṣṭiḥ yathā asat  
pārthivasya rase devāḥ bhagasya tanvaḥ bale   āyuṣyam asmai agniḥ sūryaḥ varcaḥ ā dhāt bṛhaspatiḥ  
āyuḥ asmai dhehi jātavedaḥ prajām tvaṣṭar adhinidhehi asmai   rāyaḥ poṣam savitar ā suva asmai śatam jīvāti śaradaḥ tava ayam  
āśīḥ naḥ ūrjam uta sauprajāstvam dakṣam dhattam draviṇam sacetasau   jayam kṣetrāṇi sahasā ayam indra kṛṇvānaḥ anyān adharān sapatnān  
indreṇa dattaḥ varuṇena śiṣṭaḥ marudbhiḥ ugraḥ prahitaḥ naḥ āgan   eṣa vām dyāvāpṛthivī upasthe mā kṣudhat mā tṛṣat  
ūrjam asmai ūrjasvatī dhattam payaḥ asmai payasvatī dhattam   ūrjam asmai dyāvapṛthivī adhātām viśve devāḥ marutaḥ ūrjam āpaḥ  
śivābhiḥ te hṛdayam tarpayāmi anamīvaḥ modiṣṭhāḥ su varcāḥ   sa vāsinau pibatām mantham etam aśvinaḥ rūpam paridhāya māyām  
indraḥ etām sasṛje viddhaḥ agre ūrjām svadhām ajarām sā te eṣā   tayā tvam jīva śaradaḥ su varcāḥ mā te ā susrot bhiṣajaḥ te akran  
yathā idam bhūmyāḥ adhi tṛṇam vātaḥ mathāyati   eva ā mathnāmi te manaḥ yathā mām kāminī asaḥ yathā mat na āpagāḥ asaḥ  
sam ced nayāthaḥ aśvinā kāminā sam ca vakṣathaḥ   sam vām bhagāsaḥ agmata sam cittāni sam u vratā  
yat suparṇāḥ vivakṣavaḥ anamīvāḥ vivakṣavaḥ   tatra me gacchatāt dhavam śalyaḥ iva kulmalam yathā  
yat antaram tat bāhyam yat bāhyam tat antaram   kanyānām viśva rūpāṇām manaḥ gṛbhāya auṣadhe  
ā iyam agan pati kāmā jani kāmaḥ aham āgamam   aśvaḥ kanikradat yathā bhagena aham saha agamam  
indrasya yā mahī dṛṣat krimeḥ viśvasya tarhaṇī   tayā pinaṣmi sam krimīn dṛṣadā khalvān iva  
dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam atṛham atho kurūrum atṛham   algaṇḍūn sarvān śalunān krimīn vacasā jambhayāmasi  
algaṇḍūn hanmi mahatā vadhena dūnāḥ adūnāḥ arasāḥ abhūvan   śiṣṭān aśiṣṭān ni tirāmi vācā yathā krimīṇām nakir ucchiṣātai  
anvāntryam śīrṣaṇyam atho pārṣṭeyam krimīn   avaskavam vyadhvaram krimīn vacasā jambhayāmasi  
ye krimayaḥ parvata īśu vaneṣu oṣadhīṣu paśuṣu apsu antar   ye asmākam tanvam āviviśuḥ sarvam tat dhanmi janima krimīṇām  
udyan ādityaḥ krimīn hantu nimrocan hantu raśmibhiḥ   ye antar krimayaḥ gavi  
viśva rūpam catur akṣam krimim sāraṅgam arjunam   śṛṇāmi asya pṛṣṭīḥ api vṛścāmi yat śiraḥ  
atri vat vaḥ krimayaḥ hanmi kaṇva vat jamadagni vat   agastyasya brahmaṇā sam pinaṣmi aham krimīn  
hataḥ rājā krimīṇām uta eṣām sthapatiḥ hataḥ   hataḥ hata mātā krimiḥ hata bhrātā hata svasā  
hatāsaḥ asya veśasaḥ hatāsaḥ pariveśasaḥ   atho ye kṣullakāḥ iva sarve te krimayaḥ hatāḥ  
pra te śṛṇāmi śṛṅge yābhyām vitudāyasi   bhinādmi te kuṣumbham yaḥ te viṣa dhānaḥ  
akṣībhyām te nāsikābhyām karṇābhyām chubukāt adhi   yakṣmam śīrṣaṇyam mastiṣkāt jihvāyāḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
grīvābhyaḥ te uṣṇihābhyaḥ kīkasābhyaḥ anūkyāt   yakṣmam doṣaṇyam aṃsābhyām bāhubhyām vi vṛhāmi te  
hṛdayāt te pari klomnaḥ halīkṣṇāt pārśvābhyām   yakṣmam matasnābhyām plīhnaḥ yaknaḥ te vi vṛhāmasi  
āntrebhyaḥ te gudābhyaḥ vaniṣṭhoḥ udarāt adhi   yakṣmam kukṣibhyām plāśeḥ nābhyāḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
ūrubhyām te aṣṭhīvadbhyām pārṣṇibhyām prapadābhyām   yakṣmam bhasadyam śroṇibhyām bhāsadam bhaṃsasaḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
asthibhyaḥ te majjabhyaḥ snāvabhyaḥ dhamanibhyaḥ   yakṣmam pāṇibhyām aṅgulibhyaḥ nakhebhyaḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
aṅge aṅge lomni lomni yaḥ te parvaṇi parvaṇi   yakṣmam tvacasyam te vayam kaśyapasya vībarheṇa viṣvañcam vi vṛhāmasi  
yaḥ īśe paśupatiḥ paśūnām catuṣpadām uta yaḥ dvipadām   niṣkrītaḥ sa yajñiyam bhāgam etu rāyaḥ poṣāḥ yajamānam sacantām  
pramuñcantaḥ bhuvanasya retaḥ gātum dhatta yajamānāya devāḥ   upākṛtam śaśamānam yat asthāt priyam devānām api etu pāthaḥ  
ye badhyamānam anu dīdhyānāḥ anvaikṣanta manasā cakṣuṣā ca   agniḥ tān agre pra mumoktu devaḥ viśvakarmā prajayā saṃrarāṇaḥ  
ye grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ viśva rūpāḥ virūpāḥ santaḥ bahudhā eka rūpāḥ   vāyuḥ tān agre pra mumoktu devaḥ prajāpatiḥ prajayā saṃrarāṇaḥ  
prajānantaḥ prati gṛhṇantu pūrve prāṇam aṅgebhyaḥ pari ācarantam   divam gaccha prati tiṣṭha śarīraiḥ svargam yāhi pathibhiḥ deva yānaiḥ  
ye bhakṣayantaḥ na vasūni ānṛdhuḥ yān agnayaḥ anvatapyanta dhiṣṇyāḥ   yā teṣām avayā duriṣṭiḥ su iṣṭim naḥ tām kṛṇavat viśvakarmā  
yajñapatim ṛṣayaḥ enasā āhuḥ nirbhaktam prajāḥ anutapyamānam   mathavyān stokān apa yān rarādha sam naḥ tebhiḥ sṛjatu viśvakarmā  
adānyān soma pād manyamānaḥ yajñasya vidvān samaye na dhīraḥ   yat enaḥ cakṛvān baddhaḥ eṣa tam viśvakarman pra muñca svastaye  
ghorāḥ ṛṣayaḥ namaḥ astu ebhyaḥ cakṣuḥ yat eṣām manasaḥ ca satyam   bṛhaspataye mahiṣa dyuman namaḥ viśvakarman namaḥ te pāhi asmān  
yajñasya cakṣuḥ prabhṛtiḥ mukham ca vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi   imam yajñam vitatam viśvakarmaṇā devāḥ yantu sumanasyamānāḥ  
ā naḥ agne sumatim saṃbhalaḥ gamet imām kumārīm saha naḥ bhagena   juṣṭā vareṣu samaneṣu valguḥ oṣam patyā saubhagam astu asyai  
soma juṣṭam brahma juṣṭam aryamnā saṃbhṛtam bhagam   dhātuḥ devasya satyena kṛṇomi pati vedanam  
iyam agne nārī patim videṣṭa somaḥ hi rājā subhagām kṛṇoti   suvānā putrān mahiṣī bhavāti gatvā patim subhagā vi rājatu  
yathā ākharaḥ maghavan cāruḥ eṣa priyaḥ mṛgāṇām suṣadā babhūva   eva bhagasya juṣṭā iyam astu nārī saṃpriyā patyā avirādhayantī  
bhagasya nāvam ā roha pūrṇām anupadasvatīm   tayā upapratāraya yaḥ varaḥ pratikāmyaḥ  
ā krandaya dhanapate varam āmanasam kṛṇu   sarvam pradakṣiṇam kṛṇu yaḥ varaḥ pratikāmyaḥ  
idam hiraṇyam gulgulu ayam aukṣaḥ atho bhagaḥ   ete patibhyaḥ tvām aduḥ pratikāmāya vettave   
ā te nayatu savitā nayatu patiḥ yaḥ pratikāmyaḥ   agniḥ naḥ śatrūn prati etu vidvān pratidahan abhiśastim arātim   sa senām mohayatu pareṣām nirhastān ca kṛṇavat jātavedāḥ  
yūyam ugrāḥ marutaḥ īdṛśe stha abhi preta mṛṇata sahadhvam   amīmṛṇan vasavaḥ nāthitāḥ ime agniḥ hi eṣām dūtaḥ pratyetu vidvān  
amitra senām maghavan asmān śatrūyatīm abhi   yuvam tām indra vṛtrahan agniḥ ca dahatam prati  
prasūtaḥ indra pravata haribhyām pra te vajraḥ pramṛṇan etu śatrūn   jahi pratīcaḥ anūcaḥ parācaḥ viṣvak satyam kṛṇuhi cittam eṣām  
indra senām mohaya amitrāṇām   agneḥ vātasya dhrājyā tān viṣūcaḥ vi nāśaya  
indraḥ senām mohayatu marutaḥ ghnantu ojasā   cakṣūṃsi agniḥ ā dattām punar etu parājitā  
agniḥ naḥ dūtaḥ pratyetu vidvān pratidahan abhiśastim arātim   sa cittāni mohayatu pareṣām nirhastān ca kṛṇavat jātavedāḥ  
ayam agniḥ amūmuhat yāni cittāni vaḥ hṛdi   vi vaḥ dhamatu okasaḥ pra vaḥ dhamatu sarvatas  
indra cittāni mohayan arvāṅ ākūtyā cara   agneḥ vātasya dhrājyā tān viṣūcaḥ vi nāśaya  
vi ākūtayaḥ eṣām ita atho cittāni muhyata   atha u yat adya eṣām hṛdi tat eṣām pari niḥ jahi  
amīṣām cittāni pratimohayantī gṛhāṇa aṅgāni apve parehi   abhi prehi niḥ daha hṛtsu śokaiḥ grāhya amitrān tamasā vidhya śatrūn  
asau yā senā marutaḥ pareṣām asmān aiti abhi ojasā spardhamānā   tām vidhyata tamasā apavratena yathā eṣām anyaḥ anyam na jānāt  
acikradat su apāḥ iha bhuvat agne vi acasva rodasī urūcī   yuñjantu tvā marutaḥ viśva vedasaḥ ā amum naya namasā rāta havyam  
dūre cit santam aruṣāsaḥ indram ā cyāvayantu sakhyāya vipram   yat gāyatrīm bṛhatīm arkam asmai sautrāmaṇyā dadhṛṣanta devāḥ  
adbhyaḥ tvā rāja varuṇaḥ hvayatu somaḥ tvā hvayatu parvatebhyaḥ   indraḥ tvā hvayatu viḍbhyaḥ ābhyaḥ śyenaḥ bhūtvā viśaḥ ā pata imāḥ  
śyenaḥ havyam nayatu ā parasmāt anya kṣetre aparuddham carantam   aśvinā panthām kṛṇutām sugam te imam sajātāḥ abhisaṃviśadhvam   
hvayantu tvā pratijanāḥ prati mitrāḥ avṛṣata   indra agnī viśve devāḥ te viśi kṣemam adīdharan     
yaḥ te havam vivadat sajātaḥ yaḥ ca niṣṭyaḥ   apāñcam indra tam kṛtvā atha imam iha ava gamaya                                                                                                                                                                                                        
ā tvā gan rāṣtram saha varcasā ud ihi prāṅ viśām patiḥ ekarāj tvam vi rāja   sarvāḥ tvā rājan pradiśaḥ hvayantu upasadyaḥ namasyaḥ bhava iha  
tvām viśaḥ vṛṇatām rājyāya tvām imāḥ pradiśaḥ pañca devīḥ   varṣman rāṣṭrasya kakudi śrayasva tatas naḥ ugraḥ vi bhaja vasūni  
acha tvā yantu havinaḥ sajātāḥ agniḥ dūtaḥ ajiraḥ sam carātai   jāyāḥ putrāḥ sumanasaḥ bhavantu bahum balim prati paśyāsai ugraḥ  
aśvinā tvā agre mitrāvaruṇā ubhā viśve devāḥ marutaḥ tvā hvayantu   adhā manaḥ vasu deyāya kṛṇuṣva tatas naḥ ugraḥ vi bhaja vasūni  
ā pra drava paramasyāḥ parāvataḥ śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām   tat ayam rājā varuṇaḥ tathā āha sa tvā ayam ahvat saḥ upa idam ehi  
indra indra manuṣyāḥ parehi sam hi ajñāsthāḥ varuṇaiḥ saṃvidānaḥ   sa tvā ayam ahvat sve sadhasthe sa devān yakṣat saḥ u kalpayat viśaḥ  
pathyāḥ revatīḥ bahudhā virūpāḥ sarvāḥ saṃgatya varīyaḥ te akran   tāḥ tvā sarvāḥ saṃvidānāḥ hvayantu daśamīm ugraḥ sumanāḥ vaśā iha  
ā ayam agan parṇa maṇiḥ balī balena pramṛṇan sapatnān   ojaḥ devānām payaḥ oṣadhīnām varcasā mā jinvantu a prayāvan  
mayi kṣatram parṇamaṇe mayi dhārayatāt rayim   aham rāṣṭrasya abhīvarge nijaḥ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ  
yam nidadhuḥ vanaspatau guhyam devāḥ priyam maṇim   tam asmabhyam saha āyuṣā devāḥ dadatu bhartave  
somasya parṇaḥ sahaḥ ugram āgan indreṇa dattaḥ varuṇena śiṣṭaḥ   tam priyāsam bahu rocamānaḥ dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya  
ā mā arukṣat parṇa maṇiḥ mahyāḥ ariṣṭatātaye   yathā aham uttaraḥ asāni aryamṇaḥ uta saṃvidaḥ  
ye dhīvānaḥ rathakārāḥ karmārāḥ ye manīṣiṇaḥ   upastīn parṇa mahyam tvam sarvān kṛṇu abhitas janān  
ye rājānaḥ rāja kṛtaḥ sūtāḥ grāmaṇyaḥ ca ye   upastīn parṇa mahyam tvam sarvān kṛṇu abhitas janān 
parṇaḥ asi tanū pānaḥ sayoniḥ vīraḥ vīreṇa mayā   saṃvatsarasya tejasā tena badhnāmi tvā maṇe  
pumān puṃsaḥ parijātaḥ aśvatthaḥ khadirāt adhi   sa hantu śatrūn māmakān yān aham dveṣmi ye ca mām  
tān aśvattha niḥ śṛṇīhi śatrūn vaibādha dodhataḥ   indreṇa vṛtra ghnā medī mitreṇa varuṇena ca  
yathā aśvattha nirabhanaḥ antar mahati arṇave   eva tān sarvān niḥ bhaṅgdhi yān aham dveṣmi ye ca mām  
yaḥ sahamānaḥ carasi sāsahānaḥ iva ṛṣabhaḥ   tena aśvattha tvayā vayam sapatnān sahiṣīmahi  
sinātu enān nirṛtiḥ mṛtyoḥ pāśaiḥ amokyaiḥ   aśvattha śatrūn māmakān yān aham dveṣmi ye ca mām  
yathā aśvattha vānaspatyān ārohan kṛṇuṣe adharān   eva me śatroḥ mūrdhānam viṣvak bhinddhi sahasva ca  
te adharāñcaḥ pra plavantām chinnā nauḥ iva bandhanāt   na vaibādha praṇuttānām punar asti nivartanam  
pra eṇān nude manasā pra cittena uta brahmaṇā   pra eṇān vṛkṣasya śākhayā aśvatthasya nudāmahe  
hariṇasya raghuṣyadaḥ adhi śīrṣaṇi bheṣajam   sa kṣetriyam viṣāṇayā viṣūcīnam anīnaśat  
anu tvā hariṇaḥ vṛṣā padbhiḥ caturbhiḥ akramīt   viṣāṇe vi sya guṣpitam yat asya kṣetriyam hṛdi  
adaḥ yat avarocate catuṣpakṣam iva chadiḥ   tena te sarvam kṣetriyam aṅgebhyaḥ nāśayāmasi  
amū ye divi subhage vicṛtau nāma tārake   vi kṣetriyasya muñcatām adhamam pāśam uttamam  
āpaḥ id vai u bheṣajīḥ āpaḥ amīva cātanīḥ   āpaḥ viśvasya bheṣajīḥ tāḥ tvā muñcantu kṣetriyāt  
yat āsuteḥ kriyamānāyāḥ kṣetriyam tvā vyānaśe   veda aham tasya bheṣajam kṣetriyam nāśayāmi tvat  
apavāse nakṣatrāṇām apavāse uṣasām uta   apa asmat sarvam durbhūtam apa kṣetriyam ucchatu  
ā yātu mitraḥ ṛtubhiḥ kalpamānaḥ saṃveśayan pṛthivīm usriyābhiḥ   atha asmabhyam varuṇaḥ vāyuḥ agniḥ bṛhat rāṣṭram saṃveśyam dadhātu  
dhātā rātiḥ savitā idam juśantām indraḥ tvaṣṭā prati haryantu me vacaḥ   huve devīm aditim śūra putrām sajātānām madhyameṣṭhā yathā asāni  
huve somam savitāram namobhiḥ viśvān ādityām aham uttara tve   ayam agniḥ dīdāyat dīrgham eva sajātaiḥ iddhaḥ a pratibruvadbhiḥ  
iha id asātha na paras gamātha iryaḥ gopāḥ puṣṭa patiḥ vaḥ ājat   asmai kāmāya upa kāminīḥ viśve vaḥ devāḥ upasaṃyantu  
sam vaḥ manāṃsi sam vratā sam ākūtīḥ namāmasi   amī ye vivratā sthana tān vaḥ sam namayāmasi  
aham gṛbhṇāmi manasā manāṃsi mama cittam anu cittebhiḥ eta   mama vaśeṣu hṛdayāni vaḥ kṛṇomi mama yātam anuvartmānaḥ eta  
karśaphasya viśaphasya dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā   yathā abhicakra devāḥ tathā apa kṛṇuta punar  
aśreṣmāṇaḥ adhārayan tathā tat manunā kṛtam   kṛṇomi vadhri viṣkandham muṣkābarhaḥ gavām iva  
piśaṅge sūtre khṛgalam tat ā badhnanti vedhasaḥ   śravasyum śuṣmam kābavam vadhrim kṛṇvantu bandhuraḥ  
yena śravasyavaḥ caratha devāḥ iva asura māyayā   śunām kapiḥ iva dūṣaṇaḥ bandhurā kābavasya ca  
duṣṭyai hi tvā bhatsyāmi dūṣayiṣyāmi kābavam   ud āśavaḥ rathāḥ iva śapathebhiḥ sariṣyatha  
eka śatam viṣkandhāni viṣṭhitā pṛthivīm anu   teṣām tvām agre ud jaharuḥ maṇim viṣkandha dūṣaṇam  
prathamā ha vi uvāsa sā dhenuḥ abhavat yame   sā naḥ payasvatī duhām uttarām uttarām samām  
yām devāḥ pratinandanti rātrim dhenum upāyatīm   saṃvatsarasya yā patnī sā naḥ astu su maṅgalī  
saṃvatsarasya pratimām yām tvā rātri upāsmahe   sā naḥ āyuṣmatīm prajām rāyaḥ poṣeṇa sam sṛja  
iyam eva sā yā prathamā vyauchat āsu itarāsu carati praviṣṭā   mahāntaḥ asyām mahimānaḥ antar vadhūḥ jigāya navagat janitrī  
vānaspatyāḥ grāvāṇaḥ ghoṣam akrata haviḥ kṛṇvantaḥ parivatsarīṇam   eka aṣṭake suprajasaḥ su vīrāḥ vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām  
iḍāyāḥ padam ghṛtavat sarīsṛpam jātavedaḥ prati havyā gṛbhāya   ye grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ viśva rūpāḥ teṣām saptānām mayi rantiḥ astu  
ā mā puṣṭe ca poṣe ca rātri devānām sumatau syāma   pūrṇā darve parā pata su pūrṇā punar ā pata   sarvān yajñān saṃbhuñjati iṣam ūrjam naḥ ā bhara  
ā ayam agan saṃvatsaraḥ patiḥ eka aṣṭake tava   sā naḥ āyuṣmatīm prajām rāyaḥ poṣeṇa sam sṛja  
ṛtūn yaja ṛtupatīn ārtavān uta hāyanān   samāḥ saṃvatsarān māsān bhūtasya pataye yaje  
ṛtubhyaḥ tvā ārtavebhyaḥ mādbhyaḥ saṃvatsarebhyaḥ   dhātre vidhātre samṛdhe bhūtasya pataye yaje  
iḍayā juhvataḥ vayam devān ghṛtavatā yaje   gṛhān a lubhyataḥ vayam sam viśema upa gomataḥ  
eka aṣṭakā tapasā tapyamānā jajāna garbham mahimānam indram   tena devāḥ vi asahanta śatrūn hantā dasyūnām abhavat śacīpatiḥ  
indra putre soma putre duhitā asi prajāpateḥ   kāmān asmākam pūraya prati gṛhṇāhi naḥ haviḥ  
muñcāmi tvā haviṣā jīvanāya kam ajñāta yakṣmāt uta rāja yakṣmāt   grāhiḥ jagrāha yadi etat enam tasyāḥ indra agnī pra mumuktam enam  
yadi kṣita āyuḥ yadi vā paretaḥ yadi mṛtyoḥ antikam eva   tam ā harāmi nirṛteḥ upasthāt a spārśam enam śata śāradāya  
sahasra akṣeṇa śata vīryeṇa śata āyuṣā haviṣā ahārṣam enam   indraḥ yathā enam śaradaḥ nayāti ati viśvasya duritasya pāram  
śatam jīva śaradaḥ vardhamānaḥ śatam hemantān śatam u vasantān   śatam te indraḥ agniḥ savitā bṛhaspatiḥ śata āyuṣā haviṣā ahārṣam enam  
pra viśatam prāṇa apānau anaḍvāhau iva vrajam   vi anye yantu mṛtyavaḥ yān āhuḥ itarān śatam  
iha eva stam prāṇa apānau mā apa gātam itas yuvam   śarīram asya aṅgāni jarase vahatam punar  
jarāyai tvā pari dadāmi jarāyai ni dhuvāmi tvā   jarā tvā bhadrā neṣṭa vi anye yantu mṛtyavaḥ yān āhuḥ itarān śatam  
abhi tvā jarimā ahita gām ukṣaṇam iva rajjvā   yaḥ tvā mṛtyuḥ abhyadhatta jāyamānam su pāśayā   tam te satyasya hastābhyām ud amuñcat bṛhaspatiḥ  
iha eva dhruvām ni minomi śālām kṣeme tiṣṭhāti ghṛtam ukṣamāṇā   tām tvā śāle sarva vīrāḥ su vīrāḥ ariṣṭa vīrāḥ upa sam carema  
iha eva dhruvā prati tiṣṭha śāle aśvāvatī gomatī sūnṛtāvatī   ūrjasvatī ghṛtavatī payasvatī ud śrayasva mahate saubhagāya  
dharuṇī asi śāle bṛhacchandāḥ pūti dhānyā   ā tvā vatsaḥ gamet ā kumāraḥ ā dhenavaḥ sāyam āspandamānāḥ  
imām śālām savitā vāyuḥ indraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ ni minotu prajānan   ukṣantu udnāḥ marutaḥ ghṛtena bhagaḥ naḥ rājā ni kṛṣim tanotu  
mānasya patni śaraṇā syonā devī devebhiḥ nimitā asi agre   tṛṇam vasānā sumanāḥ asaḥ tvam atha asmabhyam saha vīram rayim dāḥ  
ṛtena sthūṇām adhi roha vaṃśa ugraḥ virājan apa vṛṅkṣva śatrūn   mā te riṣan upasattāraḥ gṛhāṇām śāle śatam jīvema śaradaḥ sarva vīrāḥ  
ā imām kumāraḥ taruṇaḥ ā vatsaḥ jagatā saha   ā imām parisrutaḥ kumbhaḥ ā dadhnaḥ kalaśaiḥ aguḥ  
pūrṇam nāri pra bhara kumbham etam ghṛtasya dhārām amṛtena saṃbhṛtām   imām pātṝn amṛtena sam aṅgdhi iṣṭāpūrtam abhi rakṣāti enām  
imāḥ āpaḥ pra bharāmi a yakṣmāḥ yakṣma nāśanīḥ   gṛhān upa pra sīdāmi amṛtena saha agninā  
yat adaḥ saṃprayatīḥ ahau anadata hate   tasmāt ā nadyaḥ nāma stha tāḥ vaḥ nāmāni sindhavaḥ  
yat preṣitā varuṇena at śībham samavalgata   tat āpnot indraḥ vaḥ yatīḥ tasmāt āpaḥ anu sthana  
apakāmam syandamānāḥ avīvarata vaḥ hi kam   indraḥ vaḥ śaktibhiḥ devīḥ tasmāt vār nāma vaḥ hitam  
ekaḥ vaḥ devaḥ api atiṣṭhat syandamānāḥ yathāvaśam   ud āniṣuḥ mahīḥ iti tasmāt udakam ucyate  
āpaḥ bhadrāḥ ghṛtam id āpaḥ āsan agnīṣomau bibhrati āpaḥ id tāḥ   tīvraḥ rasaḥ madhu pṛcām araṃgamaḥ ā mā prāṇena saha varcasā gamet  
āt id paśyāmi uta vā śṛṇomi ā mā ghoṣaḥ gacchati vāc māsām   manye bhejānaḥ amṛtasya tarhi hiraṇya varṇāḥ atṛpam yadā vaḥ  
idam vaḥ āpaḥ hṛdayam ayam vatsaḥ ṛtāvarīḥ   iha ittham eta śakvarīḥ yatra idam veśayāmi vaḥ  
sam vaḥ goṣṭhena suṣadā sam rayyā sam subhūtyā   ahar jātasya yat nāma tena vaḥ sam sṛjāmasi  
sam vaḥ sṛjatu aryamā sam pūṣā sam bṛhaspatiḥ   sam indraḥ yaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ mayi puṣyata yat vasu  
saṃjagmānāḥ abibhyuṣīḥ asmin goṣṭhe karīṣiṇīḥ   bibhratīḥ somyam madhu anamīvāḥ upetana  
iha eva gāvaḥ etana iha u śakā iva puṣyata   iha eva uta pra jāyadhvam mayi saṃjñānam astu vaḥ  
śivaḥ vaḥ goṣṭhaḥ bhavatu śāriśākā iva puṣyata   iha eva uta pra jāyadhvam mayā vaḥ sam sṛjāmasi  
mayā gāvaḥ gopatinā sacadhvam ayam vaḥ goṣṭhaḥ iha poṣayiṣṇuḥ   rāyaḥ poṣeṇa bahulāḥ bhavantīḥ jīvāḥ jīvantīḥ upa vaḥ sadema  
indram aham vaṇijam codayāmi sa naḥ aitu puraetā naḥ astu   nudan arātim paripanthinam mṛgam saḥ īśānaḥ dhana dāḥ astu mahyam  
ye panthānaḥ bahavaḥ deva yānāḥ antarā dyāvāpṛthivī saṃcaranti   te mā juṣantām payasā ghṛtena yathā krītvā dhanam āharāṇi  
idhmena agne ichamānaḥ ghṛtena juhomi havyam tarase balāya   yāvat īśe brahmaṇā vandamānaḥ imām dhiyam śata seyāya devīm  
imām agne śaraṇim mīmṛṣaḥ naḥ yam adhvānam agāma dūram   śunam naḥ astu prapaṇaḥ vikrayaḥ ca pratipaṇaḥ phalinam mā kṛṇotu   idam havyam saṃvidānau juṣethām śunam naḥ astu caritam utthitam ca  
yena dhanena prapaṇam carāmi dhanena devāḥ dhanam ichamānaḥ   tat me bhūyaḥ bhavatu mā kanīyaḥ agne sātaghnaḥ devān haviṣā ni sedha  
yena dhanena prapaṇam carāmi dhanena devāḥ dhanam ichamānaḥ   tasmin me indraḥ rucim ā dadhātu prajāpatiḥ savitā somaḥ agniḥ  
upa tvā namasā vayam hotar vaiśvānara stumaḥ   sa naḥ prajāsu ātmasu goṣu prāṇeṣu jāgṛhi  
viśvāhā te sadam id bharema aśvāya iva tiṣṭhate jātavedaḥ   rāyaḥ poṣeṇa sam iṣā madantaḥ mā te agne prativeśāḥ riṣāma  
prātar agnim prātar indram havāmahe prātar mitrāvaruṇā prātar aśvinā   prātar bhagam pūṣaṇam brahmaṇaḥ patim prātar somam uta rudram havāmahe  
prātar jitam bhagam ugram havāmahe vayam putram aditeḥ yaḥ vidhartā   ādhraḥ cit yam manyamānaḥ turaḥ cit rājā cit yam bhagam bhakṣi iti āha  
bhaga praṇetar bhaga satya rādhaḥ bhaga imām dhiyam ud ava dadat naḥ   bhaga pra naḥ janaya gobhiḥ aśvaiḥ bhaga pra nṛbhiḥ nṛvantaḥ syāma  
uta idānīm bhagavantaḥ syāma uta prapitve uta madhye ahnām   uta uditau maghavan sūryasya vayam devānām sumatau syāma  
bhagaḥ eva bhagavān astu devaḥ tena vayam bhagavantaḥ syāma   tam tvā bhaga sarvaḥ id johavīmi sa naḥ bhaga puraetā bhava iha  
sam adhvarāya uṣasaḥ namanta dadhikrāvā iva śucaye padāya   arvācīnam vasu vidam bhagam me ratham iva aśvāḥ vājinaḥ ā vahantu  
aśvāvatīḥ gomatīḥ naḥ uṣāsaḥ vīravatīḥ sadam ucchantu bhadrāḥ   ghṛtam duhānāḥ viśvatas prapītāḥ yūyam pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ  
sīrā yuñjanti kavayaḥ yugā vi tanvate pṛthak   dhīrāḥ deveṣu sumnayau  
yunakta sīrā vi yugā tanota kṛte yonau vapata iha bījam   virājaḥ śnuṣṭiḥ sabharāḥ asan naḥ nedīyaḥ id sṛṇyaḥ pakvam ā yavan  
lāṅgalam pavīravat su śīmam soma satsaru   ud id vapatu gām avim prasthāvat rathavāhanam pībarīm ca prapharvyam  
indraḥ sītām ni gṛhṇātu tām pūṣā abhi rakṣatu   sā naḥ payasvatī duhām uttarām uttarām samām  
śunam su phālāḥ vi tudantu bhūmim śunam kīnāśāḥ anu yantu vāhān   śunāsīrā haviṣā tośamānā su pippalāḥ oṣadhīḥ kartam asmai  
śunam vāhāḥ śunam naraḥ śunam kṛṣatu lāṅgalam   śunam varatrā badhyantām śunam aṣṭrām ud iṅgaya  
śunāsīra iha sma me juṣethām   yat divi cakrathuḥ payaḥ tena imām upa siñcatam  
sīte vandāmahe tvā arvācī subhage bhava   yathā naḥ sumanāḥ asaḥ yathā naḥ suphalāḥ bhuvar  
ghṛtena sītā madhunā samaktā viśvaiḥ devaiḥ anumatā marudbhiḥ   sā naḥ sīte payasā abhyāvavṛtsva ūrjasvatī ghṛtavat pinvamānā  
imām khanāmi oṣadhim vīrudhām balavattamām   yayā sapatnīm bādhate yayā saṃvindate patim  
uttānaparṇe subhage deva jūte sahasvati   sapatnīm me parā nuda patim me kevalam kṛdhi  
nahi te nāma jagrāha naḥ asmin ramase patau   parām eva parāvatam sapatnīm gamayāmasi  
uttarā aham uttaraḥ uttaret uttarābhyaḥ   adhas sapatnī yā mama adharā sā adharābhyaḥ  
aham asmi sahamānā atho tvam asi sāsahiḥ   ubhe sahasvatī bhūtvā sapatnīm me sahāvahai  
abhi te adhām sahamānām upa te adhām sahīyasīm   mām anu pra te manaḥ vatsam gauḥ iva dhāvatu pathā vār iva dhāvatu  
saṃśitam me idam brahma saṃśitam vīryam balam   saṃśitam kṣatram ajaram astu jiṣṇuḥ yeṣām asmi purohitaḥ  
sam aham eṣām rāṣṭram syāmi sam ojaḥ vīryam balam   vṛścāmi śatrūṇām bāhūn anena haviṣā aham  
nīcais padyantām adhare bhavantu ye naḥ sūrim maghavānam pṛtanyān   kṣiṇāmi brahmaṇā amitrān ud nayāmi svān aham  
tīkṣṇīyāṃsaḥ paraśoḥ agneḥ tīkṣṇatarāḥ uta   indrasya vajrāt tīkṣṇīyāṃsaḥ yeṣām asmi purohitaḥ  
eṣām aham āyudhā sam syāmi eṣām rāṣṭram su vīram vardhayāmi   eṣām kṣatram ajaram astu jiṣṇu eṣām cittam viśve avantu devāḥ  
ud dharṣantām maghavan vājināni ud vīrāṇām jayatām etu ghoṣaḥ   pṛthak ghoṣāḥ ululayaḥ ketumantaḥ ud īratām   devāḥ indra jyeṣṭhāḥ marutaḥ yantu senayā  
pretāḥ jayata naraḥ ugrāḥ vaḥ santu bāhavaḥ   tīkṣṇa iṣavaḥ abala dhanvanaḥ hata ugra āyudhāḥ abalān ugra bāhavaḥ  
avasṛṣṭā parā pata śaravye brahma saṃśite   jaya amitrān pra padyasva jahi eṣām varaṃvaram mā amīṣām moci kaḥ cana  
ayam te yoniḥ ṛtviyaḥ yatas jātaḥ arocathāḥ   tam jānan agne ā roha adha naḥ vardhaya rayim  
agne achā vada iha naḥ pratyak naḥ sumanāḥ bhava   pra naḥ yaccha viśām pate dhana dāḥ asi naḥ tvam  
pra naḥ yacchatu aryamā pra bhagaḥ pra bṛhaspatiḥ   pra devīḥ pra uta sūnṛtā rayim devī dadhātu me  
somam rājānam avase agnim gīrbhiḥ havāmahe   ādityam viṣṇum sūryam brahmāṇam ca bṛhaspatim  
tvam naḥ agne agnibhiḥ brahma yajñam vardhaya   tvam naḥ deva dātave rayim dānāya codaya  
indra vāyū ubhau iha su havā iha havāmahe   yathā naḥ sarvaḥ id janaḥ saṃgatyām sumanāḥ asat dāna kāmaḥ ca naḥ bhuvat  
aryamaṇam bṛhaspatim indram dānāya codaya   vātam viṣṇum sarasvatīm savitāram ca vājinam  
vājasya nu prasave sam babhūvima imā ca viśvā bhuvanāni antar   uta āditsantam dāpayatu prajānan rayim ca naḥ sarva vīram ni yaccha  
duhrām me pañca pradiṣaḥ duhrām urvīḥ yathābalam   prāpeyam sarvāḥ ākūtīḥ manasā hṛdayena ca  
go sanim vācam udeyam varcasā mā abhyudihi   ā rundhām sarvatas vāyuḥ tvaṣṭā poṣam dadhātu me  
ye agnayaḥ apsu antar ye vṛtre ye puruṣe ye aśmasu   yaḥ āviveśa oṣadhīḥ yaḥ vanaspatīn tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
yaḥ some antar yaḥ goṣu antar yaḥ āviṣṭaḥ vayaḥsu yaḥ mṛgeṣu   yaḥ āviveśa dvipadaḥ yaḥ catuṣpadaḥ tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
yaḥ indreṇa sa ratham yāti devaḥ vaiśvānaraḥ uta viśvadāvyaḥ   yam johavīmi pṛtanāsu sāsahim tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
yaḥ devaḥ viśvāt yam u kāmam āhuḥ yam dātāram pratigṛhṇantam āhuḥ   yaḥ dhīraḥ śakraḥ paribhūḥ adābhyaḥ tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
yam tvā hotāram manasā abhi saṃviduḥ trayodaśa bhauvanāḥ pañca mānavāḥ   varcaḥ dhase yaśase sūnṛtāvate tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
ukṣa annāya vaśā annāya soma pṛṣṭhāya vedhase   vaiśvānara jyeṣṭhebhyaḥ tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
divam pṛthivīm anu antarikṣam ye vidyutam anusaṃcaranti   ye dikṣu antar ye vāte antar tebhyaḥ agnibhyaḥ hutam astu etat  
hiraṇya pāṇim savitāram indram bṛhaspatim varuṇam mitram agnim   viśvān devān aṅgirasaḥ havāmahe imam kravya adam śamayantu agnim  
śāntaḥ agniḥ kravyād śāntaḥ puruṣa reṣaṇaḥ   atha u yaḥ viśva dāvyaḥ tam kravyādam aśīśamam  
ye parvatāḥ soma pṛṣṭhāḥ āpaḥ uttāna śīvarīḥ   vātaḥ parjanyaḥ āt agniḥ te kravya adam aśīśaman  
hasti varcasam prathatām bṛhat yaśaḥ adityāḥ yat tanvaḥ saṃbabhūva   tat sarve sam aduḥ mahyam etat viśve devāḥ aditiḥ sajoṣāḥ  
mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca indraḥ rudraḥ ca cetatu   devāsaḥ viśva dhāyasaḥ te māñjantu varcasā  
yena hastī varcasā saṃbabhūva yena rājā manuṣyesu apsu antar   yena devāḥ devatām agre āyan tena mām adya varcasā agne varcasvinam kṛṇu  
yat te varcaḥ jātavedaḥ bṛhat bhavati āhuteḥ   yāvat sūryasya varcaḥ āsurasya ca hastinaḥ   tāvat me aśvinā varcaḥ ā dhattām puṣkara srajā  
yāvat catasraḥ pradiśaḥ cakṣuḥ yāvat samaśnute   tāvat samaitu indriyam mayi tat dhasti varcasam  
hastī mṛgāṇām suṣadām atiṣṭhāvān babhūva hi   tasya bhagena varcasā abhi siñcāmi mām aham  
yena vehat babhūvitha nāśayāmasi tat tvat   idam tat anyatra tvat apa dūre ni dadhmasi  
ā te yonim garbhe etu pumān bāṇaḥ iva iṣudhim   ā vīraḥ atra jāyatām putraḥ te daśamāsyaḥ  
pumāṃsam putram janaya tam pumān anu jāyatām   bhavāsi putrāṇām mātā jātānām janayāḥ ca yān  
yāni badrāṇi bījāni ṛṣabhāḥ janayanti ca   taiḥ tvam putram vindasva sā prasūḥ dhenukā bhava  
kṛṇomi te prājāpatyam ā yonim garbhe etu te   vindasva tvam putram nāri yaḥ tubhyam śam asat śam u tasmai tvam bhava  
yāsām dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā samudraḥ mūlam vīrudhām babhūva   tāḥ tvā putra vidyāya daivīḥ prāvantu oṣadhayaḥ  
payasvatīḥ oṣadhayaḥ payasvat māmakam vacaḥ   atha u payasvatīnām ā bhare aham sahasraśas  
veda aham payasvantam cakāra dhānyam bahu   saṃbhṛtvā nāma yaḥ devaḥ tam vayam havāmahe yoyo a yajvanaḥ gṛhe  
imāḥ yāḥ pañca pradiśaḥ mānavīḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ   vṛṣṭe śāpam nadīḥ iva iha sphātim samāvahān  
ud utsam śata dhāram sahasra dhāram akṣitam   eva asmāka idam dhānyam sahasra dhāram akṣitam  
śata hasta samāhara sahasra hasta sam kira   kṛtasya kāryasya ca iha sphātim samāvaha  
tisraḥ mātrāḥ gandharvāṇām catasraḥ gṛhapatnyāḥ   tāsām yā sphātimattamā tayā tvā abhi mṛśāmasi  
upohaḥ ca samūhaḥ ca kṣattārau te prajāpate   tau iha ā vahatām sphātim bahum bhūmānam akṣitam  
uttudaḥ tvā ud tudatu mā dhṛthāḥ śayane sve   iṣuḥ kāmasya yā bhīmā tayā vidhyāmi tvā hṛdi  
ādhīparṇām kāma śalyām iṣum saṃkalpa kulmalām   tām su saṃnatām kṛtvā kāmaḥ vidhyatu tvā hṛdi  
yā plīhānam śoṣayati kāmasya iṣuḥ su saṃnatā   prācīna pakṣā vyoṣā tayā vidhyāmi tvā hṛdi  
śucā viddhā vyoṣayā śuṣkā asyāḥ abhi sarpa mā   mṛduḥ nimanyuḥ kevalī priya vādinī anuvratā  
ājāmi tvājanyā pari mātuḥ atho pituḥ   yathā mama kratau asaḥ mama cittam upāyasi  
vi asyai mitrāvaruṇau hṛdaḥ cittāni asyatam   atha enām a kratum kṛtvā mama eva kṛṇutam vaśe  
ye asyām stha prācyām diśi hetayaḥ nāma devāḥ teṣām vaḥ agniḥ iṣavaḥ   te naḥ mṛḍata te naḥ adhi brūta tebhyaḥ vaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ vaḥ svāhā  
ye asyām stha dakṣiṇāyām diśi aviṣyavaḥ nāma devāḥ teṣām vaḥ kāmaḥ iṣavaḥ   te naḥ mṛḍata te naḥ adhi brūta tebhyaḥ vaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ vaḥ svāhā  
ye asyām stha pratīcyām diśi vairājāḥ nāma devāḥ teṣām vaḥ āpaḥ iṣavaḥ   te naḥ mṛḍata te naḥ adhi brūta tebhyaḥ vaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ vaḥ svāhā  
ye asyām stha udīcyām diśi pravidhyantaḥ nāma devāḥ teṣām vaḥ vātaḥ iṣavaḥ   te naḥ mṛḍata te naḥ adhi brūta tebhyaḥ vaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ vaḥ svāhā  
ye asyām stha dhruvāyām diśi nilimpāḥ nāma devāḥ teṣām vaḥ oṣadhīḥ iṣavaḥ   te naḥ mṛḍata te naḥ adhi brūta tebhyaḥ vaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ vaḥ svāhā  
ye asyām stha ūrdhvāyām diśi avasvantaḥ nāma devāḥ teṣām vaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ iṣavaḥ   te naḥ mṛḍata te naḥ adhi brūta tebhyaḥ vaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ vaḥ svāhā  
prācī diś agniḥ adhipatiḥ asitaḥ rakṣitā ādityāḥ iṣavaḥ   tebhyaḥ namaḥ adhipatibhyaḥ namaḥ rakṣitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ iṣubhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ astu   yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tam vaḥ jambhe dadhmaḥ  
dakṣiṇā diś indraḥ adhipatiḥ tiraścirājī rakṣitā pitaraḥ iṣavaḥ   tebhyaḥ namaḥ adhipatibhyaḥ namaḥ rakṣitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ iṣubhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ astu   yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tam vaḥ jambhe dadhmaḥ  
pratīcī diś varuṇaḥ adhipatiḥ pṛdākuḥ rakṣitā annam iṣavaḥ   tebhyaḥ namaḥ adhipatibhyaḥ namaḥ rakṣitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ iṣubhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ astu   yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tam vaḥ jambhe dadhmaḥ  
udīcī diś somaḥ adhipatiḥ svajaḥ rakṣitā aśaniḥ iṣavaḥ   tebhyaḥ namaḥ adhipatibhyaḥ namaḥ rakṣitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ iṣubhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ astu   yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tam vaḥ jambhe dadhmaḥ  
dhruvā diś viṣṇuḥ adhipatiḥ kalmāṣa grīvaḥ rakṣitā vīrudhaḥ iṣavaḥ   tebhyaḥ namaḥ adhipatibhyaḥ namaḥ rakṣitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ iṣubhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ astu   yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tam vaḥ jambhe dadhmaḥ  
ūrdhvā diś bṛhaspatiḥ adhipatiḥ śvitraḥ rakṣitā varṣam iṣavaḥ   tebhyaḥ namaḥ adhipatibhyaḥ namaḥ rakṣitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ iṣubhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ astu   yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tam vaḥ jambhe dadhmaḥ  
ekaikayā eṣā sṛṣṭyā sam babhūva yatra gāḥ asṛjanta bhūta kṛtaḥ viśva rūpāḥ   yatra vijāyate yaminī apartuḥ sā paśūn kṣiṇāti riphatī ruśatī  
eṣā paśūn sam kṣiṇāti kravyād bhūtvā vyadvarī   uta enām brahmaṇe dadyāt tathā syonā śivā syāt  
śivā bhava puruṣebhyaḥ gobhyaḥ aśvebhyaḥ śivā   śivā asmai sarvasmai kṣetrāya śivā naḥ iha edhi  
iha puṣṭiḥ iha rasaḥ iha sahasra sātamā bhava   paśūn yamini poṣaya  
yatra suhārdaḥ su kṛtaḥ madanti vihāya rogam tanvaḥ svāyāḥ   tam lokam yaminī abhisaṃbabhūva sā naḥ mā hiṃsīt puruṣān paśūn ca  
yatra suhārdām su kṛtām agnihotra hutām yatra lokaḥ   tam lokam yaminī abhisaṃbabhūva sā naḥ mā hiṃsīt puruṣān paśūn ca  
yat rājānaḥ vibhajante iṣṭāpūrtasya ṣoḍaśam yamasya amī sabhāsadaḥ   aviḥ tasmāt pra muñcati dattaḥ śitipād svadhā  
sarvān kāmān pūrayati ābhavan prabhavan bhavan   ākūti praḥ aviḥ dattaḥ śiti pād na upa dasyati  
yaḥ dadāti śiti pādam avim lokena saṃmitam   sa nākam abhyārohati yatra śulkaḥ na kriyate abalena balīyase  
pañca apūpam śiti pādam avim lokena saṃmitam   pradātā upa jīvati pitṝṇām loke akṣitam  
pañca apūpam śiti pādam avim lokena saṃmitam   pradātā upa jīvati sūryāmāsayoḥ akṣitam  
irā iva nā upa dasyati samudraḥ iva payaḥ mahat   devau sa vāsinau iva śitipād nā upa dasyati  
kaḥ idam kasmai adāt kāmaḥ kāmāya adāt   kāmaḥ dātā kāmaḥ pratigrahītā kāmaḥ samudram ā viveśa   kāmena tvā prati gṛhnāmi kāma etat te  
bhūmiḥ tvā prati gṛhṇātu antarikṣam idam mahat   mā aham prāṇena mā ātmanā mā prajayā pratigṛhya vi rādhiṣi  
sahṛdayam sāṃmanasyam a vidveṣam kṛṇomi vaḥ   anyaḥ anyam abhi haryata vatsam jātam iva aghnyā  
anuvrataḥ pituḥ putraḥ mātrā bhavatu saṃmanāḥ   jāyā patye madhumatīm vācam vadatu śantivām  
mā bhrātā bhrātaram dvikṣan mā svasāram uta svasā   samyañcaḥ savratāḥ bhūtvā vācam vadata bhadrayā  
yena devāḥ na viyanti na u ca vidviṣate mithas   tat kṛṇmaḥ brahma vaḥ gṛhe saṃjñānam puruṣebhyaḥ  
jyāyasvantaḥ cittinaḥ mā vi yauṣṭa saṃrādhayantaḥ sadhurāḥ carantaḥ   anyaḥ anyasmai valgu vadantaḥ eta sadhrīcīnān vaḥ saṃmanasaḥ krṇomi  
samānī prapā saha vaḥ anna bhāgaḥ samāne yoktre saha vaḥ yunajmi   samyañcaḥ agnim saparyatārāḥ nābhim iva abhitas  
sadhrīcīnān vaḥ saṃmanasaḥ kṛṇomi eka śnuṣṭīn saṃvananena sarvān   devāḥ iva amṛtam rakṣamāṇāḥ sāyaṃprātar saumanasaḥ vaḥ astu  
vi devāḥ jarasā āvṛtan vi tvam agne arātyā   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
vi ārtyā pavamānaḥ vi śakraḥ pāpa kṛtyayā   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
vi grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ āraṇyaiḥ vi āpaḥ tṛṣṇayā asaran   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
vi me dyāvāpṛthivī itas vi panthānaḥ diśaṃdiśam   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
tvaṣṭā duhitre vahatum yunakti iti idam viśvam bhuvanam vi yāti   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
agniḥ prāṇān sam dadhāti candraḥ prāṇena saṃhitaḥ   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
prāṇena viśvatas vīryam devāḥ sūryam sam airayan   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
āyuṣmatām āyuṣkṛtām prāṇena jīva mā mṛthāḥ   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
prāṇena prāṇa tām prāṇa iha eva bhava mā mṛthāḥ   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
ud āyuṣā sam āyuṣā ud oṣadhīnām rasena   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
ā parjanyasya vṛṣṭyā ud asthāma amṛtāḥ vayam   vi aham sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā  
brahma jajñānam prathamam purastāt vi sīmataḥ su rucaḥ venaḥ āvaḥ   sa budhnyāḥ upamāḥ asya viṣṭhāḥ sataḥ ca yonim asataḥ ca vi var  
iyam pitryā rāṣṭrī etu agre prathamāya januṣe bhuvaneṣṭhāḥ   tasmai etam su rucam hvāram ahyam gharmam śrīṇantu prathamāya dhāsyave  
pra yaḥ jajñe vidvān asya bandhuḥ viśvā devānām janimā vivakti   brahma brahmaṇaḥ ud jabhāra madhyāt nicais uccais svadhāḥ abhi pra tasthau  
sa hi vidaḥ sa pṛthivyāḥ ṛta sthāḥ mahī kṣemam rodasī askabhāyat   mahān mahī askabhāyat vi jātaḥ dyām sadma pārthivam ca rajaḥ  
sa bhudhnyāt āṣṭra januṣaḥ abhi agram bṛhaspatiḥ devatā tasya samrāj   ahar yat śukram jyotiṣaḥ janiṣṭa atha dyumantaḥ vi vasantu viprāḥ  
nūnam tat asya kāvyaḥ hinoti mahaḥ devasya pūrvyasya dhāma   eṣa jajñe bahubhiḥ sākam itthā pūrve ardhe viṣite sasan nu  
yaḥ atharvāṇam pitaram deva bandhum bṛhaspatim namasā ava ca gacchāt   tvam viśveṣām janitā yathā asaḥ kaviḥ devaḥ na dabhāyat svadhāvān  
yaḥ ātma dāḥ bala dāḥ yasya viśve upāsate praśiṣam yasya devāḥ   yaḥ asya īśe dvipadaḥ yaḥ catuṣpadaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
yaḥ prāṇataḥ nimiṣataḥ mahitvā ekaḥ rājā jagataḥ babhūva   yasya chāyā amṛtam yasya mṛtyuḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
yam krandasī avataḥ caskabhāne bhiyasāne rodasī ahvayethām   yasya asau panthāḥ rajasaḥ vimānaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
yasya dyauḥ urvī pṛthivī ca mahī yasya adaḥ uru antarikṣam   yasya asau sūraḥ vitataḥ mahitvā kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
yasya viśve himavantaḥ mahitvā samudre yasya rasām id āhuḥ   imāḥ ca pradiśaḥ yasya bāhū kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
āpaḥ agre viśvam āvan garbham dadhānāḥ amṛtāḥ ṛta jñāḥ   yāsu devīṣu adhi devaḥ āsīt kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
hiraṇya garbhaḥ sam avartata agre bhūtasya jātaḥ patiḥ ekaḥ āsīt   sa dādhāra pṛthivīm uta dyām kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
āpaḥ vatsam janayantīḥ garbham agre sam airayan   tasya uta jāyamānasya ulbaḥ āsīt hiraṇyayaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema  
ud itas trayaḥ akraman vyāghraḥ puruṣaḥ vṛkaḥ   hiruk ghi yanti sindhavaḥ hiruk devaḥ vanaspatiḥ hiruk namantu śatravaḥ  
pareṇa etu pathā vṛkaḥ parameṇa uta taskaraḥ   pareṇa datvatī rajjuḥ pareṇa aghāyuḥ arṣatu  
akṣyau ca te mukham ca te vyāghra jambhayāmasi   āt sarvān viṃśatim nakhān  
vyāghram datvatām vayam prathamam jambhayāmasi   āt u stenam atha u ahim yātudhānam atha u vṛkam  
yaḥ adya stenaḥ āyati sa saṃpiṣṭaḥ apāyati   pathām apadhvaṃsena etu indraḥ vajreṇa hantu tam  
mūrṇāḥ mṛgasya dantāḥ apiśīrṇāḥ u pṛṣṭayaḥ   nimruc te godhā bhavatu nīcāyat śaśayuḥ mṛgaḥ  
yat saṃyamaḥ na vi yamaḥ vi yamaḥ yat na saṃyamaḥ   indra jāḥ soma jāḥ ātharvaṇam asi vyāghra jambhanam  
yām tvā gandharvaḥ akhanat varuṇāya mṛtabhraje   tām tvā vayam khanāmasi oṣadhim śepaharṣaṇīm  
ud uṣāḥ ud u sūryaḥ ud idam māmakam vacaḥ   ud ejatu prajāpatiḥ vṛṣā śuṣmeṇa vājinā  
yathā sma te virohataḥ abhitaptam iva anati   tatas te śuṣmavattaram iyam kṛṇotu oṣadhiḥ  
ud śuṣmā oṣadhīnām sārāḥ ṛṣabhāṇām   sam puṃsām indra vṛṣṇyam asmin dhehi tanū vaśin  
apām rasaḥ prathama jaḥ atha u vanaspatīnām   uta somasya bhrātā asi uta arśam asi vṛṣṇyam  
adya agne adya savitar adya devi sarasvati   adya asya brahmaṇaḥ pate dhanuḥ iva ā tānaya pasaḥ  
ā aham tanomi te pasaḥ adhi jyām iva dhanvani   kramasva rśaḥ iva rohitam an avaglāyatā sadā  
aśvasya aśvatarasya ajasya petvasya ca   atha ṛṣabhasya ye vājāḥ tān asmin dhehi tanū vaśin 
sahasra śṛṅgaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ yaḥ samudrāt udācarat   tena sahasyena vayam ni janān svāpayāmasi  
na bhūmim vātaḥ ati vāti na ati paśyati kaś cana   striyaḥ ca sarvāḥ svāpaya śunaḥ ca indra sakhā caran  
proṣṭheśayāḥ talpeśayāḥ nārīḥ yāḥ vahya śīvarīḥ   striyaḥ yāḥ puṇya gandhayaḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ svāpayāmasi  
ejat ejat ajagrabham cakṣuḥ prāṇam ajagrabham   aṅgāni ajagrabham sarvā rātrīṇām atiśarvare  
yaḥ āste yaḥ carati yaḥ ca tiṣṭhan vipaśyati   teṣām sam dadhmaḥ akṣīṇi yathā idam harmyam tathā  
svaptu mātā svaptu pitā svaptu śvā svaptu viśpatiḥ   svapantu asyai jñātayaḥ svaptu ayam abhitas janaḥ  
svapna svapna abhikaraṇena sarvam ni svāpaya janam   otsūryam anyān svāpaya avyuṣam jāgṛtāt aham indraḥ iva ariṣṭaḥ akṣitaḥ  
brāhmaṇaḥ jajñe prathamaḥ daśa śīrṣaḥ daśa āsyaḥ   sa somam prathamaḥ papau sa cakāra arasam viṣam  
yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī varimṇā yāvat sapta sindhavaḥ vitaṣṭhire   vācam viṣasya dūṣaṇīm tām itas niḥ avādiṣam  
suparṇaḥ tvā garutmān viṣa prathamam āvayat   na amīmadaḥ na ārūrupaḥ uta asmai abhavaḥ pituḥ  
yaḥ te āsyat pañca aṅguriḥ vakrāt cit adhi dhanvanaḥ   apaskambhasya śalyāt niḥ avocam aham viṣam  
śalyāt viṣam niḥ avocam prāñjanāt uta parṇadheḥ   apāṣṭhāt śṛṅgāt kulmalāt niḥ avocam aham viṣam  
arasaḥ te iṣaḥ śalyaḥ atho te arasam viṣam   uta arasasya vṛkṣasya dhanuḥ te arasa arasam  
ye apīṣan ye adihan ye āsyan ye avāsṛjan   sarve te vadhrayaḥ kṛtāḥ vadhriḥ viṣa giriḥ kṛtaḥ  
vadhrayaḥ te khanitāraḥ vadhriḥ tvam asi oṣadhe   vadhriḥ sa parvataḥ giriḥ yatas jātam idam viṣam  
vār idam vārayātai varaṇāvatyām adhi   tatra amṛtasya āsiktam tena te vāraye viṣam  
arasam prācyam viṣam arasam yat udīcyam   atha idam adharācyam karambheṇa vi kalpate  
karambham kṛtvā tiryam pībaspākam udārathim   kṣudhā kila tvā duṣṭano jakṣivān sa na rūrupaḥ  
vi te madam madāvati śaram iva pātayāmasi   pra tvā carum iva yeṣantam vacasā sthāpayāmasi  
pari grāmam iva ācitam vacasā sthāpayāmasi   tiṣṭha vṛkṣe iva sthāmni abhri khāte na rūrupaḥ  
pavastaiḥ tvā pari akrīṇan dūrśebhiḥ ajinaiḥ uta   prakrīḥ asi tvam oṣadhe abhri khāte na rūrupaḥ  
an āptāḥ ye vaḥ prathamāḥ yāni karmāṇi cakrire   vīrān naḥ atra mā dabhan tat vaḥ etat puras dadhe  
bhūtaḥ bhūteṣu payaḥ ā dadhāti sa bhūtānām adhipatiḥ babhūva   tasya mṛtyuḥ carati rājasūyam sa rājā anu manyatām idam  
abhi prehi mā apa venaḥ ugraḥ cettā sapatna hā   ā tiṣṭha mitra vardhana tubhyam devāḥ adhi bruvan  
ātiṣṭhantam pari viśve abhūṣam śriyam vasānaḥ carati sva rociḥ   mahat tat vṛṣṇaḥ asurasya nāma ā viśva rūpaḥ amṛtāni tasthau  
vyāghraḥ adhi vaiyāghre vi kramasva diśaḥ mahīḥ   viśaḥ tvā sarvāḥ vāñchantu āpaḥ divyāḥ payasvatīḥ  
yāḥ āpaḥ divyāḥ payasā madanti antarikṣe uta vā pṛthivyām   tāsām tvā sarvāsām apām abhi siñcāmi varcasā  
abhi tvā varcasā asican āpaḥ divyāḥ payasvatīḥ   yathā asaḥ mitra vardhanaḥ tathā tvā savitā karat  
enā vyāghram pariṣasvajānāḥ siṃham hinvanti mahate saubhagāya   samudram na su bhuvaḥ tasthivāṃsam marmṛjyante dvīpinam apsu antar  
ehi jīvam trāyamāṇam parvatasya asi akṣyam   viśvebhiḥ devaiḥ dattam paridhiḥ jīvanāya kam  
paripāṇam puruṣāṇām paripāṇam gavām asi   aśvānām arvatām paripāṇāya tasthiṣe  
uta asi paripāṇam yātu jambhanam āñjana   uta amṛtasya tvam vettha atho asi jīva bhojanam atho harita bheṣajam  
yasya añjana prasarpasi aṅgam aṅgam paruḥ paruḥ   tatas yakṣmam vi bādhase ugraḥ madhyamaśīḥ iva  
na enam prāpnoti śapathaḥ na kṛtyā na abhiśocanam   na enam viṣkandham aśnute yaḥ tvā bibharti āñjana  
asat mantrāt duṣvapnyāt duṣkṛtāt śamalāt uta   durhārdaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ ghorāt tasmāt naḥ pāhi āñjana  
idam vidvān āñjana satyam vakṣyāmi na anṛtam   saneyam aśvam gām aham ātmānam tava pūruṣa  
trayaḥ dāsāḥ āñjanasya takmā balāsaḥ āt ahiḥ   varṣiṣṭhaḥ parvatānām trikakud nāma te pitā  
yat āñjanam traikakudam jātam himavataḥ pari   yātūn ca sarvān jambhayat sarvāḥ ca yātudhānyaḥ  
yadi vā asi traikakudam yadi yāmunam ucyase   ubhe te bhadre nāmnī tābhyām naḥ pāhi āñjana  
vātāt jātaḥ antarikṣāt vidyutaḥ jyotiṣaḥ pari   sa naḥ hiraṇya jāḥ śaṅkhaḥ kṛśanaḥ pātu aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ agratas rocanānām samudrāt adhi jajñiṣe   śaṅkhena hatvā rakṣāṃsi attriṇaḥ vi sahāmahe  
śaṅkhena amīvām amatim śaṅkhena uta sadānvāḥ   śaṅkhaḥ naḥ viśva bheṣajaḥ kṛśanaḥ pātu aṃhasaḥ  
divi jātaḥ samudra jaḥ sindhutas pari ābhṛtaḥ   sa naḥ hiraṇya jāḥ śaṅkhaḥ āyuṣprataraṇaḥ maṇiḥ  
samudrāt jātaḥ maṇiḥ vṛtrāt jātaḥ divākaraḥ   saḥ asmān sarvatas pātu hetyāḥ deva asurebhyaḥ  
hiraṇyānām ekaḥ asi somāt tvam adhi jajñiṣe   rathe tvam asi darśataḥ iṣudhau rocanaḥ tvam pra naḥ āyūṃṣi tāriṣat  
devānām asthi kṛśanam babhūva tat ātmanvat carati apsu antar   tat te badhnāmi āyuṣe varcase balāya dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya kārśanaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
anaḍvān dādhāra pṛthivīm uta dyām anaḍvān dādhāra uru antarikṣam   anaḍvān dādhāra pradiśaḥ ṣaṭ urvīḥ anaḍvān viśvam bhuvanam ā viveśa  
anaḍvān indraḥ sa paśubhyaḥ vi caṣṭe trayām śakraḥ vi mimīte adhvanaḥ   bhūtam bhaviṣyat bhuvanā duhānaḥ sarvā devānām carati vratāni  
indraḥ jātaḥ manuṣyeṣu antar gharmaḥ taptaḥ carati śośucānaḥ   su prajāḥ san saḥ udāre na sarṣat yaḥ na aśnīyāt anaḍuhaḥ vijānan  
anaḍvān duhe su kṛtasya loke ā enam pyāyayati pavamānaḥ purastāt   parjanyaḥ dhārāḥ marutaḥ ūdhar asya yajñaḥ payaḥ dakṣiṇā dohaḥ asya  
yasya naḥ īśe yajñapatiḥ na yajñaḥ na asya dātā īśe na pratigrahītā   yaḥ viśvajit viśvabhṛt viśvakarmā gharmam naḥ brūta yatamaḥ catuṣpād  
yena devāḥ svar āruruhuḥ hitvā śarīram amṛtasya nābhim   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam gharmasya vratena tapasā yaśasyavaḥ  
indraḥ rūpeṇa agniḥ vahena prajāpatiḥ parameṣṭhī virāj   viśvānare akramata vaiśvānare akramata anaduhi akramata   saḥ adṛṃhayata saḥ adhārayata  
madhyam etat anaḍuhaḥ yatra eṣa vahaḥ āhitaḥ   etāvat asya prācīnam yāvān pratyaṅ samāhitaḥ  
yaḥ veda anaduhaḥ dohān sapta anupadasvataḥ   prajām ca lokam ca āpnoti tathā sapta ṛṣayaḥ viduḥ  
padbhiḥ sedim avakrāman irām jaṅghābhiḥ utkhidan   srameṇa anaḍvān kīlālam kīnāśaḥ ca abhi gacchataḥ  
dvādaśa vai etāḥ rātrīḥ vratyāḥ āhuḥ prajāpateḥ   tatra upa brahma yaḥ veda tat vai anaḍuhaḥ vratam  
duhe sāyam duhe prātar duhe madhyaṃdinam pari   dohāḥ ye asya saṃyanti tān vidma anupadasvataḥ  
rohaṇī asi rohaṇī asthnaḥ chinnasya rohaṇī   rohaya idam arundhati  
yat te riṣṭam yat te dyuttam asti peṣṭram te ātmani   dhātā tat bhadrayā punar sam dadhat paruṣā paruḥ  
sam te majjā majjñā bhavatu sam u te paruṣā paruḥ   sam te māṃsasya visrastam sam asthi api rohatu  
majjā majñā sam dhīyatām carmaṇā carma rohatu   asṛk te asthi rohatu māṃsam māṃsena rohatu  
loma lomnā sam kalpaya tvacā sam kalpaya tvacam   asṛk te asthi rohatu chinnam sam dhehi oṣadhe  
saḥ ud tiṣṭha prehi pra drava rathaḥ su cakraḥ   su paviḥ su nābhiḥ prati tiṣṭha ūrdhvaḥ  
yadi kartam patitvā saṃśaśre yadi vā aśmā prahṛtaḥ jaghāna   ṛbhū rathasya iva aṅgāni sam dadhat paruṣā paruḥ  
uta devāḥ avahitam devāḥ ud nayatha punar   uta agaḥ cakruṣam devāḥ devāḥ jīvayatha punar  
dvau imau vātau vāte ā sindhoḥ ā parāvataḥ   dakṣam te anyaḥ āvātu vi anyaḥ vātu yat rapaḥ  
ā vāta vāhi bheṣajam vi vāta vāhi yat rapaḥ  tvam hi viśva bheṣaja devānām dūtaḥ īyase 
trāyantām imam devāḥ trāyantām marutām gaṇāḥ   trāyantām viśvā bhūtāni yathā ayam arapāḥ asat  
ā tvā agamam śaṃtātibhiḥ atha u ariṣṭatātibhiḥ   dakṣam te ugram ābhāriṣam parā yakṣmam suvāmi te  
ayam me hastaḥ bhagavān ayam me bhagavattaraḥ   ayam me viśva bheṣajaḥ ayam śiva abhimarśanaḥ  
hastābhyām daśa śākhābhyām jihvā vācaḥ purogavī   anāmayitnubhyām hastābhyām tābhyām tvā abhi mṛśāmasi  
ajaḥ hi agneḥ ajaniṣṭa śokāt saḥ apaśyat janitāram agre   tena devāḥ devatām agre āyan tena rohān ruruhuḥ medhyāsaḥ  
kramadhvam agninā nākam ukhyān hasteṣu bibhrataḥ   divaḥ pṛṣṭham svar gatvā miśrāḥ devebhiḥ ādhvam  
pṛṣṭhāt pṛthivyāḥ aham antarikṣam āruham antarikṣāt divam āruham   divaḥ nākasya pṛṣṭhāt svar jyotiḥ agām aham  
svar yantaḥ na apekṣante ā dyām rohanti rodasī   yajñam ye viśvatas dhāram su vidvāṃsaḥ vitenire  
agne prehi prathamaḥ devatānām cakṣuḥ devānām uta mānuṣānām   iyakṣamāṇāḥ bhṛgubhiḥ sajoṣāḥ svar yantu yajamānāḥ svasti  
ajam anajmi payasā ghṛtena divyam suparnam payasam bṛhantam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nākam uttamam  
pañca odanam pañcabhiḥ aṅgulibhiḥ darvyā uddhara pañcadhā etam odanam   prācyām diśi śiraḥ ajasya dhehi dakṣiṇāyām diśi dakṣiṇam dhehi pārśvam  
pratīcyām diśi bhasadam asya dhehi uttarasyām diśi uttaram dhehi pārśvam   ūrdhvāyām diśi ajasya anūkam dhehi diśi dhruvāyām dhehi pājasyam antarikṣe madhyataḥ madhyam asya  
śṛtam ajam śṛtayā prorṇuhi tvacā sarvaiḥ aṅgaiḥ saṃbhṛtam viśva rūpam   saḥ ud tisṭha itas abhi nākam uttamam padbhiḥ caturbhiḥ prati tiṣṭha dikṣu  
samutpatantu pradiśaḥ nabhasvatīḥ sam abhrāṇi vāta jūtāni yantu   mahā ṛṣabhasya nadataḥ nabhasvataḥ vāśrāḥ āpaḥ pṛthivīm tarpayantu  
sam īkṣayantu taviṣāḥ sudānavaḥ apām rasāḥ oṣadhībhiḥ sacantām   varṣasya sargāḥ mahayantu bhūmim pṛthak jāyantām oṣadhayaḥ viśva rūpāḥ  
sam īkṣayasva gāyataḥ nabhāṃsi apām vegāsaḥ pṛthak ud vijantām   varṣasya sargāḥ mahayantu bhūmim pṛthak jāyantām vīrudhaḥ viśva rūpāḥ  
gaṇāḥ tvā upa gāyantu mārutāḥ parjanya ghoṣiṇaḥ pṛthak   sargāḥ varṣasya varṣataḥ varṣantu pṛthivīm anu  
ud īrayata marutaḥ samudrataḥ tveṣaḥ arkaḥ nabhaḥ ud pātayātha   mahā ṛṣabhasya nadataḥ nabhasvataḥ vāśrāḥ āpaḥ pṛthivīm tarpayantu  
abhi kranda stanaya ardaya udadhim bhūmim parjanya payasā sam aṅdhi   tvayā sṛṣṭam bahulam aitu varṣam āśāraiṣī kṛśaguḥ etu astam  
sam vaḥ avantu sudānavaḥ utsāḥ ajagarāḥ uta   marudbhiḥ pracyutāḥ meghāḥ varṣantu pṛthivīm anu  
āśām āśām vi dyotatām vātāḥ vāntu diśaḥ diśaḥ   marudbhiḥ pracyutāḥ meghāḥ sam yantu pṛthivīm anu  
āpaḥ vidyut abhram varṣam sam vaḥ avantu sudānavaḥ utsāḥ ajagarāḥ uta   marudbhiḥ pracyutāḥ meghāḥ prāvantu pṛthivīm anu  
apām agniḥ tanūbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ yaḥ oṣadhīnām adhipāḥ babhūva   sa naḥ varṣam vanutām jātavedāḥ prāṇam prajābhyaḥ amṛtam divaḥ pari  
prajāpatiḥ salilāt ā samudrāt āpaḥ īrayan udadhim ardayāti   pra pyāyatām vṛṣṇaḥ aśvasya retaḥ arvān etena stanayitnunā ihi  
apaḥ niṣiñcan asuraḥ pitā naḥ śvasantu gargarāḥ apām varuṇāva nīcīḥ apaḥ sṛja   vadantu pṛśni bāhavaḥ maṇḍūkāḥ iriṇānu  
saṃvatsaram śaśayānāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vrata cāriṇaḥ   vācam parjanya jinvitām pra maṇdūkāḥ avādiṣuḥ  
upapravada maṇḍūki varṣam ā vada tāduri   madhye hradasya plavasva vigṛhya caturaḥ padaḥ  
khaṇva khāi khaima khāi madhye taduri   varṣam vanudhvam pitaraḥ marutām manaḥ ichata  
mahāntam kośam ud aca abhi siñca sa vidyutam bhavatu vātu vātaḥ   tanvatām yajñam bahudhā visṛṣṭāḥ ānandinīḥ oṣadhayaḥ bhavantu  
bṛhan eṣām adhiṣṭhātā antikāt iva paśyati   yaḥ stāyan manyate caran sarvam devāḥ idam viduḥ  
yaḥ tiṣṭhati carati yaḥ ca vañcati yaḥ nilāyam carati yaḥ prataṅkam   dvau saṃniṣadya yat mantrayete rājā tat veda varuṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ  
uta iyam bhūmiḥ varuṇasya rājñaḥ uta asau dyauḥ bṛhatī dūreantā   uta u samudrau varuṇasya kukṣī uta asmin alpe udake nilīnaḥ  
uta yaḥ dyām atisarpāt parastāt na sa mucyātai varuṇasya rājñaḥ   divaḥ spaśaḥ pra caranti idam asya sahasra akṣāḥ ati paśyanti bhūmim  
sarvam tat rājā varuṇaḥ vi caṣṭe yat antarā rodasī yat parastāt   saṃkhyātāḥ asya nimiṣaḥ janānām akṣān iva śva ghnī ni minoti tāni  
ye te pāśāḥ varuṇa sapta sapta tredhā tiṣṭhanti viṣitāḥ ruṣantaḥ   chinantu sarve anṛtam vadantam yaḥ satya vādī ati tam sṛjantu  
śatena pāśaiḥ abhi dhehi varuṇa enam mā te moci anṛtavāc nṛ cakṣaḥ   āstām jālmaḥ udaram śraṃśayitvā kośaḥ iva ābandhaḥ parikṛtyamānaḥ  
yaḥ samābhyaḥ varuṇaḥ yaḥ vyābhyaḥ yaḥ saṃdeśyaḥ varuṇaḥ yaḥ videśyaḥ   yaḥ daivaḥ varuṇaḥ yaḥ ca mānuṣaḥ  
taiḥ tvā sarvaiḥ abhi syāmi pāśaiḥ asau āmuṣyāyaṇa amuṣyāḥ putra   tān u te sarvān anusaṃdiśāmi  
īśāṇām tvā bheṣajānām ujjeṣe ā rabhāmahe   cakre sahasra vīryam sarvasmai oṣadhe tvā  
satyajitam śapatha yāvanīm sahamānām punaḥsarām   sarvāḥ sam ahvi oṣadhīḥ itas naḥ pārayāt iti  
yā śaśāpa śapanena yā agham mūram ādadhe   yā rasasya haraṇāya jātam ārebhe tokam attu sā  
yām te cakruḥ āme pātre yām cakruḥ nīlalohite   āme māṃse kṛtyām yām cakruḥ tayā kṛtyā kṛtaḥ jahi  
dauṣvapnyam daurjīvityam rakṣaḥ abhvam arāyyaḥ   durṇāmnīḥ sarvāḥ durvācaḥ tāḥ asmat nāśayāmasi  
kṣudhā māram tṛṣṇā māram a gotām anapatya tām   apāmārga tvayā vayam sarvam tat apa mṛjmahe  
tṛṣṇā māram kṣudhā māram atho akṣa parājayam   apāmārga tvayā vayam sarvam tat apa mṛjmahe  
apāmārgaḥ oṣadhīnām sarvāsām ekaḥ id vaśī   tena te mṛjmaḥ āsthitam atha tvam agadaḥ cara  
samam jyotiḥ sūryeṇa ahnā rātrī samāvatī   kṛṇomi satyam ūtaye arasāḥ santu kṛtvarīḥ  
yaḥ devāḥ kṛtyām kṛtvā harāt aviduṣaḥ gṛham   vatsaḥ dhāruḥ iva mātaram tam pratyak upa padyatām  
amā kṛtvā pāpmānam yaḥ tena anyam jighāṃsati   aśmānaḥ tasyām dagdhāyām bahulāḥ phaṭ karikrati  
sahasra dhāman viśikhān vigrīvām chāyayā tvam   prati sma cakruṣe kṛtyām priyām priyāvate hara  
anayā aham oṣadhyā sarvāḥ kṛtyāḥ adūduṣam   yām kṣetre cakruḥ yām goṣu yām vā te puruṣeṣu  
yaḥ cakāra na śaśāka kartum śaśre pādam aṅgurim   cakāra bhadram asmabhyam ātmane tapanam tu saḥ  
apāmārgaḥ apa mārṣṭu kṣetriyam śapathaḥ ca yaḥ   apa aha yātudhānīḥ apa sarvāḥ arāyyaḥ  
apamṛjya yātudhānān apa sarvāḥ arāyyaḥ   apāmārga tvayā vayam sarvam tat apa mṛjmahe  
uta u asi abandhu kṛt uta u asi nu jāmi kṛt   uta u kṛtyā kṛtaḥ prajām nadam iva ā chindhi vārṣikam  
brāhmaṇena paryuktā asi kaṇvena nārṣadena   senā iva eṣi tviṣīmatī na tatra bhayam asti yatra prāpnoṣi oṣadhe  
agram eṣi oṣadhīnām jyotiṣā iva abhidīpayan   uta trātāsi pākasya atho hantāsi rakṣasaḥ  
yat adaḥ devāḥ asurān tvayā agre nirakurvata   tatas tvam adhi oṣadhe apāmārgaḥ ajāyathāḥ  
vibhindatī śata śākhā vibhindat nāma te pitā   pratyak vi bhindhi tvam tam yaḥ asmām abhidāsati
