asat bhūmyāḥ sam abhavat tat yām eti mahat vyacaḥ   tat vai tatas vidhūpāyat pratyak kartāram ṛchatu  
pratyaṅ hi saṃbabhūvitha pratīcīna phalaḥ tvam   sarvān mat śapathām adhi varīyaḥ yāvaya vadham  
śatena mā pari pāhi sahasreṇa abhi rakṣa mā   indraḥ te vīrudhām pate ugraḥ ojmānam ā dadhat  
ā paśyati prati paśyati parā paśyati paśyati   divam antarikṣam āt bhūmim sarvam tat devi paśyati  
tisraḥ divaḥ tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ ṣaṭ ca imāḥ pradiśāḥ pṛthak   tvayā aham sarvāḥ bhūtāni paśyāni devī oṣadhe  
divyasya suparṇasya tasya hā asi kanīnikā   sā bhūmim ā rurohitha vahyam śrāntā vadhūḥ iva  
tām me sahasra akṣaḥ devaḥ dakṣiṇe haste ā dadhat  tayā aham sarvam paśyāmi yaḥ ca śūdraḥ uta āryaḥ  
āvis kṛṇuṣva rūpāni mā ātmānam apa gūhathāḥ   atho sahasra cakṣo tvam prati paśyāḥ kimīdinaḥ  
darśaya mā yātudhānān darśaya yātudhānyaḥ   piśācān sarvān darśaya iti tvā rabha oṣadhe  
kaśyapasya cakṣuḥ asi śunyāḥ ca catur akṣyāḥ   vīdhre sūryam iva sarpantam mā piśācam tiras karaḥ  
ud agrabham paripāṇāt yātudhānam kimīdinam   tena aham sarvam paśyāmi uta śūdram uta āryam  
yaḥ antarikṣeṇa patati divam yaḥ ca atisarpati   bhūmim yaḥ manyate nātham tam piśācam pra darśaya  
ā gāvaḥ agman uta bhadram akran sīdantu goṣṭhe raṇayantu asme   prajāvatīḥ puru rūpāḥ iha syuḥ indrāya pūrvīḥ uṣasaḥ duhānāḥ  
indraḥ yajvane gṛṇate ca śikṣate upa id dadāti na svam muṣāyati   bhūyas bhūyas rayim id asya vardhayan abhinne khilye ni dadhāti devayum  
na tāḥ naśanti na dabhāti taskaraḥ nāsām āmitraḥ vyathiḥ ā dadharṣati   devān ca yābhiḥ yajate dadāti ca jyok id tābhiḥ sacate gopatiḥ saha  
na tāḥ arvā reṇu kakāṭaḥ aśnute na saṃskṛtatram upa yanti tāḥ abhi   uru gāyam abhayam tasya tāḥ anu gāvaḥ martasya vi caranti yajvanaḥ  
gāvaḥ bhagaḥ gāvaḥ indraḥ me ichāt gāvaḥ somasya prathamasya bhakṣaḥ   imāḥ yāḥ gāvaḥ sa janāsaḥ indraḥ ichāmi hṛdā manasā cit indram  
yūyam gāvaḥ medayatha kṛśam cit aśrīram cit kṛṇutha supratīkam   bhadram gṛham kṛṇutha bhadra vācaḥ bṛhat vaḥ vayaḥ ucyate sabhāsu  
prajāvatīḥ sūyavase ruśantīḥ śuddhāḥ apaḥ su prapāṇe pibantīḥ   mā vaḥ stenaḥ īśata mā agha śaṃsaḥ pari vaḥ rudrasya hetiḥ vṛṇaktu  
imam indra vardhaya kṣatriyam me imam viśām eka vṛṣam kṛṇu tvam   niḥ amitrān akṣṇuhi asya sarvān tān randhaya asmai aham uttareṣu  
ā imam bhaja grāme aśveṣu goṣu niḥ tam bhaja yaḥ amitraḥ asya   varṣma kṣatrāṇām ayam astu rāja indra śatrum randhaya sarvam asmai  
ayam astu dhana patiḥ dhanānām ayam viśām viśpatiḥ astu rājā   asmin indra mahi varcāṃsi dhehi a varcasam kṛṇuhi śatrum asya  
asmai dyāvāpṛthivī bhūri vāmam duhāthām gharma dughe iva dhenū   ayam rājā priyaḥ indrasya bhūyāt priyaḥ gavām oṣadhīnām paśūnām  
yunajmi te uttarāvantam indram yena jayanti na parājayante   yaḥ tvā karat eka vṛṣam janānām uta rājñām uttamam mānavānām  
uttaraḥ tvam adhare te sapatnāḥ ye ke ca rājan pratiśatravaḥ te   eka vṛṣaḥ indra sakhā jigīvām śatrūyatām ā bhara bhojanāni  
siṃha pratīkaḥ viśaḥ addhi sarvā vyāghra pratīkaḥ ava bādhasva śatrūn   eka vṛṣaḥ indra sakhā jigīvām śatrūyatām ā khida bhojanāni  
agneḥ manve prathamasya pracetasaḥ pāñcajanyasya bahudhā yam indhate   viśoviśaḥ praviśivāṃsam īmahe sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yathā havyam vahasi jātavedaḥ yathā yajñam kalpayasi prajānan   eva devebhyaḥ sumatim naḥ ā vaha sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yāman yāman upayuktam vahiṣṭham karmaṅkarman ābhagam agnim īḍe   rakṣaḥ haṇam yajña vṛdham ghṛta āhutam sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
su jātam jātavedasam agnim vaiśvānaram vibhum   havyavāham havāmahe sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yena ṛṣayaḥ balam adyotayan yujā yena asurāṇām ayuvanta māyāḥ   yena agninā paṇīn indraḥ jigāya sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yena devāḥ amṛtam anvavindan yena oṣadhīḥ madhumatīḥ akṛṇvan   yena devāḥ svar ābharan sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yasya idam pradiśi yat virocate yat jātam janitavyam ca kevalam   staumi agnim nāthitaḥ johavīmi sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
indrasya manmahe śaśvat id asya manmahe vṛtra ghnaḥ stomāḥ upa mā ime āguḥ   yaḥ dāśuṣaḥ su kṛtaḥ havam eti sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ ugrīṇām ugra bāhuḥ yayuḥ yaḥ dānavānām balam āruroja   yena jitāḥ sindhavaḥ yena gāvaḥ sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ carṣaṇipraḥ vṛṣabhaḥ svar vid yasmai grāvāṇaḥ pravadanti nṛmṇam   yasya adhvaraḥ saptahotā madiṣṭhaḥ sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yasya vaśāsaḥ ṛṣabhāsaḥ ukṣaṇaḥ yasmai mīyante svaravaḥ svarvide   yasmai śukraḥ pavate brahma śumbhitaḥ sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yasya juṣṭim sominaḥ kāmayante yam havante iṣumantam gaviṣṭau   yasmin arkaḥ śiśriye yasmin ojaḥ sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ prathamaḥ karma kṛtyāya jajñe yasya vīryam prathamasya anubuddham   yena udyataḥ vajraḥ abhyāyata ahim sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ saṃgrāmāt nayati sam yudhe vaśī yaḥ puṣṭāni saṃsṛjati dvayāni   staumi indram nāthitaḥ johavīmi sa naḥ muñcatu aṃhasaḥ  
vāyoḥ savituḥ vidathāni manmahe yau ātmanvat viśathaḥ yau ca rakṣathaḥ   yau viśvasya paribhū babhūvathuḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yayoḥ saṃkhyātā varimā pārhivāni yābhyām rajaḥ yupitam antarikṣe   yayoḥ prāyam na anu ānaśe kaḥ cana tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
tava vrate ni viśante janāsaḥ tvayi udite prerate citra bhāno   yuvam vāyo savitā ca bhuvanāni rakṣathaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
apa itas vāyo savitā ca duṣkṛtam apa rakṣāṃsi śimidām ca sedhatam   sam hi ūrjayā sṛjathaḥ sam balena tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
rayim me poṣam savitā uta vāyuḥ tanū dakṣam ā suvatām su śevam   a yakṣmatātim mahaḥ iha dhattam tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
pra sumatim savitar vāyo ūtaye mahasvantam matsaram mādayāthaḥ   arvāk vāmasya pravataḥ ni yacchatam tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
upa śreṣṭhāḥ naḥ āśiṣaḥ devayoḥ dhāman asthiran   staumi devam savitāram ca vāyum tau naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
manve vām dyāvāpṛthivī subhojasau sacetasau ye aprathethām amitā yojanāni   pratiṣṭhe hi abhavatam vasūnām te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
pratiṣṭhe hi abhavatam vasūnām pravṛddhe devī subhage urūcī   dyāvāpṛthivī bhavatam me syone te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
a santāpe su tapasau huve aham urvī gambhīre kavibhiḥ namasye   dyāvāpṛthivī bhavatam me syone te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
ye amṛtam bibhṛthaḥ ye havīṃṣi ye srotyāḥ bibhṛthaḥ ye manuṣyān   dyāvāpṛthivī bhavatam me syone te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
ye usriyāḥ bibhṛthaḥ ye vanaspatīn yayoḥ vām viśvā bhuvanāni antar   dyāvāpṛthivī bhavatam me syone te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
ye kīlālena tarpayathaḥ ye ghṛtena yābhyām ṛte na kim cana śaknuvanti   dyāvāpṛthivī bhavatam me syone te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yat mā idam abhiśocati yena yena vā kṛtam pauruṣeyāt na daivāt   staumi dyāvāpṛthivī nāthitaḥ johavīmi te naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
marutām manve adhi me bruvantu pra imam vājam vājasāte avantu   āśūn iva su yamān ahve ūtaye te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
utsam akṣitam vyacanti ye sadā ye āsiñcanti rasam oṣadhīṣu   puras dadhe marutaḥ pṛśni mātṝn te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
payaḥ dhenūnām rasam oṣadhīnām javam arvatām kavayaḥ ye invatha   śagmāḥ bhavantu marutaḥ naḥ syonāḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
apaḥ samudrāt divam ud vahanti divaḥ pṛthivīm abhi ye sṛjanti   ye adbhiḥ īśānāḥ marutaḥ caranti te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
ye kīlālena tarpayanti ye ghṛtena ye vā vayaḥ medasā saṃsṛjanti   ye adbhiḥ īśānāḥ marutaḥ varṣayanti te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
yadi id idam marutaḥ mārutena yadi devāḥ daivyena īdṛś āra   yūyam īśidhve vasavaḥ tasya niṣkṛteḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
tigmam anīkam viditam sahasvat mārutam śardhaḥ pṛtanāsu ugram   staumi marutaḥ nāthitaḥ johavīmi te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
bhava śarvau manve vām tasya vittam yayoḥ vām idam pradiśi yat virocate   yau asya īśāthe dvipadaḥ yau catuṣpadaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yayoḥ abhyabhve uta yat dūre cit yau viditau iṣubhṛtām asiṣṭhau   yau asya īśathe dvipadaḥ yau catuṣpadaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
sahasra akṣau vṛtra hanā huveham dūregavyūtī stuvan emi ugrau   yau asya īśathe dvipadaḥ yau catuṣpadaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yau ārebhāthe bahu sākam agre pra ced asrāṣṭram abhibhām janeṣu   yau asya īśathe dvipadaḥ yau catuṣpadaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yayoḥ vadhāt na apapadyate kaḥ cana antar deveṣu uta mānuṣeṣu   yau asya īśathe dvipadaḥ yau catuṣpadaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ kṛtyā kṛt mūla kṛt yātudhānaḥ ni tasmin dhattam vajram ugrau   yau asya īśathe dvipadaḥ yau catuṣpadaḥ tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
adhi naḥ brūtam pṛtanāsu ugrau sam vajreṇa sṛjatam yaḥ kimīdī   staumi bhava aśarvau nāthitaḥ johavīmi tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
manve vām mitrāvaruṇau ṛtāvṛdhau sacetasau druhvaṇaḥ yau nudethe   pra satyāvānam avathaḥ bhareṣu tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
sacetasau druhvaṇaḥ yau nudethe pra satyāvānam avathaḥ bhareṣu   yau gacchathaḥ nṛ cakṣasau babhruṇā sutam tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yau aṅgirasam avathaḥ yau agastim mitrāvaruṇā jamadagnim attrim   yau kaśyapam avathaḥ yau vasiṣṭham tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yau śyāvāśvam avathaḥ vādhryaśvam mitrāvaruṇā purumīḍham attrim   yau vimadam avathaḥ saptavadhrim tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yau bharadvājam avathaḥ yau gaviṣṭhiram viśvāmitram varuṇa mitra kutsam   yau kakṣīvantam avathaḥ prota kaṇvam tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yau medhātithim avathaḥ yau triśokam mitrāvaruṇau uśanām kāvyam yau   yau gotamam avathaḥ prota mugdalam tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
yayoḥ rathaḥ satya vartma rju raśmiḥ mithuyā carantam abhiyāti dūṣayan   staumi mitrāvaruṇau nāthitaḥ johavīmi tau naḥ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ  
aham rudrebhiḥ vasubhiḥ carāmi aham ādityaiḥ uta viśvadevaiḥ   aham mitrāvarunā ubhā bibharmi aham indra agnī aham aśvinā ubhā  
aham rāṣṭrī saṃgamanī vasūnām cikituṣī prathamā yajñiyānām   tām mā devāḥ vi adadhuḥ purutrā bhūri sthātrām bhūri āveśayantaḥ  
aham eva svayam idam vadāmi juṣṭam devānām uta mānuṣāṇām   yam kāmaye tantam ugram kṛṇomi tam brahmāṇam tam ṛṣim tam sumedhām  
mayā saḥ annam atti yaḥ vipaśyati yaḥ prāṇati yaḥ īm śṛṇoti uktam   amantavaḥ mām te upa kṣiyanti śrudhi śruta śruddhā iyam te vadāmi  
aham rudrāya dhanuḥ ā tanomi brahma dviṣe śarave hantavai u  aham janāya samadam kṛṇomi aham dyāvāpṛthivī ā viveśa  
aham somam āhanasam bibharmi aham tvaṣṭāram uta pūṣaṇam bhagam   aham dadhāmi draviṇā haviṣmate suprāvyā yajamānāya sunvate  
aham suve pitaram asya mūrdhan mama yoniḥ apsu antar samudre   tatas vi tiṣṭhe bhuvanāni viśvā uta amūm dyām varṣmaṇā upa spṛśāmi  
aham eva vātaḥ eva pra vāmi ārabhamāṇā bhuvanāni viśvā   paras divā paras enā pṛthivyāḥ etāvatī mahimnā sam babhūva  
tvayā manyo sa ratham ārujantaḥ harṣamāṇāḥ hṛṣitāsaḥ marutvan   tigmeṣavaḥ āyudhā saṃśiśānāḥ upa pra yantu naraḥ agni rūpāḥ  
agniḥ iva manyo tviṣitaḥ sahasva senānīḥ naḥ sahure hūtaḥ edhi   hatvāya śatrūn vi bhajasva vedaḥ ojaḥ mimānaḥ vi mṛdhaḥ nudasva  
sahasva manyo abhimātim asmai rujan mṛṇan pramṛṇan prehi śatrūn   ugram te pājaḥ nanu ā rurudhre vaśī vaśam nayāsai ekaja tvam  
ekaḥ bahūnām asi manye īḍitā viśaṃviśam yuddhāya sam śiśādhi   a kṛtta ruc tvayā yujā vayam dyumantam ghoṣam vijayāya kṛṇmasi  
vijeṣa kṛt indraḥ iva anavabravaḥ asmākam manyo adhipāḥ bhava iha   priyam te nāma sahure gṛṇīmasi vidma tam utsam yatas ābabhūtha  
ābhūtyā sahajā vajra sāyaka sahaḥ bibharṣi sahabhūta uttaram   kratvā naḥ manyo saha medi edhi mahādhanasya puruhūta saṃsṛji  
saṃsṛṣṭam dhanam ubhayam samākṛtam asmabhyam dhattām varuṇaḥ ca manyuḥ   bhiyaḥ dadhānāḥ hṛdayeṣu śatravaḥ parājitāsaḥ apa ni layantām  
yaḥ te manyaḥ avidhat vajra sāyaka sahaḥ ojaḥ puṣyati viśvam ānuṣak   sāhyāma dāsam āryam tvayā yujā vayam sahaskṛtena sahasā sahasvatā  
manyuḥ indraḥ manyuḥ eva āsa devaḥ manyuḥ hotā varuṇaḥ jātavedāḥ   manyum viśaḥ īḍate mānuṣīḥ yāḥ pahi naḥ manyo tapasā sajoṣāḥ  
abhīhi manyo tavasaḥ tavīyān tapasā yujā vi jahi śatrūn   amitra hā vṛtra hā dasyu hā ca viśvā vasūni ā bhara tvam naḥ  
tvam hi manyo abhibhūti ojāḥ svayaṃbhūḥ bhāmaḥ abhimātiṣāhaḥ   viśvacarṣaṇiḥ sahuriḥ sahīyān asmāsu ojaḥ pṛtanāsu dhehi  
a bhāgaḥ san apa paretaḥ asmi tava kratvā taviṣasya pracetaḥ   tam tvā manyo a kratuḥ jihīḍa aham svā tanūḥ bala dāvā naḥ ehi  
ayam te asmi upa naḥ ehi arvāṅ pratīcīnaḥ sahure viśvadāvan   manyo vajrin abhi naḥ ā vavṛtsva hanāva dasyūn uta bodhi āpeḥ  
abhi prehi dakṣiṇatas bhava naḥ adhā vṛtrāṇi jaṅghanāva bhūri   juhomi te dharuṇam madhvaḥ agram ubhau upāṃśu prathamā pibāva  
apa naḥ śośucat agham agne śuśugdhi ā rayim   apa naḥ śośucat agham  
su kṣetriyā sugātuyā vasūyā ca yajāmahe  apa naḥ śośucat agham 
pra yat bhandiṣṭhaḥ eṣām pra asmākāsaḥ ca sūrayaḥ   apa naḥ śośucat agham  
pra yat te agne sūrayaḥ jāyemahi pra te vayam   apa naḥ śośucat agham 
pra yat agneḥ sahasvataḥ viśvatas yanti bhānavaḥ   apa naḥ śośucat agham  
tvam hi viśvatomukha viśvatas paribhūḥ asi   apa naḥ śośucat agham  
dviṣaḥ naḥ viśvatomukhā ati nāvā iva pāraya   apa naḥ śośucat agham  
sa naḥ sindhum iva nāvāti parṣa svastaye   apa naḥ śośucat agham  
brahma asya śīrṣam bṛhat asya pṛṣṭham vāmadevyam udaram odanasya   chandāṃsi pakṣau mukham asya satyam viṣṭārī jātaḥ tapasaḥ adhi yajñaḥ  
anasthāḥ pūtāḥ pavanena śuddhāḥ śucayaḥ śucim api yanti lokam   na eṣām śiśnam pra dahati jātavedāḥ svarge loke bahu straiṇam eṣām  
viṣṭāriṇam odanam ye pacanti na enān avartiḥ sacate kadā cana   āste yamaḥ upa yāti devān sam gandharvaiḥ madate somyebhiḥ  
viṣṭāriṇam odanam ye pacanti na enān yamaḥ pari muṣṇāti retaḥ   rathī ha bhūtvā rathayānaḥ īyate pakṣī ha bhūtvā ati divaḥ sam eti  
eṣa yajñānām vitataḥ vahiṣṭhaḥ viṣṭāriṇam paktvā divam ā viveśa   āṇḍīkam kumudam sam tanoti bisam śālūkam śaphakaḥ mulālī   etāḥ tvā dhārāḥ upa yantu sarvāḥ svarge loke madhumat pinvamānāḥ upa tvā tiṣṭhantu puṣkariṇīḥ samantāḥ  
ghṛtahradāḥ madhu kūlāḥ surā udakāḥ kṣīreṇa pūrṇāḥ udakena dadhnā   etāḥ tvā dhārāḥ upa yantu sarvāḥ svarge loke madhumat pinvamānāḥ upa tvā tiṣṭhantu puṣkariṇīḥ samantāḥ  
caturaḥ kumbhān caturdhā dadāmi kṣīreṇa pūrnām udakena dadhnā   etāḥ tvā dhārāḥ upa yantu sarvāḥ svarge loke madhumat pinvamānāḥ upa tvā tiṣṭhantu puṣkariṇīḥ samantāḥ  
imam odanam ni dadhe brāhmaṇeṣu viṣṭāriṇam loka jitam svargam   sa me mā kṣeṣṭa svadhayā pinvamānaḥ viśva rūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughā me astu  
yam odanam prathama jāḥ ṛtasya prajāpatiḥ tapasā brahmaṇe apacat   yaḥ lokānām vidhṛtiḥ nābhireṣāt tena odanena ati tarāṇi mṛtyum  
yena ataran bhūta kṛtaḥ ati mṛtyum yam anvavindan tapasā śrameṇa   yam papāca brahmaṇe brahma pūrvam tena odanena ati tarāṇi mṛtyum  
yaḥ dādhāra pṛthivīm viśva bhojasam yaḥ antarikṣam āpṛṇāt rasena   yaḥ astabhnāt divam ūrdhvaḥ mahimnā tena odanena ati tarāṇi mṛtyum  
yasmāt māsāḥ nirmitāḥ triṃśat arāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ yasmāt nirmitaḥ dvādaśa araḥ   ahar rātrāḥ yam pariyantaḥ na āpuḥ tena odanena ati tarāṇi mṛtyum  
yaḥ prāṇa daḥ prāṇa davān babhūva yasmai lokāḥ ghṛtavantaḥ kṣaranti   jyotiṣmatīḥ pradiśaḥ yasya sarvāḥ tena odanena ati tarāṇi mṛtyum  
yasmāt pakvāt amṛtam saṃbabhūva yaḥ gāyatryāḥ adhipatiḥ babhūva   yasmin vedāḥ nihitāḥ viśva rūpāḥ tena odanena ati tarāṇi mṛtyum  
ava bādhe dviṣantam deva pīyum sapatnāḥ ye me apa te bhavantu   brahmaudanam viśvajitam pacāmi śṛṇvantu me śraddadhānasya devāḥ  
tān satya ojāḥ pra dahatu agniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ vṛṣā   yaḥ naḥ durasyāt dipsāt ca atho yaḥ naḥ arātiyāt  
yaḥ naḥ dipsāt a dipsataḥ dipsataḥ yaḥ ca dipsati   vaiśvānarasya daṃṣṭrayoḥ agneḥ api dadhāmi tam  
yaḥ āgare mṛgayante pratikrośe amāvāsye   kravya adaḥ anyān dipsataḥ sarvān tān sahasā sahe  
sahe piśācān sahasā eṣām draviṇam dade   sarvān durasyataḥ hanmi sam me ākūtiḥ ṛdhyatām  
ye devāḥ tena hāsante sūryeṇa mimate javam   nadīṣu parvateṣu ye sam taiḥ paśubhiḥ vide  
tapanaḥ asmi piśācānām vyāghraḥ gomatām iva   śvānaḥ siṃham iva dṛṣṭvā te na vindante nyañcanam  
na piśācaiḥ sam śaknomi na stenaiḥ na vanargubhiḥ   piśācāḥ tasmāt naśyanti yam aham grāmam āviśe  
yam grāmam āviśataḥ idam ugram sahaḥ mama   piśācāḥ tasmāt naśyanti na pāpam upa jānate  
ye mā krodhayanti lapitāḥ hastinam maśakāḥ iva   tān aham manye durhitān jane alpa śayūn iva  
abhi tam nirṛtiḥ dhattām aśvam iva aśva abhidhānyā   malvaḥ yaḥ mahyam krudhyati saḥ u pāśāt na mucyate  
tvayā pūrvam atharvāṇaḥ jaghnuḥ rakṣāṃsi oṣadhe   tvayā jaghāna kaśyapaḥ tvayā kaṇvaḥ agastyaḥ  
tvayā vayam apsarasaḥ gandharvān cātayāmahe   ajaśṛṅgī aja rakṣaḥ sarvān gandhena nāśaya  
nadīm yantu apsarasaḥ apām tāram avaśvasam   gulgulūḥ pīlā naladī aukṣa gandhiḥ pramandanī   tat pareta apsarasaḥ pratibuddhāḥ abhūtana  
yatra aśvatthāḥ nyagrodhāḥ mahā vṛkṣāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ   tat pareta apsarasaḥ pratibuddhāḥ abhūtana  
yatra vaḥ preṅkhāḥ haritāḥ arjunāḥ uta yatra āghātāḥ karkaryaḥ saṃvadanti   tat pareta apsarasaḥ pratibuddhāḥ abhūtana  
iyam agan oṣadhīnām vīrudhām vīryāvatī   aja śṛṅgī arāṭakī tīkṣṇa śṛṅgī vyṛṣatu  
ānṛtyataḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ gandharvasya apsarāpateḥ   bhinadmi muṣkau api yāmi śepaḥ  
bhīmāḥ indrasya hetayaḥ śatam ṛṣṭīḥ ayasmayīḥ   tābhiḥ haviḥ adān gandharvān avakādān vyṛṣatu  
bhīmāḥ indrasya hetayaḥ śatam ṛṣṭīḥ hiraṇyayīḥ   tābhiḥ haviḥ adān gandharvān avakādān vyṛṣatu  
avakādān abhiśocān apsu jyotaya māmakān   piśācān sarvān oṣadhe pra mṛṇīhi sahasva ca  
śvā iva ekaḥ kapiḥ iva ekaḥ kumāraḥ sarva keśakaḥ   priyaḥ dṛśaḥ iva bhūtvā gandharvaḥ sacate striyaḥ   tam itas nāśayāmasi brahmaṇā vīryāvatā  
jāyāḥ id vaḥ apsarasaḥ gandharvāḥ patayaḥ yuyam   apa dhāvata amartyāḥ martyān mā sacadhvam  
udbhindatīm saṃjayantīm apsarām sādhu devinīm   glahe kṛtāni kṛṇvānām apsarām tām iha huve  
vicinvatīm ākirantīm apsarām sādhu devinīm   glahe kṛtāni gṛhṇānām apsarām tām iha huve  
yāyaiḥ parinṛtyati ādadānā kṛtam glahāt   sā naḥ kṛtāni sīṣatī prahām āpnotu māyayā   sā naḥ payasvatī aitu mā naḥ jaiṣuḥ idam dhanam  
yāḥ akṣeṣu pramodante śucam krodham ca bibhratī   ānandinīm pramodinīm apsarām tām iha huve  
sūryasya raśmīn anu yāḥ sañcaranti marīcīḥ vā yāḥ anusañcaranti   yāsām ṛṣabhaḥ dūratas vājinīvān sadyas sarvān lokān paryeti rakṣan   sa naḥ aitu homam imam jusāṇaḥ antarikṣeṇa saha vājinīvān  
antarikṣena saha vājinīvan karkīm vatsām iha rakṣa vājin   ime te stokāḥ bahulāḥ ehi arvāṅ iyam te karkī iha te manaḥ astu  
antarikṣeṇa saha vājinīvan karkīm vatsām iha rakṣa vājin   ayam ghāsaḥ ayam vraje iha vatsām ni badhnīmaḥ   yathānāma vaḥ īśmahe svāhā  
pṛthivyām agnaye sam anaman saḥ ārdhnot   yathā pṛthivyām agnaye samanaman eva mahyam saṃnamaḥ sam namantu  
pṛthivī dhenuḥ tasyāḥ agniḥ vatsaḥ   sā me agninā vatsena iṣam ūrjam kāmam duhām   āyuḥ prathamam prajām poṣam rayim svāhā  
antarikṣe vāyave sam anaman saḥ ārdhnot   yathā antarikṣe vāyave samanaman eva mahyam saṃnamaḥ sam namantu  
antarikṣam dhenuḥ tasyāḥ vatsaḥ   sā me vāyunā vatsena iṣam ūrjam kāmam duhām   āyuḥ prathamam prajām poṣam rayim svāhā  
divya ādityāya sam anaman saḥ ārdhnot   yathā divya ādityāya samanaman eva mahyam saṃnamaḥ sam namantu  
dyauḥ dhenuḥ tasyāḥ ādityaḥ vatsaḥ   sā me ādityena vatsena iṣam ūrjam kāmam duhām   āyuḥ prathamam prajām poṣam rayim svāhā  
dikṣu candrāya sam anaman saḥ ārdhnot   yathā dikṣu candrāya samanaman eva mahyam saṃnamaḥ sam namantu  
diśaḥ dhenavaḥ tāsām candraḥ vatsaḥ   tāḥ me candreṇa vatsena iṣam ūrjam kāmam duhām āyuḥ prathamam prajām posam rayim svāhā  
agnau agniḥ carati praviṣṭaḥ ṛṣīṇām putraḥ abhiśasti pāḥ u  namaskāreṇa namasā te juhomi mā devānām mithuyā karma bhāgam  
hṛdā pūtam manasā jātavedaḥ viśvāni deva vayunāni vidvān   sapta āsyāni tava jātavedaḥ tebhyaḥ juhomi sa juṣasva havyam  
ye purastāt juhvati jātavedaḥ prācyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   agnim ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
ye dakṣiṇatas juhvati jātavedaḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   yamam ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enā pratisareṇa hanmi  
ye paścāt juhvati jātavedaḥ pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   varuṇam ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
yaḥ uttaratas juhvati jātavedaḥ udīcyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   somam ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
ye adhastāt juhvati jātavedaḥ udīcyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   bhūmim ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
ye antarikṣāt juhvati jātavedaḥ vyadhvāyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   vāyum ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
yaḥ upariṣṭāt juhvati jātavedaḥ ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   sūryam ṛtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
ye diśām antardeśebhyaḥ juhvati jātavedaḥ sarvābhyaḥ digbhyaḥ abhidāsanti asmān   brahma rtvā te parāñcaḥ vyathantām pratyak enān pratisareṇa hanmi  
ṛdhak mantraḥ yonim yaḥ ābabhūva amṛta asuḥ vardhamānaḥ su janmā   adabdha asuḥ bhrājamānaḥ ahā iva tritaḥ dhartā dādhāra trīṇi  
ā yaḥ dharmāṇi prathamaḥ sasāda tatas vapūṃṣi kṛṇuṣe purūṇi   dhāsyuḥ yonim prathamaḥ ā viveśa yaḥ vācam an uditām ciketa  
yaḥ te śokāya tanvam rireca kṣarat hiraṇyam śucayaḥ anu svāḥ   atra ā dadhete amṛtāni nāma asme vastrāṇi viśaḥ erayantām  
pra yat ete prataram pūrvyam guḥ sadaḥsadaḥ ātiṣṭhantaḥ ajuryam   kaviḥ śuṣasya mātarā rihāṇe jāmyai dhuryam patim erayethām  
tat u su te mahat pṛthujman namaḥ kaviḥ kāvyena kṛṇomi   yat samyañcau abhiyantau abhi kṣām atrā mahī rodha cakre vāvṛdhete  
sapta maryādāḥ kavayaḥ tatakṣuḥ tāsām id ekām abhi aṃhuraḥ gāt   āyoḥ ha skambhaḥ upamasya nīḍe pathām visarge dharuṇeṣu tasthau  
uta amṛtāsuḥ vrate emi kṛnvan asuḥ ātmā tanvaḥ tat sumadguḥ   uta vā śakraḥ ratnam dadhāti ūrjayā vā yat sacate haviḥ dāḥ  
uta putraḥ pitaram kṣatram īḍe jyeṣṭham maryādam ahvayan svastaye   darśan nu tāḥ varuṇa yāḥ te viṣṭhāḥ āvarvratataḥ kṛṇavaḥ vapūṃṣi  
ardham ardhena payasā pṛṇakṣi ardhena śuṣma vardhase amura   avim vṛdhāma śagmiyam sakhāyam varuṇam putram adityāḥ iṣiram   kavi śastāni asmai vapūṃṣi avocāma rodasī satya vācā  
tat id āsa bhuvaneṣu jyeṣṭham yatas yajñaḥ ugraḥ tveṣa nṛmṇaḥ   sadyas jajñānaḥ ni riṇāti śatrūn anu yat enam madanti viśve ūmāḥ  
vavṛdhānaḥ śavasā bhūri ojāḥ śatruḥ dāsāya bhiyasam dadhāti   avyanat ca vyanat ca sasni sam te navanta prabhṛtāḥ madeṣu  
tve kratum api pṛñcanti bhūri dvis yat ete tris bhavanti ūmāḥ   svadoḥ svādīyaḥ svādunā sṛja sam adaḥ su madhu madhunā abhi yodhīḥ  
yadi cit nu tvā dhanā jayantam raṇeraṇe anumadanti viprāḥ   ojīyaḥ śuṣmin sthiram ā tanuṣva mā tvā dabhan durevāsaḥ kaśokāḥ  
tvayā vayam śāśadmahe raṇeṣu prapaśyantaḥ yudhenyāni bhūri   codayāmi te āyudhā vacobhiḥ sam te śiśāmi brahmaṇā vayāṃsi  
ni tat dadhiṣe avare pare ca yasmin āvitha avasā duroṇe   ā sthāpayata mātaram jigatnum atas invata karvarāṇi bhūri  
stuṣva varṣman puru vartmānam sam ṛbhvāṇam inatamam āptam āptyānām   ā darśati śavasā bhūri ojāḥ pra sakṣati pratimānam pṛthivyāḥ  
imā brahma bṛhaddivaḥ kṛṇavat indrāya śūṣam agriyaḥ svarṣāḥ   mahaḥ gotrasya kṣayati svarājā turaḥ cit viśvam arṇavat tapasvān  
eva mahān bṛhaddivaḥ atharvā avocat svām tanvam indram eva   svasārau mātaribhvarī aripre hinvanti ca ene śavasā vardhayanti ca  
mama agne varcaḥ vihaveṣu astu vayam tvā indhānāḥ tanvam puṣema   mahyam namantām pradiśaḥ catasraḥ tvayā adhyakṣeṇa pṛtanāḥ jayema  
agne manyum pratinudan pareṣām tvam naḥ gopāḥ pari pāhi viśvatas   apāñcaḥ yantu nivatāḥ durasyavaḥ amā eṣām cittam prabudhām vi neśat  
mama devāḥ vihave santu sarve indravantaḥ marutaḥ viṣṇuḥ agniḥ   mama antarikṣam uru lokam astu mahyam vātaḥ pavatām kāmāya asmai  
mahyam yajantām mama yāni iṣṭā ākūtiḥ satyā manasaḥ me astu   enaḥ mā ni gām katamat cana aham viśve devāḥ abhi rakṣantu mā iha  
mayi devāḥ draviṇam ā yajantām mayi āśīḥ astu mayi deva hūtiḥ   daivāḥ hotāraḥ saniṣan naḥ etat ariṣṭāḥ syāma tanvā su vīrāḥ  
daivīḥ ṣaṭ urvīḥ uru naḥ kṛṇota viśve devāsaḥ iha mādayadhvam   mā naḥ vidat abhibhā mā u aśastiḥ mā naḥ vidat vṛjinā dveṣyā yā  
tisraḥ devīḥ mahi naḥ śarma yacchata prajāyai naḥ tanve yat ca puṣṭam   mā hāsmahi prajayā mā tanūbhiḥ mā radhāma dviṣate soma rājan  
uru vyacāḥ naḥ mahiṣaḥ śarma yacchatu asmin have puruhūtaḥ purukṣu   sa naḥ prajāyai haryaśva mṛḍa indra mā naḥ rīriṣaḥ mā parā dāḥ  
dhātā vidhātā bhuvanasya yaḥ patiḥ devaḥ savitā abhimātiṣāhaḥ   ādityāḥ rudrāḥ aśvinā ubhā devāḥ pāntu yajamānam nirṛthāt  
ye naḥ sapatnāḥ apa te bhavantu indra agnibhyām ava bādhāmahe enān   ādityāḥ rudrāḥ uparispṛśaḥ naḥ ugram cettāram adhirājam akrata  
arvāñcam indram amutas havāmahe yaḥ go jit dhana jit aśva jit yaḥ   imam naḥ yajñam vihave śṛṇotu asmākam abhūḥ haryaśva medī  
yaḥ giriṣu ajāyathāḥ vīrudhām balavattamaḥ   kuṣṭhehi takma nāśana takmānam nāśayan itas  
suparṇa suvane girau jātam himavataḥ pari   dhanaiḥ abhi śrutvā yanti viduḥ hi takmanā aśanam  
aśvatthaḥ deva sadanaḥ tṛtīyasyām itas divi   tatra amṛtasya cakṣaṇam devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata  
hiraṇyayī nauḥ acarat hiraṇya bandhanā divi   tatra amṛtasya puṣpam devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata  
hiraṇyayāḥ panthānaḥ āsan aritrāṇi hiraṇyayā   nāvaḥ hiraṇyayīḥ āsan yābhiḥ kuṣṭham nirāvahan  
imam me kuṣṭha pūruṣam tam ā vaha tam niḥ kuru   tam u me agadam kṛdhi  
devebhyaḥ adhi jātaḥ asi somasya asi sakhā hitaḥ   sa prāṇāya vyānāya cakṣuṣe me asmai mṛḍa  
udaṅ jātaḥ himavataḥ sa prācyām nīyase janam   tatra kuṣṭhasya nāmāni uttamāni vi bhejire  
uttamaḥ nāma kuṣṭhasi uttamaḥ nāma te pitā   yakṣmam ca sarvam nāśaya takmānam ca arasam kṛdhi  
śīrṣa āmayam upahatyām akṣyoḥ tanvaḥ rapaḥ   kuṣṭhaḥ tat sarvam niḥ karat daivam samaha vṛṣṇyam  
rātrī mātā nabhaḥ pitā aryamā te pitāmahaḥ   silācī nāma vai asi sā devānām asi svasā  
yaḥ tvā pibati jīvati trāyase puruṣam tvam   bhartrī hi śaśvatām asi janānām ca nyañcanī  
vṛkṣam vṛkṣam ā rohasi vṛṣaṇyantī iva kanyalā   jayantī pratyātiṣṭhantī sparaṇī nāma vai asi  
yat daṇḍena yat iṣvā yat vāruḥ harasā kṛtam   tasya tvam asi niṣkṛtiḥ sā imam niḥ kṛdhi pūruṣam  
bhadrāt plakṣāt niḥ tiṣṭhasi aśvatthāt khadirāt dhavāt   bhadrāt nyagrodhāt parṇāt sā naḥ ehi arundhati  
hiraṇya varṇe subhage sūrya varṇe vapuṣṭame   rutam gacchāsi niṣkṛte niṣkṛtiḥ nāma vai asi  
hiraṇya varṇe subhage śuṣme lomaśa vakṣane   apām asi svasā lākṣe vātaḥ ha ātmā babhūva te  
silācī nāma kānīnaḥ ajababhru pitā tava   aśvaḥ yamasya yaḥ śyāvaḥ tasya hāsnā asi ukṣitā  
aśvasya asnaḥ saṃpatitā sā vṛkṣām abhi siṣyade   sarā patatriṇī bhūtvā sā naḥ ehi arundhati  
brahma jajñānam prathamam purastāt vi sīmataḥ su rucaḥ venaḥ āvaḥ   sa budhnyāḥ upamāḥ asya viṣṭhāḥ sataḥ ca yonim asataḥ ca vi var  
an āptāḥ ye vaḥ prathamāḥ yāni karmāṇi cakrire   vīrān naḥ atra mā dabhan tat vaḥ etat puras dadhe  
sahasra dhāre eva te sam asvaran divaḥ nāke madhu jihvāḥ asaścataḥ   tasya spaśaḥ na ni miṣanti bhūrṇayaḥ padepade pāśinaḥ santi setave  
pari u su pra dhanva vājasātaye pari vṛtrāṇi sakṣaṇiḥ   dviṣaḥ tat adhi arṇavena īyase sanisrasaḥ nāma asi trayodaśaḥ māsaḥ indrasya gṛhaḥ  
nu etena arātsīḥ asau svāhā   tigma āyudhau tigma hetī su śevau somārudrau iha su mṛḍatam naḥ  
ava etena arātsīḥ asau svāhā   tigma āyudhau tigma hetī su śevau somārudrau iha su mṛḍatam naḥ  
apa etena arātsīḥ asau svāhā   tigma āyudhau tigma hetī su śevau somārudrau iha su mṛḍatam naḥ  
mumuktam asmān duritāt avadyāt juṣethām yajñam amṛtam asmāsu dhattam  
cakṣuṣaḥ hete manasaḥ hete brahmaṇaḥ hete tapasaḥ ca hete   menyā meniḥ asi amenayaḥ te santu ye asmām abhyaghāyanti  
yaḥ asmān cakṣuṣā manasā cittyā ākūtyā ca yaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   tvam tān agne menyā menīn kṛṇu svāhā  
indrasya gṛhaḥ asi   tam tvā pra padye tam tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarva pūruṣaḥ sarva ātmā sarva tanūḥ saha yat me asti tena  
indrasya śarmā asi   tam tvā pra padye tam tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarva pūruṣaḥ sarva ātmā sarva tanūḥ saha yat me asti tena  
indrasya varmā asi   tam tvā pra padye tam tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarva pūruṣaḥ sarva ātmā sarva tanūḥ saha yat me asti tena  
indrasya varūtham asi   tam tvā pra padye tam tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarva pūruṣaḥ sarva ātmā sarva tanūḥ saha yat me asti tena  
ā naḥ bhara mā pari stha arāte mā naḥ rakṣīḥ dakṣiṇām nīyamānām   namaḥ vīrtsāyāḥ asamṛddhaye namaḥ astu arātaye  
yam arāte purodhatse puruṣam parirāpiṇam   namaḥ te tasmai kṛṇmaḥ mā vanim vyathayīḥ mama  
pra naḥ vaniḥ deva kṛtā divā naktam ca kalpatām   arātim anupremaḥ vayam namaḥ astu arātaye  
sarasvatīm anumatim bhagam yantaḥ havāmahe   vācam juṣṭām madhumatīm avādiṣam devānām deva hūtiṣu  
yam yācāmi aham vācā sarasvatyā manaḥ yujā   śraddhā tam adya vindatu dattā somena babhruṇā  
mā vanim mā vācam naḥ vīrtsīḥ ubhau indra agnī ā bharatām naḥ vasūni   sarve naḥ adya ditsantaḥ arātim prati haryata  
paras apehi asamṛddhe vi te hetim nayāmasi   veda tvā aham nimīvantīm nitudantīm arāte  
uta nagnā bobhuvatī svapnayā sacase janam   arāte cittam vīrtsanti ākūtim puruṣasya ca  
yā mahatī mahā unmānā viśvāḥ āśāḥ vyānaśe   tasyai hiraṇyakeśyai nirṛtyai akaram namaḥ  
hiraṇya varṇā subhagā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ mahī   tasyai hiraṇya drāpaye arātyai akaram namaḥ  
vaikaṅkatena idhmena devebhyaḥ ājyam vaha   agne tām iha mādaya sarve ā yantu me havam  
indra ā yāhi me havam idam kariṣyāmi tat śṛṇu   ime aindrāḥ atisarāḥ ākūtim sam namantu me   tebhiḥ śakema vīryam jātavedaḥ tanū vaśin  
yat asau amutas devāḥ adevaḥ saṃścikīrṣati   mā tasya agniḥ havyam vākṣīt dhavam devāḥ asya mā upa guḥ mama eva havam etana  
ati dhāvata atisarāḥ indrasya vacasā hata   avim vṛkaḥ iva mathnīta sa vaḥ jīvan mā moci prāṇam asya api nahyata  
yam amī purodadhire brahmāṇam apabhūtaye   indra sa te adhaspadam tam prati asyāmi mṛtyave  
yadi preyuḥ deva purā brahma varmāṇi cakrire   tanū pānam paripāṇam kṛṇvānāḥ yat upocire sarvam tat arasam kṛdhi  
yān asau atisarān cakāra kṛṇavat ca yān   tvam tān indra vṛtrahan pratīcaḥ punar ā kṛdhi yathā amum tṛṇa hām janam  
yathā indraḥ udvācanam labdhvā cakre adhaspadam   kṛṇve aham adharān tathā amūn śaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyaḥ  
atra enān indra vṛtrahan ugraḥ marmaṇi vidhya   atra eva enān abhi tiṣṭha indra medi aham tava   anu tvā indra ā rabhāmahe syāma sumatau tava  
dive svāhā 
pṛthivyai svāhā 
antarikṣāya svāhā 
antarikṣāya svāhā 
dive svāhā 
pṛthivyai svāhā 
sūryaḥ me cakṣuḥ vātaḥ prāṇaḥ antarikṣam ātmā pṛthivī śarīram   astṛtaḥ nāma aham ayam asmi saḥ ātmānam ni dadhe dyāvāpṛthivībhyām gopīthāya  
ud āyuḥ ud balam ud kṛtam ud kṛtyām ud manīṣām ud indriyam   āyuṣkṛt āyuṣpatnī svadhāvantau gopāḥ me stam gopāyatam mā   ātma sadau me stam mā mā hiṃsiṣṭam  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā prācyāḥ diśaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā udīcyāḥ diśaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
aśma varma me asi yaḥ mā diśām antardeśebhyaḥ aghāyuḥ abhidāsāt   etat saḥ ṛchāt  
bṛhatā manaḥ upa hvaye mātariśvanā prāṇa apānau   sūryāt cakṣuḥ antarikṣāt śrotram pṛthivyāḥ śarīram   sarasvatyāḥ vācam upa hvayāmahe manaḥ yujā  
katham mahe asurāya abravīḥ iha katham pitre haraye tveṣa nṛmṇaḥ   pṛśnim varuṇa dakṣiṇām dadāvān punarmagha tvam manasā acikitsīḥ  
na kāmena punarmaghaḥ bhavāmi sam cakṣe kam pṛśnim etām upāje   kena nu tvam atharvan kāvyena kena jātena asi jātavedāḥ  
satyam aham gabhīraḥ kāvyena satyam jātena asmi jātavedāḥ   na me dāsaḥ nāryaḥ mahitvā vratam mīmāya yat aham dhariṣye  
na tvat anyaḥ kavitaraḥ na medhayā dhīrataraḥ varuṇa svadhāvan   tvam tā viśvā bhuvanāni vettha sa cit nu tvat janaḥ māyī bibhāya  
tvam hi aṅga varuṇa svadhāvan viśvā vettha janima su praṇīte   kim rajasaḥ enā paraḥ anyat asti enā kim pareṇa avaram amura  
ekam rajasaḥ enā paras anyat asti enā paras ekena durṇaśam cit arvāk   tat te vidvān varuṇa pra bravīmi adhas vacasaḥ paṇayaḥ bhavantu nīcais dāsāḥ upa sarpantu bhūmim  
tvam hi aṅga varuṇa bravīṣi punarmagheṣu avadyāni bhūri   mā u su paṇīn abhi etāvataḥ bhūt mā tvā vocan arādhasam janāsaḥ  
mā mā vocan arādhasam janāsaḥ punar te pṛśnim jaritar dadāmi   stotram me viśvam ā yāhi śacībhiḥ antar viśvāsu mānuṣīṣu dikṣu  
ā te stotrāṇi udyatāni yantu antar viśvāsu mānuṣīṣu dikṣu   dehi nu me yat me a dattaḥ asi yujyaḥ me sapta padaḥ sakhā asi  
samā nau bandhuḥ varuṇa samā jā veda aham tat yat nau eṣā samā jā   dadāmi tat yat te a dattaḥ asmi yujyaḥ te sapta padaḥ sakhā asmi  
devaḥ devāya gṛṇate vayodhāḥ vipraḥ viprāya stuvate sumedhāḥ   ajījanaḥ hi varuṇa svadhāvan atharvāṇam pitaram deva bandhum   tasmai u rādhaḥ kṛṇuhi su praśastam sakhā naḥ asi paramam ca bandhuḥ  
samiddhaḥ adya manuṣaḥ duroṇe devaḥ devān yajasi jātavedaḥ   ā ca vaha mitra mahaḥ cikitvān tvam dūtaḥ kaviḥ asi pracetāḥ  
tanūnapāt pathaḥ ṛtasya yānāt madhvā samañjan svadaya su jihva   manmāni dhībhiḥ uta yajñam ṛndhan devatrā ca kṛṇuhi adhvaram naḥ  
ājuhvānaḥ īḍyaḥ bandyaḥ ca ā yāhi agne vasubhiḥ sajoṣāḥ   tvam devānām asi yahva hotā saḥ enān yakṣīṣitaḥ yajīyān  
prācīnam barhiḥ pradiśā pṛthivyāḥ vastoḥ asyāḥ vṛjyate agre ahnām   vi u prathate vitaram varīyaḥ devebhyaḥ aditaye syonam  
vyacasvatīḥ urviyāḥ vi śrayantām patibhyaḥ na janayaḥ śumbhamānāḥ   devīḥ dvāraḥ bṛhatīḥ viśvaminvāḥ devebhyaḥ bhavata suprāyaṇāḥ  
ā suṣvayantī yajate upāke uṣāsānaktā sadatām ni yonau   divye yoṣaṇe bṛhatī su rukme adhi śriyam śukrapiśam dadhāne  
daivyā hotārā prathamā su vācā mimānā yajñam manuṣaḥ yajadhyai   pracodayantā vidatheṣu kārū prācīnam jyotiḥ pradiśā diśantā  
ā naḥ yajñam bhāratī tūyam etu iḍā manuṣvat iha cetayantī   tisraḥ devīḥ barhiḥ ā idam syonam sarasvatīḥ su apasaḥ sadantām  
yaḥ ime dyāvāpṛthivī janitrī rūpaiḥ apiṃśat bhuvanāni viśvā   tam adya hotar iṣitaḥ yajīyān devam tvaṣṭāram iha yakṣi vidvān  
upa avasṛja tmanyā samañjan devānām pāthaḥ ṛtuthā havīṃṣi   vanaspatiḥ śamitā devaḥ agniḥ svadantu havyam madhunā ghṛtena  
sadyas jātaḥ vi amimīta yajñam agniḥ devānām abhavat purogāḥ   asya hotuḥ praśiṣi ṛtasya vāci svāhākṛtam haviḥ adantu devāḥ  
dadiḥ hi mahyam varuṇaḥ divaḥ kaviḥ vacobhiḥ ugraiḥ ni riṇāmi te viṣam   khātam akhātam uta saktam agrabham irā iva dhanvan ni jajāsa te viṣam  
yat te apodakam viṣam tat te etāsu agrabham   gṛhṇāmi te madhyamam uttamam rasam uta avamam bhiyasā neśat āt u te  
vṛṣā me ravaḥ nabhasā na tanyatuḥ ugreṇa te vacasā bādhaḥ āt u te   aham tam asya nṛbhiḥ agrabham rasam tamasaḥ iva jyotiḥ ud etu sūryaḥ  
cakṣuṣā te cakṣuḥ hanmi viṣeṇa hanmi te viṣam   ahe mriyasva mā jīvīḥ pratyak abhi etu tvā viṣam  
kairāta pṛśnaḥ upatṛṇya babhro ā me śṛṇuta asitāḥ alīkāḥ   mā me sakhyuḥ stāmānam api ṣṭhāta āśrāvayantaḥ ni viṣe ramadhvam  
asitasya taimātasya babhroḥ apodakasya ca   sātrāsāhasya aham manyoḥ ava jyām iva dhanvanaḥ vi muñcāmi rathān iva  
āligī ca viligī ca pitā ca matā ca   vidma vaḥ sarvatas bandhu arasāḥ kim kariṣyatha  
urugūlāyāḥ duhitā jātā dāsī asiknyā   prataṅkam dadruṣīṇām sarvāsām arasam viṣam  
karṇā śvāvidh tat abravīt gireḥ avacarantikā   yāḥ kāḥ ca imāḥ khanitrimāḥ tāsām arasatamam viṣam  
tābuvam na tābuvam na gha id tvam asi tābuvam   tābuvena arasam viṣam  
tastuvam na tastuvam na gha id tvam asi tastuvam   tastuvena arasam viṣam  
suparṇaḥ tvā anu avindat sūkaraḥ tvā akhanat nasā   dipsā oṣadhe tvam dipsantam ava kṛtyā kṛtam jahi  
ava jahi yātudhānān ava kṛtyā kṛtam jahi   atha u yaḥ asmān dipsati tam u tvam jahi oṣadhe  
riśyasya iva parīśāsam parikṛtya pari tvacaḥ   kṛtyām kṛtyā kṛte devāḥ niṣkam iva prati muñcata  
punar kṛtyām kṛtyā kṛte hasta gṛhya parā naya   samakṣam asmai ā dhehi yathā kṛtyā kṛtam hanat  
kṛtyāḥ santu kṛtyā kṛte śapathaḥ śapathīyate   sukhaḥ rathaḥ iva vartatām kṛtyā kṛtyā kṛtam punar  
yadi strī yadi vā pumān kṛtyām cakāra pāpmane   tām u tasmai nayāmasi aśvam iva aśva abhidhānyā  
yadi vā asi deva kṛtā yadi vā puruṣaiḥ kṛtā   tām tvā punar nayāmasi indreṇa sayujā vayam  
agne pṛtanāṣāh pṛtanāḥ sahasva   punar kṛtyām kṛtyā kṛte pratiharaṇena harāmasi  
kṛta vyadhani vidhya tam yaḥ cakāra tam id jahi   na tvām acakruṣe vayam vadhāya sam śiśīmahi  
putraḥ iva pitaram gaccha svajaḥ iva abhiṣṭhitaḥ daśa   bandham iva avakrāmī gaccha kṛtye kṛtyā kṛtam punar  
ud eṇī iva vāraṇī abhiskandam mṛgī iva   kṛtyā kartāram ṛchatu  
iṣvā ṛjīyaḥ patatu dyāvāpṛthivī tam prati   sā tam mṛgam iva gṛhṇātu kṛtyā kṛtyā kṛtam punar  
agniḥ iva etu pratikūlam anukūlam iva udakam   sukhaḥ rathaḥ iva vartatām kṛtyā kṛtyā kṛtam punar  
ekā ca me daśa ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
dve ca me viṃśatiḥ ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
tisraḥ ca me triṃśat ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
catasraḥ ca me catvāriṃśat ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
pañca ca me pañcāśat ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
ṣaṭ ca me ṣaṣṭiḥ ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
sapta ca me saptatiḥ ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
aṣṭa ca me aśītiḥ ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
nava ca me navatiḥ ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
daśa ca me śatam ca me apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
śatam ca me sahasram ca apavaktāraḥ oṣadhe   ṛta jāte ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ  
yadi eka vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi dvi vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi trivṛsaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi catur vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi pañca vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi ṣaṣ vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi sapta vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi aṣṭa vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi nava vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi daśa vṛṣaḥ asi sṛja arasaḥ asi 
yadi ekādaśaḥ asi saḥ apodakaḥ asi  
te avadan prathamāḥ brahma kilbiṣe akūpāraḥ salilaḥ mātariśvā   vīḍu harāḥ tapaḥ ugram mayaḥ bhūḥ āpaḥ devīḥ prathama jāḥ ṛtasya  
somaḥ rājā prathamaḥ brahma jāyām punar prāyacchat a hṛṇīyamānaḥ   anvartitā varuṇaḥ mitraḥ āsīt agniḥ hotā hasta gṛhyā nināya  
hastena eva grāhyaḥ ādhiḥ asyāḥ brahma jāyā iti ced avocat   na dūtāya praheyā tasthe eṣā tathā rāṣṭram gupitam kṣatriyasya  
yām āhuḥ tārakā eṣā vikeśī iti duchunām grāmam avapadyamānām   sā brahma jāyā vi dunoti rāṣṭram yatra prāpādi śaśaḥ ulkuṣīmān  
brahmacārī carati veviṣat viṣaḥ sa devānām bhavati ekam aṅgam   tena jāyām anu avindat bṛhaspatiḥ somena nītām juhvam na devāḥ  
devāḥ vai etasyām avadanta pūrve sapta ṛṣayaḥ tapasā ye niṣeduḥ   bhīmā jāyā brāhmaṇasya apanītā durdhām dadhāti parame vyoman  
ye garbhāḥ avapadyante jagat yat ca apalupyate   vīrāḥ ye tṛhyante mithas brahma jāyāḥ hinasti tān  
uta yat patayaḥ daśa striyāḥ pūrve abrāhmaṇāḥ   brahmā ced hastam agrahīt saḥ eva patiḥ ekadhā  
brāhmaṇaḥ eva patiḥ na rājanyaḥ na vaiśyaḥ   tat sūryaḥ prabruvan eti pañcabhyaḥ mānavebhyaḥ  
punar vai devāḥ adaduḥ punar manuṣyāḥ adaduḥ   rājānaḥ satyam gṛhṇānāḥ brahma jāyām punar daduḥ  
punar dāya brahma jāyām kṛtvā devaiḥ nikilbiṣam   ūrjam pṛthivyāḥ bhaktvā uru gāyam upāsate  
na asya jāyā śata vāhī kalyāṇī talpam ā śaye   yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahma jāyā acittyā  
na vikarṇaḥ pṛthu śirāḥ tasmin veśmani jāyate   yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahma jāyā acittyā  
na asya kṣattā niṣka grīvaḥ sūnānām eti agratas   yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahma jāyā acittyā  
na asya śvetaḥ kṛṣṇakarṇaḥ dhuri yuktaḥ mahīyate   yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahma jāyā acittyā  
na asya kṣetre puṣkariṇī nāṇḍīkam jāyate bisam   yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahma jāyā acittyā  
na asmai pṛśnim vi duhanti ye asyāḥ doham upāsate   yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahma jāyā acittyā  
na asya dhenuḥ kalyāṇī na anaḍvān sahate dhuram   vijāniḥ yatra brahmaṇaḥ rātrim vasati pāpayā  
na etām te devāḥ adaduḥ tubhyam nṛpate attave   mā brāhmaṇasya rājanya gām jighatso anādyām  
akṣa drugdhaḥ rājanyaḥ pāpaḥ ātma parājitaḥ   sa brāhmaṇasya gām adyāt adya jīvāni mā śvas  
āviṣṭita agha viṣā pṛdākūḥ iva carmaṇā   sā brāhmaṇasya rājanya tṛṣṭā eṣā gauḥ anādyā  
niḥ vai kṣatram nayati hanti varcaḥ agniḥ iva ārabdhaḥ vi dunoti sarvam   yaḥ brāhmaṇam manyate annam eva sa viṣasya pibati taimātasya  
yaḥ enam hanti mṛdum manyamānaḥ deva pīyuḥ dhana kāmaḥ na cittāt   sam tasya indraḥ hṛdaye agnim indhe ubhe enam dviṣṭaḥ nabhasī carantam  
na brāhmaṇaḥ hiṃsitavyaḥ agniḥ priya tanoḥ iva   somaḥ hi asya dāyādaḥ indraḥ asya abhiśasti pāḥ  
śata apāṣṭhām ni girati tām na śaknoti niḥkhidam   annam yaḥ brahmaṇām malvaḥ svādu admi iti manyate  
jihvā jyā bhavati kulmalam vāc nāḍīkā dantāḥ tapasā abhidigdhāḥ   tebhiḥ brahmā vidhyati deva pīyūn hṛd balaiḥ dhanurbhiḥ deva jūtaiḥ  
tīkṣṇa iṣavaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ hetimantaḥ yām asyanti śaravyām na sā mṛṣā   anuhāya tapasā manyunā ca uta durāt ava bhindanti enam  
ye sahasram arājan āsan daśa śatāḥ uta   te brāhmaṇasya gām jagdhvā vaitahavyāḥ parābhavan  
gauḥ eva tān hanyamānā vaitahavyām avātirat   ye kesara prābandhāyāḥ caramājām apeciran  
eka śatam tāḥ janatāḥ yāḥ bhūmiḥ vyadhūnuta   prajām hiṃsitvā brāhmaṇīm asaṃbhavyam parābhavan  
deva pīyuḥ carati martyeṣu gara gīrṇaḥ bhavati asthi bhūyān   yaḥ brāhmaṇam deva bandhum hinasti na sa pitṛyāṇam api eti lokam  
agniḥ vai naḥ padavāyaḥ somaḥ dāyādaḥ ucyate   hantā abhiśasta indraḥ tathā tat vedhasaḥ viduḥ  
iṣuḥ iva digdhā nṛpate pṛdākūḥ iva gopate   sā brāhmaṇasya iṣuḥ ghorā tayā vidhyati pīyataḥ  
atimātram avardhanta na ud iva divam aspṛśan   bhṛgum hiṃsitvā sṛñjayāḥ vaitahavyāḥ parābhavan  
ye bṛhatsāmānam āṅgirasam ārpayan brāhmaṇam janāḥ   petvaḥ teṣām ubhaya adam aviḥ tokāni āvayat  
ye brāhmaṇam pratyaṣṭhīvan ye vā asmin śulkam īṣire   asnaḥ te madhye kulyāyāḥ keśān khādantaḥ āsate  
brahmagavī pacyamānā yāvat sā abhi vijaṅgahe   tejaḥ rāṣṭrasya niḥ hanti na vīraḥ jāyate vṛṣā  
krūram asyāḥ āśasanam tṛṣṭam piśitam asyate   kṣīram yat asyāḥ pīyate tat vai pitṛṣu kilbiṣam  
ugraḥ rājā manyamānaḥ brāhmaṇam yaḥ jighatsati   parā tat sicyate rāṣṭram brāhmaṇaḥ yatra jīyate  
aṣṭāpadī catur akṣī catur śrotrā catur hanuḥ   dvi āsyā dvi jihvā bhūtvā sā rāṣṭram ava dhūnute brahmajyasya  
tat vai rāṣṭram ā sravati nāvam bhinnām iva udakam   brahmāṇam yatra hiṃsanti tat rāṣṭram hanti duchunā  
tam vṛkṣāḥ apa sedhanti chāyām naḥ mā upa gāḥ iti   yaḥ brāhmaṇasya sat dhanam abhi nārada manyate  
viṣam etat deva kṛtam rājā varuṇaḥ abravīt   na brāhmaṇasya gām jagdhvā rāstre jāgāra kaḥ cana  
nava eva tāḥ navatayaḥ yāḥ bhūmiḥ vyadhūnuta   prajām hiṃsitvā brāhmaṇīm asaṃbhavyam parābhavan  
yām mṛtāya anubadhnanti kūdyam pada yopanīm   tat vai brahmajya te devāḥ upastaraṇam abruvan  
aśrūṇi kṛpamānasya yāni jītasya vāvṛtuḥ   tam vai brahmajya te devāḥ apām bhāgam adhārayan  
yena mṛtam snapayanti śmaśrūṇi yena undate   tam vai brahmajya te devāḥ apām bhāgam adhārayan  
na varṣam maitrāvaruṇam brahmajyam abhi varṣati   na asmai samitiḥ kalpate na mitram nayate vaśam  
uccais ghoṣaḥ dundubhiḥ satvanāyan vānaspatyaḥ saṃbhṛtaḥ usṛiyābhiḥ   vācam kṣuṇuvānaḥ damayan sapatnān siṃhaḥ iva jeṣyan abhi taṃstanīhi  
siṃhaḥ iva astānīt druvayaḥ vibaddhaḥ abhikrandan ṛṣabhaḥ vāsitām iva   vṛṣā tvam vadhrayaḥ te sapatnāḥ aindraḥ te śuṣmaḥ abhimātiṣāhaḥ  
vṛṣā iva yūthe sahasā vidānaḥ gavyan abhi ruva saṃdhanājit   śucā vidhya hṛdayam pareṣām hitvā grāmān pracyutāḥ yantu śatravaḥ  
saṃjayan pṛtanāḥ ūrdhvam āyuḥ gṛhyāḥ gṛhṇānaḥ bahudhā vi cakṣva   daivīm vācam dundubhe ā gurasva vedhāḥ śatrūṇām upa bharasva vedaḥ  
dundubheḥ vācam prayatām vadantīm āśṛṇvatī nāthitā ghoṣa buddhā   nārī putram dhāvatu hasta gṛhya amitrī bhītā samare vadhānām  
pūrvaḥ dundubhe pra vadāsi vācam bhūmyāḥ pṛṣṭhe vada rocamānaḥ   amitra senām abhijañjabhānaḥ dyumat vada dundubhe sūnṛtāvat  
antarā ime nabhasī ghoṣaḥ astu pṛthak te dhvanayaḥ yantu śībham   abhi kranda stanaya utpipānaḥ śloka kṛt mitra tūryāya svardhī  
dhībhiḥ kṛtaḥ pra vadāti vācam ud dharṣaya satvanām āyudhāni   indramedī satvanaḥ ni hvayasva mitraiḥ amitrām ava jaṅghanīhi  
saṃkrandanaḥ pravadaḥ dhṛṣṇuṣeṇaḥ praveda kṛt bahudhā grāma ghoṣī   śriyaḥ vanvanaḥ vayunāni vidvān kīrtim bahubhyaḥ vi hara dvirāje  
śreyaḥ ketaḥ vasu jit sahīyān saṃgrāma jit saṃśitaḥ brahmaṇā asi   aṃśūn iva grāvā adhiṣavaṇe adriḥ gavyan dundubhe adhi nṛtya vedaḥ  
śatrūṣāh nīṣāt abhimātiṣāhaḥ gaveṣaṇaḥ sahamānaḥ udbhid   vāgvī iva mantram pra bharasva vācam sāṃgrāma jityāya iṣam ud vada iha  
acyuta cyut samadaḥ gamiṣṭhaḥ mṛdhaḥ jetā puraeta ayodhyaḥ   indreṇa guptaḥ vidathā nicikyat dhṛddyotanaḥ dviṣatām yāhi śībham  
vihṛdayam vaimanasyam vada amitreṣu dundubhe   vidveṣam kaśmaśam bhayam amitreṣu ni dadhmasi ava enān dundubhe jahi  
udvepamānāḥ manasā cakṣuṣā hṛdayena ca   dhāvantu bibhyataḥ amitrāḥ pratrāsena ājye hute  
vānaspatyaḥ saṃbhṛtaḥ usriyābhiḥ viśva gotryaḥ   pratrāsam amitrebhyaḥ vada ājyena abhighāritaḥ  
yathā mṛgāḥ saṃvijante āraṇyāḥ puruṣāt adhi   eva tvam dundubhe amitrān abhi kranda pra trāsaya atho cittāni mohaya  
yathā vṛkāt aja avayaḥ dhāvanti bahu bibhyatīḥ   eva tvam dundubhe amitrān abhi kranda pra trāsaya atho cittāni mohaya  
yathā śyenāt patatriṇaḥ saṃvijante ahardivi siṃhasya stanathoḥ yathā   eva tvam dundubhe amitrān abhi kranda pra trāsaya atho cittāni mohaya  
parā amitrān dundubhinā hariṇasya ajinena ca   sarve devāḥ atitrasan ye saṃgrāmasya īṣate  
yaiḥ indraḥ prakrīḍate pad ghoṣaiḥ chāyayā saha   taiḥ amitrāḥ trasantu naḥ amī ye yanti anīkaśas  
jyā ghoṣāḥ dundubhayaḥ abhi krośantu yāḥ diśaḥ   senāḥ parājitāḥ yatīḥ amitrāṇām anīkaśas  
āditya cakṣuḥ ā datsva marīcayaḥ anu dhāvata   patsaṅginīḥ ā sajantu vigate bāhu vīrye  
yūyam ugrāḥ marutaḥ pṛśni mātaraḥ indreṇa yujā pra mṛnīta śatrūn   somaḥ rājā varuṇaḥ rājā mahādevaḥ uta mṛtyuḥ indraḥ  
etāḥ deva senāḥ sūrya ketavaḥ sacetasaḥ   amitrān naḥ jayantu svāhā  
agniḥ takmānam apa bādhatām itas somaḥ grāvā varuṇaḥ pūta dakṣāḥ   vediḥ barhiḥ samidhaḥ śośucānāḥ apa dveṣāṃsi amuyā bhavantu  
ayam yaḥ viśvān haritān kṛṇoṣi ucchocayan agniḥ iva abhidunvan   adhā hi takman arasaḥ hi bhūyāḥ adhā nyaṅ adharān vā parehi  
yaḥ paruṣaḥ pāruṣeyaḥ avadhvaṃsaḥ iva aruṇaḥ   takmānam viśvadhā vīrya adharāñcam parā suva  
adharāñcam pra hiṇomi namaḥ kṛtvā takmane   śakambharasya muṣṭi hā punar etu mahā vṛṣān  
okaḥ asya mūjavantaḥ okaḥ asya mahā vṛṣāḥ   yāvat jātaḥ takman tāvān asi balhikeṣu nyocaraḥ  
takman vyāla vi gada vyaṅga bhūri yāvaya   dāsīm niṣṭakvarīm icha tām vajreṇa sam arpaya  
takman mūjavataḥ gaccha balhikān vā parastarām   śūdrām icha prapharvyam tām takman vi iva dhūnuhi  
mahāvṛṣāt mūjavataḥ bandhu addhi paretya   pra etāni takmane brūmaḥ anya kṣetrāṇi vai imā  
anya kṣetre na ramase vaśī san mṛḍayāsi naḥ   abhūt u prārthaḥ takmā sa gamiṣyati balhikān  
yat tvam śītaḥ atho rūraḥ saha kāsāvepayaḥ   bhīmāḥ te takman hetayaḥ tābhiḥ sma pari vṛṅgdhi naḥ  
mā sma etān sakhīn kuruthāḥ balāsam kāsam udyugam   mā sma atas arvāṅ aiḥ punar tat tvā takman upa bruve  
takman bhrātrā balāsena svasrā kāsikayā saha   pāpmā bhrātṛvyeṇa saha gaccha amum araṇam janam  
tṛtīyakam vitṛtīyam sadandim uta śāradam   takmānam śītam rūram graiṣmam nāśaya vārṣikam  
gandhāribhyaḥ mūjavadbhyaḥ aṅgebhyaḥ magadhebhyaḥ   praiṣyan janam iva śevadhim takmānam pari dadmasi  
ote me dyāvāpṛthivī otā devī sarasvatī   otau me indraḥ ca agniḥ ca krimim jambhayatām iti  
asya indra kumārasya krimīn dhanapate jahi   hatāḥ viśvāḥ arātayaḥ ugreṇa vacasā mama  
yaḥ akṣyau parisarpati yaḥ nāse parisarpati   datām yaḥ madhyam gacchati tam krimim jambhayāmasi  
sarūpau dvau virūpau dvau kṛṣṇau dvau rohitau dvau   babhruḥ ca babhrukarṇaḥ ca gṛdhraḥ kokaḥ ca te hatāḥ  
ye krimayaḥ śiti kakṣāḥ ye kṛṣṇāḥ śiti bāhavaḥ   ye ke ca viśva rūpāḥ tān krimīn jambhayāmasi  
ud purastāt sūryaḥ eti viśva dṛṣṭaḥ adṛṣṭa hā   dṛṣṭān ca ghnan adṛṣṭān ca sarvān ca pramṛṇan krimīn  
yeva āṣāsaḥ kaṣkaṣāsaḥ ejatkāḥ śipavitnukāḥ   dṛṣṭaḥ ca hanyatām krimiḥ uta adṛṣṭaḥ ca hanyatām  
hataḥ yevāṣaḥ krimīṇām hataḥ nadanimā uta   sarvān ni maṣmaṣākaram dṛṣadā khalvān iva  
tri śīrṣāṇam trikakudam krimim sāraṅgam arjunam   śṛṇāmi asya pṛṣṭīḥ api vṛścāmi yat śiraḥ  
atri vat vaḥ krimayaḥ hanmi kaṇva vat jamadagni vat   agastyasya brahmaṇā sam pinaṣmi aham krimīn  
hataḥ rājā krimīṇām uta eṣām sthapatiḥ hataḥ   hataḥ hata mātā krimiḥ hata bhrātā hata svasā  
hatāsaḥ asya veśasaḥ hatāsaḥ pariveśasaḥ   atho ye kṣullakāḥ iva sarve te krimayaḥ hatāḥ  
sarveṣām ca krimīṇām sarvāsām ca krimīnām   bhinadmi aśmanā śiraḥ dahāmi agninā mukham  
savitā prasavānām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
agniḥ vanaspatīnām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
dyāvāpṛthivī dātṝṇām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
varuṇaḥ apām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
mitrāvaruṇau vṛṣṭyā adhipatī tau māvatām   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
marutaḥ parvatānām adhipatayaḥ te mā avantu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
somaḥ vīrudhām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
vāyuḥ antarikṣasya adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
sūryaḥ cakṣuṣām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
candramāḥ nakṣatrāṇām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
indraḥ divaḥ adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
marutām pitā paśūnām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
mṛtyuḥ prajānām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
yamaḥ pitṝṇām adhipatiḥ sa mā avatu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
pitaraḥ pare te mā avantu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
tatas avare te mā avantu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratisṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
tatas tatāmahāḥ te mā avantu   asmin brahmaṇi asmin karmaṇi asyām purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyām   cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣi asyām deva hūtyām svāhā  
parvatāt divaḥ yoneḥ aṅgāt aṅgāt samābhṛtam   śepaḥ garbhasya retaḥ dhāḥ sarau parṇam iva ā dadhat  
yathā iyam pṛthivī mahī bhūtānām garbham ādadhe   eva ā dadhāmi te garbham tasmai tvām avase huve  
garbham dhehi sinīvāli garbham dhehi sarasvati   garbham te aśvinā ubhā dhattām puṣkara srajā  
garbham te mitrāvaruṇau garbham devaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ   garbham te indraḥ ca agniḥ ca garbham dhātā dadhātu te  
viṣṇuḥ yonim kalpayatu tvaṣṭā rūpāṇi piṃśatu   ā siñcatu prajāpatiḥ dhātā garbham dadhātu te  
yat veda rājā varuṇaḥ yat vā devī sarasvatī   yat indraḥ vṛtra hā veda tat garbha karaṇam piba  
garbhaḥ asi oṣadhīnām garbhaḥ vanaspatīnām   garbhaḥ viśvasya bhūtasya saḥ agne garbham ā iha dhāḥ  
adhi skanda vīrayasva garbham ā dhehi yonyām   vṛṣā asi vṛṣṇyāvan prajāyai tvā nayāmasi  
vi jihīṣva bārhatsāme garbhaḥ te yonim ā śayām   aduḥ te devāḥ putram soma pāḥ ubhayāvinam  
dhātar śreṣṭhena rūpeṇa asyāḥ nāryāḥ gavīnyoḥ   pumāṃsam putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave  
tvaṣṭar śreṣṭhena rūpeṇa asyāḥ nāryāḥ gavīnyoḥ   pumāṃsam putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave  
savitar śreṣṭhena rūpeṇa asyāḥ nāryāḥ gavīnyoḥ   pumāṃsam putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave  
prajāpate śreṣṭhena rūpeṇa asyāḥ nāryāḥ gavīnyoḥ   pumāṃsam putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave  
yajūṃṣi yajñe samidhaḥ svāhā agniḥ pravidvān iha vaḥ yunaktu  
yunaktu devaḥ savitā prajānan asmin yajñe mahiṣaḥ svāhā 
indraḥ ukthāmadāni asmin yajñe pravidvān yunaktu su yujaḥ svāhā  
pra eṣāḥ yajñe nividaḥ svāhā śiṣṭāḥ patnībhiḥ vahata iha yuktāḥ 
chandāṃsi yajñe marutaḥ svāhā mātā iva putram pipṛta iha yuktāḥ 
ā iyam agan barhiṣā prokṣaṇībhiḥ yajñam tanvānā aditiḥ svāhā 
viṣṇuḥ yunaktu bahudhā tapāṃsi asmin yajñe su yujaḥ svāhā  
tvaṣṭā yunaktu bahudhā nu rūpāḥ asmin yajñe yunaktu su yujaḥ svāhā  
bhagaḥ yunaktu āśiṣaḥ nu asmai asmin yajñe pravidvān yunaktu su yujaḥ svāhā  
somaḥ yunaktu bahudhā payāṃsi asmin yajñe su yujaḥ svāhā  
indraḥ yunaktu bahudhā payāṃsi asmin yajñe su yujaḥ svāhā  
aśvinā brahmaṇā yātam arvāñcau vaṣaṭkāreṇa yajñam vardhayantau   bṛhaspate brahmaṇā yāhi arvāṅ yajñaḥ ayam svar idam yajamānāya svāhā  
ūrdhvāḥ asya samidhaḥ bhavanti ūrdhvā śukrā śocīṣī agneḥ   dyumattamā supratīkaḥ sa sūnuḥ tanūnapād asuraḥ bhūri pāṇiḥ  
devaḥ deveṣu devaḥ pathaḥ anakti madhvā ghṛtena 
madhvā yajñam nakṣati praiṇānaḥ narāśaṃsaḥ agniḥ su kṛt devaḥ savitā viśva vāraḥ 
achā ayam eti śavasā ghṛtā cit īdānaḥ vahniḥ namasā 
agniḥ srucaḥ adhvareṣu prayakṣu sa yakṣat asya mahimānam agneḥ 
tarī mandrāsu prayakṣu vasavaḥ ca atiṣṭhan vasudhātaraḥ ca 
dvāraḥ devīḥ anu asya viśve vratam rakṣanti viśvahā 
uru vyacasā agneḥ dhāmnā patyamāne   ā suṣvayantī yajate upāke uṣāsānaktā imam yajñam avatām adhvaram naḥ  
daivāḥ hotāraḥ ūrdhvam adhvaram naḥ agneḥ jihvayā abhi gṛnata gṛnata naḥ su iṣṭaye   tisraḥ devīḥ barhiḥ ā idam sadantām iḍā sarasvatī mahī bhāratī gṛṇānā  
tat naḥ turīpam adbhutam purukṣu   deva tvaṣṭā rāyaḥ poṣam vi sya nābhim asya  
vanaspate ava sṛja rarāṇaḥ   tmanā devebhyaḥ agniḥ havyam śamitā svadayatu  
agne svāhā kṛṇuhi jātavedaḥ   indrāya yajñam viśve devāḥ haviḥ idam juṣantām  
nava prāṇān navabhiḥ sam mimīte dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya   harite trīṇi rajate trīṇi ayasi trīṇi tapasā āviṣṭitāni  
agniḥ sūryaḥ candramāḥ bhūmiḥ āpaḥ dyauḥ antarikṣam pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca   ārtavāḥ ṛtubhiḥ saṃvidānāḥ anena mā trivṛtā pārayantu  
trayaḥ poṣāḥ trivṛti śrayantām anaktu pūṣā payasā ghṛtena   annasya bhūmā puruṣasya bhūmā bhūmā paśūnām te iha śrayantām  
imam ādityāḥ vasunā sam ukṣata imam agne vardhaya vavṛdhānaḥ   imam indra sam sṛja vīryeṇa asmin trivṛt śrayatām poṣayiṣṇu  
bhūmiḥ tvā pātu haritena viśva bhṛt agniḥ pipartu ayasā sajoṣāḥ   vīrudbhiḥ te arjunam saṃvidānam dakṣam dadhātu sumanasyamānam  
tredhā jātam janmanā idam hiraṇyam agneḥ ekam priyatamam babhūva somasya ekam hiṃsitasya parāpatat   apām ekam vedhasām retaḥ āhuḥ tat te hiraṇyam trivṛt astu āyuṣe  
tri āyuṣam jamadagneḥ kaśyapasya tri āyuṣam   tredhā amṛtasya cakṣaṇam trīṇi āyūṃṣi te akaram  
trayaḥ suparṇāḥ trivṛtā yat āyan eka akṣaram abhisaṃbhūya śakrāḥ   prati auhat mṛtyum amṛtena sākam antardadhānāḥ duritāni viśvā  
divaḥ tvā pātu haritam madhyāt tvā pātu arjunam   bhūmyāḥ ayasmayam pātu prāgāt deva purāḥ ayam  
imāḥ tisraḥ deva purāḥ tāḥ tvā rakṣantu sarvatas   tāḥ tvam bibhrat varcasvī uttaraḥ dviṣatām bhava  
puram devānām amṛtam hiraṇyam yaḥ ābedhe prathamaḥ devaḥ agre   tasmai namaḥ daśa prācīḥ kṛṇomi anu manyatām trivṛt ābadhe me  
ā tvā cṛtatu aryamā pūṣā bṛhaspatiḥ   ahar jātasya yat nāma tena tvā ati cṛtāmasi  
ṛtubhiḥ tvā ārtavaiḥ āyuṣe varcase tvā   saṃvatsarasya tejasā tena saṃhanu kṛṇmasi  
ghṛtāt ulluptam madhunā samaktam bhūmi dṛṃham acyutam pārayiṣṇu   bhindat sapatnān adharān ca kṛṇvat ā mā roha mahate saubhagāya  
purastāt yuktaḥ vaha jātavedaḥ agne viddhi kriyamāṇam yathā idam   tvam bhiṣaj bheṣajasya asi kartā tvayā gām aśvam puruṣam sanema  
tathā tat agne kṛṇu jātavedaḥ viśvebhiḥ devaiḥ saha saṃvidānaḥ   yaḥ naḥ dideva yatamaḥ jaghāsa yathā saḥ asya paridhiḥ patāti  
yathā saḥ asya paridhiḥ patāti tathā tat agne kṛṇu jātavedaḥ   viśvebhiḥ devaiḥ saha saṃvidānaḥ  
akṣyau ni vidhya hṛdayam ni vidhya jihvām ni tṛnddhi pra dataḥ mṛṇīhi   piśācaḥ asya yatamaḥ jaghāsa agne yaviṣṭha prati śṛṇīhi  
yat asya hṛtam vihṛtam yat parābhṛtam ātmanaḥ jagdham yatamat piśācaiḥ   tat agne vidvān punar ā bhara tvam śarīre māṃsam asum erayāmaḥ  
āme su pakve śabale vipakve yaḥ mā piśācaḥ aśane dadambha   tat ātmanā prajayā piśācāḥ vi yātayantām agadaḥ ayam astu  
kṣire mā manthe yatamaḥ dadambha ākṛṣṭapacye aśane dhānye yaḥ   tat ātmanā prajayā piśācāḥ vi yātayantām agadaḥ ayam astu  
apām mā pāne yatamaḥ dadambha kravyād yātūnām śayane śayānam   tat ātmanā prajayā piśācāḥ vi yātayantām agadaḥ ayam astu  
divā mā naktam yatamaḥ dadambha kravyād yātūnām śayane śayānam   tat ātmanā prajayā piśācāḥ vi yātayantām agadaḥ ayam astu  
kravya adam agne rudhiram piśācam manohanam jahi jātavedaḥ   tam indraḥ vājī vajreṇa hantu chinattu somaḥ śiraḥ asya dhṛṣṇuḥ  
sanāt agne mṛṇasi yātudhānān na tvā rakṣāṃsi pṛtanāsu jigyuḥ   sahamūrān anu daha kravya adaḥ mā te hetyāḥ mukṣata daivyāyāḥ  
samāhara jātavedaḥ yat dhṛtam yat parābhṛtam   gātrāṇi asya vardhantām aṃśuḥ iva ā pyāyatām ayam  
somasya iva jātavedaḥ aṃśuḥ ā pyāyatām ayam   agne virapśinam medhyam a yakṣmam kṛṇu jīvatu  
etāḥ te agne samidhaḥ piśāca jambhanīḥ   tāḥ tvam juṣasva prati ca enāḥ gṛhāṇa jātavedaḥ  
tārṣṭā aghīḥ agne samidhaḥ prati gṛhṇāhi arciṣā   jahātu kravyād rūpam yaḥ asya māṃsam jihīrṣati  
āvataḥ te āvataḥ parāvataḥ te āvataḥ   iha eva bhava mā nu gāḥ mā pūrvān anu gāḥ pitṝn asum badhnāmi te dṛḍham  
yat tvā abhiceruḥ puruṣaḥ svaḥ yat araṇaḥ janaḥ   unmocana pramocane ubhe vācā vadāmi te  
yat dudrohitha śepiṣe striyai puṃse acittyā   unmocana pramocane ubhe vācā vadāmi te  
yat enasaḥ mātṛ kṛtāt śeṣe pitṛ kṛtāt ca yat   unmocana pramocane ubhe vācā vadāmi te  
yat te mātā yat te pitā jamiḥ bhrātā ca sarjataḥ   pratyak sevasva bheṣajam jaradaṣṭim kṛṇomi tvā  
iha edhi puruṣa sarveṇa manasā saha   dūtau yamasya mānu gāḥ adhi jīva purā ihi  
anuhūtaḥ punar ehi vidvān udayanam pathaḥ   ārohaṇam ākramaṇam jīvataḥ jīvataḥ ayanam  
mā bibheḥ na mariṣyasi jaradaṣṭim kṛṇomi tvā   niḥ avocam aham yakṣmam aṅgebhyaḥ aṅga jvaram tava  
aṅga bhedaḥ aṅga jvaraḥ yaḥ ca te hṛdaya āmayaḥ   yakṣmaḥ śyenaḥ iva prāpaptat vacā sāḍhaḥ parastarām  
ṛṣī bodha pratībodhau asvapnaḥ yaḥ ca jāgṛviḥ   tau te prāṇasya goptārau divā naktam ca jāgṛtām  
ayam agniḥ upasadyaḥ iha sūryaḥ ud etu te   udehi mṛtyoḥ gambhīrāt kṛṣṇāt cit tamasaḥ pari  
namaḥ yamāya namaḥ astu mṛtyave namaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ uta ye nayanti   utpāraṇasya yaḥ veda tam agnim puras dadhe asmai ariṣṭatātaye  
aitu prāṇaḥ aitu manaḥ aitu cakṣuḥ atho balam   śarīram asya sam vidām tat padbhyām prati tiṣṭhatu  
prāṇena agne cakṣuṣā sam sṛja imam sam īraya tanvā sam balena   vettha amṛtasya mā nu gāt mā nu bhūmi gṛhaḥ bhuvat  
mā te prāṇaḥ upa dasat mā u apānaḥ api dhāyi te   sūryaḥ tvā adhipatiḥ mṛtyoḥ udāyacchatu raśmibhiḥ  
iyam antar vadati jihvā baddhā paniṣpadā   tvayā yakṣmam niḥ avocam śatam ropīḥ ca takmanaḥ  
ayam lokaḥ priyatamaḥ devānām aparājitaḥ   yasmai tvam iha mṛtyave diṣṭaḥ puruṣa jajñiṣe   sa ca tvā anu hvayāmasi mā purā jarasaḥ mṛthāḥ  
yām te cakruḥ āme pātre yām cakruḥ miśra dhānye   āme māṃse kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ kṛkavākau aje vā yām kurīriṇi   avyām te kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ ekaśaphe paśūnām ubhayādati   gardabhe kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ amūlāyām valagam vā narācyām   kṣetre te kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ gārhapatye pūrvāgnau uta duścitaḥ   śālāyām kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ sabhāyām yām cakruḥ adhidevane   akṣeṣu kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ senāyām yām cakruḥ iṣvāyudhe   dundubhau kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te kṛtyām kūpe avadadhuḥ śmaśāne vā nicakhnuḥ   sadmani kṛtyām yām cakruḥ punar prati harāmi tām  
yām te cakruḥ puruṣa āsthe agnau saṃkasuke ca yām   mrokam nirdāham kravya adam punar prati harāmi tām  
apathena ā jabhāra enām tām pathā itas pra hiṇmasi   adhīraḥ maryā adhīrebhyaḥ sam jabhāra acittyā  
yaḥ cakāra na śaśāka kartum śaśre pādam aṅgurim   cakāra bhadram asmabhyam abhagaḥ bhagavadbhyaḥ  
kṛtyā kṛtam valaginam mūlinam śapatheyyam   indraḥ tam hantu mahatā vadhena agniḥ vidhyatu astayā  
doṣaḥ gāya bṛhat gāya dyumat dhehi   ātharvaṇaḥ stuhi devam savitāram  
tam u stuhi yaḥ antar sindhau sūnuḥ   satyasya yuvānam adrogha vācam su śevam  
sa ghā naḥ devaḥ savitā sāviṣat amṛtāni bhūri   ubhe suṣṭutī sugātave  
indrāya somam ṛtvijaḥ sunota ca dhāvata   stotuḥ yaḥ vacaḥ śṛṇavat dhavam ca me  
ā yam viśanti indavaḥ vayaḥ na vṛkṣam andhasaḥ   virapśin vi mṛdhaḥ jahi rakṣasvinīḥ  
sunota soma pāvne somam indrāya vajriṇe   yuvā jeta īśānaḥ sa puruṣṭutaḥ  
pātam naḥ indrāpūṣaṇā aditiḥ pāntu marutaḥ   apām napāt sindhavaḥ sapta pātana pātu naḥ viṣṇuḥ uta dyauḥ  
pātām naḥ dyāvāpṛthivī abhiṣṭaye pātu grāvā pātu somaḥ naḥ aṃhasaḥ   pātu naḥ devī subhagā sarasvatī pātu agniḥ śivā ye asya pāyavaḥ  
pātām naḥ deva aśvinā śubhaḥ patī uṣāsānakta uta naḥ uruṣyatām   apām napāt abhihrutī gayasya cit deva tvaṣṭar vardhaya sarvatātaye  
tvaṣṭā me daivyam vacaḥ parjanyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ patiḥ   putraiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ aditiḥ nu pātu naḥ duṣṭaram trāyamāṇam sahaḥ  
aṃśaḥ bhagaḥ varuṇaḥ mitraḥ aryamā aditiḥ pāntu marutaḥ   apa tasya dveṣaḥ gamet abhihrutaḥ yāvayat śatrum antitam  
dhiye sam aśvinā prāvatam naḥ uruṣyāḥ naḥ urujman aprayuchan   dyauḥ pitar yāvaya duchunā yā  
ud enam uttaram naya agne ghṛtena āhuta   sam enam varcasā sṛja prajayā ca bahum kṛdhi  
indra imam prataram kṛdhi sajātānām asat vaśī   rāyaḥ poṣeṇa sam sṛja jīvātave jarase naya  
yasya kṛṇmaḥ haviḥ gṛhe tam agne vardhaya tvam   tasmai somaḥ adhi bravat ayam ca brahmaṇas patiḥ  
yaḥ asmān brahmaṇas pate a devaḥ abhimanyate   sarvam tam randhayāsi me yajamānāya sunvate  
yaḥ naḥ soma su śaṃsinaḥ duḥśaṃsaḥ ādideśati   vajreṇa asya mukhe jahi sa saṃpiṣṭaḥ apāyati  
yaḥ naḥ soma abhidāsati sanābhiḥ yaḥ ca niṣṭyaḥ   apa tasya balam tira mahī iva dyauḥ vadhatmanā  
yena soma aditiḥ pathā mitrāḥ vā yanti adruhaḥ   tena naḥ avasā gahi  
yena soma sāhantyā asurān randhayāsi naḥ   tena naḥ adhi vocata  
yena devāḥ asurāṇām ojāṃsi avṛṇīdhvam   tena naḥ śarma yacchata  
yathā vṛkṣam libujā samantam pariṣasvaje   eva pari svajasva mām yathā mām kāminī asaḥ yathā mat na āpagāḥ asaḥ  
yathā suparṇaḥ prapatan pakṣau nihanti bhūmyām   eva ni hanmi te manaḥ yathā mām kāminī asaḥ yathā mat na āpagāḥ asaḥ  
yathā ime dyāvāpṛthivī sadyas paryeti sūryaḥ   eva pari emi te manaḥ yathā mām kāminī asaḥ yathā mat na āpagāḥ asaḥ  
vāñcha me tanvam pādau vāñcha akṣyau vāñcha sakthyau   akṣyau vṛṣaṇyantyāḥ keśāḥ mām te kāmena śuṣyantu  
mama tvā doṣaṇi śriṣam kṛṇomi hṛdaya śriṣam   yathā mama kratau asaḥ mama cittam upāyasi  
yāsām nābhiḥ ārehaṇam hṛdi saṃvananam kṛtam gāvaḥ ghṛtasya mātaraḥ amūm sam vānayantu me 
pṛthivyai śrotrāya vanaspatibhyaḥ agnaye adhipataye svāhā  
prāṇāya antarikṣāya vayobhyaḥ vāyave adhipataye svāhā 
dive cakṣuṣe nakṣatrebhyaḥ sūryāya adhipataye svāhā  
śamīm aśvatthe ārūḍhaḥ tatra puṃsuvanam kṛtam   tat vai putrasya vedanam tat strīṣu ā bharāmasi  
puṃsi vai retaḥ bhavati tat striyām anu sicyate   tat vai putrasya vedanam tat prajāpatiḥ abravīt  
prajāpatiḥ anumatiḥ sinīvālī acīkḷpat   straiṣūyam anyatra dadhat pumāṃsam u dadhat iha  
pari dyām iva sūryaḥ ahīnām janima agamam   rātrī jagat iva anyat dhaṃsāt tena te vāraye viṣam  
yat brahmabhiḥ yat ṛṣibhiḥ yat devaiḥ viditam purā   yat bhūtam bhavyam āsanvat tena te vāraye viṣam  
madhvā pṛñce nadyaḥ parvatāḥ girayaḥ madhu   madhu paruṣṇī śīpālā śam āsne astu śam hṛde  
namaḥ deva vadhebhyaḥ namaḥ rāja vadhebhyaḥ   atho ye viśyānām vadhāḥ tebhyaḥ mṛtyo namaḥ astu te  
namaḥ te adhivākāya parāvākāya te namaḥ   sumatyai mṛtyo te namaḥ durmatyai te idam namaḥ  
namaḥ te yātudhānebhyaḥ namaḥ te bheṣajebhyaḥ   namaḥ te mṛtyo mūlebhyaḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ idam namaḥ  
asthi sraṃsam paru sraṃsam āsthitam hṛdaya āmayam   balāsam sarvam nāśaya aṅgeṣṭhāḥ yaḥ ca parvasu  
niḥ balāsam balāsinaḥ kṣiṇomi muṣkaram yathā   chinadmi asya bandhanam mūlam urvārvā iva  
niḥ balāsā itas pra pata aśuṅgaḥ śiśukaḥ yathā   atha u itas iva hāyanaḥ apa drāhi avīra hā  
uttamaḥ asi oṣadhīnām tava vṛkṣāḥ upastayaḥ   upastiḥ astu saḥ asmākam yaḥ asmām abhidāsati  
sabandhuḥ ca asabandhuḥ ca yaḥ asmām abhidāsati   teṣām sā vṛkṣāṇām iva aham bhūyāsam uttamaḥ  
yathā somaḥ oṣadhīnām uttamaḥ haviṣām kṛtaḥ   talāśāḥ vṛkṣāṇām iva aham bhūyāsam uttamaḥ  
ābayaḥ anābayaḥ rasaḥ te ugraḥ ābayo   ā te karambham admasi   ā te karambham admasi  
vihahlaḥ nāma te pitā madāvatī nāma te mātā   sa hina tvam asi yaḥ tvam ātmānam āvayaḥ  
tauvilike avelaya ava ayam ailaba ailayīt   babhruḥ ca babhrukarṇaḥ ca apehi niḥ āla  
alasāla asi pūrva silāñjāla asi uttarā  nīlāgalasāla 
yathā iyam pṛthivī mahī bhūtānām garbham ādadhe   eva te dhriyatām garbhaḥ anu sūtum savitave  
yathā iyam pṛthivī mahī dādhāra imān vanaspatīn   eva te dhriyatām garbhaḥ anu sūtum savitave  
yathā iyam pṛthivī mahī dādhāra parvatān girīn   eva te dhriyatām garbhaḥ anu sūtum savitave  
yathā iyam pṛthivī mahī dādhāra viṣṭhitam jagat  eva te dhriyatām garbhaḥ anu sūtum savitave  
īrṣyāyāḥ dhrājim prathamām prathamasyāḥ uta aparām   agnim hṛdayyam śokam tam te niḥ vāpayāmasi  
yathā bhūmiḥ mṛta manāḥ mṛtāt mṛta manastarā   yathā uta mamruṣaḥ manaḥ eva īrṣyoḥ mṛtam manaḥ  
adaḥ yat te hṛdi śritam manaskam patayiṣṇukam   tatas te īrṣyām muñcāmi niḥ ūṣmāṇam dṛteḥ iva  
punantu mā deva janāḥ punantu manavaḥ dhiyā   punantu viśvā bhūtāni pavamānaḥ punātu mā  
pavamānaḥ punātu mā kratve dakṣāya jīvase   atha u ariṣṭatātaye  
ubhābhyām deva savitar pavitreṇa savena ca   asmān punīhi cakṣase  
agneḥ iva asya dahataḥ eti śuṣmiṇaḥ uta iva mattaḥ vilapan apāyati   anyam asmat icchatu kam cit avrataḥ tapuḥ vadhāya namaḥ astu takmane  
namaḥ rudrāya namaḥ astu takmane namaḥ rājñe varuṇāya tviṣīmate   namaḥ dive namaḥ pṛthivyai namaḥ oṣadhībhyaḥ  
ayam yaḥ abhiśocayiṣṇuḥ viśvā rūpāṇi haritā kṛṇoṣi   tasmai te aruṇāya babhrave namaḥ kṛṇomi vanyāya takmane  
imāḥ yāḥ tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ tāsām ha bhūmiḥ uttamā   tāsām adhi tvacaḥ aham bheṣajam sam u jagrabham  
śreṣṭham asi bheṣajānām vasiṣṭham vīrudhānām   somaḥ bhagaḥ iva yāmeṣu deveṣu varuṇaḥ yathā  
revatīḥ anādhṛṣaḥ siṣāsavaḥ siṣāsatha   uta stha keśa dṛmhaṇīḥ atha u ha keśa vardhanīḥ  
kṛṣṇam niyānam harayaḥ suparṇāḥ apaḥ vasānāḥ divam ud patanti   te āvavṛtran sadanāt ṛtasya āt id ghṛtena pṛthivīm vi ūduḥ  
payasvatīḥ kṛṇutha apaḥ oṣadhīḥ śivāḥ yat ejatha marutaḥ rukma vakṣasaḥ   ūrjam ca tatra sumatim ca pinvata yatra naraḥ marutaḥ siñcatha madhu  
uda prutaḥ marutaḥ tām iyarta vṛṣṭiḥ yā viśvā nivataḥ pṛṇāti   ejāti glahā kanyā iva tunnairum tundānā patyā iva jāyā  
sasruṣīḥ tat apasaḥ divā naktam ca sasruṣīḥ   vareṇya kratuḥ aham apaḥ devīḥ upa hvaye  
otāḥ āpaḥ karmaṇyāḥ muñcantu itas praṇītaye   sadyas kṛṇvantu etave  
devasya savituḥ save karma kṛṇvantu mānuṣāḥ   śam naḥ bhavantu apaḥ oṣadhīḥ śivāḥ  
himavataḥ pra sravanti sindhau samaha saṅgamaḥ   āpaḥ ha mahyam tat devīḥ dadan hṛd dyota bheṣajam  
yat me akṣyoḥ ādidyota pārṣṇyoḥ prapadoḥ ca yat   āpaḥ tat sarvam niḥ karan bhiṣajām subhiṣaktamāḥ  
sindhu patnīḥ sindhu rājñīḥ sarvāḥ yāḥ nadyaḥ sthana   datta naḥ tasya bheṣajam tena vaḥ bhunajāmahai  
pañca ca yāḥ pañcāśat ca saṃyanti manyāḥ abhi   itas tāḥ sarvāḥ naśyantu vākāḥ apacitām iva  
sapta ca yāḥ saptatiḥ ca saṃyanti graivyāḥ abhi   itas tāḥ sarvāḥ naśyantu vākāḥ apacitām iva  
nava ca yāḥ navatiḥ ca saṃyanti skandhyāḥ abhi   itas tāḥ sarvāḥ naśyantu vākāḥ apacitām iva  
ava mā pāpman sṛja vaśī san mṛdayā asi naḥ   ā mā bhadrasya loke pāpman dhehi a vihrutam  
yaḥ naḥ pāpman na jahāsi tam u tvā jahimaḥ vayam   pathām anu vyāvartane anyam pāpmā anu padyatām  
anyatra asmat ni ucyatu sahasra akṣaḥ amartyaḥ   yam dveṣāma tam ṛchatu yam u dviṣmaḥ tam id jahi  
devāḥ kapotaḥ iṣitaḥ yat ichan dūtaḥ nirṛtyāḥ idam ājagāma   tasmai arcāma kṛṇavāma niṣkṛtim śam naḥ astu dvipade śam catuṣpade  
śivaḥ kapotaḥ iṣitaḥ naḥ astu anāgāḥ devāḥ śakunaḥ gṛham naḥ   agniḥ hi vipraḥ juṣatām haviḥ naḥ pari hetiḥ pakṣiṇī naḥ vṛṇaktu  
hetiḥ pakṣiṇī na dabhāti asmān āṣṭrī padam kṛṇute agnidhāne   śivaḥ gobhyaḥ uta puruṣebhyaḥ naḥ astu mā naḥ devāḥ iha hiṃsīt kapota  
ṛcā kapotam nudata praṇodam iṣam madantaḥ pari gām nayāmaḥ   saṃlobhayantaḥ duritā padāni hitvā naḥ ūrjam pra padāt pathiṣṭhaḥ  
pari ime agnim arṣata pari ime gām aneṣata   deveṣu akrata śravaḥ kaḥ imān ā dadharṣati  
yaḥ prathamaḥ pravatam āsasāda bahubhyaḥ panthām an upaspaśānaḥ   yaḥ asya īśe dvipadaḥ yaḥ catuṣpadaḥ tasmai yamāya namaḥ astu mṛtyave  
amūn hetiḥ patatriṇī ni etu yat ulūkaḥ vadati mogham etat   yat vā kapota padam agnau kṛṇoti  
yau te dūtau nirṛte idam etaḥ a prahitau prahitau vā gṛham naḥ   kapota ulūkābhyām a padam tat astu  
avairahatyāya idam ā papatyāt su vīra tāyai idam ā sasadyāt   parāṅ eva parā vada parācīm anu saṃvatam   yathā yamasya tvā gṛhe arasam praticākaśān ābhūkam praticākaśān  
devāḥ imam madhunā saṃyutam yavam sarasvatyām adhi maṇau acarkṛṣuḥ   indraḥ āsīt sīra patiḥ śatakratuḥ kīnāśāḥ āsan marutaḥ sudānavaḥ  
yaḥ te madaḥ avakeśaḥ vikeśaḥ yena abhihasyam puruṣam kṛṇoṣi   ārāt tvat anyā vanāni vṛkṣi tvam śami śata valśā vi roha  
bṛhat palāśe subhage varṣa vṛddhe ṛtāvari   mātā iva putrebhyaḥ mṛḍa keśebhyaḥ śami  
ā ayam gauḥ pṛśniḥ akramīt asadat mātaram puras   pitaram ca prayan svar  
antar carati rocanā asya prāṇāt apānataḥ   vi akhyat mahiṣaḥ svar  
triṃśat dhāmā vi rājati vāc pataṅgaḥ aśiśriyat   prati vastoḥ ahar dyubhiḥ  
antardāve juhuta su etat yātudhāna kṣayaṇam ghṛtena   ārāt rakṣāṃsi prati daha tvam agne na naḥ gṛhāṇām upa tītapāsi  
rudraḥ vaḥ grīvāḥ aśarait piśācāḥ pṛṣṭīḥ vaḥ api śṛṇātu yātudhānāḥ   vīrudh vaḥ viśvatovīryā yamena sam ajīgamat  
abhayam mitrāvaruṇau iha astu naḥ arciṣā attriṇaḥ nudatam pratīcaḥ   mā jñātāram mā pratiṣṭhām vidanta mithas vighnānāḥ upa yantu mṛtyum  
yasya idam ā rajaḥ yujaḥ tuje janā navam svar   indrasya rantyam bṛhat  
na ādhṛṣaḥ ā dadhṛṣate dhṛṣāṇaḥ dhṛṣitaḥ śavaḥ   purā yathā vyathiḥ śravaḥ indrasya naḥ ādhṛṣe śavaḥ  
sa naḥ dadātu tām rayim urum piśaṅga saṃdṛśam   indraḥ patiḥ tuviṣṭamaḥ janeṣu ā  
pra agnaye vācam īraya vṛṣabhāya kṣitīnām   sa naḥ parṣat ati dviṣaḥ  
yaḥ rakṣāṃsi nijūrvati agniḥ tigmena śociṣā   sa naḥ parṣat ati dviṣaḥ  
yaḥ parasyāḥ parāvataḥ tiras dhanva atirocate   sa naḥ parṣat ati dviṣaḥ  
yaḥ viśvā abhi vipaśyati bhuvanā sam ca paśyati   sa naḥ parṣat ati dviṣaḥ  
yaḥ asya pāre rajasaḥ śukraḥ agniḥ ajāyata   sa naḥ parṣat ati dviṣaḥ  
vaiśvānaraḥ naḥ ūtaye ā pra yātu parāvataḥ   agniḥ naḥ suṣṭutīḥ upa  
vaiśvānaraḥ naḥ āgamat imam yajñam sajūs upa   agniḥ uktheṣu aṃhasu  
vaiśvānaraḥ aṅgirasām stomam uktham ca cākḷpat  ā eṣu dyumnam svar yamat 
ṛtāvānam vaiśvānaram ṛtasya jyotiṣaḥ patim  ajasram gharmam īmahe 
sa viśvā prati cākḷpa ṛtūṃr ud sṛjate vaśī   yajñasya vayaḥ uttiran  
agniḥ pareṣu dhāmasu kāmaḥ bhūtasya bhavyasya   samrāt ekaḥ vi rājati  
upa prāgāt sahasrākṣaḥ yuktvā śapathaḥ ratham   śaptāram anvichat mama vṛkaḥ iva avimataḥ gṛham  
pari naḥ vṛṅgdhi śapatha hradam agniḥ iva ā dahan   śaptāram atra naḥ jahi divaḥ vṛkṣam iva aśaniḥ  
yaḥ naḥ śapāt a śapataḥ śapataḥ yaḥ ca naḥ śapāt   śune peṣṭram iva avakṣāmam tam prati asyāmi mṛtyave  
siṃhe vyāghraḥ uta yā pṛdākau tviṣiḥ agnau brāhmaṇe sūrye yā   indram yā devī subhagā jajāna sā naḥ aitu varcasā saṃvidānā  
yā hastini dvīpini yā hiraṇye tviṣiḥ apsu goṣu yā puruṣeṣu   indram yā devī subhagā jajāna sā naḥ aitu varcasā saṃvidānā  
rathe akṣeṣu ṛṣabhasya vāje vāte parjanye varuṇasya śuṣme   indram yā devī subhagā jajāna sā naḥ aitu varcasā saṃvidānā  
rājanye dundubhau āyatāyām aśvasya vāje puruṣasya māyau   indram yā devī subhagā jajāna sā naḥ aitu varcasā samvidānā  
yaśaḥ haviḥ vardhatām indra jūtam sahasra vīryam su bhṛtam sahaskṛtam   prasarsrāṇam anu dīrghāya cakṣase haviṣmantam mā vardhaya jyeṣṭhatātaye  
achā naḥ indram yaśasam yaśobhiḥ yaśasvinam namasānāḥ vidhema   sa naḥ rāsva rāṣṭram indra jūtam tasya te rātau yaśasaḥ syāma  
yaśāḥ indraḥ yaśāḥ agniḥ yaśāḥ somaḥ ajāyata   yaśāḥ viśvasya bhūtasya aham asmi yaśastamaḥ  
abhayam dyāvāpṛthivī iha astu naḥ abhayam somaḥ savitā naḥ kṛṇotu   abhayam naḥ astu uru antarikṣam sapta ṛṣīṇām ca haviṣā abhayam naḥ astu  
asmai grāmāya pradiśaḥ catasraḥ ūrjam su bhūtam svasti savitā naḥ kṛṇotu   a śatru indraḥ abhayam naḥ kṛṇotu anyatra rājñām abhi yātu manyuḥ  
anamitram naḥ adharāt anamitram naḥ uttarāt   indra anamitram naḥ paścāt anamitram puras kṛdhi  
manase cetase dhiyaḥ ākūtaye uta cittaye   matyai śrutāya cakṣase vidhema haviṣā vayam  
apānāya vyānāya prāṇāya bhūri dhāyase   sarasvatyāḥ uru vyace vidhema haviṣā vayam  
mā naḥ hāsiṣuḥ ṛṣayaḥ daivyāḥ ye tanū pāḥ ye naḥ tanvaḥ tanūjāḥ   amartyāḥ martyām abhi naḥ sacadhvam āyuḥ dhatta prataram jīvase naḥ  
ava jyām iva dhanvanaḥ manyum tanomi te hṛdaḥ   yathā saṃmanasau bhūtvā sakhāyau iva sacāvahai  
sakhāyau iva sacāvahai ava manyum tanomi te   adhas te aśmanaḥ manyum upāsyāmasi yaḥ guruḥ  
abhi tiṣṭhāmi te manyum pārṣṇyā prapadena ca   yathā avaśaḥ na vādiṣaḥ mama cittam upāyasi  
ayam darbhaḥ vimanyukaḥ svāya cāraṇāya ca   manyoḥ vimanyukasya ayam manyu śamanaḥ ucyate  
ayam yaḥ bhūri mūlaḥ samudram avatiṣṭhati   darbhaḥ pṛthivyāḥ utthitaḥ manyu śamanaḥ ucyate  
vi te hanavyām śaraṇim vi te mukhyām nayāmasi   yathā avaśaḥ na vādiṣaḥ mama cittam upāyasi  
asthāt dyauḥ asthāt pṛthivī asthāt viśvam idam jagat   asthuḥ vṛkṣāḥ ūrdhva svapnāḥ tiṣṭhāt rogaḥ ayam tava  
śatam yāḥ bheṣajāni te sahasram saṃgatāni ca   śreṣṭham āsrāva bheṣajam vasiṣṭham roga nāśanam  
rudrasya mūtram asi amṛtasya nābhiḥ   viṣāṇakā nāma vai asi pitṝṇām mūlāt utthitā vātīkṛta nāśanī  
paras apehi manaspāpa kim aśastāni śaṃsasi   parehi na tvā kāmaye vṛkṣām vanāni sam cara gṛheṣu goṣu me manaḥ  
avaśasā niḥśasā yat parāśasā upārima jāgrataḥ yat svapantaḥ   agniḥ viśvāni apa duṣkṛtāni a juṣṭāni āre asmat dadhātu  
yat indra brahmaṇas pate api mṛṣā carāmasi   pracetāḥ naḥ āṅgirasaḥ duritāt pātu aṃhasaḥ  
yaḥ na jīvaḥ asi na mṛtaḥ devānām amṛta garbhaḥ asi svapna   varuṇānī te mātā yamaḥ pitā araruḥ nāma asi  
vidma te svapna janitram deva jāmīnām putraḥ asi yamasya karaṇaḥ   antakaḥ asi mṛtyuḥ asi tam tvā svapna tathā sam vidma sa naḥ svapna duṣvapnyāt pāhi  
yathā kalām yathā śapham yatharṇam saṃnayanti   eva duṣvapnyam sarvam dviṣate sam nayāmasi  
agniḥ prātaḥsavane pātu asmān vaiśvānaraḥ viśva kṛt viśva śaṃbhūḥ   sa naḥ pāvakaḥ draviṇe dadhātu āyuṣmantaḥ sahabhakṣāḥ syāma  
viśve devāḥ marutaḥ indraḥ asmān asmin dvitīye savane na jahyuḥ   āyuṣmantaḥ priyam eṣām vadantaḥ vayam devānām sumatau syāma  
idam tṛtīyam savanam kavīnām ṛtena ye camasam airayanta   te saudhanvanāḥ svar ānaśānāḥ su iṣṭim naḥ abhi vasyaḥ nayantu  
śyenaḥ asi gāyatra chandāḥ anu tvā rabhe   svasti mā sam vaha asya yajñasya udṛci svāhā  
ṛbhuḥ asi jagacchandāḥ anu tvā rabhe   svasti mā sam vaha asya yajñasya udṛci svāhā  
vṛṣā asi triṣṭubh chandāḥ anu tvā rabhe   svasti mā sam vaha asya yajñasya udṛci svāhā  
nahi te agne tanvaḥ krūram ānaṃśa martyaḥ   kapiḥ babhasti tejanam svam jarāyu gauḥ iva  
meṣaḥ iva vai sam ca vi ca uru acyase yat uttaradrau uparaḥ ca khādataḥ   śīrṣṇā śiraḥ apsasā apsaḥ ardayan aṃśūn babhasti haritebhiḥ āsabhiḥ  
suparṇā vācam akrata upa dyavi ākhare kṛṣṇāḥ iṣirāḥ anartiṣuḥ   ni yat niyanti uparasya niṣkṛtim purū retaḥ dadhire sūrya śritaḥ  
hatam tardam samaṅkam ākhum aśvinā chintam śiraḥ api pṛṣṭīḥ śṛṇītam   yavān na id adān api nahyatam mukham atha abhayam kṛṇutam dhānyāya  
tarda hai pataṅga hai jabhya hā upakvasa   brahma iva a saṃsthitam haviḥ anadantaḥ imān yavān a hiṃsantaḥ apodita  
tardāpate vaghāpate tṛṣṭa jambhāḥ ā śṛṇota me   ye āraṇyāḥ vyadvarāḥ ye ke ca stha vyadvarāḥ tān sarvān jambhayāmasi  
vāyoḥ pūtaḥ pavitreṇa pratyaṅ somaḥ ati drutaḥ   indrasya yujaḥ sakhā  
āpaḥ asmāt mātaraḥ sūdayantu ghṛtena naḥ ghṛtapvaḥ punantu   viśvam hi ripram pravahanti devīḥ ud id ābhyaḥ śuciḥ ā pūtaḥ emi  
yat kim ca idam varuṇa daivye jane abhidroham manuṣyāḥ caranti   acittyā ced tava dharma yuyopima mā naḥ tasmāt enasaḥ deva rīriṣaḥ  
ud sūryaḥ divaḥ eti puras rakṣāṃsi nijūrvan   ādityaḥ parvatebhyaḥ viśva dṛṣṭaḥ adṛṣṭa hā  
ni gāvaḥ goṣṭhe asadan ni mṛgāsaḥ avikṣata   ni ūrmayaḥ nadīnam ni adṛṣṭāḥ alipsata  
āyuḥ dadam vipaścitam śrutām kaṇvasya vīrudham   ābhāriṣam viśva bheṣajīm asya adṛṣṭāt ni śamayat  
dyauḥ ca me idam pṛthivī ca pracetasau śukraḥ bṛhan dakṣiṇayā pipartu   anu svadhā cikitām somaḥ agniḥ vāyuḥ naḥ pātu savitā bhagaḥ ca  
punar prāṇaḥ punar ātmā naḥ aitu punar cakṣuḥ punar asuḥ naḥ aitu   vaiśvānaraḥ naḥ adabdhaḥ tanū pāḥ antar tiṣṭhāti duritāni viśvā  
sam varcasā payasā sam tanūbhiḥ aganmahi manasā sam śivena   tvaṣṭā naḥ atra varīyaḥ kṛṇotu anu naḥ mārṣṭu tanvaḥ yat viriṣṭam  
idam tat yujaḥ uttaram indram śumbhāmi aṣṭaye   asya kṣatram śriyam mahīm vṛṣṭiḥ iva vardhaya tṛṇam  
asmai kṣatram agnīṣomau asmai dhārayatam rayim   imam rāṣṭrasya abhīvarge kṛṇutam yujaḥ uttaram  
sabandhuḥ ca a sabandhuḥ ca yaḥ asmām abhidāsati   sarvam tam randhayāsi me yajamānāya sunvate  
ye panthānaḥ bahavaḥ deva yānāḥ antarā dyāvāpṛthivī saṃcaranti   teṣām ajyānim yatamaḥ vahāti tasmai mā devāḥ pari datta iha sarve  
grīṣmaḥ hemantaḥ śiśiraḥ vasantaḥ śarad varṣāḥ svite naḥ dadhāta   ā naḥ goṣu bhajata prajāyām nivāte id vaḥ śaraṇe syāma  
idāvatsarāya parivatsarāya saṃvatsarāya kṛṇuta bṛhat namaḥ   teṣām vayam sumatau yajñiyānām api bhadre sau manase syāma  
mā naḥ devāḥ ahiḥ vadhīt satokān saha puruṣān   samyatam na vi sparat vyāttam na sam yamat namaḥ deva janebhyaḥ   namaḥ astu asitāya namaḥ tiraścirājaye   svajāya babhrave namaḥ namaḥ deva janebhyaḥ  
sam te hanmi datā dataḥ sam u te hanvā hanū   sam te jihvayā jihvām sam u āsnāhaḥ āsyam  
idam id vai u bheṣajam idam rudrasya bheṣajam   yena iṣum eka tejanām śata śalyām apabravat  
jālāṣeṇa abhi siñcata jālāṣeṇa upa siñcata   jālāṣam ugram bheṣajam tena naḥ mṛḍa jīvase  
śam ca naḥ mayaḥ ca naḥ mā ca naḥ kim cana amamat   kṣamā rapaḥ viśvam naḥ astu bheṣajam sarvam naḥ astu bheṣajam  
yaśasam mā indraḥ maghavān kṛṇotu yaśasam dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime   yaśasam mā devaḥ savitā kṛṇotu priyaḥ dātuḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ iha syām  
yathā indraḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ yaśasvān yathā apaḥ oṣadhīṣu yaśasvatīḥ   eva viśveṣu deveṣu vayam sarveṣu yaśasaḥ syāma  
yaśāḥ indraḥ yaśāḥ agniḥ yaśāḥ somaḥ ajāyata   yaśāḥ viśvasya bhūtasya aham asmi yaśastamaḥ  
anaḍudbhyaḥ tvam prathamam dhenubhyaḥ tvam arundhati   a dhenave vayase śarma yaccha catuṣpade  
śarma yacchatu oṣadhiḥ saha devīḥ arundhatī   karat payasvantam goṣṭham ayakṣmān uta pūruṣān  
viśva rūpām subhagām achāvadāmi jīvalām   sā naḥ rudrasya āstām hetim dūram nayatu gobhyaḥ  
ayam ā yāti aryamā purastāt viṣita stupaḥ   asyāḥ ichan agruvai patim uta jāyām a jānaye  
aśramat iyam aryaman anyāsām samanam yatī   aṅga u nu aryaman asyāḥ anyāḥ samanam āyati  
dhātā dādhāra pṛthivīm dhātā dyām uta sūryam   dhātā asyai agruvai patim dadhātu pratikāmyam  
mahyam āpaḥ madhumat erayantām mahyam sūraḥ abharat jyotiṣe kam   mahyam devāḥ uta viśve tapaḥ jāḥ mahyam devaḥ savitā vyacaḥ dhāt  
aham viveca pṛthivīm uta dyām aham ṛtūṃr ajanayam sapta sākam   aham satyam anṛtam yat vadāmi aham daivīm pari vācam viśaḥ ca  
aham jajāna pṛthivīm uta dyām aham ṛtūṃr ajanayam sapta sindhūn   aham satvam anṛtam yat vadāmi yaḥ agnīṣomau ajuṣe sakhāyā  
vaiśvānaraḥ raśmibhiḥ naḥ punātu vātaḥ prāṇena iṣiraḥ nabhobhiḥ   dyāvāpṛthivī payasā payasvatī ṛtāvarī yajñiye na punītām  
vaiśvānarīm sūnṛtām ā rabhadhvam yasyāḥ āśāḥ tanvaḥ vīta pṛṣṭhāḥ   tayā gṛṇantaḥ sadhamādeṣu vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīnām  
vaiśvānarīm varcasaḥ ā rabhadhvam śuddhāḥ bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ   iha iḍayā sadhamādam madantaḥ jyok paśyema sūryam uccarantam  
yat te devī nirṛtiḥ ābabandha dāma grīvāsu avimokyam yat   tat te vi syāmi āyuṣe varcase balāya adomadam annam addhi prasūtaḥ  
namaḥ astu te nirṛte tigma tejaḥ ayasmayān vi cṛtā bandha pāśān   yamaḥ mahyam punar id tvām dadāti tasmai yamāya namaḥ astu mṛtyave  
ayasmaye drupade bedhiṣe iha abhihitaḥ mṛtyubhiḥ ye sahasram   yamena tvam pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ uttamam nākam adhi rohaya imam  
saṃsam id yuvase vṛṣan agne viśvāni aryaḥ ā   iḍaḥ pade sam idhyase sa naḥ vasūni ā bhara  
sam jānīdhvam sam pṛcyadhvam sam vaḥ manāṃsi jānatām   devāḥ bhāgam yathā pūrve samjānānāḥ upāsate
