samānaḥ mantraḥ samitiḥ samānī samānam vratam saha cittam eṣām   samānena vaḥ haviṣā juhomi samānam cetaḥ abhisaṃviśadhvam  
samānī vaḥ ākūtiḥ samānā hṛdayāni vaḥ   samānam astu vaḥ manaḥ yathā vaḥ su sahā asati  
ava manyuḥ avāyata ava bāhū manaḥ yujā   parāśara tvam teṣām parāñcam śuṣmam ardaya adha naḥ rayim ā kṛdhi  
nirhastebhyaḥ nairhastam yam devāḥ śarum asyatha   vṛścāmi śatrūṇām bāhūn anena haviṣā aham  
indraḥ cakāra prathamam nairhastam asurebhyaḥ   jayantu satvānaḥ mama sthireṇa indreṇa medinā  
nirhastaḥ śatruḥ abhidāsan astu ye senābhiḥ yudham āyanti asmān   sam arpaya indra mahatā vadhena drātu eṣām agha hāraḥ vividdhaḥ  
ātanvānāḥ āyacchantaḥ asyantaḥ ye ca dhāvatha   nirhastāḥ śatravaḥ sthana indraḥ vaḥ adya parāśarīt  
nirhastāḥ santu śatravaḥ aṅga eṣām mlāpayāmasi   atha eṣām indra vedāṃsi śataśas vi bhajāmahai  
pari vartmāni sarvatas indraḥ pūṣā ca sasratuḥ   muhyantu adya amūḥ senāḥ amitrāṇām parastarām  
mūḍhāḥ amitrāḥ carata aśīrṣāṇaḥ iva ahayaḥ   teṣām vaḥ agni mūḍhānām indraḥ hantu varaṃvaram  
ā eṣu nahya vṛṣā ajinam hariṇasya bhiyam kṛdhi   parāṅ amitraḥ eṣatu arvācī gauḥ upeṣatu  
ā ayam agan savitā kṣureṇa uṣṇena vāyo udakena ihi   ādityāḥ rudrāḥ vasavaḥ undantu sacetasaḥ somasya rājñaḥ vapata pracetasaḥ  
aditiḥ śmaśru vapatu āpaḥ undantu varcasā   cikitsatu prajāpatiḥ dīrgha āyu tvāya cakṣase  
yena avapat savitā kṣureṇa somasya rājñaḥ varuṇasya vidvān   tena brahmāṇaḥ vapata idam asya gomān aśvavān ayam astu prajāvān  
girau aragarāṭeṣu hiranye goṣu yat yaśaḥ   surāyām sicyamānāyām kīlāle madhu tat mayi  
aśvinā sāragheṇa mā madhunā aṅktam śubhaḥ patī   yathā bhargasvatīm vācam āvadāni janām anu  
mayi varcaḥ atha u yaśaḥ atha u yajñasya yat payaḥ   tat mayi prajāpatiḥ divi dyām iva dṛṃhatu  
yathā māṃsam yathā surā yathā akṣāḥ adhidevane   yathā puṃsaḥ vṛṣaṇyataḥ striyām nihanyate manaḥ   eva te aghnye manaḥ adhi vatse ni hanyatām  
yathā hastī hastinyāḥ padena padam udyuje   yathā puṃsaḥ vṛṣaṇyataḥ striyām nihanyate manaḥ   eva te aghnye manaḥ adhi vatse ni hanyatām  
yathā pradhiḥ yathā upadhiḥ yathā nabhyam pradhau adhi   yathā puṃsaḥ vṛṣaṇyataḥ striyām nihanyate manaḥ   eva te aghnye manaḥ adhi vatse ni hanyatām  
yat annam admi bahudhā virūpam hiraṇyam aśvam uta gām ajām avim   yat eva kim ca pratijagraha aham agniḥ tat hotā su hutam kṛnotu  
yat mā hutam ahutam ājagāma dattam pitṛbhiḥ anumatam manuṣyaiḥ   yasmāt me manaḥ ud iva rārajīti agniḥ tat hotā su hutam kṛṇotu  
yat annam admi anṛtena devāḥ dāsyan a dāsyan uta saṃgṛṇāmi   vaiśvānarasya mahataḥ mahimnā śivam mahyam madhumat astu annam  
yathā asitaḥ prathayate vaśām anu vapūṃṣi kṛṇvan asurasya māyayā   eva te śepaḥ sahasā ayam arkaḥ aṅgena aṅgam saṃsamakam kṛṇotu  
yathā pasaḥ tāya ādaram vātena sthūlabham kṛtam   yāvat parasvataḥ pasaḥ tāvat te vardhatām pasaḥ  
yāvat aṅgīnam pārasvatam hāstinam gārdabham ca yat  yāvat aśvasya vājinaḥ tāvat te vardhatām pasaḥ 
ā iha yātu varuṇaḥ somaḥ agniḥ bṛhaspatiḥ vasubhiḥ ā iha yātu   asya śriyam upasaṃyāta sarvaḥ ugrasya cettuḥ saṃmanasaḥ sajātāḥ  
yaḥ vaḥ śuṣmaḥ hṛdayeṣu antar ākūtiḥ yā vaḥ manasi praviṣṭā   tān sīvayāmi haviṣā ghṛtena mayi sajātā ramatiḥ vaḥ astu  
iha eva sta mā apa yāta adhi asmat pūṣā parastāt apatham vaḥ kṛṇotu   vāstoḥ patiḥ anu vaḥ johavītu mayi sajātā ramatiḥ vaḥ astu  
sam vaḥ pṛcyantām tanvaḥ sam manāṃsi sam u vratā   sam vaḥ ayam brahmaṇaḥ patiḥ bhagaḥ sam vaḥ ajīgamat  
samjñapanam vaḥ manasaḥ atho samjñapanam hṛdaḥ   atho bhagasya yat śrāntam tena saṃjñapayāmi vaḥ  
yathā ādityāḥ vasubhiḥ sambabhūvuḥ marudbhiḥ ugrāḥ a hṛṇīyamānāḥ   eva tri nāman a hṛṇīyamānaḥ imān janān saṃmanasaḥ kṛdhi iha  
niḥ amum nude okasaḥ sapatnaḥ yaḥ pṛtanyati   nairbādhyena haviṣā indraḥ enam parāśarīt  
paramām tam parāvatam indraḥ nudatu vṛtrahā   yatas na punar āyati śaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyaḥ  
etu tisraḥ parāvataḥ etu pañca janām ati   etu tisraḥ ati rocanāḥ yatas na punar āyati   śaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyaḥ yāvat sūryaḥ asat divi  
ye enam pariṣīdanti samādadhati cakṣase   saṃpreddhaḥ agniḥ jihvābhiḥ ud etu hṛdayāt adhi  
agneḥ sāmtapanasya aham āyuṣe padam ā rabhe   addhātiḥ yasya paśyati dhūmam udyantam āsyataḥ  
yaḥ asya samidham veda kṣatriyeṇa samāhitām   nābhihvāre padam ni dadhāti sa mṛtyave  
na enam ghnanti paryāyiṇaḥ na sannām ava gacchati   agneḥ yaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vidvān nāma gṛhnāti āyuṣe  
asthāt dyauḥ asthāt pṛthivī asthāt viśvam idam jagat   āsthāne parvatāḥ asthuḥ sthāmni aśvām atiṣṭhipam  
yaḥ udānat parāyaṇam yaḥ udānaṭ nyāyanam   āvartanam nivartanam yaḥ gopāḥ api tam huve  
jātavedaḥ ni vartaya śatam te santu āvṛtaḥ   sahasram te upāvṛtaḥ tābhiḥ naḥ punar ā kṛdhi  
tena bhūtena haviṣā ayam ā pyāyatām punar   jāyām yām asmai āvākṣuḥ tām rasena abhi vardhatām  
abhi vardhatām payasā abhi rāṣṭreṇa vardhatām   rayyā sahasra varcasā imau stām an upakṣitau  
tvaṣṭā jāyām ajanayat tvaṣṭā asyai tvām patim   tvaṣṭā sahasram āyuṃṣi dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu vām  
ayam naḥ nabhasaḥ patiḥ saṃsphānaḥ abhi rakṣatu   asamātim gṛheṣu naḥ  
tvam naḥ nabhasas pate ūrjam gṛhesu dhāraya   ā puṣṭam etu ā vasu  
deva saṃsphāna sahasrāpoṣasya īśiṣe   tasya naḥ rāsva tasya naḥ dhehi tasya te bhaktivāmsaḥ syāma  
antarikṣeṇa patati viśvā bhūtā avacākaśat   śunaḥ divyasya yat mahaḥ tena te haviṣā vidhema  
ye trayaḥ kālakāñjāḥ divi devāḥ iva śritāḥ   tān sarvān ahve ūtaye asmai ariṣṭatātaye  
apsu te janma divi te sadhastham samudre antar mahimā te pṛthivyām   śunaḥ divyasya yat mahaḥ tena te haviṣā vidhema  
yantā asi yacchase hastau apa rakṣāṃsi sedhasi   prajām dhanam ca gṛhṇānaḥ parihastaḥ abhūt ayam  
parihasta vi dhāraya yonim garbhāya dhātave   maryāde putram ā dhehi tam tvam ā gamaya āgame  
yam parihastam abibhar aditiḥ putra kāmyā   tvaṣṭā tam asyāḥ ā badhnāt yathā putram janāt  
āgacchataḥ āgatasya nāma gṛhṇāmi āyataḥ   indrasya vṛtra ghnaḥ vanve vāsavasya śatakratoḥ  
yena sūryām sāvitrīm aśvinā ūhatuḥ pathā   tena mām abravīt bhagaḥ jayām ā vahatāt iti  
yaḥ te aṅkuśaḥ vasu dānaḥ bṛhan indra hiraṇyayaḥ   tena janiyate jāyām mahyam dhehi śacīpate  
apacitaḥ pra patata suparṇaḥ vasateḥ iva   sūryaḥ kṛṇotu bheṣajam candramāḥ vaḥ apocchatu  
enī ekā śyenī ekā kṛṣṇā ekā rohiṇī dve   sarvāsām agrabham nāma avīra ghnīḥ apetana  
asūtikā rāmāyaṇī apacit pra patiṣyati   glauḥ itas pra patiṣyati sa galuntaḥ naśiṣyati  
vīhi svām āhutim juṣānaḥ manasā svāhā manasā yat idam juhomi 
yasyāḥ te āsani ghore juhomi eṣām baddhānām avasarjanāya kam   bhūmiḥ iti tvā abhipramanvate janāḥ nirṛtiḥ iti tvā aham pari veda sarvatas  
bhūte haviṣmatī bhava eṣa te bhāgaḥ yaḥ asmāsu   muñca imān amūn enasaḥ svāhā  
eva u su asmat nirṛte anehā tvam ayasmayān vi cṛtā bandha pāśān   yamaḥ mahyam punar id tvām dadāti tasmai yamāya namaḥ astu mṛtyave  
ayasmaye drupade bedhiṣe iha abhihitaḥ mṛtyubhiḥ ye sahasram   yamena tvam pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ uttamam nākam adhi rohaya imam  
varaṇaḥ vārayātai ayam devaḥ vanaspatiḥ   yakṣmaḥ yaḥ asmin āviṣṭaḥ tam u devāḥ avīvaran  
indrasya vacasā vayam mitrasya varuṇasya ca   devānām sarveṣām vācā yakṣmam te vārayāmahe  
yathā vṛtraḥ imāḥ āpaḥ tastambha viśvadhā yatīḥ   eva te agninā yakṣmam vaiśvānareṇa vāraye  
vṛṣā indrasya vṛṣā divaḥ vṛsā pṛthivyāḥ ayam   vṛṣā viśvasya bhūtasya tvam eka vṛṣaḥ bhava  
samudraḥ īśe sravatām agniḥ pṛthivyāḥ vaśī   candramāḥ nakṣatrāṇām īśe tvam eka vṛṣaḥ bhava  
samrāj asi asurāṇām kakud manuṣyānām   devānām ardha bhāj asi tvam eka vṛṣaḥ bhava  
ā tvā ahārṣam antar abhūḥ dhruvaḥ tiṣṭha avicācalat   viśaḥ tvā sarvāḥ vāñchantu mā tvat rāṣṭram adhi bhraśat  
iha eva edhi mā apa cyoṣṭhāḥ parvataḥ iva avicācalat   indraḥ iva iha dhruvaḥ tiṣṭha iha rāṣṭram u dhāraya  
indraḥ etam adīdharat dhruvam dhruveṇa haviṣā   tasmai somaḥ adhi bravat ayam ca brahmaṇas patiḥ  
dhruvā dyauḥ dhruvā pṛthivī dhruvam viśvam idam jagat   dhruvāsaḥ parvatāḥ ime dhruvaḥ rājā viśām ayam  
dhruvam te rājā varuṇaḥ dhruvam devaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ   dhruvam te indraḥ ca agniḥ ca rāṣṭram dhārayatām dhruvam  
dhruvaḥ acyutaḥ pra mṛṇīhi śatrūn śatrūyataḥ adharān pādayasva   sarvāḥ diśaḥ saṃmanasaḥ sadhrīcīḥ dhruvāya te samitiḥ kalpatām iha  
idam yat preṇyaḥ śiraḥ dattam somena vṛṣṇyam   tatas pari prajātena hārdim te śocayāmasi  
śocayāmasi te hārdim śocayāmasi te manaḥ   vātam dhūmaḥ iva sadhryak mām eva anu etu ye manaḥ  
mahyam tvā mitrāvaruṇau mahyam devī sarasvatī   mahyam tvā madhyam bhūmyāḥ ubhau antau sam asyatām  
yām te rudraḥ iṣum āsyat aṅgebhyaḥ hṛdayāya ca   idam tām adya tvat vayam viṣūcīm vi vṛhāmasi  
yāḥ te śatam dhamanayaḥ aṅgāni anu viṣṭhitāḥ   tāsām te sarvāsām vayam niḥ viṣāṇi hvayāmasi  
namaḥ te rudra asyate namaḥ pratihitāyai   namaḥ visṛjyamānāyai namaḥ nipatitāyai  
imam yavam aṣṭa āyogaiḥ ṣat yogebhiḥ acarkṛṣuḥ   tena te tanvaḥ rapaḥ apācīnam apa vyaye  
nyak vātaḥ vāti nyak tapati sūryaḥ   nīcīnam aghnyā duhe nyak bhavatu te rapaḥ  
āpaḥ id vai u bheṣajīḥ āpaḥ amīva cātanīḥ   āpaḥ viśvasya bheṣajīḥ tāḥ te kṛṇvantu bheṣajam  
vāta raṃhāḥ bhava vājin yujamānaḥ indrasya yāhi prasave manaḥ javāḥ   yuñjantu tvā marutaḥ viśva vedasaḥ ā te tvastā patsu javam dadhātu  
javaḥ te arvan nihitaḥ guhā yaḥ śyene vāte uta yaḥ acarat parīttaḥ   tena tvam vājin balavān balena ājim jaya samane parayiṣṇuḥ  
tanūḥ te vājin tanvam nayantī vāmam asmabhyam dhāvatu śarma tubhyam   a hrutaḥ mahaḥ dharuṇāya devaḥ divi iva jyotiḥ svam ā mimīyāt  
yamaḥ mṛtyuḥ aghamāraḥ nirṛthaḥ babhruḥ śarvaḥ astā nīla śikhaṇḍaḥ   deva janāḥ senayā uttasthivāṃsaḥ te asmākam pari vṛñjantu vīrān  
manasā homaiḥ harasā ghṛtena śarvāya astre uta rājñe bhavāya   namasyebhyaḥ namaḥ ebhyaḥ kṛṇomi anyatra asmat agha viṣāḥ nayantu  
trāyadhvam naḥ agha viṣābhyaḥ vadhāt viśve devāḥ marutaḥ viśva vedasaḥ   agnīṣomāḥ varuṇaḥ pūta dakṣāḥ vātāparjanyayoḥ sumatau syāma  
sam vaḥ manāṃsi sam vratā sam ākūtīḥ namāmasi   amī ye vivratā sthana tān vaḥ sam namayāmasi  
aham gṛbhṇāmi manasā manāṃsi mama cittam anu cittebhiḥ eta   mama vaśeṣu hṛdayāni vaḥ kṛṇomi mama yātam anuvartmānaḥ eta  
ote me dyāvāpṛthivī otā devī sarasvatī   otau me indraḥ ca agniḥ ca rdhyāsma idam sarasvati  
aśvatthaḥ deva sadanaḥ tṛtīyasyām itas divi   tatra amṛtasya cakṣaṇam devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata  
hiraṇyayī nauḥ acarat hiraṇya bandhanā divi   tatra amṛtasya puṣpam devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata  
garbhaḥ asi oṣadhīnām garbhaḥ himavatām uta   garbhaḥ viśvasya bhūtasya imam me agadam kṛdhi  
yāḥ oṣadhayaḥ soma rājñīḥ bahvīḥ śata vicakṣaṇāḥ   bṛhaspati prasūtāḥ tāḥ naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
muñcantu mā śapathyāt atha u varuṇyāt uta   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt  
yat cakṣuṣā manasā yat ca vācā upārima jāgrataḥ yat svapantaḥ   somaḥ tāni svadhayā naḥ punātu  
abhibhūḥ yajñaḥ abhibhūḥ agniḥ abhibhūḥ somaḥ abhibhūḥ indraḥ   abhi aham viśvāḥ pṛtanāḥ yathā āsāni eva vidhema agnihotrāḥ idam haviḥ  
svadhā astu mitrāvaruṇā vipaścitā prajāvat kṣatram madhunā iha pinvatam   bādhethām dūram nirṛtim parācais kṛtam cit enaḥ pra mumuktam asmat  
imam vīram anu harṣadhvam ugram indram sakhāyaḥ anu sam rabhadhvam   grāma jitam go jitam vajra bāhum jayantam ajma pramṛṇantam ojasā  
indraḥ jayāti na parā jayātai adhirājaḥ rājasu rājayātai   carkṛtyaḥ īḍyaḥ vandyaḥ ca upasadyaḥ namasyū bhava iha  
tvam indra adhirājaḥ śravasyuḥ tvam bhūḥ abhibhūtiḥ janānām   tvam daivīḥ viśaḥ imāḥ vi rāja āyuṣmat kṣatram ajaram te astu  
prācyāḥ diśaḥ tvam indra asi rājā ūtā udīcyāḥ diśaḥ vṛtrahan śatruhaḥ asi   yatra yanti srotyāḥ tat jitam te dakṣiṇatas vṛṣabhaḥ eṣi havyaḥ  
abhi tvā indra varimataḥ purā tvā aṃhūraṇāt dhuve   hvayāmi ugram cettāram puruṇāmānam ekajam  
yaḥ adya senyaḥ vadhaḥ jighāṃsan naḥ udīrate   indrasya tatra bāhū samantam pari dadmaḥ  
pari dadmaḥ indrasya bāhū samantam trātuḥ trāyatām naḥ   deva savitar soma rājan sumanasam mā kṛṇu svastaye  
devāḥ aduḥ sūryaḥ dyauḥ adāt pṛthivī adāt   tisraḥ sarasvatiḥ aduḥ sa cittāḥ viṣa dūṣaṇam  
yat vaḥ devāḥ upajīkāḥ āsiñcan dhanvani udakam   tena deva prasūtena idam dūṣayata viṣam  
asurāṇām duhitā asi sā devānām asi svasā   divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ saṃbhūtā sā cakartha arasam viṣam  
ā vṛṣāyasva śvasihi vardhasva prathayasva ca   yathāṅgam vardhatām śepaḥ tena yoṣitam id jahi  
yena kṛṣam vājayanti yena hinvanti āturam   tena asya brahmaṇas pate dhanuḥ iva ā tānaya pasaḥ  
ā aham tanomi te pasaḥ adhi jyām iva dhanvani   kramasva ṛṣaḥ iva rohitam an avaglāyatā sadā  
yathā ayam vāhaḥ aśvinā samaiti sam ca vartate   eva mām abhi te manaḥ samaitu sam ca vartatām  
ā aham khidāmi te manaḥ rāja aśvaḥ pṛṣṭyām iva   reṣma chinnam yathā tṛṇam mayi te veṣṭatām manaḥ  
āñjanasya madughasya kuṣṭhasya naladasya ca   turaḥ bhagasya hastābhyām anurodhanam ud bhare  
saṃdānam vaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ saṃdānam savitā karat   saṃdānam mitraḥ aryamā saṃdānam bhagaḥ aśvinā  
sam paramān sam avamān atho sam dyāmi madhyamān   indraḥ tān pari ahār dāmnā tān agne sam dyā tvam  
amī ye yudham āyanti ketūn kṛtvā anīkaśas   indraḥ tān pari ahār dāmna tān agne sam dyā tvam  
ādānena saṃdānena amitrān ā dyāmasi   apānāḥ ye ca eṣām prāṇāḥ asunā asūn sam achidan  
idam ādānam akaram tapasā indreṇa saṃśitam   amitrāḥ ye atra naḥ santi tān agne ā dyā tvam  
ā enān dyatām indra agnī somaḥ rājā ca medinau   indraḥ marutvān ādānam amitrebhyaḥ kṛṇotu naḥ  
yathā manaḥ manasketaiḥ parāpatati āśumat   eva tvam kāse pra pata manasaḥ anu pravāyyam  
yathā bāṇaḥ su saṃśitaḥ parāpatati āśumat   eva tvam kāse pra pata pṛthivyāḥ anu saṃvatam  
yathā sūryasya raśmayaḥ parāpatanti āśumat   eva tvam kāse pra pata samudrasya anu vikṣaram  
āyane te parāyane dūrvāḥ rohantu puṣpiṇīḥ   utsaḥ vā tatra jāyatām hradaḥ vā puṇḍarīkavān  
apām idam nyayanam samudrasya niveśanam   madhye hradasya naḥ gṛhāḥ parācīnāḥ mukhā kṛdhi  
himasya tvā jarāyuṇā śāle pari vyayāmasi   śītahradā hi naḥ bhuvaḥ agniḥ kṛṇotu bheṣajam  
viśvajit trāyamāṇāyai mā pari dehi   trāyamāṇe dvipād ca sarvam naḥ rakṣa catuṣpād yat ca naḥ svam  
trāyamāṇe viśvajite mā pari dehi   viśvajit dvipād ca sarvam naḥ rakṣa catuṣpād yat ca naḥ svam  
viśvajit kalyāṇyai mā pari dehi   kalyāṇi dvipād ca sarvam naḥ rakṣa catuṣpād yat ca naḥ svam  
kalyāṇi sarva vide mā pari dehi   sarva vid dvi pād ca sarvam naḥ rakṣa catuṣpād yat ca naḥ svam  
tvam naḥ medhe prathamā gobhiḥ aśvebhiḥ ā gahi   tvam sūryasya raśmibhiḥ tvam naḥ asi yajñiyā  
medhām aham prathamām brahmaṇvatīm brahma jūtām ṛṣiṣṭutām   prapītām brahmacāribhiḥ devānām avase huve  
yām medhām ṛbhavaḥ viduḥ yām medhām asurāḥ viduḥ   ṛṣayaḥ bhadrām medhām yām viduḥ tām mayi ā veśayāmasi  
yām ṛṣayaḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ medhām medhāvinaḥ viduḥ   tayā mām adya medhayā agne medhāvinam kṛṇu  
medhām sāyam medhām prātar medhām madhyandinam pari   medhām sūryasya raśmibhiḥ vacasā veśayāmahe  
pippalī kṣipta bheṣajī uta atividdha bheṣajī   tām devāḥ sam akalpayan iyam jīvitavai alam  
pippalyaḥ sam avadanta āyatīḥ jananāt adhi   yam jīvam aśnavāmahai na sa riṣyāti pūruṣaḥ  
asurāḥ tvā ni akhanan devāḥ tvā ud avapan punar   vātīkṛtasya bheṣajīm atho kṣiptasya bheṣajīm  
pratnaḥ hi kam īḍyaḥ adhvareṣu sanāt ca hotā navyaḥ ca satsi   svām ca agne tanvam piprāyasva asmabhyam ca saubhagam ā yajasva  
jyeṣṭha ghnyām jātaḥ vicṛtoḥ yamasya mūla barhaṇāt pari pāhi enam   ati enam neṣat duritāni viśvā dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya  
vyāghre ahni ajaniṣṭa vīraḥ nakṣatra jāḥ jāyamānaḥ su vīraḥ   sa mā vadhīt pitaram vardhamānaḥ mā mātaram pra minīt janitrīm  
imam me agne puruṣam mumugdhi ayam yaḥ baddhaḥ su yataḥ lālapīti   atas adhi te kṛṇavat bhāgadheyam yadā anunmaditaḥ asati  
agniḥ te ni śamayatu yadi te manaḥ udyutam   kṛṇomi vidvān bheṣajam yathā an unmaditaḥ asasi  
deva enasāt unmaditam unmattam rakṣasaḥ pari   kṛṇomi vidvān bheṣajam yadā an unmaditaḥ asati  
punar tvā duḥ apsarasaḥ punar indraḥ punar bhagaḥ   punar tvā duḥ viśve devāḥ yathā anunmaditaḥ asasi  
mā jyeṣṭham vadhīt ayam agne eṣām mūla barhaṇāt pari pāhi enam   sa grāhyāḥ pāśān vi cṛta prajānan tubhyam devāḥ anu jānantu viśve  
ud muñca pāśān tvam agne eṣām trayaḥ tribhiḥ utsitāḥ yebhiḥ āsan   sa grāhyāḥ pāśān vi cṛta prajānan pitāputrau mātaram muñca sarvān  
yebhiḥ pāśaiḥ parivittaḥ vibaddhaḥ aṅgeaṅge ārpitaḥ utsitaḥ ca   vi te mucyantam vimucaḥ hi santi bhrūṇa ghni pūṣan duritāni mṛkṣva  
trite devāḥ amṛjata etat enaḥ tritaḥ enat manuṣyeṣu mamṛje   tatas yadi tvā grāhiḥ ānaśe tām te devāḥ brahmaṇā nāśayantu  
marīcīḥ dhūmān pra viśa anu pāpman udārān gacchota vā nīhārān   nadīnam phenām anu tān vi naśya bhrūṇa ghni pūṣan duritāni mṛkṣva  
dvādaśadhā nihitam tritasya apamṛṣṭam manuṣya enasāni   tatas yadi tvā grāhiḥ ānaśe tām te devāḥ brahmaṇā nāśayantu  
yat devāḥ deva heḍanam devāsaḥ cakṛma vayam   ādityāḥ tasmāt naḥ yuyam ṛtasya ṛtena muñcata  
ṛtasya ṛtena ādityāḥ yajatrāḥ muñcata iha naḥ   yajñam yat yajña vāhasaḥ śikṣantaḥ na upaśekima  
medasvatā yajamānāḥ srucā ājyāni juhvataḥ   akāmāḥ viśve vaḥ devāḥ śikṣantaḥ na upa śekima  
yat vidvāṃsaḥ yat a vidvāṃsaḥ enāṃsi cakṛma vayam   yūyam naḥ tasmāt muñcata viśve devāḥ sajoṣasaḥ  
yadi jāgrat yadi svapan enaḥ enasyaḥ akaram   bhūtam mā tasmāt bhavyam ca drupadāt iva muñcatām  
drupadāt iva mumucānaḥ svinnaḥ snātvā malāt iva   pūtam pavitreṇa iva ājyam viśve śumbhantu mā enasaḥ  
yat yāmam cakruḥ nikhanantaḥ agre kārṣīvaṇāḥ anna vidaḥ na vidyayā   vaivasvate rājani tat juhomi atha yajñiyam madhumat astu naḥ annam  
vaivasvataḥ kṛṇavat bhāgadheyam madhu bhāgaḥ madhunā sam sṛjāti   mātuḥ yat enaḥ iṣitam naḥ āgan yat vā pitā aparāddhaḥ jihīde  
yadi idam mātuḥ yadi pituḥ naḥ pari bhrātuḥ putrāt cetasaḥ enaḥ āgan   yāvantaḥ asmān pitaraḥ sacante teṣām sarveṣām śivaḥ astu manyuḥ  
apamityam a pratīttam yat asmi yamasya yena balinā carāmi   idam tat agne anṛṇaḥ bhavāmi tvam pāśān vicṛtam vettha sarvān  
iha eva santaḥ prati dadmaḥ enat jīvāḥ jīvebhyaḥ ni harāmaḥ enat   apamitya dhānyam yat jaghasā aham idam tat agne anṛṇaḥ bhavāmi  
anṛṇāḥ asmin anṛṇāḥ parasmin tṛtīye loke anṛṇāḥ syāma   ye deva yānāḥ pitṛyāṇaḥ ca lokāḥ sarvān pathaḥ anṛṇāḥ ā kṣiyema  
yat dhastābhyām cakṛma kilbiṣāṇi akṣāṇām gatnum upalipsamānāḥ   ugraṃpaśye ugrajitau tat adya apsarasau anu dattām ṛṇam naḥ  
ugram paśye rāṣṭrabhṛt kilbiṣāṇi yat akṣa vṛttam anu dattam naḥ etat   ṛṇāt naḥ naḥ ṛṇam ertsamānaḥ yamasya loke adhirajjuḥ āyat  
yasmai ṛṇam yasya jāyām upaimi yam yācamānaḥ abhyaimi devāḥ   te vācam vādiṣuḥ mā uttarām mat deva patnī apsarasau adhītam  
yat a dīvyan ṛṇam aham kṛṇomi a dāsyan agne uta saṃgṛṇāmi   vaiśvānaraḥ naḥ adhipāḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ud id nayāti su kṛtasya lokam  
vaiśvānarāya prati vedayāmi yadi ṛṇam saṃgaraḥ devatāsu   saḥ etān pāśān vicṛtam veda sarvān atha pakvena saha sam bhavema  
vaiśvānaraḥ pavitā mā punātu yat saṃgaram abhidhāvāmi āśām   an ājānan manasā yācamānaḥ yat tatra enaḥ apa tat suvāmi  
yat antarikṣam pṛthivīm uta dyām yat mātaram pitaram vā jihiṃsima   ayam tasmāt gārhapatyaḥ naḥ agniḥ ud id nayāti sukṛtasya lokam  
bhūmiḥ mātā aditiḥ naḥ janitram bhrātā antarikṣam abhiśastyā naḥ   dyauḥ naḥ pitā pitryāt śam bhavāti jāmim ṛtvā mā ava patsi lokāt  
yatra suhārdaḥ su kṛtaḥ madanti vihāya rogam tanvaḥ svāyāḥ   aślonāḥ aṅgaiḥ a hrutāḥ svarge tatra paśyema pitarau ca putrān  
viṣāṇā pāśān vi sya adhi asmat ye uttamāḥ adhamāḥ vāruṇāḥ ye   duṣvapnyam duritam ni sva asmat atha gacchema su kṛtasya lokam  
yat dāruṇi badhyase yat ca rajjvām yat bhūmyām badhyase yat ca vācā   ayam tasmāt gārhapatyaḥ naḥ agniḥ ud id nayāti su kṛtasya lokam  
ud agātām bhagavatī vicṛtau nāma tārake   preha amṛtasya yacchatām praitu baddhaka mocanam  
vi jihīṣva lokam kṛṇu bandhāt muñcāsi baddhakam   yonyāḥ iva pracyutaḥ garbhaḥ pathaḥ sarvām anu kṣiya  
etam bhāgam pari dadāmi vidvān viśvakarman prathama jāḥ ṛtasya   asmābhiḥ dattam jarasaḥ parastāt achinnam tantum anu sam tarema  
tatam tantum anu eke taranti yeṣām dattam pitryam āyanena   a bandhu eke dadataḥ prayacchantaḥ dātum ced śikṣān sa svarge eva  
anvārabhethām anusaṃrabhethām etam lokam śraddadhānāḥ sacante   yat vām pakvam pariviṣṭam agnau tasya guptaye dampatī sam śrayethām  
yajñam yantam manasā bṛhantam anvārohāmi tapasā sayoniḥ   upahūtāḥ agne jarasaḥ parastāt tṛtīye nāke sadhamādam madema  
śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ yoṣitaḥ yajñiyāḥ imāḥ brahmaṇām hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi   yad kāmaḥ idam abhiṣiñcāmi vaḥ aham indraḥ marutvān sa dadātu tat me  
etam sadhasthāḥ pari vaḥ dadāmi yam śevadhim āvahāt jātavedaḥ   anvāgantā yajamānaḥ svasti tam sma jānīta parame vyoman  
jānīta sma enam parame vyoman devāḥ sadhasthāḥ vida lokam atra   anvāgantā yajamānaḥ svasti iṣṭāpūrtam sma kṛṇuta āvis asmai  
devāḥ pitaraḥ pitaraḥ devāḥ   yaḥ asmi saḥ asmi  
sa pacāmi sa dadāmi   sa yaje sa dattāt mā yūṣam  
nāke rājan prati tiṣṭha tatra etat prati tiṣṭhatu   viddhi pūrtasya naḥ rājan sa deva sumanāḥ bhava  
divaḥ nu mām bṛhataḥ antarikṣāt apām stokaḥ abhī apaptat rasena   sam indriyena payasā aham agne chandobhiḥ yajñaiḥ su kṛtām kṛtena  
yadi vṛkṣāt abhyapaptat phalam tat yadi antarikṣāt saḥ u vāyuḥ eva   yatra aspṛkṣat tanvaḥ yat ca vāsasaḥ āpaḥ nudantu nirṛtim parācais  
abhyañjanam surabhi sā samṛddhiḥ hiraṇyam varcaḥ tat u pūtrimam eva   sarvā pavitrā vitatā adhi asmat tat mā tārīt nirṛtiḥ mā u arātiḥ  
vanaspate vīḍu aṅgaḥ hi bhūyāḥ asmad sakhā prataraṇaḥ su vīraḥ   gobhiḥ saṃnaddhaḥ asi vīḍayasva āsthātā te jayatu jetvāni  
divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pari ojaḥ udbhṛtam vanaspatibhyaḥ pari ābhṛtam sahaḥ   apām ojmānam pari gobhiḥ āvṛtam indrasya vajram haviṣā ratham yaja  
indrasya ojaḥ marutām anīkam mitrasya garbhaḥ varuṇasya nābhiḥ   saḥ imām naḥ havya dātim juṣāṇaḥ deva ratha prati havyā gṛbhāya  
upa śvāsaya pṛthivīm uta dyam purutrā te vanvatām viṣṭhitam jagat   sa dundubhe sajūs indreṇa devaiḥ dūrāt davīyaḥ apa sedha śatrūn  
ā krandaya balam ojaḥ naḥ ā dhāḥ abhi stana duritā bādhamānaḥ   apa sedha dundubhe duchunām itas indrasya muṣṭiḥ asi vīḍayasva  
pra amūm jaya abhīme jayantu ketumat dundubhiḥ vāvadītu   sam aśva parṇāḥ patantu naḥ naraḥ asmākam indra rathinaḥ jayantu  
vidradhasya balāsasya lohitasya vanaspate   visalpakasya auṣadhe mā ud śiṣaḥ piśitam cana  
yau te balāsa tiṣṭhataḥ kakṣe muṣkau apaśritau   veda aham tasya bheṣajam cīpudruḥ abhicakṣaṇam  
yaḥ aṅgyaḥ yaḥ karṇyaḥ yaḥ akṣyoḥ visalpakaḥ   vi vṛhāmaḥ visalpakam vidradham hṛdaya āmayam   parā tam a jñātam yakṣmam adharāñcam suvāmasi  
śakadhūmam nakṣatrāṇi yat rājānam akurvata   bhadra aham asmai prāyacchan idam rāṣṭram asāt iti  
bhadra aham naḥ madhyaṃdine bhadra aham sāyam astu naḥ   bhadra aham naḥ ahnām prātā rātrī bhadra aham astu naḥ  
ahar rātrābhyām nakṣatrebhyaḥ suryācandramasābhyām   bhadra aham asmabhyam rājan śakadhūma tvam kṛdhi  
yaḥ naḥ bhadra aham akaraḥ sāyam naktam atho divā   tasmai te nakṣatra rāja śakadhūma sadā namaḥ  
bhagena mā śāṃśapena sākam indreṇa medinā   kṛṇomi bhaginam mā apa drāntu arātayaḥ  
yena vṛkṣām abhyabhavaḥ bhagena varcasā saha   tena mā bhaginam kṛṇu apa drāntu arātayaḥ  
yaḥ andhaḥ yaḥ punaḥsaraḥ bhagaḥ vṛkṣeṣu āhitaḥ   tena mā bhaginam kṛṇu apa drāntu arātayaḥ  
ratha jitām rātha jiteyīnām apsarasām ayam smaraḥ   devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu  
asau me smaratāt iti priyaḥ me smaratāt iti   devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu  
yathā mama smarāt asau na amuṣya aham kadā cana   devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu  
ud mādayata marutaḥ ud antarikṣa mādaya   agne ud mādaya tvam asau mām anu śocatu  
ni śīrṣataḥ ni pattataḥ ādhyaḥ ni tirāmi te   devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu  
anumate anu idam manyasva akute sam idam namaḥ   devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu  
yat dhāvasi tri yojanam pañca yojanam āśvinam   tatas tvam punar āyasi putrāṇām naḥ asaḥ pitā  
yam devāḥ smaram asiñcan apsu antar śośucānam saha adhyā   tam te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā  
yam viśve devāḥ smaram asiñcan apsu antar śośucānam saha adhyā   tam te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā  
yam indrāṇī smaram asiñcat apsu antar śośucānam saha adhyā   tam te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā  
yam indra agnī smaram asiñcatām apsu antar śośucānam saha adhyā   tam te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā  
yam mitrāvaruṇau smaram asiñcatām apsu antar śośucānam saha adhyā   tam te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā  
yaḥ imām devaḥ mekhalām ābabandha yaḥ saṃnanāha yaḥ u naḥ yuyoja   yasya devasya praśiṣā carāmaḥ sa pāram ichāt saḥ u naḥ vi muñcāt  
āhutā asi abhihuta ṛṣīṇām asi āyudham   pūrvā vratasya prāśnatī vīra ghnī bhava mekhale  
mṛtyoḥ aham brahmacārī yat asmi niryācan bhūtāt puruṣam yamāya   tam aham brahmaṇā tapasā śrameṇa anayā enam mekhalayā sināmi  
śraddhāyāḥ duhitā tapasaḥ adhi jātā svasā ṛṣīṇām bhūta kṛtām babhūva   sā naḥ mekhale matim ā dhehi medhām atha u naḥ dhehi tapaḥ indriyam ca  
yām tvā pūrve bhūta kṛtaḥ ṛṣayaḥ paribedhire   sā tvam pari svajasva mām dīrgha āyu tvāya mekhale  
ayam vajraḥ tarpayatām ṛtasya ava asya rāṣṭram apa hantu jīvitam   śṛṇātu grīvāḥ pra śṛṇātu uṣṇihāḥ vṛtrasya iva śacīpatiḥ  
adharaḥ adharaḥ uttarebhyaḥ gūḍhaḥ pṛthivyāḥ mā ud sṛpat   vajreṇa avahataḥ śayām  
yaḥ jināti tam anviccha yaḥ jināti tam id jahi   jinataḥ vajra tvam sīmantam anvañcam anu pātaya  
yat aśnāmi balam kurve ittham vajram ā dade   skandhān amuṣya śātayan vṛtrasya iva śacīpatiḥ  
yat pibāmi sam pibāmi samudraḥ iva saṃpibaḥ   prāṇān amuṣya saṃpāya sam pibāmaḥ amum vayam  
yat girāmi sam girāmi samudraḥ iva saṃgiraḥ   prāṇān amuṣya saṃgīrya sam girāmaḥ amum vayam  
devī devyām adhi jātā pṛthivyām asi oṣadhe   tām tvā nitatni keśebhyaḥ dṛṃhaṇāya khanāmasi  
dṛṃha pratnān janaya a jātān jātān u varṣīyasaḥ kṛdhi 
yaḥ te keśaḥ avapadyate sa mūlaḥ yaḥ ca vṛścate   idam tam viśva bheṣajyā abhi siñcāmi vīrudhā  
yām jamadagniḥ akhanat duhitre keśa vardhanīm   tām vītahavyaḥ ābharat asitasya gṛhebhyaḥ  
abhīśunā meyāḥ āsan vyāmena anumeyāḥ   keśāḥ naḍāḥ iva vardhantām śīrṣṇaḥ te asitāḥ pari  
dṛṃha mūlam āgram yaccha vi madhyam yāmaya oṣadhe   keśāḥ naḍāḥ iva vardhantām śīrṣṇaḥ te asitāḥ pari  
tvam vīrudhām śreṣṭhatamā abhiśrutā asi oṣadhe   imam me adya puruṣam klībam opaśinam kṛdhi  
klībam kṛdhi opaśinam atha u kurīriṇam kṛdhi   atha asya indraḥ grāvabhyām ubhe bhinattu āṇḍyau  
klība klībam tvā akaram vadhre vadhrim tvā akaram arasa arasam tvā akaram   kurīram asya śīrṣaṇi kumbam ca adhinidadhmasi  
ye te nādyau deva kṛte yayoḥ tiṣṭhati vṛṣṇyam   te te bhinadmi śamyayā amuṣyāḥ adhi muṣkayoḥ  
yathā naḍam kaśipune striyaḥ bhindanti aśmanā   eva bhinadmi te śepaḥ amuṣyāḥ adhi muṣkayoḥ  
nyastikā rurohitha subhagaṃkaraṇī mama   śatam tava pratānāḥ trayastriṃśat nitānāḥ  
tayā sahasraparṇyā hṛdayam śoṣayāmi te 
śuṣyatu mayi te hṛdayam atho śuṣyatu āsyam   atho ni śuṣya mām kāmena atho śuṣka āsyā cara  
saṃvananī samuṣpalā babhru kalyāṇi sam nuda   amūm ca mām ca sam nuda samānam hṛdayam kṛdhi  
yathā udakam apapuṣaḥ apaśuṣyati āsyam   eva ni śuṣya mām kāmena atho śuṣka āsyā cara  
yathā nakulaḥ vichidya saṃdadhāti ahim punar   eva kāmasya vichinnam sam dhehi vīryāvati  
yau vyāghrau avarūdhau jighatsataḥ pitaram mātaram ca   tau dantam brahmaṇas pate śivau kṛṇu jātavedaḥ  
vrīhim attam yavam attam atho māṣam atho tilam   eṣa vām bhāgaḥ nihitaḥ ratna dheyāya dantau mā hiṃsiṣṭam pitaram mātaram ca  
upahūtau sayujau syonau dantau su maṅgalau   anyatra vām ghoram tanvaḥ paraitu dantau mā hiṃsiṣṭam pitaram mātaram ca  
vāyuḥ enāḥ samākarat tvaṣṭā poṣāya dhriyatām   indraḥ ābhyaḥ adhi bravat rudraḥ bhūmne cikitsatu  
lohitena svadhitinā mithunam karṇayoḥ kṛdhi   akartām aśvinā lakṣma tat astu prajayā bahu  
yathā cakruḥ deva asurāḥ yathā manuṣyāḥ uta   eva sahasra poṣāya kṛṇutam lakṣmā aśvinā  
ud śrayasva bahuḥ bhava svena mahasā yava   mṛṇīhi viśvā pātrāṇi mā tvā divyā aśaniḥ vadhīt  
āśṛṇvantam yavam devam yatra tvā āchāvadāmasi   tat ud śrayasva dyauḥ iva samudraḥ iva edhi akṣitaḥ  
akṣitāḥ te upasadaḥ akṣitāḥ santu rāśayaḥ   pṛṇantaḥ akṣitāḥ santu attāraḥ santu akṣitāḥ  
dhītī vā ye anayan vācaḥ agram manasā vā ye avadan ṛtāni   tṛtīyena brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānāḥ turīyeṇa amanvata nāma dhenoḥ  
sa veda putraḥ pitaram sa mātaram sa sūnuḥ bhuvat sa bhuvat punarmaghaḥ   sa dyām aurṇot antarikṣam svar saḥ idam viśvam abhavat saḥ ābharat  
atharvāṇam pitaram deva bandhum mātuḥ garbham pituḥ asum yuvānam   yaḥ imam yajñam manasā ciketa pra naḥ vocaḥ tam iha iha bravaḥ  
ayā viṣṭhā janayan karvarāṇi sa hi ghṛṇiḥ uruḥ varāya gātuḥ   sa pratyudait dharuṇam madhvaḥ agram svayā tanvā tanvam airayata  
ekayā ca daśabhiḥ ca su hute dvābhyām iṣṭaye viṃśatyā ca   tisṛbhiḥ ca vahase triṃśatā ca viyugbhiḥ vāyo iha tāḥ vi muñca  
yajñena yajñam ayajanta devāḥ tāni dharmāṇi prathamāni āsan   te ha nākam mahimānaḥ sacanta yatra pūrve sādhyāḥ santi devāḥ  
yajñaḥ babhūva saḥ ā babhūva sa pra jajñe saḥ u vāvṛdhe punar   sa devānām adhipatiḥ babhūva saḥ asmāsu draviṇam ā dadhātu  
yat devāḥ devān haviṣā ayajanta amartyān manasā martyena   madema tatra parame vyoman paśyema tat uditau sūryasya  
yat puruṣeṇa haviṣā yajñam devāḥ atanvata   asti nu tasmāt ojīyaḥ yat vihavyena ijire  
mugdhāḥ devāḥ uta śunā ayajanta uta goḥ aṅgaiḥ purudhā ayajanta   yaḥ imam yajñam manasā ciketa pra naḥ vocaḥ tam iha iha bravaḥ  
aditiḥ dyauḥ aditiḥ antarikṣam aditiḥ mātā sa pitā sa putraḥ   viśve devāḥ aditiḥ pañca janāḥ aditiḥ jātam aditiḥ janitvam  
mahīm u su mātaram suvratānām ṛtasya patnīm avase havāmahe   tuvi kṣatrām ajarantīm urūcīm su śarmāṇam aditim su praṇītim  
su trāmāṇam pṛthivīm dyām anehasam su śarmāṇam aditim su praṇītim   daivīm nāvam svaritrām anāgasaḥ asravantīm ā ruhema svastaye  
vājasya nu prasave mātaram mahīm aditim nāma vacasā karāmahe   yasyāḥ upasthe uru antarikṣam sā naḥ śarma tri varūtham ni yacchāt  
diteḥ putrāṇām aditeḥ akāriṣam ava devānām bṛhatām anarmaṇām   teṣām hi dhāma gabhiṣak samudriyam na enān namasā paraḥ asti kaścana  
bhadrāt adhi śreyaḥ prehi bṛhaspatiḥ puraetā te astu   atha imam asyāḥ vare ā pṛthivyāḥ āreśatrum kṛṇuhi sarva vīram  
prapathe pathām ajaniṣṭa pūṣā prapathe divaḥ prapathe pṛthivyāḥ   ubhe abhi priyatame sadhasthe ā ca parā ca carati prajānan  
pūṣā imāḥ āśāḥ anu veda sarvāḥ saḥ asmām abhayatamena neṣat   svasti dāḥ āghṛṇiḥ sarva vīraḥ a prayucchan puras etu prajānan  
pūṣan tava vrate vayam na riṣyema kadā cana   stotāraḥ te iha smasi  
pari pūṣā parastāt hastam dadhātu dakṣiṇam   punar naḥ naṣṭam ājatu sam naṣṭena gamemahi  
yaḥ te stanaḥ śaśayuḥ yaḥ mayobhūḥ yaḥ sumnayuḥ su havaḥ yaḥ su datraḥ   yena viśvā puṣyasi vāryāṇi sarasvati tam iha dhātave kaḥ  
yaḥ te pṛthu stanayitnuḥ yaḥ ṛṣvaḥ daivaḥ ketuḥ viśvam ābhūṣati idam   mā naḥ vadhīḥ vidyutā deva sasyam mā uta vadhiḥ raśmibhiḥ sūryasya  
sabhā ca mā samitiḥ ca avatām prajāpateḥ duhitarau saṃvidāne   yena saṃgacchāḥ upa mā sa śikṣāt cāru vadāni pitaraḥ saṃgateṣu  
vidma te sabhe nāma nariṣṭā nāma vai asi   ye te ke ca sabhāsadaḥ te me santu savācasaḥ  
eṣām aham samāsīnānām varcaḥ vijñānam ā dade   asyāḥ sarvasyāḥ saṃsadaḥ mām indra bhaginam kṛṇu  
yat vaḥ manaḥ parāgatam yat baddham iha vā iha vā   tat vaḥ ā vartayāmasi mayi vaḥ ramatām manaḥ  
yathā sūryaḥ nakṣatrāṇām udyan tejāṃsi ādade   eva strīṇām ca puṃsām ca dviṣatām varcaḥ ā dade  
yāvantaḥ mā sapatnānām āyantam pratipaśyatha   udyan sūryaḥ iva suptānām dviṣatām varcaḥ ā dade  
abhi tyam devam savitāram oṇyoḥ kavi kratum   arcāmi satya savam ratna dhām abhi priyam matim  
urdhvā yasya amatiḥ bhās adidyutat savīmani   hiraṇya pāṇiḥ amimīta sukratuḥ kṛpāt svar  
sāvīḥ hi deva prathamāya pitre varṣmāṇam asmai varimāṇam asmai   atha asmabhyam savitar vāryāṇi divodivaḥ ā suva bhūri paśvaḥ  
damūnāḥ devaḥ savitā vareṇyaḥ dadhat ratnam pitṛbhyaḥ āyūṃṣi   pibāt somam mamadat enam iṣṭe parijmā cit kramate asya dharmaṇi  
tām savitar satya savām su citrām āham vṛṇe sumatim viśva vārām   yām asya kaṇvaḥ aduhat prapīnām sahasra dhārām mahiṣaḥ bhagāya  
bṛhaspate savitar vardhaya enam jyotaya enam mahate saubhagāya   saṃśitam cit saṃtaram sam śiśādhi viśve enam anu madantu devāḥ  
dhātā dadhātu naḥ rayim īśānaḥ jagataḥ patiḥ   sa naḥ pūrṇena yacchatu  
dhātā dadhātu dāśuṣe prācīm jīvātum akṣitām   vayam devasya dhīmahi sumatim viśva rādhasaḥ  
dhātā viśvā vāryā dadhātu prajā kāmāya dāśuṣe duroṇe   tasmai devāḥ amṛtam sam vyayantu viśve devāḥ aditiḥ sajoṣāḥ  
dhātā rātiḥ savitā idam juṣantām prajāpatiḥ nidhi patiḥ naḥ agniḥ   tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ prajayā saṃrarāṇaḥ yajamānāya draviṇam dadhātu  
pra nabhasva pṛthivi bhinddhi idam divyam nabhaḥ   udnaḥ divyasya naḥ dhātar īśānaḥ vi syāḥ dṛtim  
na ghraṃs tatāpa na himaḥ jaghāna pra nabhatām pṛthivī jīra dānuḥ   āpaḥ cit asmai ghṛtam id kṣaranti yatra somaḥ sadam id tatra bhadram  
prajāpatiḥ janayati prajāḥ imāḥ dhātā dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ   saṃjānānāḥ saṃmanasaḥ sayonayaḥ mayi puṣṭam puṣṭa patiḥ dadhātu  
anu adya naḥ anumatiḥ yajñam deveṣu manyatām   agniḥ ca havyavāhanaḥ bhavatām dāśuṣe mama  
anu id anumate tvam maṃsase śam ca naḥ kṛdhi   juṣasva havyam āhutam prajām devi rarāsva naḥ  
anu manyatām anumanyamānaḥ prajāvantam rayim a kṣīyamāṇam   tasya vayam heḍasi mā api bhūma su mṛḍīke asya sumatau syāma  
yat te nāma su havam su praṇīte anumate anumatam sudānu   tena naḥ yajñam pipṛhi viśva vāre rayim naḥ dhehi subhage su vīram  
ā imam yajñam anumatiḥ jagāma su kṣetra tāyai su vīra tāyai su jātam   bhadrā hi asyāḥ pramatiḥ babhūva sā imam yajñam avatu deva gopā  
anumatiḥ sarvam idam babhūva yat tiṣṭhati carati yat u ca viśvam ejati   tasyāḥ te devi sumatau syāma anumate anu hi maṃsase naḥ  
sameta viśve vacasā patim divaḥ ekaḥ vibhūḥ atithiḥ janānām   sa pūrvyaḥ nūtanam āvivāsat tam vartaniḥ anu vāvṛte ekam id puru  
ayam sahasram ā naḥ dṛśe kavīnām matiḥ jyotiḥ vidharmaṇi 
bradhnaḥ samīcīḥ uṣasaḥ sam airayan   arepasaḥ sacetasaḥ svasare manyumattamāḥ cite goḥ  
dauṣvapnyam daurjīvityam rakṣaḥ abhvam arāyyaḥ   durṇāmnīḥ sarvāḥ durvācaḥ tāḥ asmat nāśayāmasi  
yat naḥ indraḥ akhanat yat agniḥ viśve devāḥ marutaḥ yat su arkāḥ   tat asmabhyam savitā satya dharmā prajāpatiḥ anumatiḥ ni yacchāt  
yayoḥ ojasā skabhitā rajāṃsi yau vīryaiḥ vīratamā śaviṣṭhā   yau patyete apratītau sahobhiḥ viṣṇum agan varuṇam pūrvahūtiḥ  
yasya idam pradiśi yat virocate pra ca anati vi ca caṣṭe śacībhiḥ   purā devasya dharmaṇā sahobhiḥ viṣṇum agan varuṇam pūrva hūtiḥ  
viṣṇoḥ nu kam pra vocam vīryāṇi yaḥ pārthivāni vimame rajāṃsi   yaḥ askabhāyat uttaram sadhastham vicakramāṇaḥ tredhā uru gāyaḥ  
pra tat viṣṇuḥ stavate vīryāṇi mṛgaḥ na bhīmaḥ kucaraḥ giriṣṭhāḥ   parāvataḥ ā jagamyāt parasyāḥ  
yasya uruṣu triṣu vikramaneṣu adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā   uru viṣṇo vi kramasva uru kṣayāya naḥ kṛdhi   ghṛtam ghṛta yone piba prapra yajñapatim tira  
idam viṣṇuḥ vi cakrame tredhā ni dadhe padā   samūḍham asya paṃsure  
trīṇi padā vi cakrame viṣṇuḥ gopāḥ adābhyaḥ   itas dharmāṇi dhārayan  
viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyata yatas vratāni paspaśe   indrasya yujyaḥ sakhā  
tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ   divi iva cakṣuḥ ātatam  
divaḥ viṣṇo uta pṛthivyāḥ mahaḥ viṣṇo uroḥ antarikṣāt   hastau pṛṇasva bahubhiḥ vasavyaiḥ āprayaccha dakṣiṇāt ā uta savyāt  
iḍā eva asmām anu vastām vratena yasyāḥ pade punate devayantaḥ   ghṛtapadī śakvarī soma pṛṣṭhā upa yajñam asthita vaiśvadevī  
vedaḥ svastiḥ drughaṇaḥ svastiḥ paraśuḥ vediḥ paraśuḥ naḥ svasti   haviṣkṛtaḥ yajñiyāḥ yajña kāmāḥ te devāsaḥ yajñam imam juṣantām  
agnāviṣṇū mahi tat vām mahitvam pāthaḥ ghṛtasya guhyasya nāma   damedame sapta ratnā dadhānau prati vām jihvā ghṛtam ā caraṇyāt  
agnāviṣṇū mahi dhāma priyam vām vīthaḥ ghṛtasya guhyā juṣāṇau   damedame suṣṭutyā vāvṛdhānau prati vām jihvā ghṛtam ud caraṇyāt  
svāktam me dyāvāpṛthivī svāktam mitraḥ akaḥ ayam   svāktam me brahmaṇaḥ patiḥ svāktam savitā karat  
indra ūtibhiḥ bahulābhiḥ naḥ adya yāvat śreṣṭhābhiḥ maghavan śūra jinva   yaḥ naḥ dveṣṭi adhara saḥ padīṣṭa yam u dviṣmaḥ tam u prāṇaḥ jahātu  
upa priyam panipnatam yuvānam āhutīvṛdham   aganma bibhrataḥ namaḥ dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu me  
sam mā siñcantu marutaḥ sam pūṣā sam bṛhaspatiḥ   sam mā ayam agniḥ siñcatu prajayā ca dhanena ca dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu me  
agne jātān pra nuda me sapatnān prati a jātān jātavedaḥ nudasva   adhaspadam kṛṇuṣva ye pṛtanyavaḥ anāgasaḥ te vayam aditaye syāma  
pra anyān sapatnān sahasā sahasva prati a jātān jātavedaḥ nudasva   idam rāṣṭram pipṛhi saubhagāya viśve enam anu madantu devāḥ  
imāḥ yāḥ te śatam hirāḥ sahasram dhamanīḥ uta   tāsām te sarvāsām aham aśmanā bilam api adhām  
param yoneḥ avaram te kṛṇomi mā tvā prajā abhi bhūt mā uta sūtuḥ   asvam tvā aprajasam kṛṇomi aśmānam te apidhānam kṛṇomi  
akṣyau nau madhu saṃkāśe anīkam nau samañjanam   antar kṛṣṇuṣva mām hṛdi manaḥ id nau saha asati  
abhi tvā manu jātena dadhāmi mama vāsasā   yāthā asaḥ mama kevalaḥ na anyāsām kīrtayāḥ cana  
idam khanāmi bheṣajam māṃpaśyam abhirorudam   parāyataḥ nivartanam āyataḥ pratinandanam  
yena nicakre āsurī indram devebhyaḥ pari   tena ni kurve tvām aham yathā te asāni su priyā  
pratīcī somam asi pratīcī uta sūryam   pratīcī viśvān devān tām tvā achāvadāmasi  
aham vadāmi na id tvam sabhāyām aha tvam vada   mama id asaḥ tvam kevalaḥ na anyāsām kīrtayāḥ cana  
yadi vā asi tirojanam yadi vā nadyaḥ tiraḥi   iyam ha mahyam tvām oṣadhiḥ baddhvā iva nyānayat  
divyam suparṇam payasam bṛhantam apām garbham vṛṣabham oṣadhīnām   abhīpataḥ vṛṣṭyā tarpayantam ā naḥ goṣṭhe rayiṣṭhām sthāpayāti  
yasya vratam paśavaḥ yanti sarve yasya vrate upatiṣṭhante āpaḥ   yasya vrate puṣṭa patiḥ niviṣṭaḥ tam sarasvantam avase havāmahe  
ā pratyañcam dāśuṣe dāśvaṃsam sarasvantam puṣṭa patim rayiṣṭhām   rāyaḥ poṣam śravasyum vasānāḥ iha sadanam rayīṇām  
ati dhanvāni ati apaḥ tatarda śyenaḥ nṛ cakṣāḥ avasāna darśaḥ   taran viśvāni avarā rajaṃsi indreṇa sakhyā śivaḥ ā jagamyāt  
śyenaḥ nṛ cakṣāḥ divyaḥ suparṇaḥ sahasra pād śata yoniḥ vayodhāḥ   sa naḥ ni yacchāt vasu yat parābhṛtam asmākam astu pitṛṣu svadhāvat  
somārudrā vi vṛhatam viṣūcīm amīvā yā naḥ gayam āviveśa   bādhethām dūram nirṛtim parācais kṛtam cit enaḥ pra mumuktam asmat  
somārudrā yuvam etāni asmat viśvā tanūṣu bheṣajāni dhattam   ava syatam muñcatam yat naḥ asat tanūṣu baddham kṛtam enaḥ asmat  
śivāḥ te ekāḥ aśivāḥ te ekāḥ sarvāḥ bibharṣi sumanasyamānaḥ   tisraḥ vācaḥ nihitāḥ antar asmin tāsām ekā vi papāta anu ghoṣam  
ubhā jigyathuḥ na parā jayethe na parā jigye kataraḥ cana enayoḥ   indraḥ ca viṣṇo yat apaspṛdhethām tredhā sahasram vi tat airayethām  
janāt viśvajanīnāt sindhutaḥ pari ābhṛtam   dūrāt tvā manye udbhṛtam īrṣyāyāḥ nāma bheṣajam  
agneḥ iva asya dahataḥ dāvasya dahataḥ pṛthak   etām etasya īrṣyām udra agnim iva śamaya  
sinīvāli pṛthuṣṭuke yā devānām asi svasā   juṣasva havyam āhutam prajām devi didiḍḍhi naḥ  
yā su bāhuḥ su aṅguriḥ suṣūmā bahu sūvarī   tasyai viśpatnyai haviḥ sinīvālyai juhotana  
yā viśpatnī indram asi pratīcī sahasra stukā abhiyantī devī   viṣṇoḥ patni tubhyam rātā havīṃṣi patim devi rādhase codayasva  
kuhūm devīm su kṛtam vidmanā apasam asmin yajñe su havā johavīmi   sā naḥ rayim viśva vāram ni yacchāt dadātu vīram śata dāyam ukthyam  
kuhūḥ devānām amṛtasya patnī havyā naḥ asya haviṣaḥ juṣeta   śṛnotu yajñam uśatī naḥ adya rāyaḥ poṣam cikituṣī dadhātu  
rākām aham su havā suṣṭutī huve śṛṇotu naḥ subhagā bodhatu tmanā   sīvyatu apaḥ sūcyā āchidyamānayā dadātu vīram śata dāyam ukthyam  
yāḥ te rāke sumatayaḥ supeśasaḥ yābhiḥ dadāsi dāśuṣe vasūni   tābhiḥ naḥ adya sumanāḥ upāgahi sahasrāpoṣam subhage rarāṇā  
devānām patnīḥ uśatīḥ avantu naḥ prāvantu naḥ tujaye vājasātaye   yāḥ pārthivāsaḥ yāḥ apām api vrate tāḥ naḥ devīḥ su havāḥ śarma yacchantu  
uta gnāḥ vyantu deva patnīḥ indrāṇī agnāyī aśvinī rāj   ā rodasī varunānī śṛṇotu vyantu devīḥ yaḥ ṛtuḥ janīnām  
yathā vṛkṣam aśaniḥ viśvāhā hanti aprati   eva aham adya kitavān akṣaiḥ badhyāsam aprati  
turāṇām aturāṇām viśām avarjuṣīṇām   samaitu viśvatas bhagaḥ antarhastam kṛtam mama  
īḍe agnim svāvasum namobhiḥ iha prasaktaḥ vi cayat kṛtam naḥ   rathaiḥ iva pra bhare vājayadbhiḥ pradakṣiṇam marutām stomam ṛdhyām  
vayam jayema tvayā yujā vṛtam asmākam aṃśam ud ava bharebhare   asmabhyam indra varīyaḥ sugam kṛdhi pra śatrūṇām maghavan vṛṣṇyā ruja  
ajaiṣam tvā saṃlikhitam ajaiṣam uta saṃrudham   avim vṛkaḥ yathā mathat eva mathnāmi te kṛtam  
uta prahām atidīvā jayati kṛtam iva śvaghnī vi cinoti kāle   yaḥ deva kāmaḥ na dhanam ruṇaddhi sam id tam rāyaḥ sṛjati svadhābhiḥ  
gobhiḥ tarema amatim durevām yavena vā kṣudham puruhūta viśve   vayam rājasu prathamā dhanāni ariṣṭāsaḥ vṛjanībhiḥ jayema  
kṛtam me dakṣiṇe haste jayaḥ me savyaḥ āhitaḥ   go jit bhūyāsam aśva jit dhanaṃjayaḥ hiraṇya jit  
akṣāḥ phalavatīm dyuvam datta gām kṣīriṇīm iva   sam mā kṛtasya dhārayā dhanuḥ snāvnā iva nahyata  
bṛhaspatiḥ naḥ pari pātu paścāt uta uttarasmāt adharāt aghayoḥ   indraḥ purastāt uta madhyataḥ naḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ varīyaḥ kṛṇotu  
saṃjñānam naḥ svebhiḥ saṃjñānam araṇebhiḥ   saṃjñānam aśvinā yuvam iha asmāsu ni yacchatam  
sam jānāmahai manasā sam cikitvāḥ mā yuṣmahi manasā daivyena   mā ghoṣāḥ ud sthuḥ bahule vinirhate mā iṣuḥ paptat indrasya ahani āgate  
amutrabhūyāt adhi yat yamasya bṛhaspate abhiśasteḥ amuñcaḥ   prati auhatām aśvinā mṛtyum asmat devānām agne bhiṣajā śacībhiḥ  
sam krāmatam mā jahītam śarīram prāṇa apānau te sayujau iha stām   śatam jīva śaradaḥ vardhamānaḥ agniḥ te gopāḥ adhipāḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ  
āyuḥ yat te atihitam parācais apānaḥ prāṇaḥ punar ā tau itām   agniḥ tat āhār nirṛteḥ upasthāt tat ātmani punar ā veśayāmi te  
mā imam prāṇaḥ ha āsīt mā u apānaḥ avahāya parā gāt   saptarṣibhyaḥ enam pari dadāmi te enam svasti jarase vahantu  
pra viṣatam prāṇa apānau anaḍvāhau iva vrajam   ayam jarimnaḥ śevadhiḥ ariṣṭaḥ iha vardhatām  
ā te prāṇam suvāmasi parā yakṣmam suvāmi te   āyuḥ naḥ viśvatas dadhat ayam agniḥ vareṇyaḥ  
ud vayam tamasaḥ pari rohantaḥ nākam uttamam   devam devatrā sūryam aganma jyotiḥ uttamam  
ṛcam sāma yajāmahe yābhyām karmāṇi kurvate   ete sadasi rājataḥ yajñam deveṣu yacchataḥ  
ṛcam sāma yat aprākṣam haviḥ ojaḥ yajuḥ balam   eṣa mā tasmāt mā hiṃsīt vedaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ śacīpate  
ye te panthānaḥ ava divaḥ yebhiḥ viśvam airayaḥ   tebhiḥ sumnayā dhehi naḥ vaso  
tiraści rājeḥ asitāt pṛdākoḥ pari saṃbhṛtam   tat kaṅka parvaṇaḥ viṣam iyam vīrudh anīnaśat  
iyam vīrudh madhu jātā madhuścut madhulā madhūḥ   sā vihrutasya bheṣajī atho maśaka jambhanī  
yatas daṣṭam yatas dhītam tatas te niḥ hvayāmasi   arbhasya tṛpra daṃśinaḥ maśakasya arasam viṣam  
ayam yaḥ vakraḥ viparuḥ vyaṅgaḥ mukhāni vakrā vṛjinā kṛṇoṣi   tāni tvam brahmaṇas pate iṣīkām iva sam namaḥ  
arasasya śarkoṭasya nīcīnasya upasarpataḥ  viṣam hi asya ādiṣi atha u enam ajījabham 
na te bāhvoḥ balam asti na śīrṣe na uta madhyataḥ   atha kim pāpayā amuyā puche bibharṣi arbhakam  
adanti tvā pipīlikāḥ vi vṛścanti mayūryaḥ   sarve bhala bravātha śārkoṭam arasam viṣam  
yaḥ ubhābhyām praharasi puchena ca āsyena ca   āsye na te viṣam kim u te puchadhau asat  
yat āśasā vadataḥ me vicukṣubhe yat yācamānasya carataḥ janām anu   yat ātmani tanvaḥ me viriṣṭam sarasvatī tat ā pṛṇat ghṛtena  
sapta kṣaranti siśave marutvate pitre putrāsaḥ api avīvṛtan ṛtāni   ubhe id asya ubhe asya rājate ubhe yatete ubhe asya puṣyataḥ  
indrāvaruṇā suta pau imam sutam somam pibatam madyam dhṛta vratau   yuvaḥ rathaḥ adhvaraḥ deva vītaye prati svasaram upa yātu pītaye  
indrāvaruṇā madhumattamasya vṛṣṇaḥ somasya vṛṣaṇā vṛṣethām   idam vām andhaḥ pariṣiktam āsadya asmin barhiṣi mādayethām  
yaḥ naḥ śapāt a śapataḥ śapataḥ yaḥ ca naḥ śapāt   vṛkṣaḥ iva vidyutā hataḥ ā mūlāt anu śuṣyatu  
ūrjam bibhrat vasu vaniḥ sumedhāḥ aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā mitriyeṇa   gṛhān aimi sumanāḥ vandamānaḥ ramadhvam mā bibhīta mat  
ime gṛhāḥ mayobhuvaḥ ūrjasvantaḥ payasvantaḥ   pūrṇāḥ vāmena tiṣṭhantaḥ te naḥ jānantu āyataḥ  
yeṣām adhyeti pravasan yeṣu saumanasaḥ bahuḥ   gṛhān upa hvayāmahe te naḥ jānantu āyataḥ  
upahūtāḥ bhūri dhanāḥ sakhāyaḥ svādu saṃmudaḥ   akṣudhyāḥ atṛṣyāḥ sta gṛhāḥ mā asmat bibhītana  
upahūtāḥ iha gāvaḥ upahūtāḥ aja avayaḥ   atha u annasya kīlālaḥ upahūtaḥ gṛheṣu  
sūnṛtāvantaḥ subhagāḥ irāvantaḥ hasāmudāḥ   atṛṣyāḥ akṣudhyāḥ sta gṛhāḥ mā asmat bibhītana  
iha eva sta mā anu gāta viśvā rūpāṇi puṣyata   aiṣyāmi bhadreṇa saha bhūyāṃsaḥ bhavatā mayā  
yat agne tapasā tapaḥ upatapyāmahe tapaḥ   priyāḥ śrutasya bhūyāsma āyuṣmantaḥ sumedhasaḥ  
agne tapaḥ tapyāmahe upa tapyāmahe tapaḥ   śrutāni śṛṇvantaḥ vayam āyuṣmantaḥ sumedhasaḥ  
ayam agniḥ sat patiḥ vṛddha vṛṣṇaḥ rathī iva pattīn ajayat purohitaḥ   nābhā pṛthivyām nihitaḥ davidyutat adhaspadam kṛṇutām ye pṛtanyavaḥ  
pṛtanājitam sahamānam agnim ukthyaiḥ havāmahe paramāt sadhasthāt   sa naḥ parṣat ati durgāṇi viśvā kṣāmat devaḥ ati duritāni agniḥ  
idam yat kṛṣṇaḥ śakuniḥ abhiniṣpatan apīpatat   āpaḥ mā tasmāt sarvasmāt duritāt pāntu aṃhasaḥ  
idam yat kṛṣṇaḥ śakuniḥ avāmṛkṣat nirṛte te mukhena   agniḥ mā tasmāt enasaḥ gārhapatyaḥ pra muñcatu  
pratīcīna phalaḥ hi tvam apāmārga rurohitha   sarvān mat śapathām adhi varīyaḥ yavayāḥ itas  
yat duṣkṛtam yat śamalam yat vā cerima pāpayā   tvayā tat viśvatomukha apāmārga apa mṛjmahe  
śyāvadatā kunakhinā baṇḍena yat saha āsima   apāmārga tvayā vayam sarvam tat apa mṛjmahe  
yadi antarikṣe yadi vātaḥ āsa yadi vṛkṣeṣu yadi vā ulapeṣu   yat aśravan paśavaḥ udyamānam tat brāhmaṇam punar asmān upaitu  
punar mā aitu indriyam punar ātmā draviṇam brāhmaṇam ca   punar agnayaḥ dhiṣṇyāḥ yathāsthāma kalpayantām iha eva  
sarasvati vrateṣu te divyeṣu devi dhāmasu   juṣasva havyam āhutam prajām devi rarāsva naḥ  
idam te havyam ghṛtavat sarasvatī idam pitṝṇām haviḥ āsyam yat   imāni te uditā śamtamāni tebhiḥ vayam madhumantaḥ syāma  
śivā naḥ śaṃtamā bhava su mṛḍīkā sarasvati   mā te yuyoma saṃdṛśaḥ  
śam naḥ vātaḥ vātu śam naḥ tapatu sūryaḥ   ahāni śam bhavantu naḥ śam rātrī prati dhīyatām   śam uṣāḥ naḥ vi uchatu  
yat kim ca asau manasā yat ca vācā yajñaiḥ juhoti haviṣā yajuṣā   tat mṛtyunā nirṛtiḥ saṃvidānā purā satyāt āhutim hantu asya  
yātudhānāḥ nirṛtiḥ āt u rakṣaḥ te asya ghnantu anṛtena satyam   indra iṣitāḥ devāḥ ājam asya mathnantu mā tat sam pādi yat asau juhoti  
ajira adhirājau śyenau saṃpātinau iva   ājyam pṛtanyataḥ hatām yaḥ naḥ kaḥ ca abhyaghāyati  
apāñcau te ubhau bāhū api nahyāmi āsyam   agneḥ devasya manyunā tena te avadhiṣam haviḥ  
api nahyāmi te bāhū api nahyāmi āsyam   agneḥ ghorasya manyunā tena avadhiṣam haviḥ  
pari tvā agne puram vayam vipram sahasya dhīmahi   dhṛṣat varṇam divedive hantāram bhaṅgurāvataḥ  
ud tiṣṭhata ava paśyata indrasya bhāgam ṛtviyam   yadi śrātam juhotana yadi a śrātam mamattana  
śrātam haviḥ ā u su indra pra yāhi jagāma sūraḥ adhvanaḥ vi madhyam   pari tvā āsate nidhibhiḥ sakhāyaḥ kulapāḥ na vrāja patim carantam  
śrātam manye ūdhani śrātam agnau su śṛtam manye tat ṛtam navīyaḥ   mādhyandinasya savanasya dadhnaḥ piba indra vajrin puru kṛt juṣāṇaḥ  
samiddhaḥ agniḥ vṛṣaṇā rathī divaḥ taptaḥ gharmaḥ duhyate vām iṣe madhu   vayam hi vām purudamāsaḥ aśvinā havāmahe sadhamādeṣu kāravaḥ  
samiddhaḥ agniḥ aśvinā taptaḥ vām gharme ā gatam   duhyante nūnam vṛṣaṇā iha dhenavaḥ dasrā madanti vedhasaḥ  
iva ahākṛtaḥ śuciḥ deveṣu yajñaḥ yaḥ aśvinoḥ camasaḥ deva pānaḥ   tam u viśve amṛtāsaḥ juṣāṇāḥ gandharvasya prati āsnā rihanti  
yat usriyāsu āhutam ghṛtam payaḥ ayam sa vām aśvinā bhāgaḥ ā gatam   mādhvī dhartārā vidathasya satpatī taptam gharmam pibatam divaḥ  
taptaḥ vām gharmaḥ nakṣatu sva hotā pra vām adhvaryuḥ caratu payasvān   madhoḥ dugdhasya aśvinā tanāyāḥ vītam pātam payasaḥ usriyāyāḥ  
upa drava payasā go dhuk oṣam ā gharme siñca payaḥ usriyāyāḥ   vi nākam akhyat savitā vareṇyaḥ anuprayāṇam uṣasaḥ vi rājati  
upa hvaye su dughām dhenum etām su hastaḥ go dhuk uta dohat enām   śreṣṭham savam savitā sāviṣat naḥ abhīddhaḥ gharmaḥ tat u su pra vocat  
hiṅkṛṇvatī vasu patnī vasūnām vatsam ichantī manasā nyāgan   duhām aśvibhyām payaḥ aghnyā iyam sā vardhatām mahate saubhagāya  
juṣṭaḥ damūnāḥ atithiḥ duroṇe imam naḥ yajñam upa yāhi vidvān   viśvāḥ agne abhiyujaḥ vihatya śatrūyatām ā bhara bhojanāni  
agne śardha mahate saubhagāya tava dyumnāni uttamāni santu   sam jāspatyam suyamam ā kṛṇuṣva śatrūyatām abhi tiṣṭha mahāṃsi  
sūyavasāt bhagavatī hi bhūyāḥ adhā vayam bhagavantaḥ syāma   addhi tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī  
apacitām lohinīnām kṛṣṇā mātā iti śuśruma   muneḥ devasya mūlena sarvāḥ vidhyāmi tāḥ aham  
vidhyāmi āsām prathamām vidhyāmi uta madhyamām   idam jaghanyām āsām ā chinadmi stukām iva  
tvāṣṭreṇa aham vacasā vi te īrṣyām amīmadam   atha u yaḥ manyuḥ te pate tam u te śamayāmasi  
vratena tvam vratapate samaktaḥ viśvāhā sumanāḥ dīdihi iha   tam tvā vayam jātavedaḥ samiddham prajāvantaḥ upa sadema sarve  
prajāvatīḥ sūyavase ruśantīḥ śuddhāḥ apaḥ su prapāṇe pibantīḥ   mā vaḥ stenaḥ īśata mā agha śaṃsaḥ pari vaḥ rudrasya hetiḥ vṛṇaktu  
pada jñāḥ stha ramatayaḥ saṃhitāḥ viśva nāmnīḥ   upa mā devīḥ devebhiḥ eta   imam goṣṭham idam sadaḥ ghṛtena asmān sam ukṣata  
ā susrasaḥ susrasaḥ asatībhyaḥ asattarāḥ   sehoḥ arasatarāḥ havaṇāt vikledīyasīḥ  
yāḥ graivyāḥ apacitaḥ atha u yāḥ upapakṣyāḥ   vijāmni yāḥ apacitaḥ svayaṃsrasaḥ  
yaḥ kīkasāḥ praśṛṇāti talīdyam avatiṣṭhati   niḥ hāḥ tam sarvam jāyānyam yaḥ kaḥ ca kakudi śritaḥ  
pakṣī jāyānyaḥ patati saḥ ā viśati pūruṣam   tat akṣitasya bheṣajam ubhayoḥ su kṣatasya ca  
vidma vai te jāyānya jānam yatas jāyānya jāyase   katham ha tatra tvam hanaḥ yasya kṛṇmaḥ haviḥ gṛhe  
dhṛṣat piba kalaśe somam indra vṛtra hā śūra samare vasūnām   mādhyandine savane ā vṛṣasva rayiṣṭhānaḥ rayim asmāsu dhehi  
sāṃtapanāḥ idam haviḥ marutaḥ tat jujuṣṭana   asmākotī riśādasaḥ  
yaḥ naḥ martaḥ marutaḥ durhṛṇāyuḥ tiras cittāni vasavaḥ jighāṃsati   druhaḥ pāśān prati muñcatām saḥ tapiṣṭhena tapasā hantana tam  
samvatsarīṇāḥ marutaḥ su arkāḥ uru kṣayāḥ sa gaṇāḥ mānuṣāsaḥ   te asmat pāśān pra muñcantu enasaḥ sāṃtapanāḥ matsarāḥ mādayiṣṇavaḥ  
vi te muñcāmi raśanām vi yoktram vi niyojanam   iha eva tvam ajasraḥ edhi agne  
asmai kṣatrāṇi dhārayantam agne yunajmi tvā brahmaṇā daivyena   dīdihi asmabhyam draviṇā iha bhadram pra imam vocaḥ haviḥ dām devatāsu  
yat te devāḥ akṛṇvan bhāgadheyam amāvāsye saṃvasantaḥ mahitvā   tena naḥ yajñam pipṛhi viśva vāre rayim naḥ dhehi subhage su vīram  
aham eva asmi amāvāsyāḥ mām ā vasanti su kṛtaḥ mayi ime   mayi devāḥ ubhaye sādyāḥ ca indra jyeṣṭhāḥ sam agacchanta sarve  
āgan rātrī saṅgamanī vasūnām ūrjam puṣṭam vasu āveśayantī   amāvāsyāyai haviṣa vidhema ūrjam duhānā payasā naḥ āgan  
amāvāsye na tvat etāni anyaḥ viśvā rūpāṇi paribhūḥ jajāna   yad kāmāḥ te juhumaḥ tat naḥ astu vayam syāma patayaḥ rayiṇām  
paurṇamāsī jigāya   tasyām devaiḥ saṃvasantaḥ mahitvā nākasya pṛṣṭhe sam iṣā madema  
vṛṣabham vājinam vayam paurṇamāsam yajāmahe   sa naḥ dadātu akṣitām rayim anupadasvatīm  
prajāpate na tvat etāni anyaḥ viśvā rūpāṇi paribhūḥ jajāna   yad kāmāḥ te juhumaḥ tat naḥ astu vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām  
paurṇamāsī prathamā yajñiyā āsīt ahnām rātrīṇām ati śarvareṣu   ye tvām yajñaiḥ yajñiye ardhayanti amī te nāke su kṛtaḥ praviṣṭāḥ  
pūrva aparam carataḥ mayayā etau śiśū krīḍantau pari yātaḥ arṇavam   viśvā anyaḥ bhuvanā vicaṣṭe ṛtūṃr anyaḥ vidadhat jāyase navaḥ  
navaḥ navaḥ bhavasi jāyamānaḥ ahnām ketuḥ uṣasām eṣi agram   bhāgam devebhyaḥ vi dadhāsi āyan pra candramaḥ tirase dhīrgham āyuḥ  
somasya amśaḥ yudhām pate anūnaḥ nāma vai asi   anūnam darśa mā kṛdhi prajayā ca dhanena ca  
darśaḥ asi darśataḥ asi samagraḥ asi samantaḥ   samagraḥ samantaḥ bhūyāsam gobhiḥ aśvaiḥ prajayā paśubhiḥ gṛhaiḥ dhanena  
yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ tasya tvam prāṇena ā pyāyasva   ā vayam pyāsiṣīmahi gobhiḥ aśvaiḥ prajayā paśubhiḥ gṛhaiḥ dhanena  
yam devāḥ aṃśum āpyāyayanti yam akṣitam akṣitāḥ bhakṣayanti   tena asmān indraḥ varuṇaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ ā pyāyayantu bhuvanasya gopāḥ  
abhi arcata suṣṭutim gavyam ājim asmāsu bhadrā draviṇāni dhatta   imam yajñam nayata devatā naḥ ghṛtasya dhārāḥ madhumat pavantām  
mayi agre agnim gṛhṇāmi saha kṣatreṇa varcasā balena   mayi prajām mayi āyuḥ dadhāmi svāhā mayi agnim  
iha eva agne adhi dhāraya rayim mā tvā ni kran pūrva cittāḥ nikāriṇaḥ   kṣatreṇa agne suyamam astu tubhyam upasattā vardhatām te a niṣṭṛtaḥ  
anu agniḥ uṣasām agram akhyat anu ahāni prathamaḥ jātavedāḥ   anu sūryaḥ uṣasaḥ anu raśmīn anu dyāvāpṛthivī ā viveśa  
prati agniḥ uṣasām agram akhyat prati ahāni prathamaḥ jātavedāḥ   prati sūryasya purudhā ca raśmīn prati dyāvāpṛthivī ā tatāna  
ghṛtam te agne divye sadhasthe ghṛtena tvām manuḥ adyā sam indhe   ghṛtam te devīḥ naptyaḥ ā vahantu ghṛtam tubhyam duhratām gāvaḥ agne  
apsu te rājan varuṇa gṛhaḥ hiraṇyayaḥ mitaḥ   tatas dhṛta vrataḥ rājā sarvā dhāmāni muñcatu  
dāmnaḥ udāmnaḥ rājan itas varuṇa muñca naḥ   yat āpaḥ aghnyāḥ iti varuṇa iti yat ūcima tatas varuṇa muñca naḥ  
ud uttamam varuṇa pāśam asmat ava adhamam vi madhyamam śrathāya   adha vayam āditya vrate tava anāgasaḥ aditaye syāma  
pra asmat pāśān varuṇa muñca sarvān ye uttamāḥ adhamāḥ vāruṇāḥ ye   duṣvapnyam duritam ni sva asmat atha gacchema su kṛtasya lokam  
anādhṛṣyaḥ jātavedāḥ amartyaḥ virāj agne kṣatra bhṛt dīdihi iha   viśvāḥ amīvāḥ pramuñcan mānuṣībhiḥ śivābhiḥ adya pari pāhi naḥ gayam  
indra kṣatram abhi vāmam ojaḥ ajāyathāḥ vṛṣabha carṣaṇīnām   apānudaḥ janam amitrayantam urum devebhyaḥ akṛṇoḥ u lokam  
mṛgaḥ na bhīmaḥ kucaraḥ giriṣṭhāḥ parāvataḥ ā jagamyāt parasyāḥ   sṛkam saṃśāya pavim indra tigmam vi śatrūn tāḍhi vi mṛdhaḥ nudasva  
tyam u su vājinam deva jūtam sahovānam tarutāram rathānām   ariṣṭa nemim pṛtanājim āśum svastaye tārkṣyam iha ā huvema  
trātāram indram avitāram indram have ihave su havam śūram indram   huve nu śakram puruhūtam indram svasti naḥ indraḥ maghavā kṛṇotu  
yaḥ agnau rudraḥ yaḥ apsu antar yaḥ oṣadhīḥ vīrudhaḥ āviveśa   yaḥ imā viśvā bhuvanāni ca ākḷpe tasmai rudrāya namaḥ astu agnaye  
apehi ariḥ asi ariḥ vai asi viṣe viṣam apṛkthāḥ viṣam id vai apṛkthāḥ   ahim eva abhyapehi tam jahi  
apaḥ divyāḥ acāyiṣam rasena sam apṛkṣmahi   payasvān agne āgamam tam mā sam sṛja varcasā  
sam mā agne varcasā sṛja sam prajayā sam āyuṣā   vidyuḥ me asya devāḥ indraḥ vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ  
idam āpaḥ pra vahata avadyam ca malam ca yat   yat ca abhidudroha anṛtam yat ca śepe abhīruṇam  
edhaḥ asi edhiṣīya samidh asi sam edhiṣīya   tejaḥ asi tejaḥ mayi dhehi  
api vṛśca purāṇa vat vratateḥ iva guṣpitam   ojaḥ dāsasya dambhaya  
vayam tat asya sambhṛtam vasu indrena vi bhajāmahai   mlāpayāmi bhrajaḥ śibhram varuṇasya vratena te  
yathā śepaḥ apāyātai strīṣu ca asat anāvayāḥ   avasthasya knadīvataḥ śāṅkurasya nitodinaḥ   yat ātatam ava tat tanu yat uttatam ni tat tanu  
indraḥ sutrāmā svavām avobhiḥ su mṛḍīkaḥ bhavatu viśva vedāḥ   bādhatām dveṣaḥ abhayam naḥ kṛṇotu su vīryasya patayaḥ syāma  
sa sutrāmā svavān indraḥ asmat ārāt cit dveṣaḥ sanutar yuyotu   tasya vayam sumatau yajñiyasya api bhadre saumanase syāma  
indreṇa manyunā vayam abhi syāma pṛtanyataḥ   ghnantaḥ vṛtrāṇi aprati  
dhruvam dhruveṇa haviṣā ava somam nayāmasi   yathā naḥ indraḥ kevalīḥ viśaḥ saṃmanasaḥ karat  
ud asya śyāvau vithurau gṛdhrau dyām iva petatuḥ   ucchocana praśocanau asya ucchocanau hṛdaḥ  
aham enau ud atiṣṭhipam gāvau śrānta sadau iva   kurkurau iva kūjantau udavantau vṛkau iva  
ātodinau nitodinau atho saṃtodinau uta   api nahyāmi asya meḍhram yaḥ itas strī pumān jabhāra  
asadan gāvaḥ sadane apaptat vasatim vayaḥ   āsthāne parvatāḥ asthuḥ sthāmni vṛkkau atiṣṭhipam  
yat adya tvā prayati yajñe asmin hotar cikitvan avṛṇīmahi iha   dhruvam ayaḥ dhruvam uta śaviṣṭhai pravidvān yajñam upa yāhi somam  
sam indra naḥ manasā neṣa gobhiḥ sam sūribhiḥ harivan sam svastyā   sam brahmaṇā deva hitam yat asti sam devānām sumatau yajñiyānām  
yān āvahaḥ uśataḥ deva devān tān preraya sve agne sadhasthe   jakṣivāṃsaḥ papivāṃsaḥ madhūni asmai dhatta vasavaḥ vasūni  
sugā vaḥ devāḥ sadanāḥ akarma yaḥ ājagma savane mā juṣāṇāḥ   vahamānāḥ bharamāṇāḥ svā vasūni vasum gharmam divam ā rohata anu  
yajña yajñam gaccha yajñapatim gaccha   svām yonim gaccha svāhā  
eṣa te yajñaḥ yajñapate sahasūktavākaḥ   su vīryaḥ svāhā  
vaṣaṭ dhutebhyaḥ vaṣaṭ a hutebhyaḥ   devāḥ gātu vidaḥ gātum vittvā gātum ita  
manasaḥ pate imam naḥ divi deveṣu yajñam   svāhā divi svāhā pṛthivyām svāhā antarikṣe svāhā vāte dhām svāhā  
sam barhiḥ aktam haviṣā ghṛtena sam indreṇa vasunā sam marudbhiḥ   sam devaiḥ viśva devebhiḥ aktam indram gacchatu haviḥ svāhā  
pari stṛṇīhi pari dhehi vedim mā jāmim moṣīḥ amuyā śayānām   hotṛṣadanam haritam hiraṇyayam niṣkāḥ ete yajamānasya loke  
paryāvarte duṣvapnyāt pāpāt svapnyāt abhūtyāḥ   brahma aham antaram kṛṇve parā svapna mukhāḥ śucaḥ  
yat svapne annam aśnāmi na prātar adhigamyate   sarvam tat astu me śivam nahi tat dṛṣyate divā  
namaskṛtya dyāvāpṛthivībhyām antarikṣāya mṛtyave   mekṣāmi ūrdhvaḥ tiṣṭhat mā mā hiṃsiṣuḥ īśvarāḥ  
kaḥ asyāḥ naḥ druhaḥ avadyavatyai ud neṣyati kṣatriyaḥ vasyaḥ ichan   kaḥ yajña kāmaḥ kaḥ u pūrti kāmaḥ kaḥ deveṣu vanute dīrgham āyuḥ  
kaḥ pṛśnim dhenum varuṇena dattām atharvane su dughām nitya vatsām   bṛhaspatinā sakhyam juṣaṇaḥ yathāvaśam tanvaḥ kalpayāti  
apakrāman pauruṣeyāt vṛṇānaḥ daivyam vacaḥ   praṇītīḥ abhyāvartasva viśvebhiḥ sakhibhiḥ saha  
yat asmṛti cakṛma kim cit agne upārima caraṇe jātavedaḥ   tatas pāhi tvam naḥ pracetaḥ śubhe sakhibhyaḥ amṛta tvam astu naḥ  
ava divaḥ tārayanti sapta sūryasya raśmayaḥ   āpaḥ samudriyāḥ dhārāḥ tāḥ śalyam asisrasan  
yaḥ naḥ stāyat dipsati yaḥ naḥ āvis svaḥ vidvān araṇaḥ vā naḥ agne   pratīcī etu araṇī datvatī tān mā eṣām agne vā astu bhūt mā u apatyam  
yaḥ naḥ suptān jāgrataḥ vā abhidāsāt tiṣṭhataḥ vā carataḥ jātavedaḥ   vaiśvānareṇa sayujā sajoṣāḥ tān pratīcaḥ niḥ daha jātavedaḥ  
idam ugrāya babhrave namaḥ yaḥ akṣeṣu tanū vaśī   ghṛtena kalim śikṣāmi sa naḥ mṛḍāti īdṛśe  
ghṛtam apsarābhyaḥ vaha tvam agne pāṃsūn akṣebhyaḥ sikatāḥ apaḥ ca   yathābhagam havya dātim juṣāṇāḥ madanti devāḥ ubhayāni havyā  
apsarasaḥ sadhamādam madanti havirdhānam antarā sūryam ca   tāḥ me hastau sam sṛjantu ghṛtena sapatnam me kitavam randhayantu  
ādinavam pratidīvne ghṛtena asmām abhi kṣara   vṛkṣam iva aśanyā jahi yaḥ asmān pratidīvyati  
yaḥ naḥ dyuve dhanam idam cakāra yaḥ akṣāṇām glahanam śeṣaṇam ca   sa naḥ devaḥ haviḥ idam juṣāṇaḥ gandharvebhiḥ sadhamādam madema  
saṃvasavaḥ iti vaḥ nāmadheyam ugraṃpaśyāḥ rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ hi akṣāḥ   tebhyaḥ vaḥ indavaḥ haviṣā vidhema vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām  
devān yat nāthitaḥ huve brahmacaryam yat ūṣima   akṣān yat babhrūn ālabhe te naḥ mṛḍantu īdṛśe  
agne indraḥ ca dāśuṣe hataḥ vṛtrāṇi aprati   ubhā hi vṛtra hantamā  
yābhyām ajayan svar agre eva yau ātasthatuḥ bhuvanāni viśvā   pra carṣaṇī vṛṣaṇā vajra bāhū agnim indram vṛtra haṇā huve aham  
upa tvā devaḥ agramīt camasena bṛhaspatiḥ   indra gīrbhiḥ naḥ ā viśa yajamānāya sunvate  
indrasya kukṣiḥ asi soma dhānaḥ ātmā devānām uta mānuṣāṇām   iha prajāḥ janaya yāḥ te āsu yāḥ anyatra iha tāḥ te ramantām  
śumbhanī dyāvāpṛthivī antisumne mahivrate   āpaḥ sapta susruvuḥ devīḥ tāḥ naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
muñcantu mā śapathyāt atha u varuṇyāt uta   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt  
tṛṣṭike tṛṣṭa vandanaḥ ud amūm chindhi tṛṣṭike   yathā kṛta dviṣṭāsaḥ amuṣmai śepyāvate  
tṛṣṭā asi tṛṣṭikā viṣā viṣātakī asi   parivṛktā yathā asasi ṛṣabhasya vaśā iva  
ā te dade vakṣaṇābhyaḥ ā te aham hṛdayāt dade   ā te mukhasya saṅkāśāt sarvam te varcaḥ ā dade  
pra itas yantu vyādhyaḥ pra anudhyāḥ pra u aśastayaḥ   agniḥ rakṣasvinīḥ hantu somaḥ hantu durasyatīḥ  
pra pata itas pāpi lakṣmi naśyetaḥ pra amutas pata   ayasmayena aṅkena dviṣate tvā sajāmasi  
yā mā lakṣmīḥ patayālūḥ ajuṣṭā abhicaskanda vandanā iva vṛkṣam   anyatra asmat savitar tām itas dhāḥ hiraṇya hastaḥ vasu naḥ rarāṇaḥ  
eka śatam lakṣmyaḥ martyasya sākam tanvā januṣaḥ adhi jātāḥ   tāsām pāpiṣṭhāḥ niḥ itas pra hiṇmaḥ śivāḥ asmabhyam jātavedaḥ niyaccha  
etāḥ enāḥ vyākaram khile gāḥ viṣṭhitāḥ iva   ramantām puṇyā lakṣmīḥ yāḥ pāpīḥ tāḥ anīnaśam  
namaḥ rūrāya cyavanāya nodanāya dhṛṣṇave   namaḥ śītāya pūrva kāma kṛtvane  
yaḥ anyedyus ubhayadyus abhyeti imam maṇḍūkam   abhi etu avrataḥ  
ā mandraiḥ indra haribhiḥ yāhi mayūra romabhiḥ   mā tvā ke cit vi yaman vim na pāśinaḥ ati dhanva iva tām ihi  
marmāṇi te varmaṇā chādayāmi somaḥ tvā rājā amṛtena anu vastām   uroḥ varīyaḥ varuṇaḥ te kṛṇotu jayantam tvā anu devāḥ madantu  
antakāya mṛtyave namaḥ prānāḥ apānāḥ iha te ramantām   iha ayam astu puruṣaḥ saha asunā sūryasya bhāge amṛtasya loke  
ud enam bhagaḥ agrabhīt ud enam somaḥ aṃśumān   ud enam marutaḥ devāḥ ud indra agnī svastaye  
iha te asuḥ iha prāṇaḥ iha āyuḥ iha te manaḥ   ud tvā nirṛtyāḥ pāśebhyaḥ daivyā vacā bharāmasi  
ud krāma atas puruṣa mā ava patthāḥ mṛtyoḥ paḍvīṣam avamuñcamānaḥ   mā chitthāḥ asmāt lokāt agneḥ sūryasya saṃdṛśaḥ  
tubhyam vātaḥ pavatām mātariśvā tubhyam varṣantu amṛtāni āpaḥ   sūryaḥ te tanve śam tapāti tvām mṛtyuḥ dayatām mā pra meṣṭhāḥ  
udyānam te puruṣa na avayānam jīvātum te dakṣatātim kṛnomi   ā hi roha imam amṛtam sukham ratham atha jirviḥ vidatham ā vadāsi  
mā te manaḥ tatra gāt mā tiras bhūt mā jīvebhyaḥ pra madaḥ mā anu gāḥ pitṝn   viśve devāḥ abhi rakṣantu tvā iha  
mā gatānām ā dīdhīthāḥ ye nayanti parāvatam   ā roha tamasaḥ jyotiḥ ehi ā te hastau rabhāmahe  
śyāmaḥ ca tvā mā śabalaḥ ca preṣitau yamasya yau pathirakṣī śvānau   arvāṅ ehi mā vi dīdhyaḥ mā atra tiṣṭhaḥ parāṅmanāḥ  
 mā etam panthām anu gāḥ bhīmaḥ eṣa yena pūrvam neyatha tam bravīmi   tamaḥ etat puruṣa mā pra patthāḥ bhayam parastāt abhayam te arvāk   tamaḥ etat puruṣa mā pra patthāḥ bhayam parastāt abhayam te arvāk   te arvāk   tamaḥ etat puruṣa mā pra patthāḥ bhayam parastāt abhayam te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te arvāk   te ar
rakṣantu tvā agnayaḥ ye apsu antā rakṣatu tvā manuṣyāḥ yam indhate   vaiśvānaraḥ rakṣatu jātavedāḥ divyaḥ tvā mā pra dhāk vidyutā saha  
mā tvā kravyād abhi maṃstārāt saṃkasukāt cara rakṣatu tvā dyauḥ rakṣatu   pṛthivī sūryaḥ ca tvā rakṣatām candramāḥ ca   antarikṣam rakṣatu deva hetyāḥ  
bodhaḥ ca tvā pratibodhaḥ ca rakṣatām asvapnaḥ ca tvā anavadrāṇaḥ ca rakṣatām   gopāyan ca tvā jāgṛviḥ ca rakṣatām   gopāyan ca tvā jāgṛviḥ ca rakṣatām   gopāyan ca tvā jāgṛviḥ ca rakṣatām  
te tvā rakṣantu te tvā gopāyantu tebhyaḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ svāhā  
jīvebhyaḥ tvā samude vāyuḥ indraḥ dhātā dadhātu savitā trāyamāṇaḥ   mā tvā prāṇaḥ balam ha āsīt asum te anu hvayāmasi  
mā tvā jambhaḥ saṃhanuḥ mā tamaḥ vidat mā jihvā barhiḥ pramayuḥ kathā syāḥ   ud tvā ādityāḥ vasavaḥ bharantu ud indra agnī svastaye  
ud tvā dyauḥ ud pṛthivī ud prajāpatiḥ agrabhīt   ud tvā mṛtyoḥ oṣadhayaḥ soma rājñīḥ apīparan  
ayam devāḥ iha eva astu ayam mā amutra gāt itas   imam sahasra vīryeṇa mṛtyoḥ ud pārayāmasi  
ud tvā mṛtyoḥ apīparam sam dhamantu vayodhasaḥ   mā tvā vyasta keśyaḥ mā tvā agharudaḥ rudan  
āhārṣam avidam tvā punar āgāḥ punarṇavaḥ   sarva aṅga sarvam te cakṣuḥ sarvam āyuḥ ca te avidam  
vi avāt te jyotiḥ abhūt apa tvat tamaḥ akramīt   apa tvat mṛtyum nirṛtim apa yakṣmam ni dadhmasi     
ā rabhasva imām amṛtasya śnuṣṭim a chidyamānā jaradaṣṭiḥ astu te   asum te āyuḥ punar ā bharāmi rajaḥ tamaḥ mā upa gāḥ mā pra meṣṭhāḥ  
jīvatām jyotiḥ abhyehi arvāṅ ā tvā harāmi śata śāradāya   avamuñcat mṛtyu pāśān aśastim drāghīyaḥ āyuḥ prataram te dadhāmi  
vātāt te prānam avidam sūryāt cakṣuḥ aham tava   yat te manaḥ tvayi tat dhārayāmi sam vitsva aṅgaiḥ vada jihvayā ālapan  
prāṇena tvā dvipadām catuṣpadām agnim iva jātam abhi sam dhamāmi   namaḥ te mṛtyo cakṣuṣe namaḥ prāṇāya te akaram  
ayam jīvatu mā mṛtaḥ imam sam īrayāmasi   kṛṇomi asmai bheṣajam mṛtyo mā puruṣam vadhīḥ  
jīvalām naghāriṣām jīvantīm oṣadhīm aham   trāyamāṇām sahamānām sahasvatīm iha huve asmai ariṣṭatātaye  
adhi brūhi mā rabhathāḥ sṛja imam tava eva san sarva hāyāḥ iha astu   bhava aśarvau mṛḍatam śarma yacchatam apasidhya duritam dhattam āyuḥ  
asmai mṛtyo adhi brūhi imam dayasva ud itas ayam etu   ariṣṭaḥ sarva aṅgaḥ su śrut jarasā śata hāyanaḥ ātmanā bhujam aśnutām  
devānām hetiḥ pari tvā vṛṇaktu pārayāmi tvā rajasaḥ ud tvā mṛtyoḥ apīparam   ārāt agnim kravya adam nirūham jīvātave te paridhim dadhāmi  
 yat te niyānam rajasam mṛtyo an avadharṣyam   pathaḥ imam tasmāt rakṣantaḥ brahma asmai varma kṛṇmasi                                                                                                                                      
kṛṇomi te prāṇa apānau jarām mṛtyum dīrgham āyuḥ svasti   vaivasvatena prahitān yama dūtān carataḥ apa sedhāmi sarvān  
ārāt arātim nirṛtim paras grāhim kravya adaḥ piśācān   rakṣaḥ yat sarvam durbhūtam tat tamaḥ iva apa hanmasi  
agneḥ ta prānam amṛtāt āyuṣmataḥ vanve jātavedasaḥ   yathā na riṣyāḥ amṛtaḥ sajūs asaḥ tat te kṛṇomi tat u te sam ṛdhyatām  
śive te stām dyāvāpṛthivī asaṃtāpe abhiśriyau   śam te sūryaḥ ā tapatu śam vātaḥ vātu te hṛde   śivāḥ abhi kṣarantu tvāpaḥ divyāḥ payasvatīḥ  
śivāḥ te santu oṣadhayaḥ ud tvā ahārṣam adharasyāḥ uttarām pṛthivīm abhi  tatra tvā ādityau rakṣatām sūryācandramasau ubhā 
yat te vāsaḥ paridhānam yām nīvim kṛṇuṣe tvam   śivam te tanve tat kṛṇmaḥ saṃsparśe adrūkṣṇam astu te  
yat kṣureṇa marcayatā su tejasā vaptā vapasi keśa śmaśru   śubham mukham mā naḥ āyuḥ pra moṣīḥ  
śivau te stām vrīhi yavau abalāsau adomadhau   etau yakṣmam vi bādhete etau muñcataḥ aṃhasaḥ  
yat aśnāsi yat pibasi dhānyam kṛṣyāḥ payaḥ   yat ādyam yat anādyam sarvam te annam aviṣam kṛṇomi  
ahne ca tvā rātraye ca ubhābhyām pari dadmasi   arāyebhyaḥ jighatsubhyaḥ imam me pari rakṣata     
śatam te ayutam hāyanān dve yuge trīṇi catvāri kṛṇmaḥ   indra agnī viśve devāḥ te anu manyantām a hṛṇīyamānāḥ  
śarade tvā hemantāya vasantāya grīṣmāya pari dadmasi   varṣāṇi tubhyam syonāni yeṣu vardhante oṣadhīḥ  
mṛtyuḥ īśe dvipadām mṛtyuḥ īśe catuṣpadām   tasmāt tvām mṛtyoḥ gopateḥ ud bharāmi sa mā bibheḥ  
saḥ ariṣṭa na mariṣyasi na mariṣyasi mā bibheḥ   na vai tatra mriyante naḥ yanti adhamam tamaḥ  
sarvaḥ vai tatra jīvati gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ   yatra idam brahma kriyate paridhiḥ jīvanāya kam  
pari tvā pātu samānebhyaḥ abhicārāt sabandhubhyaḥ   amamriḥ bhava amṛtaḥ atijīvaḥ mā te hāsiṣuḥ asavaḥ śarīram  
ye mṛtyavaḥ eka śatam yāḥ nāṣṭrāḥ atitāryāḥ   muñcantu tasmāt tvām devāḥ agneḥ vaiśvānarāt adhi  
agneḥ śarīram asi pārayiṣṇu rakṣaḥ hā asi sapatna hā   atha u amīva cātanaḥ pūtudruḥ nāma bheṣajam     
rakṣaḥ haṇam vājinam ā jigharmi mitram prathiṣṭham upa yāmi śarma   śiśānaḥ agniḥ kratubhiḥ samiddhaḥ sa naḥ divā sa riṣaḥ pātu naktam  
ayaḥ daṃṣṭraḥ arciṣā yātudhānān upa spṛśa jātavedaḥ samiddhaḥ   ā jihvayā mūradevān rabhasva kravya adaḥ vṛṣṭvā api dhatsva āsan  
ubhā ubhayāvin upa dhehi daṃṣṭrau hiṃsraḥ śiśānaḥ avaram param ca   uta antarikṣe pari yāhi agne jambhaiḥ sam dhehi abhi yātudhānān  
agne tvacam yātudhānasya bhindhi hiṃsra aśaniḥ harasā hantu enam   pra parvāṇi jātavedaḥ śṛṇīhi kravyād kraviṣṇuḥ vi cinotu enam  
yatra idānīm paśyasi jātavedaḥ tiṣṭhantam agne uta vā carantam   uta antarikṣe patantam yātudhānam tam astā vidhya śarvā śiśānaḥ  
yajñaiḥ iṣūḥ saṃnamamānaḥ agne iva ācā śalyām aśanibhiḥ dihānaḥ   tābhiḥ vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān pratīcaḥ bāhūn prati bhaṅgdhi eṣām  
uta ārabdhān spṛnuhi jātavedaḥ uta ārebhāṇām ṛṣṭibhiḥ yātudhānān   agne pūrvaḥ ni jahi śośucānaḥ āma adaḥ kṣviṅkāḥ tam adantu enīḥ  
iha pra brūhi yatamaḥ saḥ agne yātudhānaḥ yaḥ idam kṛṇoti   tam ā rabhasva samidhā yaviṣṭha nṛ cakṣasaḥ cakṣuṣe randhaya enam  
tīkṣṇena agne cakṣuṣā rakṣa yajñam prāñcam vasubhyaḥ pra naya pracetaḥ   hiṃsram rakṣāṃsi abhi śośucānam mā tvā dabhan yātudhānāḥ nṛ cakṣaḥ

tris yātudhānaḥ prasitim te etu ṛtam yaḥ agne anṛtena hanti   tam arciṣā sphūrjayan jātavedaḥ samakṣam enam gṛṇate ni yuṅgdhi  
yat agne adya mithunā śapātaḥ yat vācaḥ tṛṣṭam janayanta rebhāḥ   manyoḥ manasaḥ śaravyā jāyate yā tayā vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān  
parā śṛṇīhi tapasā yātudhānān parā agne rakṣaḥ harasā śṛṇīhi   parā arciṣā mūradevān śṛṇīhi parā asutṛpaḥ śośucataḥ śṛṇīhi  
parā adya devāḥ vṛjinam śṛṇantu pratyak enam śapathāḥ yantu sṛṣṭāḥ   vācā stenam śaravaḥ ṛchantu marman viśvasya etu prasitim yātudhānaḥ  
yaḥ pauruṣeyeṇa kraviṣā samaṅkte yaḥ aśvyena paśunā yātudhānaḥ   yaḥ aghnyāyāḥ bharati kṣīram agne teṣām śīrṣāṇi harasā api vṛśca  
viṣam gavām yātudhānāḥ bharantām ā vṛścantām aditaye durevāḥ   para eṇān devaḥ savitā dadātu parā bhāgam oṣadhīnām jayantām  
saṃvatsarīṇam payaḥ usriyāyāḥ tasya mā aśīt yātudhānaḥ nṛ cakṣaḥ   pīyūṣam agne yatamaḥ titṛpsāt tam pratyañcam arciṣā vidhya marmaṇi  
sanāt agne mṛṇasi yātudhānān na tvā rakṣāṃsi pṛtanāsu jigyuḥ   sahamūrān anu daha kravya adaḥ mā te hetyāḥ mukṣata daivyāyāḥ  
tvam naḥ agne adharāt udaktaḥ tvam paścāt uta rakṣā purastāt   prati tye te ajarāsaḥ tapiṣṭhāḥ agha śaṃsam śośucataḥ dahantu

tat agne cakṣuḥ prati dhehi rebhe śaphārujaḥ yena paśyasi yātudhānān   atharvavat jyotiṣā daivyena satyam dhūrvantam acitam nyoṣa  
pari tvā agne puram vayam vipram sahasya dhīmahi   dhṛṣat varṇam divedive hantāram bhaṅgurāvataḥ  
viṣeṇa bhaṅgurāvataḥ prati sma rakṣasaḥ jahi   agne tigmena śociṣā tapuḥ agrābhiḥ arcibhiḥ  
vi jyotiṣā bṛhatā bhāti agniḥ āvis viśvāni kṛṇute mahitvā   pra adevīḥ māyāḥ sahate durevāḥ śiśīte śṛṅge rakṣobhyaḥ vinikṣe  
ye te śṛṅge ajare jātavedaḥ tigma hetī brahma saṃśite   tābhyām durhārdam abhidāsantam kimīdinam   pratyañcam arciṣā jātavedaḥ vi nikṣva  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
indrāsomā tapatam rakṣaḥ ubjatam ni arpayatam vṛṣaṇā tamaḥ vṛdhaḥ   parā śṛṇītam acitaḥ ni oṣatam hatam nudethām ni śiśītam attriṇaḥ  
indrāsomā sam agha śaṃsam abhi agham tapuḥ yayastu caruḥ agnimān iva   brahma dviṣe kravya ade ghora cakṣase dveṣaḥ dhattam an avāyam kimīdine  
indrāsomāḥ duṣkṛtaḥ vavre antar anārambhaṇe tamasi pra vidhyatam   yatas na eṣām punar ekaḥ cana udayat tat vām astu sahase manyumat śavaḥ  
indrāsomā vartayatam divaḥ vadham sam pṛthivyāḥ agha śaṃsāya tarhaṇam   ud takṣatam svaryam parvatebhyaḥ yena rakṣaḥ vāvṛdhānam nijūrvathaḥ  
indrāsomāḥ vartayatam divaḥ pari agni taptebhiḥ yuvam aśma hanmabhiḥ   tapuḥ vadhebhiḥ ajarebhiḥ attriṇaḥ ni parśāne vidhyatam yantu nisvaram  
indrāsomā pari vām bhūtu viśvatas iyam matiḥ kakṣyā aśvā iva vājinā   yām vām hotrām parihinomi medhayā imā brahmāṇi nṛpatī iva jinvatam  
prati smarethām tujayadbhiḥ evaiḥ hatam druhaḥ rakṣasaḥ bhaṅgurāvataḥ   indrāsomāḥ duṣkṛte mā sugam bhūt yaḥ mā kadā cit abhidāsati druhuḥ  
yaḥ mā pākena manasā carantam abhicaṣṭe anṛtebhiḥ vacobhiḥ   āpaḥ iva kāśinā samgṛbhītāḥ asan astu asataḥ indra vaktā  
ye pāka śaṃsam viharante evaiḥ ye vā bhadram dūṣayanti svadhābhiḥ   ahaye vā tān pradadātu somaḥ ā vā dadhātu nirṛteḥ upaṣṭhe
