paras saḥ astu tanvā tanā ca tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ adhas astu viśvāḥ   prati śuṣyatu yaśaḥ asya devāḥ yaḥ mā divā dipsati yaḥ ca naktam  
su vijñānam cikituṣe janāya sat ca asat ca vacasī paspṛdhāte   tasyoḥ yat satyam yatarat ṛjīyaḥ tat id somaḥ avati hanti asat  
na vai u somaḥ vṛjinam hinoti na kṣatriyam mithuyā dhārayantam   hanti rakṣaḥ hanti āsat vadantam ubhau indrasya prasitau śayāte  
yadi vā aham anṛta devaḥ asmi mogham vā devām apyūhe agne   kim asmabhyam jātavedaḥ hṛṇīṣe drogha vācaḥ te nirṛtham sacantām  
adyā murīya yadi yātudhānaḥ asmi yadi vāyuḥ tatapa puruṣasya   adhā sa vīraiḥ daśabhiḥ vi yūyāḥ yaḥ mā mogham yātudhāna iti āha  
yaḥ mā ayātum yātudhāna iti āha yaḥ vā rakṣāḥ śiciḥ asmi iti āha   indraḥ tam hantu mahatā vadhena viśvasya jantoḥ adhamaḥ padīṣṭa  
pra yā jigāti khargalā iva naktam apa druhuḥ tanvam gūhamānā   vavram anantam ava sā padīṣṭia grāvāṇaḥ ghnantu rakṣasaḥ upabdaiḥ  
vi tiṣṭhadhvam marutaḥ vikṣu ichata gṛbhāyata rakṣasaḥ sam pinaṣṭan   vayaḥ ye bhūtvā patayanti naktabhiḥ ye vā ripaḥ dadhire deve adhvare  
pra vartaya divaḥ aśmānam indra soma śitam maghavan sam śiśādhi   prāktaḥ apāktaḥ adharāt udaktaḥ abhi jahi rakṣasaḥ parvatena  
ete u tye patayanti śva yātavaḥ indram dipsanti dipsavaḥ adābhyam   śiśīte śakraḥ piśunebhyaḥ vadham nunam sṛjat aśanim yātumadbhyaḥ   śiśīte śakraḥ piśunebhyaḥ vadham nunam sṛjat aśanim yātumadbhyaḥ   śiśīte śakraḥ piśunebhyaḥ vadham nunam sṛjat aśanim yātumadbhyaḥ   śiśīte śakraḥ piśunebhyaḥ vadham nunam sṛjat aśanim yātumadbhyaḥ   śiśīte śakraḥ piśunebhyaḥ vadham nunam sṛjat aśanim yātumadbhyaḥ   śiśīte śakr
indraḥ yātūnām abhavat parāśaraḥ havirmathīnām abhi āvivāsatām   abhi id u śakraḥ paraśuḥ yathā vanam pātrā iva bhindan sataḥ etu rakṣasaḥ  
ulūka yātum śuśulūka yātum jahi śva yātum uta koka yātum   suparṇa yātum uta gṛdhra yātum dṛṣadā iva pra mṛṇa rakṣaḥ indra  
mā naḥ rakṣaḥ abhi naṭ yātumāvat apocchantu mithunāḥ ye kimīdinaḥ   pṛthivī naḥ pārthivāt pātu aṃhasaḥ antarikṣam divyāt pātu asmān  
indra jahi pumāṃsam yātudhānam uta striyam māyayā śāśadānām   vigrīvāsaḥ mūradevāḥ ṛdantu mā te dṛśan sūryam uccarantam  
 prati cakṣva vi cakṣva indraḥ ca soma jāgṛtam   rakṣobhyaḥ vadham asyatam aśanim yātumadbhyaḥ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
ayam pratisaraḥ maṇiḥ vīraḥ vīrāya badhyate   vīryavān sapatna hā śūra vīraḥ paripāṇaḥ su maṅgalaḥ  
ayam maṇiḥ sapatna hā su vīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamānaḥ ugraḥ   pratyak kṛtyā dūṣayan eti vīraḥ  
anena indraḥ maṇinā vṛtram ahan anena asurān parābhāvayat manīṣī   anena ajayat dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime anena ajayat pradiśaḥ catasraḥ  
ayam srāktyaḥ maṇiḥ pratīvartaḥ pratisaraḥ   ojasvān vimṛdhaḥ vaśī saḥ asmān pātu sarvatas  
tat agniḥ āha tat u somaḥ āha bṛhaspatiḥ savitā tat indraḥ   te me devāḥ purohitāḥ pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ pratisaraiḥ ajantu  
antar dadhe dyāvāpṛthivī uta ahar uta sūryam   te me devāḥ purohitāḥ pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ pratisaraiḥ ajantu  
ye srāktyam maṇim janāḥ varmāṇi kṛṇvate   sūryaḥ iva divam āruhya vi kṛtyā bādhate vaśī  
srāktyena maṇinā ṛṣiṇā iva manīṣiṇā   ajaiṣam sarvāḥ pṛtanāḥ vi mṛdhaḥ hanmi rakṣasaḥ  
yāḥ kṛtyāḥ āṅgirasīḥ yāḥ kṛtyāḥ āsurīḥ yāḥ   kṛtyāḥ svayaṃkṛtāḥ yāḥ u ca anyebhiḥ ābhṛtāḥ   ubhayīḥ tāḥ parā yantu parāvataḥ navatim nāvyāḥ ati  
asmai maṇim varma badhnantu devāḥ indraḥ viṣṇuḥ savitā rudraḥ agniḥ   prajāpatiḥ parameṣṭhī virāj vaiśvānaraḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca sarve        
uttamaḥ asi oṣadhīnām anaḍvān jagatām iva vyāghraḥ śvapadām iva   yam aichāma avidāma tam pratispāśanam antitam  
saḥ id vyāghraḥ bhavati atha u siṃhaḥ atha u vṛṣā   atha u sapatna karśanaḥ yaḥ bibharti imam maṇim  
na enam ghnanti apsarasaḥ na gandharvāḥ na martyāḥ   sarvāḥ diśaḥ vi rājati yaḥ bibharti imam maṇim  
kaśyapaḥ tvām asṛjata kaśyapaḥ tvā sam airayat   abibhar tvā indraḥ mānuṣe bibhrat saṃśreṣiṇe ajayat   maṇim sahasra vīryam varma devāḥ akṛṇvata  
yaḥ tvā kṛtyābhiḥ yaḥ tvā dīkṣābhiḥ yajñaiḥ yaḥ tvā jighāṃsati   pratyak tvam indra tam jahi vajreṇa śata parvaṇā  
ayam id vai pratīvartaḥ ojasvān saṃjayaḥ maṇiḥ   prajām dhanam ca rakṣatu paripāṇaḥ su maṅgalaḥ  
asapatnam naḥ adharāt asapatnam naḥ uttarāt   indra asapatnam naḥ paścāt jyotiḥ śūra puras kṛdhi  
varma me dyāvāpṛthivī varma ahar varma sūryaḥ   varma me indraḥ ca agniḥ ca varma dhātā dadhātu me  
aindrāgnam varma bahulam yat ugram viśve devāḥ na atividhyanti sarve   tat me tanvam trāyatām sarvatas bṛhat āyuṣmān jaradaṣṭiḥ yathā asāni  
ā mārukṣat deva maṇiḥ mahyāḥ ariṣṭatātaye   imam methim abhisaṃviśadhvam tanūpānam tri varūtham ojase  
asmin indraḥ ni dadhātu nṛmṇam imam devāsaḥ abhisaṃviśadhvam   dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya āyuṣmān jaradaṣṭiḥ yathā asat  
svasti dāḥ viśām patiḥ vṛtra hā vimṛdhaḥ vaśī   indraḥ badhnātu te maṇim jigīvām aparājitaḥ   soma pāḥ abhayaṅkaraḥ vṛṣā   yau te mātā unmamārja jātāyāḥ pati vedanau   durṇāmā tatra mā gṛdhat aliṃśaḥ uta vatsapaḥ  
palāla anupalālau śarkum kokam malimlucam palījakam   āśreṣam vavrivāsasam ṛkṣagrīvam pramīlinam  
mā sam vṛtaḥ mā upa sṛpaḥ ūrū mā ava sṛpaḥ antarā   kṛṇomi asyai bheṣajam bajam durṇāma cātanam  
durṇāmā ca sunāmā ca ubhā samvṛtam ichataḥ   arāyān apa hanmaḥ sunāmā straiṇam ichatām  
yaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ keśī asura stamba jaḥ uta tuṇḍikaḥ   arāyān asyāḥ muṣkābhyām bhaṃsasaḥ apa hanmasi  
anujighram pramṛśantam kravya adam uta reriham   arāyām śvakiṣkiṇaḥ bajaḥ piṅgaḥ anīnaśat  
yaḥ tvā svapne nipadyate bhrātā bhūtvā pitā iva ca   bajaḥ tān sahatām itas klība rūpān tirīṭinaḥ  
yaḥ tvā svapantīm tsarati yaḥ tvā dipsati jāgratīm   chāyām iva pra tān sūryaḥ parikrāman anīnaśat  
yaḥ kṛṇoti mṛta vatsām avatokām imām striyam   tam oṣadhe tvam nāśaya asyāḥ kamalam añjivam  
ye śālāḥ parinṛtyanti sāyam gardabha nādinaḥ   kusūlāḥ ye ca kukṣilāḥ kakubhāḥ karumāḥ srimāḥ   tān oṣadhe tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya     tvam gandhena viṣūcīnā
ye ku kundhāḥ ku kirabhāḥ kṛttīḥ dūrśāni bibhrati   klībāḥ iva pranṛtyantaḥ vane ye kurvate ghoṣam tān itas nāśayāmasi  
ye sūryam na titikṣante ātapantam amum divaḥ   arāyān basta vāsinaḥ durgandhīn lohita āsyān makakān nāśayāmasi  
yaḥ ātmānam atimātram aṃse ādhāya bibhrati   strīṇām śroṇi pratodinaḥ indra rakṣāṃsi nāśaya  
ye pūrve badhvaḥ yanti haste śṛṅgāni bibhrataḥ   āpākesthāḥ prahāsinaḥ stambe ye kurvate jyotiḥ tān itas nāśayāmasi  
yeṣām paścāt prapadāni puras pārṣṇīḥ puras mukhā   khala jāḥ śakadhūma jāḥ uruṇḍāḥ ye ca maṭmaṭāḥ kumbha muṣkāḥ ayāśavaḥ   tān asyāḥ brahmaṇas pate pratībodhena nāśaya  
paryasta akṣāḥ a pracaṅkaśāḥ astraiṇāḥ santu paṇḍagāḥ   ava bheṣaja pādaya yaḥ imām saṃvivṛtsati a patiḥ sva patim striyam  
uddharṣiṇam muni keśam jambhayantam marīmṛśam   upeṣantam udumbalam tuṇḍelam uta śāluḍam   padā pra vidhya pārṣṇyā sthālīm gauḥ iva spandanā  
yaḥ te garbham pratimṛśāt jātam vā mārayāti te   piṅgaḥ tam ugra dhanvā kṛṇotu hṛdayāvidham  
ye amnaḥ jatān mārayanti sūtikāḥ anuśerate   strī bhāgān piṅgaḥ gandharvān vātaḥ abhram iva ajatu  
parisṛṣṭam dharayatu yat dhitam mā ava pādi tat   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvi bhāryau   garbham te ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau
pavīnasāt taṅgalvāt chāyakāt uta nagnakāt   prajāyai patye tvā piṅgaḥ pari pātu kimīdinaḥ  
dvi āsyāt catur akṣāt pañca padāt anaṅgureḥ   vṛntāt abhi prasarpataḥ pari pāhi varīvṛtāt  
ye āmam māṃsam adanti pauruṣeyam ca ye kraviḥ   garbhān khādanti keśavāḥ tān itas nāśayāmasi  
ye sūryāt parisarpanti snuṣā iva śvaśurāt adhi   bajaḥ ca teṣām piṅgaḥ ca hṛdaye adhi ni vidhyatām  
piṅga rakṣa jāyamānam mā pumāṃsam striyam kran   āṇḍa ādaḥ garbhāt mā dabhan bādhasva itas kimīdinaḥ  
aprajāstvam mārtavatsam āt rodam agham āvayam   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye prati muñca tat   vṛkṣāt iva srajam kṛtvā apriye
yāḥ babhravaḥ yāḥ ca śukrāḥ rohiṇīḥ uta pṛśnayaḥ   asiknīḥ kṛṣṇāḥ oṣadhīḥ sarvāḥ achāvadāmasi  
trāyantām imam purusam yakṣmāt deva iṣitāt adhi   yāsām dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā samudraḥ mūlam vīrudhām babhūva  
āpaḥ agram divyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ   tāḥ te yakṣmam enasyam aṅgāt aṅgāt anīnaśan  
prastṛṇatī stambinīḥ eka śuṅgāḥ pratanvatīḥ oṣadhīḥ ā vadāmi   aṃśumatīḥ kaṇḍinīḥ yāḥ viśākhāḥ hvayāmi te vīrudhaḥ vaiśvadevīḥ ugrāḥ puruṣa jīvanīḥ  
yat vaḥ sahaḥ sahamānāḥ vīryam yat ca vaḥ balam   tena imam asmāt yakṣmāt puruṣam muñcata oṣadhīḥ atho kṛṇomi bheṣajam  
jīvalām naghāriṣām jīvantīm oṣadhīm aham   arundhatīm unnayantīm puṣpām madhumatīm iha huve asmai ariṣṭatātaye  
iha ā yantu pracetasaḥ medinīḥ vacasaḥ mama   yathā imam pārayāmasi puruṣam duritāt adhi  
agneḥ ghāsaḥ apām garbhaḥ yāḥ rohanti punarṇavāḥ   dhruvāḥ sahasra nāmnīḥ bheṣajīḥ santu ābhṛtāḥ  
avakā ulbāḥ udaka ātmānaḥ oṣadhayaḥ   vyṛṣantu duritam tīkṣṇa śṛṅgyaḥ  
 unmuñcantīḥ vivaruṇāḥ ugrāḥ yāḥ viṣa dūṣanāḥ   atha u balāsana aśanīḥ kṛtyāḥ dūṣaṇīḥ ca yāḥ tāḥ iha ā yantu oṣadhīḥ                                                                                                        
apakrītāḥ sahīyasīḥ vīrudhaḥ yāḥ abhiṣṭutāḥ   trāyantām asmin grāme gām aśvam puruṣam paśum  
madhumat mūlam madhumat agram āsām madhumat madhyam vīrudhām babhūva   madhumat parṇam madhumat puṣpam āsām madhoḥ sambhaktāḥ amṛtasya bhakṣaḥ ghṛtam annam duhratām go purogavam  
yāvatīḥ kiyatīḥ ca imāḥ pṛthivyām adhi oṣadhīḥ   tāḥ mā sahasra parṇyaḥ mṛtyoḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
vaiyāghraḥ maṇiḥ vīrudhām trāyamānaḥ abhiśasti pāḥ   amīvāḥ sarvāḥ rakṣāṃsi apa hantu adhi dūram asmat  
siṃhasya iva stanathoḥ sam vijante agneḥ iva vijante ābhṛtābhyaḥ   gavām yakṣmaḥ puruṣāṇām vīrudbhiḥ atinuttaḥ nāvyāḥ etu srotyāḥ  
mumucānāḥ oṣadhayaḥ agneḥ vaiśvānarāt adhi   bhūmim saṃtanvatīḥ ita yāsām rājā vanaspatiḥ  
yāḥ rohanti āṅgirasīḥ parvateṣu sameṣu ca   tāḥ naḥ payasvatīḥ śivāḥ oṣadhīḥ santu śam hṛde  
yāḥ ca aham veda vīrudhaḥ yāḥ ca paśyāmi cakṣuṣā   ajñātāḥ jānīmaḥ ca yāḥ yāsu vidma ca saṃbhṛtam  
sarvāḥ samagrāḥ oṣadhīḥ bodhantu vacasaḥ mama   yathā imam pārayāmasi puruṣam duritāt adhi  
aśvatthaḥ darbhaḥ vīrudhām somaḥ rājā amṛtam haviḥ   vrīhiḥ yavaḥ ca bheṣajau divasi putrau amartyau   vrīhiḥ yavaḥ ca bheṣajau divasi putrau amartyau   vrīhiḥ yavaḥ ca bheṣajau divasi putrau amartyau   vrīhiḥ yavaḥ ca bheṣajau divasi putrau amartyau   vrīhiḥ yavaḥ ca bheṣajau divasi putrau amartyau   vrīhiḥ yavaḥ ca bheṣajau divasi putrau amartyau                                               
ud jihīdhve stanayati abhikrandati oṣadhīḥ   yadā vaḥ pṛśni mātaraḥ parjanyaḥ retasāvati  
tasya amṛtasya imam balam puruṣam payayāmasi   atha u kṛṇomi bheṣajam yathā asat śata hāyanaḥ  
varāhaḥ veda vīrudham nakulaḥ veda bheṣajīm   sarpāḥ gandharvāḥ yāḥ viduḥ tāḥ asmai avase huve  
yāḥ suparṇāḥ āṅgirasīḥ divyāḥ yāḥ raghataḥ viduḥ   vayāṃsi haṃsāḥ yāḥ viduḥ yāḥ ca sarve patatriṇaḥ   mṛgāḥ yāḥ viduḥ oṣadhīḥ tāḥ asmai avase huve  
yāvatīnām oṣadhīnām gāvaḥ prāśnanti aghnyāḥ yavatīnām aja avayaḥ   tāvatīḥ tubhyam oṣadhīḥ śarma yacchantu ābhṛtāḥ  
yāvatīṣu manuṣyāḥ bheṣajam bhiṣajaḥ viduḥ   tāvatīḥ viśva bheṣajīḥ ā bharāmi tvām abhi  
puṣpavatīḥ prasūmatīḥ phalinīḥ aphalāḥ uta   saṃmātaraḥ iva duhrām asmai ariṣṭatātaye  
ud tvā ahārṣam pañca śalāt atha u daśa śalāt uta   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt   atha u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt     tvā u yamasya paḍvīśāt viśvasmāt deva kilbiṣāt     tvā
indraḥ manthatu manthitā śakraḥ śūraḥ puraṃdaraḥ   yathā hanāma senāḥ amitrāṇām sahasraśas  
pūti rajjuḥ upadhmānī pūtim senām kṛṇotu amūm   dhūmam agnim parādṛśyā amitrāḥ hṛtsu ā dadhatām bhayam  
amūn aśvattha niḥ śṛṇīhi khāda amūn khadira ajiram   tājat bhaṅgaḥ iva bhajantām hantu enān vadhakaḥ vadhaiḥ  
paruṣān amūn paruṣa āhvaḥ kṛṇotu hantu enān vadhakaḥ vadhaiḥ   kṣipram śaraḥ iva bhajantām bṛhat jālena saṃditāḥ  
antarikṣam jālam āsīt jāla daṇḍāḥ diśaḥ mahīḥ   tena abhidhāya dasyūnām śakraḥ senām apāvapat  
bṛhat hi jālam bṛhataḥ śakrasya vājinīvataḥ   tena śatrūn abhi sarvān ni ubja yathā na mucyātai katamaḥ cana eṣām  
bṛhat te jālam bṛhataḥ indra śūra sahasra arghasya śata vīryasya   tena śatam sahasram ayutam nyarbudam jaghāna śakraḥ dasyūnām abhidhāya senayā  
ayam lokaḥ jālam āsīt śakrasya mahataḥ mahān   tena aham indra jālena amūn tamasā abhi dadhāmi sarvān  
sediḥ ugrā vyṛddhiḥ ārtiḥ ca anapavācanā   śramaḥ tandrīḥ ca mohaḥ ca taiḥ amūn abhi dadhāmi sarvān  
mṛtyave amūn pra yacchāmi mṛtyu pāśaiḥ amī sitāḥ   mṛtyoḥ ye aghalāḥ dūtāḥ tebhyaḥ enān prati nayāmi baddhvā       tebhyaḥ enān prati nayāmi baddhvā                                     tebhyaḥ enān prati nayāmi baddhvā                   tebhyaḥ enān prati nayāmi baddhvā                     tebhyaḥ enān prati nayāmi baddhvā                              
nayata amūn mṛtyu dūtāḥ yama dūtāḥ apombhata   paraḥsahasrā hanyantām tṛṇa īḍhu enān matyam bhavasya  
sādhyāḥ ekam jāla daṇḍam udyatya yanti ojasā   rudrāḥ ekam vasavaḥ ekam ādityaiḥ ekaḥ udyataḥ  
viśve devāḥ upariṣṭāt ubjantaḥ yantu ojasā   madhyena ghnantaḥ yantu senām aṅgirasaḥ mahīm  
vanaspatīn vānaspatyān oṣadhīḥ uta vīrudhaḥ   dvipād catuṣpād iṣṇāmi yathā senām amūm hanan  
gandharva apsarasaḥ sarpān devān puṇyajanān pitṝn   dṛṣṭān adṛṣṭān iṣṇāmi yathā senām amūm hanan  
ime uptāḥ mṛtyu pāśāḥ yān ākramya na mucyase   amuṣyāḥ hantu senāyāḥ idam kūṭam sahasraśas  
gharmaḥ samiddhaḥ agninā ayam homaḥ sahasrahaḥ   bhavaḥ ca pṛśni bāhuḥ ca śarva senām amūm hatam  
mṛtyoḥ āṣam ā padyantām kṣudham sedim vadham bhayam   indraḥ ca akṣu jālābhyām śarva senām amūm hatam  
parājitāḥ pra trasata amitrāḥ nuttāḥ dhāvata brahmaṇā   bṛhaspati pranuttānām mā amīṣām moci kaḥ cana  
ava padyantām eṣām āyudhāni mā śakan pratidhām iṣum   atha eṣām bahu bibhyatām iṣavaḥ ghnantu marmaṇi  
sam krośatām enān dyāvāpṛthivī sam antarikṣam saha devatābhiḥ   mā jñātāram mā pratiṣṭhām vidanta mithas vighnānāḥ upa yantu mṛtyum  
diśaḥ catasraḥ aśvataryaḥ deva rathasya purodāśāḥ śaphāḥ antarikṣam uddhiḥ   dyāvāpṛthivī pakṣasī ṛtavaḥ abhīśavaḥ antardeśāḥ kimkarā vāc parirathyam  
saṃvatsaraḥ rathaḥ parivatsaraḥ rathopasthaḥ virāj īṣā agniḥ ratha mukham   indraḥ savyaṣṭhāḥ candramāḥ sārathiḥ  
itas jaya itas vi jaya sam jaya jaya svāhā   ime jayantu parā amī jayantām svāhā ebhyaḥ durāhāḥ amībhyaḥ   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlalohitena amūn abhyavatanomi   nīlal
kutas tau jātau katamaḥ saḥ ardhaḥ kasmāt lokāt katamasyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ   vatsau virājaḥ salilāt ud ā etām tau tvā pṛchāmi katareṇa dugdhā  
yaḥ akrandayat salilam mahitvā yonim kṛtvā tri bhujam śayānaḥ   vatsaḥ kāmadughaḥ virājaḥ sa guhā cakre tanvaḥ parācais  
yāni trīṇi bṛhanti yeṣām caturtham viyunakti vācam   brahma enat vidyāt tapasā vipaścit yasmin ekam yujyate yasmin ekam  
bṛhataḥ pari sāmāni ṣaṣṭhāt pañca adhi nirmitā   bṛhat bṛhatyāḥ nirmitam kutas adhi bṛhatī mitā  
bṛhatī pari mātrāyāḥ mātuḥ mātrā adhi nirmitā   māyā ha jajñe māyāyāḥ māyāyāḥ mātalī pari  
vaiśvānarasya pratimā upari dyauḥ yāvat rodasī vibabādhe agniḥ   tatas ṣaṣṭhāt ā amutas yanti stomāḥ ud itas yanti abhi ṣaṣṭham ahnaḥ  
ṣaṭ tvā pṛchāmaḥ ṛṣayaḥ kaśyapa ime tvam hi yuktam yuyukṣe yogyam ca   virājam āhuḥ brahmaṇaḥ pitaram tām naḥ vi dhehi yatidhā sakhibhyaḥ  
yām pracyutām anu yajñāḥ pracyavantaḥ upatiṣṭhante upatiṣṭhamānām   yasyāḥ vrate prasave yakṣam ejati sā virāj ṛṣayaḥ parame vyoman  
a prāṇaiti prāṇena prāṇatīnām virāj svarājam abhi eti paścāt   viśvam mṛśantīm abhirūpām virājam paśyanti tve na tve paśyanti enām  
kaḥ virājaḥ mithuna tvam pra veda kaḥ ṛtūn kaḥ u kalpam asyāḥ   kramān kaḥ asyāḥ katidhā vidugdhān kaḥ asyāḥ dhāma katidhā vyuṣṭīḥ                                                                                                                                                                            
iyam eva sā yā prathamā vyauchat āsu itarāsu carati praviṣṭā   mahāntaḥ asyām mahimānaḥ antar vadhūḥ jigāya navagat janitrī  
chandaḥ pakṣe uṣasā pepiśāne samānam yonim anu sam careme   sūrya patnī sam carataḥ prajānatī ketumatī ajare bhūri retasā  
ṛtasya panthām anu tisraḥ āguḥ trayaḥ gharmāḥ anu retaḥ āguḥ   prajām ekā jinvati ūrjam ekā rāṣṭram ekā rakṣati devayūnām  
agnīṣomau adadhuḥ yā turīyā āsīt yajñasya pakṣau ṛṣayaḥ kalpayantaḥ   gāyatrīm triṣṭubham jagatīm anuṣṭubham bṛhat arkīm yajamānāya svar ābharantīm  
pañca vyuṣṭīḥ anu pañca dohāḥ gām pañca nāmnīm ṛtavaḥ anu pañca   pañca diśaḥ pañcadaśena kḷptāḥ tāḥ eka mūrdhnīḥ abhi lokam ekam  
ṣaṭ jātāḥ bhūtā prathama jāḥ ṛtasya ṣaṭ u sāmāni ṣaṭ aham vahanti   ṣaṣ yogam sīram anu sāmasāma ṣaṭ āhuḥ dyāvāpṛthivīḥ ṣaṭ urvīḥ  
ṣaṭ āhuḥ śītān ṣaṭ u māsaḥ uṣṇān ṛtum naḥ brūta yatamaḥ atiriktaḥ   sapta suparṇāḥ kavayaḥ ni seduḥ sapta chandāṃsi anu sapta dīkṣāḥ  
sapta homāḥ samidhaḥ ha sapta madhūni sapta ṛtavaḥ ha sapta   sapta ājyāni pari bhūtam āyan tāḥ sapta gṛdhrāḥ iti śuśruma vayam  
sapta chandāṃsi catur uttarāṇi anyaḥ anyasmin adhi ārpitāni   katham stomāḥ prati tiṣṭhanti teṣu tāni stomeṣu katham ārpitāni  
 trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭubh katham ekaviṃśaḥ   traya
aṣṭa jātāḥ bhūtā prathama jāḥ ṛtasya aṣṭa indraḥ ṛtvijaḥ daivyāḥ ye  aṣṭa yoniḥ aditiḥ aṣṭa putra astamīm rātrim abhi havyam eti  
ittham śreyaḥ manyamānā idam āgamam yuṣmākam sakhye aham asmi śevā   samāna janmā kratuḥ asti vaḥ śivaḥ sa vaḥ sarvāḥ sam carati prajānan  
aṣṭa indrasya ṣaṭ yamasya ṛṣīṇām sapta saptadhā   apaḥ manuṣyān oṣadhīḥ tām u pañca anu secire  
kevalī indrāya duduhe hi gṛṣṭiḥ vaśam pīyūṣam prathamam duhānā   atha atarpayat caturaḥ caturdhā devān manuṣyān asurān uta ṛṣīn  
kaḥ nu gauḥ kaḥ eka ṛṣiḥ kim u dhāma kāḥ āśiṣaḥ   yakṣam pṛthivyām ekavṛt eka ṛtuḥ katamaḥ nu saḥ  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
virāj vai idam agre āsīt tasyāḥ jātāyāḥ sarvam abibhet iyam eva idam bhaviṣyati iti 
sā ud akrāmat sā gārhapatye ni akrāmat   gṛhamedhī gṛhapatiḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā āhavanīye ni akrāmat   yanti asya devāḥ deva hūtim priyaḥ devānām bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā dakṣiṇāgnau ni akrāmat   yajña ṛtaḥ dakṣiṇīyaḥ vāsateyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā sabhāyām ni akrāmat   yanti asya sabhām sabhyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā samitau ni akrāmat   yanti asya samitim sāmityaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā āmantraṇe ni akrāmat   yanti asya āmantraṇam āmantraṇīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda                
sā ud akrāmat sā antarikṣe caturdhā vikrāntā atiṣṭhat 
tām deva manuṣyāḥ abruvan iyam eva tat veda yat ubhayaḥ upajīvema imām upa hvayāmahai iti 
tām upāhvayanta 
ūrjaḥ ehi svadhaḥ ehi sūnṛte ehi irāvatī ehi iti 
tasyāḥ indraḥ vatsaḥ āsīt gāyatrī abhidhānī abhram ūdhar 
bṛhat ca rathaṃtaram ca dvau stanau āstām yajñāyajñiyam ca vāmadevyam ca dvau 
oṣadhīḥ eva rathaṃtareṇa devāḥ aduhran vyacaḥ bṛhatā 
apaḥ vāmadevyena yajñam yajñāyajñiyena 
oṣadhīḥ eva asmai rathaṃtaram duhe vyacaḥ bṛhat 
 apaḥ vāmadevyam yajñam yajñāyajñiyam ya veda         śatru vāmadevyam yajñam yajñāyajñiyam ya veda          śatru vāmadevyam yajñam yajñāyajñiyam ya veda          śatru śatru vāmadevyam yajñam yajñāyajñiyam ya veda                                                                                                                                                                                    
sā ud akrāmat sā vanaspatīn āgacchat tām vanaspatayaḥ aghnata sā saṃvatsare sam abhavat   tasmāt vanaspatīnām saṃvatsare vṛkṇam api rohati vṛścate asya apriyaḥ bhrātṛvyaḥ yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā pitṝn āgacchat tām pitaraḥ aghnata sā māsi sam abhavat   tasmāt pitṛbhyaḥ māsi upamāsyam dadati pra pitṛyāṇam panthām jānāti yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā devān āgacchat tām devāḥ aghnata sā ardha māse sam abhavat   tasmāt devebhyaḥ ardha māse vaṣaṭ kurvanti pra deva yānam panthām jānāti yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā manuṣyān āgacchat tām manuṣyāḥ aghnata sā sadyas sam abhavat   tasmāt manuṣyebhyaḥ ubhayadyus upa haranti upa asya gṛhe haranti yaḥ evam veda   tasmāt manuṣyebhyaḥ ubhayadyus upa haranti upa asya gṛhe haranti yaḥ evam veda   tasmāt manuṣyebhyaḥ ubhayadyus upa haranti upa asya gṛhe haranti yaḥ evam veda   tasmāt manuṣyebhyaḥ ubhayadyus upa haranti upa asya gṛhe haranti yaḥ evam veda   tasmāt manuṣyebhyaḥ ubhayadyus upa haranti upa 
sā ud akrāmat sā asurān āgacchat tām asurāḥ upāhvayanta māyaḥ ehi iti   tasyāḥ virocanaḥ prāhrādiḥ vatsaḥ āsīt ayaspātram pātram   tām dvi mūrdhā ārtvyaḥ adhok tām māyām eva adhok  
tām māyām asurāḥ upa jīvanti upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda 
sā ud akrāmat sā pitṝn āgacchat tām pitaraḥ upāhvayanta svadhaḥ ehi iti   tasyāḥ yamaḥ rājā vatsaḥ āsīt rajata pātram pātram   tām antakaḥ mārtyavaḥ adhok tām svadhām eva adhok   tām svadhām pitaraḥ upa jīvanti upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā manuṣyān āgacchat tām manuṣyāḥ upāhvayanterāvatī ehi iti   tasyāḥ manuḥ vaivasvataḥ vatsaḥ āsīt pṛthivī pātram   tām pṛthī vainyaḥ adhok tām kṛṣim ca sasyam ca adhok   te svadhām kṛṣim ca sasyam ca manuṣyāḥ upa jīvanti kṛṣṭa rādhiḥ upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā sapta ṛṣīn āgacchat tām sapta ṛṣayaḥ upāhvayanta brahmaṇvatī ehi iti   tasyāḥ somaḥ rājā vatsaḥ āsīt chandaḥ pātram   tām bṛhaspatiḥ āṅgirasaḥ adhok tām brahma ca tapaḥ ca adhok   tat brahma ca tapaḥ ca sapta ṛṣayaḥ upa jīvanti brahmavarcasī upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā devān āgacchat tām devāḥ upāhvayanta ūrjaḥ ehi iti   tasyāḥ indraḥ vatsaḥ āsīt camasaḥ pātram   tām devaḥ savitā adhok tām ūrjām eva adhok   tām ūrjām devāḥ upa jīvanti upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā gandharva apsarasaḥ āgacchat tām gandharva apsarasaḥ upāhvayanta puṇya gandhaḥ ehi iti   tasyāḥ citrarathaḥ saurya varcasaḥ vatsaḥ āsīt puṣkara parṇam pātram   tām vasu ruciḥ saurya varcasaḥ adhok tām puṇyam eva gandham adhok   tam puṇyam gandham gandharva apsarasaḥ upa jīvanti puṇya gandhiḥ upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā itarajanān āgacchat tām itarajanāḥ upāhvayanta tirodhaḥ ehi iti   tasyāḥ kuberaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ vatsaḥ āsīt āma pātram pātram   tām rajata nābhiḥ kaberakaḥ adhok tām tirodhām eva adhok   tām tirodhām a tirajanā pitaraḥ upa jīvanti tiras dhatte sarvam pāpmānam upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda  
sā ud akrāmat sā sarpān āgacchat tām sarpāḥ upāhvayanta viṣavatī ehi iti   tasyāḥ takṣakaḥ vaiśaleyaḥ vatsaḥ āsīt alābu pātram pātram   tām dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ airāvataḥ adhok tām viṣam eva adhok   tat viṣam sarvāḥ upa jīvanti upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda     tat viṣam sarvāḥ upa jīvanti upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda     tat viṣam sarvāḥ upa jīvanti upajīvanīyaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda     tat viṣam sarvāḥ upa
tat yasmai evam viduṣe alābunā abhiṣiñcet pratyāhanyāt 
na ca pratyāhanyāt manasā tvā pratyāhanmi iti pratyāhanyāt 
yat pratyāhanti viṣam eva tat pratyāhanti 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ antarikṣāt samudrāt agneḥ vātāt madhukaśāḥ hi jajñe   tām cāyitvā amṛtam vasānām hṛdbhiḥ prajāḥ prati nandanti sarvāḥ  
mahat payaḥ viśva rūpam asyāḥ samudrasya tvota retaḥ āhuḥ   yatas aiti madhukaśā rarāṇā tat prāṇaḥ tat amṛtam niviṣṭam  
paśyanti asyāḥ caritam pṛthivyām pṛthak naraḥ bahudhā mīmāṃsamānāḥ   agneḥ vātāt madhukaśāḥ hi jajñe marutām ugrā naptiḥ  
mātā ādityānām duhitā vasūnām prāṇaḥ prajānām amṛtasya nābhiḥ   hiraṇya varṇā madhu kaśā ghṛtācī mahān bhargaḥ carati martyeṣu  
madhoḥ kaśām ajanayanta devāḥ tasyāḥ garbhaḥ abhavat viśva rūpaḥ   tam jātam taruṇam piparti mātā sa jātaḥ viśvā bhuvanā vi caṣṭe  
kaḥ tam pra veda kaḥ u tam ciketa yaḥ asyāḥ hṛdaḥ kalaśaḥ soma dhānaḥ akṣitaḥ   brahmā sumedhāḥ saḥ asmin madeta  
sa tau pra veda saḥ u tau ciketa yau asyāḥ stanau sahasra dhārau akṣitau   ūrjam duhāte an apasphurantau  
hiṅkarikratī bṛhatī vayodhāḥ uccairghoṣā abhyeti yā vratam   trīn gharmān abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyum payate payobhiḥ  
yām āpīnām upasīdanti āpaḥ śākvarāḥ vṛṣabhāḥ ye svarājaḥ   te varṣanti te varṣayanti tat vide kāmam ūrjam āpaḥ  
stanayitnuḥ te vāc prajāpate vṛṣā śuṣmam kṣipasi bhūmyām adhi   agneḥ vātāt madhu kaśā hi jajñe marutām ugrā naptiḥ     
yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane aśvinoḥ bhavati priyaḥ   eva me aśvinā varcaḥ ātmani dhriyatām  
yathā somaḥ dvitīye savane indra agnyoḥ bhavati priyaḥ   eva me indra agnī varcaḥ ātmani dhriyatām  
yathā somaḥ tṛtīye savane ṛbhūṇām bhavati priyaḥ   eva me ṛbhavaḥ varcaḥ ātmani dhriyatām  
madhu janiṣīya madhu vaṃsiṣīya   payasvān agne āgamam tam mā sam sṛja varcasā  
sam mā agne varcasā sṛja sam prajayā sam āyuṣā   vidyuḥ me asya devāḥ indraḥ vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ  
yathā madhu madhukṛtaḥ saṃbharanti madhau adhi   eva me aśvinā varcaḥ ātmani dhriyatām  
yathā makṣāḥ idam madhu nyañjanti madhau adhi   eva me aśvinā varcaḥ tejaḥ balam ojaḥ ca dhriyatām  
yat giriṣu parvateṣu goṣu aśveṣu yat madhu   surāyām sicyamānāyām yat tatra madhu tat mayi  
aśvinā sāragheṇa mā madhunā aṅktam śubhaḥ patī   yathā varcasvatīm vācam āvadāni janām anu  
stanayitnuḥ te vāc prajāpate vṛṣā śuṣmam kṣipasi bhūmyām divi   tām paśavaḥ upa jīvanti sarve tena u seṣam ūrjam piparti  
pṛthivī daṇḍaḥ antarikṣam garbhaḥ dyauḥ kaśā vidyut prakaśaḥ hiraṇyayaḥ binduḥ 
yaḥ vai kaśāyāḥ sapta madhūni veda madhumān bhavati   brāhmaṇaḥ ca rājā ca dhenuḥ ca anaḍvān ca vrīhiḥ ca yavaḥ ca madhu saptamam  
madhumān bhavati madhumat asya āhāryam bhavati   madhumataḥ lokān jayati yaḥ evam veda  
 yat vīdhre stanayati prajāpatiḥ eva tat prajābhyaḥ prādur bhavati   tasmāt prācīnopavītaḥ tiṣṭhe prajāpate anu mā budhyasva iti   anu enam prajāḥ anu prajāpatiḥ budhyate yaḥ evam veda     tasmāt prācīnopavītaḥ tiṣṭhe prajāpate anu mā budhyasva iti   anu enam prajāḥ anu prajāpatiḥ budhyate yaḥ evam veda     taḥ evam veda     tat evam veda     tat evam veda     tat evam veda     tat evam veda     tat evam veda     tat evam veda     tat 
sapatna hanam ṛṣabham ghṛtena kāmam śikṣāmi haviṣā ājyena   nīcais sapatnān mama padaya tvam abhiṣṭutaḥ mahatā vīryeṇa  
yat me manasaḥ na priyam cakṣuṣaḥ yat me babhasti na abhinandati   tat duṣvapnyam prati muñcāmi sapatne kāmam stutvā ud aham bhideyam  
duṣvapnyam kāma duritam ca kama aprajastām asvagatām avartim   ugraḥ īśānaḥ prati muñca tasmin yaḥ asmabhyam aṃhūraṇā cikitsāt  
nudasva kāma pra nudasva kāma āvartim yantu mama ye sapatnāḥ   teṣām nuttānām adhamā tamāṃsi agne vāstūni niḥ daha tvam  
sā te kāma duhitā dhenuḥ ucyate yām āhuḥ vācam kavayaḥ virājam   tayā sapatnān pari vṛṅgdhi ye mama pari enān prāṇaḥ paśavaḥ jīvanam vṛṇaktu  
kāmasya indrasya varuṇasya rājñaḥ viṣṇoḥ balena savituḥ savena   agneḥ hotreṇa pra nude sapatnām chambī iva nāvam udakeṣu dhīraḥ  
adhyakṣaḥ vājī mama kāmaḥ ugraḥ kṛṇotu mahyam asapatnam eva   viśve devāḥ mama nātham bhavantu sarve devāḥ havam ā yantu me imam  
idam ājyam ghṛtavat juṣāṇāḥ kāma jyeṣṭhāḥ iha mādayadhvam   kṛṇvantaḥ mahyam asapatnam eva  
indra agnī kāma sa ratham hi bhūtvā nīcais sapatnān mama pādayāthaḥ   teṣām pannānām adhamā tamāṃsi agne vāstūni anunirdaha tvam  
jahi tvam kāma mama ye sapatnāḥ andhā tamāṃsi ava pādaya enān   nirindriyāḥ arasāḥ santu sarve mā te jīviṣuḥ katamat cana ahar                                            santu sarve mā te jīviṣuḥ katamat cana ahar      
avadhīt kāmaḥ mama ye sapatnāḥ urum lokam akarat mahyam edhatum   mahyam namantām pradiśaḥ catasraḥ mahyam ṣaṭ urvīḥ ghṛtam ā vahantu  
te adharāñcaḥ pra plavantām chinnā nauḥ iva bandhanāt   na sāyaka praṇuttānām punar asti nivartanam  
agniḥ yavaḥ indraḥ yavaḥ somaḥ yavaḥ   yava yāvānaḥ devāḥ yavayantu enam  
a sarva vīraḥ caratu praṇuttaḥ dveṣyaḥ mitrānām parivargyaḥ svānām   uta pṛthivyām ava syanti vidyutaḥ ugraḥ vaḥ devaḥ pra mṛṇat sapatnān  
cyutā ca iyam bṛhatī acyutā ca vidyut bibharti stanayitnūn ca sarvān   udyan ādityaḥ draviṇena tejasā nīcais sapatnān nudatām me sahasvān  
yat te kāma śarma tri varūtham udbhu brahma varma vitatam an ativyādhyam kṛtam   tena sapatnān pari vṛṅgdhi ye mama pari enān prāṇaḥ paśavaḥ jīvanam vṛṇaktu  
yena devāḥ asurān prāṇudanta yena indraḥ dasyūn adhamam tamaḥ nināya   tena tvam kāma mama ye sapatnāḥ tān asmāt lokāt pra nudasva dūram  
yathā devāḥ asurān prāṇudanta yathā indraḥ dasyūn adhamam tamaḥ babādhe   tathā tvam kāma mama ye sapatnāḥ tān asmāt lokāt pra nudasva dūram  
kāmaḥ jajñe prathamaḥ na enam devāḥ āpuḥ pitaraḥ na martyāḥ   tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahān tasmai te kāma namaḥ id kṛnomi  
yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī varimṇā yāvat āpaḥ siṣyaduḥ yāvat agniḥ   tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahān tasmai te kāma namaḥ id kṛṇomi   tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahān tasmai te kāma namaḥ id kṛṇomi   tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahān tasmai te kāma namaḥ id kṛṇomi   tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahān tasmai te kāma namaḥ id kṛṇomi   tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahān tasmai te kāma namaḥ id kṛṇomi   tatas tvam a

yā dvi pakṣā catuṣpakṣā ṣaṣ pakṣā yā nimīyate   aṣṭāpakṣām daśa pakṣām śālām mānasya patnīm agniḥ garbhaḥ iva ā śaye  
pratīcīm tvā pratīcīnaḥ śāle praimi a hiṃsatīm   agniḥ hi antar āpaḥ ca ṛtasya prathamāḥ dvār  
imāḥ āpaḥ pra bharāmi a yakṣmāḥ yakṣma nāśanīḥ   gṛhān upa pra sīdāmi amṛtena saha agninā  
mā naḥ pāśam prati mucaḥ guruḥ bhāraḥ laghuḥ bhava   vadhūm iva tvā śāle yatrakāmam bharāmasi  
prācyāḥ diśaḥ śālāyāḥ namaḥ mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ śālāyāḥ namaḥ mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ śālāyāḥ namaḥ mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ

sāhasraḥ tveṣaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ payasvān viśvā rūpāṇi vakṣaṇāsu bibhrat   bhadram dātre yajamānāya śīkṣan bārhaspatyaḥ usriyaḥ tantum ātān  
apām yaḥ agne pratimā babhūva prabhūḥ sarvasmai pṛthivī iva devī   pitā vatsānām patiḥ aghnyānām sāhasre poṣe api naḥ kṛṇotu  
pumān antarvān sthaviraḥ payasvān vasoḥ kabandham ṛṣabhaḥ bibharti   tam indrāya pathibhiḥ deva yānaiḥ hutam agniḥ vahatu jātavedāḥ  
pitā vatsānām patiḥ aghnyānām atho pitā mahatām gargarāṇām   vatsaḥ jarāyu pratidhuk pīyūṣaḥ āmikṣā ghṛtam tat u asya retaḥ  
devānām bhāgaḥ upanāhaḥ eṣaḥ apām rasaḥ oṣadhīnām ghṛtasya   somasya bhakṣam avṛṇīta śakraḥ bṛhan adriḥ abhavat yat śarīram  
somena pūrṇam kalaśam bibharṣi tvastā rupāṇām janitā paśūnām   śivāḥ te santu prajanvaḥ iha yāḥ imāḥ ni asmabhyam svadhite yaccha yāḥ amūḥ  
ājam bibharti ghṛtam asya retaḥ sāhasraḥ poṣaḥ tam u yajñam āhuḥ   indrasya rūpam ṛṣabhaḥ vasānaḥ saḥ asmān devāḥ śiva aitu dattaḥ  
indrasya ojaḥ varuṇasya bāhū aśvinoḥ aṃsau marutām iyam kakud   bṛhaspatim saṃbhṛtam etam āhuḥ ye dhīrāsaḥ kavayaḥ ye manīṣiṇaḥ  
daivīḥ viśaḥ payasvān ā tanoṣi tvām indram tvām sarasvantam āhuḥ   sahasram saḥ eka mukhā dadāti yaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ ṛṣabham ājuhoti  
bṛhaspatiḥ savitā te vayaḥ dadhau tvaṣṭuḥ vāyoḥ pari ātmā te ābhṛtaḥ   antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiḥ te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām     tvā   antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiḥ te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām     tvā   antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiḥ te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām   tvā   antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiḥ te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām   tvā   antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiḥ te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām
yaḥ indraḥ iva deveṣu goṣu eti vivāvadat   tasya ṛṣabhasya aṅgāni brahmā sam stautu bhadrayā  
pārśve āstām anumatyā bhagasya āstām anūvṛjau   aṣṭhīvantau abravīt mitraḥ mama etau kevalau iti  
bhasat āsīt ādityānām śroṇī āstām bṛhaspateḥ   pucham vātasya devasya tena dhūnoti oṣadhīḥ  
gudāḥ āsan sinīvālyāḥ sūryāyāḥ tvacam abruvan   utthātuḥ abruvan pade ṛṣabham yat akalpayan  
kroḍaḥ āsīt jāmiśaṃsasya somasya klaśaḥ dhṛtaḥ   devāḥ saṃgatya yat sarve ṛṣabham vyakalpayan  
te kuṣṭhikāḥ saramāyai kurmebhyaḥ adadhuḥ śaphān   ūbadhyam asya kītebhyaḥ śva vartebhyaḥ adhārayan  
śṛṅgābhyām rakṣaḥ ṛṣati avartim hanti cakṣuṣā   śṛṇoti bhadram karṇābhyām gavām yaḥ patiḥ aghnyaḥ  
śata yājam sa yajate na enam dunvanti agnayaḥ   jinvanti viśve tam devāḥ yaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ ṛṣabham ājuhoti  
brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ṛṣabham dattvā varīyaḥ kṛṇute manaḥ   puṣṭim saḥ aghnyānām sve goṣṭhe ava paśyate  
gāvaḥ santu prajāḥ santu atha u astu tanū balam   tat sarvam anu manyantām devāḥ ṛṣabha dāyine  
ayam pipānaḥ indraḥ id rayim dadhātu cetanīm   ayam dhenum su dughām nitya vatsām vaśam duhām vipaścitam paras divaḥ  
piśaṅga rūpaḥ nabhasaḥ vayodhāḥ aindraḥ śuṣmaḥ viśva rūpaḥ naḥ āgan   āyuḥ asmabhyam dadhat prajām ca rāyaḥ ca poṣaiḥ abhi naḥ sacatām  
upa iha upaparcana asmin goṣṭhe upa pṛñca naḥ   upa ṛṣabhasya yat retaḥ upa indra tava vīryam

ā naya etam ā rabhasva su kṛtām lokam api gacchatu prajānan   tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā mahānti ajaḥ nākam ā kramatām tṛtīyam  
indrāya bhāgam pari tvā nayāmi asmin yajñe yajamānāya sūrim   ye naḥ dviṣanti anu tān rabhasva anāgasaḥ yajamānasya vīrāḥ  
pra padaḥ ava nenigdhi duścaritam yat cacāra śuddhaiḥ śaphaiḥ ā kramatām prajānan   tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā vipaśyan ajaḥ nākam ā kramatām tṛtīyam  
anuchya śyāmena tvacam etām viśastar yathā paru asinā mā abhi maṃsthāḥ   mā abhi druhaḥ paruśas kalpaya enam tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śraya enam  
ṛcā kumbhīm adhi agnau śrayāmi ā siñca udakam ava dhehi enam   paryādhatta agninā śamitāraḥ śṛtaḥ gacchatu su kṛtām yatra lokaḥ  
ud krāma atas pari ced a taptaḥ taptāt caroḥ adhi nākam tṛtīyam   agneḥ agniḥ adhi sam babhūvitha jyotiṣmantam abhi lokam jaya etam  
ajaḥ agniḥ ajam u jyotiḥ āhuḥ ajam jīvatā brahmaṇe deyam āhuḥ   ajaḥ tamāṃsi apa hanti dūram asmin loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ  
pañca odanaḥ pañcadhā vi kramatām ākraṃsyamānaḥ trīṇi jyotīṃṣi   ījānānām su kṛtām prehi madhyam tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva  
ajā roha su kṛtām yatra lokaḥ śarabhaḥ na cattaḥ ati durgāni eṣaḥ   pañca odanaḥ brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ sa dātāram tṛptyā tarpayāti  
ajaḥ tri nāke tridive tri pṛṣṭhe nākasya pṛṣṭhe dadivāṃsam dadhāti   pañca odanaḥ brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ viśva rūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughā asi ekā     pañca odanaḥ brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ viśva rūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughā asi ekā     pañca odanaḥ brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ viśva rūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughā asi ekā     tri  dīyamānaḥ viśva rūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughāḥ asi
etat vaḥ jyotiḥ pitaraḥ tṛtīyam pañca odanam brahmaṇe ajam dadāti   ajaḥ tamāṃsi apa hanti dūram asmin loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ  
ījānānām su kṛtām lokam īpsan pañca odanam brahmaṇe ajam dadāti   sa vyāptim abhi lokam jaya etam śivaḥ asmabhyam pratigṛhītaḥ astu  
ajaḥ hi agneḥ ajaniṣṭa śokāt vipraḥ viprasya sahasaḥ vipaścit   iṣṭam pūrtam abhipūrtam vaṣaṭkṛtam tat devāḥ ṛtuśas kalpayantu  
amotam vāsaḥ dadyāt hiraṇyam api dakṣiṇām   tathā lokān sam āpnoti ye divyāḥ ye ca pārthivāḥ  
etāḥ tvā ajāḥ upa yantu dhārāḥ somyāḥ devīḥ ghṛta pṛṣṭhāḥ madhuścutaḥ   stabhān pṛthivīm uta dyām nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi sapta raśmau  
ajaḥ asi aja svargaḥ asi tvayā lokam aṅgirasaḥ prājānan   tam lokam puṇyam pra jñeṣam

satyam ca rtam ca cakṣuṣī viśvam satyam śraddhā prāṇaḥ virāj śiraḥ   eṣa vai aparimitaḥ yajñaḥ yat ajaḥ pañca odanaḥ  
aparimitam eva yajñam āpnoti aparimitam lokam ava runddhe   yaḥ ajam pañca odanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣam dadāti  
na asya asthīni bhindyāt na majjñaḥ niḥ dhayet   sarvam enam samādāya idam idam pra veśayet

pañca rukmā pañca navāni vastrā pañca asmai dhenavaḥ kāmadughāḥ bhavanti   yaḥ ajam pañca odanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣam dadāti  
pañca rukmāḥ jyotiḥ asmai bhavanti varma vāsāṃsi tanve bhavanti   svargam lokam aśnute yaḥ ajam pañca odanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣam dadāti  
yā pūrvam patim vittvā atha anyam vindate aparam   pañca odanam ca tau ajam dadātaḥ na vi yoṣataḥ

anupūrva vatsām dhenum anaḍvāham upabarhaṇam   vāsaḥ hiraṇyam dattvā te yanti divam uttamām  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
yaḥ vai naidāgham nāma rtum veda   eṣa vai naidāghaḥ nāma rtuḥ yat ajaḥ pañca odanaḥ   niḥ eva apriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyam dahati bhavati ātmanā   yaḥ vai kurvantam nāma rtum veda   kurvatīm kurvatīm eva apriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyam ā datte   eṣa vai kurvat nāma rtuḥ yat ajaḥ pañca odanaḥ   yaḥ vai saṃyantam nāma rtum veda   saṃyatīm saṃyatīm eva apriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyam ā datte   eṣa vai saṃyat nāma rtuḥ yat ajaḥ pañca

yat vai atithi patiḥ atithīn pratipaśyati devayajanam prekṣate 
yat abhivadati dīkṣām upaiti yat udakam yācati apaḥ pra nayati 
yāḥ eva yajñe āpaḥ praṇīyante tāḥ eva tāḥ  
yat tarpaṇam āharanti yaḥ eva agnīṣomīyaḥ paśuḥ badhyate saḥ eva saḥ

yat upastṛṇanti barhiḥ eva tat

iṣṭam ca vai eṣa pūrtam ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvaḥ atitheḥ aśnāti  
payaḥ ca vai eṣa rasam ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvaḥ atitheḥ aśnāti  
ūrjām ca vai eṣa sphātim ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvaḥ atitheḥ aśnāti  
prajām vai eṣa paśūn ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvaḥ atitheḥ aśnāti

sa yaḥ evam vidvān kṣīram upasicya upaharati   yāvat agniṣṭomena iṣṭvā su samṛddhena avarunddhe tāvat enena ava runddhe  
sa yaḥ evam vidvān sarpiḥ upasicya upaharati   yāvat atirātreṇa iṣṭvā su samṛddhena avarunddhe tāvat enena ava runddhe  
sa yaḥ evam vidvān madhūpasicya upaharati   yāvat sattra sadyena iṣṭvā su samṛddhena avarunddhe tāvat enena ava runddhe  
sa yaḥ evam vidvān māṃsam upasicya upaharati   yāvat dvādaśa ahena iṣṭvā su samṛddhena avarunddhe tāvat enena ava runddhe  
 sa yaḥ evam vidvān udakam upasicya upaharati   prajānām prajananāya gacchati pratiṣṭhām priyaḥ prajānām bhavati yaḥ evam vidvān upasicya upaharati

yat sabhāgayati dakṣiṇāḥ sabhāgayati yat anutiṣṭhate udavasyati eva tat 
saḥ upahūtaḥ pṛthivyām bhakṣayati upahūtaḥ tasmin yat pṛthivyām viśva rūpam

 jyotiṣmataḥ lokān jayati yaḥ evam veda                                                                                                           
prajāpatiḥ ca parameṣṭhī ca śṛṅge indraḥ śiraḥ agniḥ lalāṭam yamaḥ kṛkāṭam  
somaḥ rājā mastiṣkaḥ dyauḥ uttarahanuḥ pṛthivī adharahanuḥ 
vidyut jihvā marutaḥ dantāḥ revatiḥ grīvāḥ kṛttikā skandhāḥ gharmaḥ vahaḥ 
viśvam vāyuḥ svargaḥ lokaḥ kṛṣṇadram vidharaṇī niveṣyaḥ 
śyenaḥ krotaḥ antarikṣam pājasyam bṛhaspatiḥ kakud bṛhatīḥ kīkasāḥ  
devānām patnīḥ pṛṣṭayaḥ upasadaḥ parśavaḥ 
mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca aṃsau tvaṣṭā ca aryamā ca doṣaṇī mahādevaḥ bāhū 
indrāṇī bhasat vāyuḥ pucham pavamānaḥ bālāḥ

dhātā ca savitā ca aṣṭhīvantau jaṅghā gandharvāḥ apsarasaḥ kuṣṭhikāḥ aditiḥ śaphāḥ

śīrṣaktim śīrṣa āmayam karṇa śūlam vilohitam   sarvam śīrṣanyam te rogam bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
karṇābhyām te kaṅkūṣebhyaḥ karṇa śūlam visalpakam   sarvam śīrṣanyam te rogam bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
yasya hetoḥ pracyavate yakṣmaḥ karṇataḥ āsyataḥ   sarvam śīrṣanyam te rogam bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
yaḥ kṛṇoti pramotam andham kṛṇoti pūruṣam   sarvam śīrṣanyam te rogam bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
aṅgabhedam aṅgajvaram viśvāṅgyam visalpakam   sarvam śīrṣanyam te rogam bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
yasya bhīmaḥ pratīkāśaḥ udvepayati pūruṣam   takmānam viśva śāradam bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
yaḥ ūrū anusarpati atha u eti gavīnike   yakṣmam te antar aṅgebhyaḥ bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
yadi kāmāt apakāmāt dhṛdayāt jāyate pari   hṛdaḥ balāsam aṅgebhyaḥ bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
harimāṇam te aṅgebhyaḥ apvām antarā udarāt   yakṣmodhām antar ātmanaḥ bahis niḥ mantrayāmahe  
āsaḥ balāsaḥ bhavatu mūtram bhavatu āmayat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat   yakṣmāṇām s
bahis bilam niḥ dravatu kāhā bāham tava udarāt   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat  
udarāt te klomnaḥ nābhyāḥ hṛdayāt adhi   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat  
yāḥ sīmānam virujanti mūrdhānam prati arṣanīḥ   a hiṃsantīḥ anāmayāḥ niḥ dravantu bahis bilam  
yāḥ hṛdayam uparṣanti anutanvanti kīkasāḥ   a hiṃsantīḥ anāmayāḥ niḥ dravantu bahis bilam  
yāḥ pārśve uparṣanti anunikṣanti pṛṣṭīḥ   a hiṃsantīḥ anāmayāḥ niḥ dravantu bahis bilam  
yāḥ tiraścīḥ uparṣanti arṣaṇīḥ vakṣaṇāsu te   a hiṃsantīḥ anāmayāḥ niḥ dravantu bahis bilam  
yāḥ gudāḥ anusarpanti āntrāṇi mohayanti ca   a hiṃsantīḥ anāmayāḥ niḥ dravantu bahis bilam  
yāḥ majjñaḥ nirdhayanti parūṃṣi virujanti ca   a hiṃsantīḥ anāmayāḥ niḥ dravantu bahis bilam  
ye aṅgāni madayanti yakṣmāsaḥ ropaṇāḥ tava   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat  
visalpasya vidradhasya vātīkārasya vālajeḥ   yakṣmāṇām sarveṣām viṣam niḥ avocam aham tvat  
pādābhyām te jānubhyām śroṇibhyām pari bhaṃsasaḥ   anūkāt arṣaṇīḥ uṣṇihābhyaḥ śīrṣṇaḥ rogam anīnaśam  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
asya vāmasya palitasya hotuḥ tasya bhrātā madhyamaḥ asti aśnaḥ   tṛtīyaḥ bhrātā ghṛta pṛṣṭhaḥ asya atra apaśyam viśpatim sapta putram  
sapta yuñjanti ratham eka cakram ekaḥ aśvaḥ vahati sapta nāmā   tri nābhi cakram ajaram anarvam yatra imā viśvā bhuvanā adhi tasthuḥ  
imam ratham adhi ye sapta tasthuḥ sapta cakram sapta vahanti aśvāḥ   sapta svasāraḥ abhi sam navanta yatra gavām nihitā sapta nāma  
kaḥ dadarśa prathamam jāyamānam a sthanvantam yat anasthā bibharti   bhūmyāḥ asuḥ asṛk ātmā kva svid kaḥ vidvāṃsam upa gāt praṣṭum etat  
iha bravītu yaḥ īm aṅga veda asya vāmasya nihitam padam veḥ   śīrṣṇaḥ kṣīram duhrate gāvaḥ asya vavrim vasānāḥ udakam padā apuḥ  
pākaḥ pṛchāmi manasā a vijānan devānām enā nihitā padāni   vatse baṣkaye adhi sapta tantūn vi tatnire kavayaḥ otavai u  
acikitvān cikituṣaḥ cit atra kavīn pṛchāmi vidvanaḥ na vidvān   vi yaḥ tastambha ṣaṭ imā rajāṃsi ajasya rūpe kim api svid ekam  
mātā pitaram ṛte ā babhāja adhi iti agre manasā sam hi jagme   sā bībhatsuḥ garbha rasā nividdhā namasvantaḥ id upavākam īyuḥ  
yuktā mātā asit dhuri dakṣiṇāyāḥ atiṣṭhat garbhaḥ vṛjanīṣu antar   amīmet vatsaḥ anu gām apaśyat viśvarūpyam triṣu yoganeṣu  
tisraḥ matṝḥ trīn pitṝn bibhrat ekaḥ urdhvaḥ tasthau na īm ava glāpayanta   mantrayante divaḥ amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśva vidaḥ vācam aviśva vidnām     mantrayante divaḥ amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśva vidaḥ vācam aviśva vidnām     mantrayante divaḥ amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśva vidaḥ vācam aviśva vidnām     mantrayante divaḥ amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśva vidaḥ vācam aviśva vidnām       mantrayante divaḥ amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśva vidaḥ vācam aviśva 
pañca are cakre parivartamāne yasmin ātasthuḥ bhuvanāni viśvā   tasya na akṣaḥ tapyate bhūri bhāraḥ sanāt eva na chidyate sanābhiḥ  
pañca pādam pitaram dvādaśa ākṛtim divaḥ āhuḥ pare ardhe purīṣiṇam   atha ime anye upare vicakṣaṇe sapta cakre ṣaṣ are āhuḥ arpitam  
dvādaśa aram nahi tat jarāya varvarti cakram pari dyām ṛtasya   ā putrāḥ agne mithunāsaḥ atra sapta śatāni viṃśatiḥ ca tasthuḥ  
sanemi cakram ajaram vi vavṛte uttānāyām daśa yuktāḥ vahanti   sūryasya cakṣuḥ rajasā eti āvṛtam yasmin ātasthuḥ bhuvanāni viśvā  
striyaḥ satīḥ tām u me puṃsaḥ āhuḥ paśyat akṣaṇvān vi cetat andhaḥ   kaviḥ yaḥ putraḥ saḥ īm ā ciketa yaḥ tāḥ vijānāt sa pituḥ pitā asat  
sākaṃjānām saptatham āhuḥ ekajam ṣaṭ id yamāḥ ṛṣayaḥ deva jāḥ iti   teṣām iṣṭāni vihitāni dhāmaśas sthātre rejante vikṛtāni rūpaśas  
avas pareṇa paras enāḥ avareṇa padā vatsam bibhratī gauḥ ud asthāt   sā kadrīcī kam svid ardham parāgāt kva svid sūte nahi yūthe asmin  
avas pareṇa pitaram yaḥ asya veda avas pareṇa paras enā avareṇa   kavīyamānaḥ kaḥ iha pra vocat devam manaḥ kutas adhi prajātam  
ye arvāñcaḥ tām u parācaḥ āhuḥ ye parāñcaḥ tām u arvācaḥ āhuḥ   indraḥ ca yā cakrathuḥ soma tāni dhurā na yuktāḥ rajasaḥ vahanti  
dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānam vṛkṣam pari sasvajāte   tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti an aśnan anyaḥ abhi cākaśīti  
yasmin vṛkṣe madhu adaḥ suparṇāḥ niviśante suvate ca adhi viśve   tasya yat āhuḥ pippalam svādu agre tat na ud naśat yaḥ pitaram na veda  
yatra suparṇāḥ amṛtasya bhakṣam animeṣam vidathāḥ abhisvaranti   enā viśvasya bhuvanasya gopāḥ sa mā dhīraḥ pākam atrā viveśa       viveśa       viśvasya bhuvanasya gopāḥ sa mā dhīraḥ pākam atrā viveśa       
yat gāyatre adhi gāyatram āhitam traiṣṭubham vā traiṣṭubhāt niratakṣata   yat vā jagat jagati āhitam padam ye id tat viduḥ te amṛta tvam ānuśuḥ  
gāyatreṇa prati mimīte arkam arkeṇa sāma traiṣṭubhena vākam   vākena vākam dvipadā catuṣpadā akṣareṇa mimate sapta vāṇīḥ  
jagatā sindhum divi askabhāyat rathaṃtare sūryam pari apaśyat   gāyatrasya samidhaḥ tisraḥ āhuḥ tatas mahnā pra ririce mahitvā  
upa hvaye su dughām dhenum etām su hastaḥ go dhuk uta dohat enām   śreṣṭham savam savitā sāviṣat naḥ abhīddhaḥ gharmaḥ tat u su pra vocat  
hiṅkṛṇvatī vasu patnī vasūnām vatsam ichantī manasā abhyāgāt   duhām aśvibhyām payaḥ aghnyā iyam sā vardhatām mahate saubhagāya  
gauḥ amīmet abhi vatsam miṣantam mūrdhānam hiṅ akṛṇot mātave u  sṛkvāṇam gharmam abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyum payate payobhiḥ  
ayam sa śiṅkte yena gauḥ abhivṛtā mimāti mayum dhvasanau adhi śritā   sā cittibhiḥ ni hi cakāra martyān vidyut bhavantī prati vavrim auhata  
anat śaye turagātu jīvam ejat dhruvam madhye ā pastyānām   jīvaḥ mṛtasya carati svadhābhiḥ amartyaḥ martyena sayoniḥ  
vidhum dadrāṇam salilasya pṛṣṭhe yuvānam santam palitaḥ jagāra   devasya paśya kāvyam mahitvā adya mamāra sa hyaḥ sam āna  
yaḥ īm cakāra na saḥ asya veda yaḥ īm dadarśa hiruk id nu tasmāt   sa mātuḥ yonā parivītaḥ antar bahu prajāḥ nirṛtiḥ ā viveśa   sa mātuḥ yonā parivītaḥ antar bahu prajāḥ nirṛtiḥ ā viveśa     sa mātuḥ yonā parivītaḥ antar bahu prajāḥ nirṛtiḥ ā viveśa     sa mātuḥ yonā parivītaḥ antar bahu prajāḥ nirṛtiḥ ā viveśa     sa mātuḥ yonā parivītaḥ antar bahu prajāḥ nirṛtiḥ ā viveśa     sa mātuḥ yonā par
apaśyam gopām a nipadyamānam ā ca parā ca pathibhiḥ carantam   sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viṣūcīḥ vasānaḥ ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣu antar  
dyauḥ naḥ pitā janitā nābhiḥ atra bandhuḥ naḥ mātā pṛthivī mahī iyam   uttānayoḥ camvoḥ yoniḥ antar atrā pitā duhituḥ garbham ādhāt  
pṛchāmi tvā param antam pṛthivyāḥ pṛchāmi vṛṣṇaḥ aśvasya retaḥ   pṛchāmi viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhim pṛchāmi vācaḥ paramam vyoma  
iyam vediḥ paraḥ antar pṛthivyāḥ ayam somaḥ vṛṣṇaḥ aśvasya retaḥ   ayam yajñaḥ viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhiḥ brahmā ayam vācaḥ paramam vyoma  
na vi jānāmi yat iva idam asmi niṇyaḥ saṃnaddhaḥ manasā carāmi   yadā mā agan prathama jāḥ ṛtasya āt id vācaḥ aśnuve bhāgam asyāḥ

sapta ardha garbhāḥ bhuvanasya retaḥ viṣṇoḥ tiṣṭhanti pradiśā vidharmaṇi   te dhītibhiḥ manasā te vipaścitaḥ paribhuvaḥ pari bhavanti viśvatas  
ṛcaḥ akṣare parame vyoman yasmin devāḥ adhi viśve niṣeduḥ   yaḥ tat na veda kim ṛcā kariṣyati ye id tat viduḥ te amī sam āsate  
ṛcaḥ padam mātrayā kalpayantaḥ ardharcena cakḷpuḥ viśvam ejat   tripād brahma puru rūpam vi taṣṭhe tena jīvanti pradiśaḥ catasraḥ  
sūyavasāt bhagavatī hi bhūyāḥ adhā vayam bhagavantaḥ syāma   addhi tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī   tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī   tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī   tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī   tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī   tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm piba śuddham udakam ācarantī   tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīm
gauḥ id mimāya salilāni takṣatī ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpadī   aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī sahasra akṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktiḥ tasyāḥ samudrāḥ adhi vi kṣaranti  
kṛṣṇam niyānam harayaḥ suparṇāḥ apaḥ vasānāḥ divam ud patanti   tam āvavṛtran sadanāt ṛtasya āt id ghṛtena pṛthivīm vi ūduḥ  
apād eti prathamā padvatīnām kaḥ tat vām mitrāvaruṇā ciketa   garbhaḥ bhāram bharati ā cit asyāḥ ṛtam piparti anṛtam ni pāti  
virāj vāc virāj pṛthivī virāj antarikṣam virāj prajāpatiḥ   virāj mṛtyuḥ sādhyānām adhirājaḥ babhūva tasya bhūtam bhavyam vaśe sa me bhūtam bhavyam vaśe kṛṇotu  
śaka mayam dhūmam ārāt apaśyam viṣūvatā paras enā avareṇa   ukṣāṇam pṛśnim apacanta vīrāḥ tāni dharmāṇi prathamāni āsan  
trayaḥ keśinaḥ ṛtuthā vi cakṣate saṃvatsare vapate ekaḥ eṣām   viśvam anyaḥ abhicaṣṭe śacībhiḥ dhrājiḥ ekasya dadṛśe na rūpam  
catvāri vāc parimitā padāni tāni viduḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ye manīṣiṇaḥ   guhā trīṇi nihitā na iṅgayanti turīyam vācaḥ manuṣyāḥ vadanti  
indram mitram varuṇam agnim āhuḥ atha u divyaḥ sa suparṇaḥ garutmān   ekam sat viprāḥ bahudhā vadanti agnim yamam mātariśvānam āhuḥ                                                                                                                                                                                   
yām kalpayanti vahatau vadhūm iva viśva rūpām hasta kṛtām cikitsavaḥ   sārāt etu apa nudāmaḥ enām  
śīrṣaṇvatī nasvatī karṇiṇī kṛtyā kṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśva rūpā   sārāt etu apa nudāmaḥ enām  
śūdra kṛtā rāja kṛtā strī kṛtā brahmabhiḥ kṛtā   jāyā patyā nuttā iva kartāram bandhu ṛchatu  
anayā aham oṣadhyā sarvāḥ kṛtyāḥ adūduṣam   yām kṣetre cakruḥ yām goṣu yām vā te puruṣeṣu  
agham astu agha kṛte śapathaḥ śapathīyate   pratyak pratiprahiṇmaḥ yathā kṛtyā kṛtam hanat  
pratīcīnaḥ āṅgirasaḥ adhyakṣaḥ naḥ purohitaḥ   pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ ākṛtya amūn kṛtyākṛtaḥ jahi  
yaḥ tvā uvāca parehi iti pratikūlam udāyyam   tam kṛtye abhinivartasva mā asmān ichaḥ anāgasaḥ  
yaḥ te parūṃṣi saṃdadhau rathasya iva rbhuḥ dhiyā   tam gaccha tatra te ayanam a jñātaḥ te ayam janaḥ  
ye tvā kṛtvā ālebhire vidvalāḥ abhicāriṇaḥ   śaṃbhu idam kṛtyā dūṣaṇam prativartma punaḥsaram tena tvā snapayāmasi  
yat durbhagām prasnapitām mṛta vatsām upeyima   apaitu sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpam draviṇam mā upa tiṣṭhatu       sarvam mat pāpa
yat te pitṛbhyaḥ dadataḥ yajñe vā nāma jagṛhuḥ   saṃdeśyāt sarvasmāt pāpāt imāḥ muñcantu tvā oṣadhīḥ  
deva enasāt pitryāt nāma grāhāt saṃdeśyāt abhiniṣkṛtāt   muñcantu tvā vīrudhaḥ vīryeṇa brahmaṇā ṛgbhiḥ payasā ṛṣīṇām  
yathā vātaḥ cyāvayati bhūmyāḥ reṇum antarikṣāt ca abhram   eva mat sarvam durbhūtam brahma nuttam apāyati  
apa krāma nānadatī vinaddhā gardabhī iva   kartṝn nakṣasva itas nuttā brahmaṇā vīryāvatā  
ayam panthāḥ kṛtyā iti tvā nayāmaḥ abhiprahitām prati tvā pra hiṇmaḥ   tena abhi yāhi bhañjati anasvatī iva vāhinī viśva rūpā kurūtinī  
parāk te jyotiḥ apatham te arvāk anyatra asmat ayanā kṛṇuṣva   pareṇa ihi navatim nāvyāḥ ati durgāḥ srotyāḥ mā kṣaṇiṣṭhāḥ parehi  
vātaḥ iva vṛkṣān ni mṛṇīhi pādaya mā gām aśvam puruṣam ud śiṣaḥ eṣām   kartṝn nivṛtya itas kṛtye a prajāstvāya bodhaya  
yām te barhiṣi yām śmaśāne kṣetre kṛtyām valagam vā nicakhnuḥ   agnau vā tvā gārhapatye abhiceruḥ pākam santam dhīratarāḥ anāgasam  
upāhṛtam anubuddham nikhātam vairam tsārī anu avidāma kartram   tat etu yatas ābhṛtam tatra aśvaḥ iva vi vartatām hantu kṛtyākṛtaḥ prajām  
 tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi itas a jñāte kim iha icchasi     tiṣṭha eva parehi
grīvāḥ te kṛtye pādau ca api kartsyāmi niḥ drava   indra agnī asmān rakṣatām yau prajānām prajāvatī  
somaḥ rājā adhipāḥ mṛḍitā ca bhūtasya naḥ patayaḥ mṛḍayantu  
bhava śarvau asyatām pāpa kṛte kṛtyā kṛte   duṣkṛte vidyutam deva hetim  
yadi eyatha dvipadī catuṣpadī kṛtyā kṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśva rūpā   sā itas aṣṭāpadī bhūtvā punar parehi duchune  
abhyakta aktā svaraṃkṛtā sarvam bharantī duritam parehi   jānīhi kṛtye kartāram duhitā iva pitaram svam  
parehi kṛtye mā tiṣṭhaḥ viddhasya iva padam naya   mṛgaḥ sa mṛgayuḥ tvam na tvā nikartum arhati  
uta hanti pūrva asinam pratyādāya aparaḥ iṣvā   uta pūrvasya nighnataḥ ni hanti aparaḥ prati  
etat hi śṛṇu me vacaḥ atha ihi yatas eyatha   yaḥ tvā cakāra tam prati  
anāgohatyā vai bhīmā kṛtye mā naḥ gām aśvam puruṣam vadhīḥ   yatra yatra asi nihitā tatas tvā ud thāpayāmasi parṇāt laghīyasī bhava  
yadi stha tamasā āvṛtāḥ jālena abhihitāḥ iva   sarvāḥ saṃlupya itas kṛtyāḥ punar kartre pra hiṇmasi  
kṛtyā kṛtaḥ valaginaḥ abhiniṣkāriṇaḥ prajām   mṛṇīhi kṛtye mā ud śiṣaḥ amūn kṛtyā kṛtaḥ jahi  
 eva aham sarvam durbhūtam kartram kṛtyā kṛtā kṛtam hastī iva rajaḥ duritam jahāmi      iva rajaḥ duritam jahāmi                                                                                                                                                                                             
kena pārṣṇī ābhṛte pūruṣasya kena māṃsam saṃbhṛtam kena gulphau   kena aṅgulīḥ peśanīḥ kena khāni kena ucchlaṅkhau madhyataḥ kaḥ pratiṣṭhām  
kasmāt nu gulphau adharau akṛṇvan aṣṭhīvantau uttarau puruṣasya   jaṅghe nirṛtya ni adadhuḥ kva svid jānunoḥ saṃdhī kaḥ u tat ciketa  
catuṣṭayam yujate saṃhitā antam jānubhyām ūrdhvam śithiram kabandham   śroṇī yat ūrū kaḥ u tat jajāna yābhyām kusindham su dṛḍham babhūva  
kati devāḥ katame te āsan ye uraḥ grīvāḥ cikyuḥ puruṣasya   kati stanau vi adadhuḥ kaḥ kaphodau kati skandhān kati pṛṣṭīḥ acinvan  
kaḥ asya bāhū sam abharat vīryām karavāt iti   aṃsau kaḥ asya tat devaḥ kusindhe adhi ā dadhau 
kaḥ sapta khāni vi tatarda śīrṣaṇi karṇau imau nāsike cakṣaṇī mukham   yeṣām purutrā vijayasya mahnani catuṣpādaḥ dvipadaḥ yanti yāmam  
hanvoḥ hi jihvām adadhāt purūcīm adhāḥ mahīm adhi śiśrāya vācam   saḥ ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣu antar apaḥ vasānaḥ kaḥ u tat ciketa  
mastiṣkam asya yatamaḥ lalātam kakāṭikām prathamaḥ yaḥ kapālam   citvā cityam hanvoḥ pūruṣasya divam ruroha katamaḥ sa devaḥ  
priya apriyāṇi bahulā svapnam saṃbādha tandyaḥ   ānandān ugraḥ nandān ca kasmāt vahati pūruṣaḥ  
ārtiḥ avartiḥ nirṛtiḥ kutas nu puruṣe amatiḥ   rāddhiḥ samṛddhiḥ avyṛddhiḥ matiḥ uditayaḥ kutas                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
kaḥ asmin āpaḥ vi adadhāt viṣūvṛtaḥ purūvṛtaḥ sindhusṛtyāya jātāḥ   tīvrāḥ aruṇāḥ lohinīḥ tāmra dhūmrāḥ ūrdhvāḥ avācīḥ puruṣe tiraścīḥ  
kaḥ asmin rūpam adadhāt kaḥ mahmānam ca nāma ca   gātum kaḥ asmin kaḥ ketum kaḥ caritrāni puruṣe  
kaḥ asmin prāṇam avayat kaḥ apānam vyānam u  samānam asmin kaḥ devaḥ adhi śiśrāya puruṣe  
kaḥ asmin yajñam adadhāt ekaḥ devaḥ adhi puruṣe   kaḥ asmin satyam kaḥ anṛtam kutas mṛtyuḥ kutas amṛtam  
kaḥ asmai vāsaḥ pari adadhāt kaḥ asya āyuḥ akalpayat   balam kaḥ asmai prāyacchat kaḥ asya akalpayat javam  
kena apaḥ anu atanuta kena ahar akarot ruce   uṣasam kena anu ainddha kena sāyaṃbhavam dade  
kaḥ asmin retaḥ ni adadhāt tantuḥ ā tāyatām iti   medhām kaḥ asmin adhi auhat kaḥ bāṇam kaḥ nṛtaḥ dadhau  
kena imām bhūmim aurṇot kena pari abhavat divam   kena abhi mahnā parvatān kena karmāṇi puruṣaḥ  
kena parjanyam anu eti kena somam vicakṣaṇam   kena yajñam ca śraddhām ca kena asmin nihitam manaḥ  
kena śrotriyam āpnoti kena imam parameṣṭhinam   kena imam agnim pūruṣaḥ kena saṃvatsaram mame       
brahma śrotriyam āpnoti brahma imam parameṣṭhinam   brahma imam agnim pūruṣaḥ brahma saṃvatsaram mame  
kena devām anu kṣiyati kena daivajanīḥ viśaḥ   kena idam anyat nakṣatram kena sat kṣatram ucyate  
brahma devām anu kṣiyati brahma daivajanīḥ viśaḥ   brahma idam anyat nakṣatram brahma sat kṣatram ucyate  
kena iyam bhūmiḥ vihitā kena dyauḥ uttarā hitā   kena idam ūrdhvam tiryak ca antarikṣam vyacaḥ hitam  
brahmaṇā bhūmiḥ vihitā brahma dyauḥ uttarā hitā   brahma idam ūrdhvam tiryak ca antarikṣam vyacaḥ hitam  
mūrdhānam asya saṃsīvya atharvā hṛdayam ca yat   mastiṣkāt ūrdhvaḥ prairayat pavamānaḥ adhi śīrṣataḥ  
tat vai atharvaṇaḥ śiraḥ deva kośaḥ samubjitaḥ   tat prāṇaḥ abhi rakṣati śiraḥ annam atha u manaḥ  
ūrdhvaḥ nu sṛṣṭaḥ tiryak nu sṛṣṭaḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ puruṣaḥ ā babhūva am   puram yaḥ brahmaṇaḥ veda yasyāḥ puruṣaḥ ucyate  
yaḥ vai tām brahmaṇaḥ veda amṛtena āvṛtām puram   tasmai brahma ca brāhmāḥ ca cakṣuḥ prāṇam prajām daduḥ  
na vai tam cakṣuḥ jahāti na prāṇaḥ jarasaḥ purā   puram yaḥ brahmaṇaḥ veda yasyāḥ puruṣaḥ ucyate  
aṣṭācakrā nava dvārā devānām pūḥ ayodhyā   tasyām hiraṇyayaḥ kośaḥ svargaḥ jyotiṣā āvṛtaḥ  
tasmin hiraṇyaye kośe tri are tri pratiṣṭhite   tasmin yat yakṣam ātmanvat tat vai brahma vidaḥ viduḥ  
prabhrājamānām hariṇīm yaśasā saṃparīvṛtām   puram hiraṇyayīm brahmā viveśa aparājitām                                                                                                                                                                                                          
ayam me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ sapatna kṣayaṇaḥ vṛṣā   tena ā rabhasva tvam śatrūn pra mṛṇīhi durasyataḥ  
pra eṇān śṛṇīhi pra mṛṇā rabhasva maṇiḥ te astu puraetā purastāt   avārayanta varaṇena devāḥ abhyācāram asurāṇām śvas śvas  
ayam maṇiḥ varaṇaḥ viśva bheṣajaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ haritaḥ hiraṇyayaḥ   sa te śatrūn adharān pādayāti pūrvaḥ tān dabhnuhi ye tvā dviṣanti  
ayam te kṛtyām vitatām pauruṣeyāt ayam bhayāt   ayam tvā sarvasmāt pāpāt varaṇaḥ vārayiṣyate  
varaṇaḥ vārayātai ayam devaḥ vanaspatiḥ   yakṣmaḥ yaḥ asmin āviṣṭaḥ tam u devāḥ avīvaran  
svapnam suptvā yadi paśyāsi pāpam mṛgaḥ sṛtim yati dhāvāt ajuṣṭām   parikṣavāt śakuneḥ pāpa vādāt ayam maṇiḥ varaṇaḥ vārayiṣyate  
arātyāḥ tvā nirṛtyāḥ abhicārāt atho bhayāt   mṛtyoḥ ojīyasaḥ vadhāt varaṇaḥ vārayiṣyate  
yat me mātā yat me pitā bhrātaraḥ yat ca me svāḥ yat enaḥ cakṛma vayam   tatas naḥ vārayiṣyate ayam devaḥ vanaspatiḥ  
varaṇena pravyathitāḥ bhrātṛvyāḥ me sabandhavaḥ   asūrtam rajaḥ api aguḥ te yantu adhamam tamaḥ  
 tam mā ayam varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ pari pātu diśaḥ diśaḥ                                                                                                            
ayam me varaṇaḥ urasi rājā devaḥ vanaspatiḥ   sa me śatrūn vi bādhatām indraḥ dasyūn iva asurān  
imam bibharmi varaṇam āyuṣmān śata śāradaḥ   sa me rāṣṭram ca kṣatram ca paśūn ojaḥ ca me dadhat  
yathā vātaḥ vanaspatīn vṛkṣān bhanakti ojasā   eva sapatnān me bhaṅgdhi pūrvān jātām uta aparān varaṇaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
yathā vātaḥ ca agniḥ ca vṛkṣān psātaḥ vanaspatīn   eva sapatnān me psāhi pūrvān jātām uta aparān varaṇaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
yathā vātena prakṣīṇāḥ vṛkṣāḥ śere nyarpitāḥ   eva sapatnān tvam mama pra kṣiṇīhi ni arpaya   pūrvān jātām uta aparān varaṇaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
tān tvam pra chinddhi varaṇa purā diṣṭāt purā āyuṣaḥ   ye enam paśuṣu dipsanti ye ca asya rāṣṭra dipsavaḥ  
yathā sūryaḥ atibhāti yathā asmin tejaḥ āhitam   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā yaśaḥ candramasi āditye ca nṛ cakṣasi   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā yaśaḥ pṛthivyām yathā asmin jātavedasi   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā yaśaḥ kanyāyām yathā asmin saṃbhṛte rathe   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā
yathā yaśaḥ soma pīthe madhuparke yathā yaśaḥ   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā yaśaḥ agnihotre vaṣaṭkāre yathā yaśaḥ   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā yaśaḥ yajamāne yathā asmin yajñe āhitam   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā yaśaḥ prajāpatau yathā asmin parameṣṭhini   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
yathā deveṣu amṛtam yathā eṣu satyam āhitam   eva me varaṇaḥ maṇiḥ kīrtim bhūtim ni yacchatu   tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā     tejasā m
indrasya prathamaḥ rathaḥ devānām aparaḥ rathaḥ varuṇasya tṛtīyaḥ id   ahīnām apamā ratha sthānum ārat atha arṣat  
darbhaḥ śociḥ tarūṇakam aśvasya vāraḥ paruṣasya vāraḥ   rathasya bandhuram  
ava śveta padā jahi pūrveṇa ca apareṇa ca   udaplutam iva dāru ahīnām arasam viṣam vār ugram  
araṃghuṣaḥ nimajya unmaja punar abravīt   udaplutam iva dāru ahīnām arasam viṣam vār ugram  
paidvaḥ hanti kasarṇīlam paidvaḥ śvitram uta asitam   paidvaḥ ratharvyāḥ śiraḥ sam bibheda pṛdākvāḥ  
paidva prehi prathamaḥ anu tvā vayam emasi   ahīn vi asyatāt pathaḥ yena smā vayam emasi  
idam paidvaḥ ajāyata idam asya parāyaṇam   imāni arvataḥ padā ahi ghnyaḥ vājinīvataḥ  
saṃyatam na vi sparat vyāttam na sam yamat   asmin kṣetre dvau ahī strī ca pumān ca tau ubhau arasā  
arasāsaḥ iha ahayaḥ ye anti ye ca dūrake   ghanena hanmi vṛścikam ahim daṇḍena āgatam

a riprāḥ āpaḥ apa ripram asmat   pra asmat enaḥ duritam su pratīkāḥ pra duṣvapnyam pra malam vahantu  
viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā pṛthivī saṃśitaḥ agni tejāḥ   pṛthivīm anu vi krame aham pṛthivyāḥ tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jīvīt tam prānaḥ jahātu  
viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā antarikṣa saṃśitaḥ vāyu tejāḥ   antarikṣam anu vi krame aham antarikṣāt tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jīvīt tam prānaḥ jahātu  
viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā dyau saṃśitaḥ sūrya tejāḥ   divam anu vi krame aham divaḥ tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jivīt tam prānaḥ jahātu  
viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā diś saṃśitaḥ manaḥ tejāḥ   diśaḥ anu vi krame aham digbhyaḥ tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jīvīt tam prānaḥ jahātu  
viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā āśā saṃśitaḥ vāta tejāḥ   āśāḥ anu vi krame aham āśābhyaḥ tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jīvīt tam prānaḥ jahātu

viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā apsu saṃśitaḥ varuṇa tejāḥ   apaḥ anu vi krame aham adbhyaḥ tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jīvīt tam prānaḥ jahātu  
viṣṇoḥ kramaḥ asi sapatna hā kṛṣi saṃśitaḥ anna tejāḥ   kṛṣim anu vi krame aham kṛṣyāḥ tam niḥ bhajāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ   sa mā jīvīt tam prānaḥ jahātu

yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ maṇim phālam ghṛtaścutam ugram khadiram ojase   tam bibhrat candramāḥ maṇim asurāṇām puras ajayat dānavānām hiraṇyayīḥ   saḥ asmai śriyam id duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam dviṣataḥ jahi   tvam 
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   saḥ asmai vājinam id duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   tena imām maṇinā kṛṣim aśvinau abhi rakṣataḥ   sa bhiṣagbhyām mahaḥ duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   tam bibhrat savitā maṇim tena idam ajayat svar   saḥ asmai sūnṛtām duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   tam āpaḥ bibhratīḥ maṇim sadā dhāvanti akṣitāḥ   saḥ ābhyaḥ amṛtam id duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   tam rājā varuṇaḥ maṇim prati amuñcata śaṃbhuvam   saḥ asmai satyam id duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   tam devāḥ bibhrataḥ maṇim sarvān lokān yudhā ajayan   saḥ ebhyaḥ jitim id duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ vātāya maṇim āśave   tam imam devatāḥ maṇim prati amuñcanta śambhuvam   saḥ ābhyaḥ viśvam id duhe bhūyas bhūyas śvas śvas tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi  
ṛtavaḥ tam abadhnata ārtavāḥ tam abadhnata   saṃvatsaraḥ tam baddhvā sarvam bhūtam vi rakṣati  
antardeśāḥ abadhnata pradiśaḥ tam abadhnata   prajāpati sṛṣṭaḥ maṇiḥ dviṣataḥ me adharām akaḥ
