tam dhātā prati amuñcata sa bhūtam vi akalpayat  tena tvam dviṣataḥ jahi 
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat rasena saha varcasā  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat saha gobhiḥ aja avibhiḥ annena prajayā saha  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat saha vrīhi yavābhyām mahasā bhūtyā saha  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat madhoḥ ghṛtasya dhārayā kīlālena maṇiḥ saha  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat ūrjayā payasā saha draviṇena śriyā saha  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat tejasā tviṣyā saha yaśasā kīrtyā saha  
yam abadhnāt bṛhaspatiḥ devebhyaḥ asura kṣitim   sa mā ayam maṇiḥ āgamat sarvābhiḥ bhūtibhiḥ saha  
tam imam devatāḥ maṇim mahyam dadatu puṣṭaye   abhibhum kṣatra vardhanam sapatna dambhanam maṇim  
brahmaṇā tejasā saha prati muñcāmi me śivam   asapatnaḥ sapatna hā sapatnāt me adharām akaḥ                                                                                                                                                                                                           
uttaram dviṣataḥ mām ayam maṇiḥ kṛṇotu deva jāḥ   yasya lokāḥ ime trayaḥ payaḥ dugdham upāsate   sa mā ayam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ  
yam devāḥ pitaraḥ manuṣyāḥ upajīvanti sarvadā   sa mā ayam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ  
yathā bījam urvarāyām kṛṣṭe phālena rohati   eva mayi prajā paśavaḥ annam annam vi rohatu  
yasmai tvā yajñavardhana maṇe pratyamucam śivam   tam tvam śata dakṣiṇa maṇe śraiṣṭhyāya jinvatāt  
etam idhmam samāhitam juṣaṇaḥ agne prati harya homaiḥ   tasmin vidhema sumatim svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūn samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā   tasmin vidhema sumatim svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūn samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā   tasmin vidhema sumatim svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūn samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā   tasmin vidhema sumatim svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūn samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā   tasmin vidhema sumatim svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūn samiddhe jā
kasmin aṅge tapaḥ asya adhi tiṣṭhati kasmin aṅge ṛtam asya adhi āhitam   kva vratam kva śraddhā asya tiṣṭhati kasmin aṅge satyam asya pratiṣṭhitam  
kasmāt aṅgāt dīpyate agniḥ asya kasmāt aṅgāt pavate mātariśva   kasmāt aṅgāt vi mimīte adhi candramāḥ mahaḥ skambhasya mimānaḥ aṅgam  
bhūmiḥ asya kasmin aṅge tiṣṭhati antarikṣam   kasmin aṅge tiṣṭhati āhitā dyauḥ kasmin aṅge tiṣṭhati uttaram divaḥ  
kva prepsan dīpyate ūrdhvaḥ agniḥ kva prepsan pavate mātariśvā   yatra prepsantīḥ abhiyanti āvṛtaḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
kva ardha māsāḥ kva yanti māsāḥ saṃvatsareṇa saha saṃvidānāḥ   yatra yanti ṛtavaḥ yatra ārtavāḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
kva prepsantī yuvatī virūpe ahar rātre dravataḥ saṃvidāne   yatra prepsantīḥ abhiyanti āpaḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yasmin stabdhvā prajāpatiḥ lokān sarvān adhārayat   skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yat paramam avamam yat ca madhyamam prajāpatiḥ sasṛje viśva rūpam   kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra yat na prāviśat kiyat tat babhūva  
kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa bhūtam kiyat bhaviṣyat anvāśaye asya   ekam yat aṅgam akṛṇot sahasradhā kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra  
yatra lokām ca kośān ca apaḥ brahma janāḥ viduḥ   asat ca yatra sat ca anta skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ     tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ         tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ         tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ           tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ           tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ           tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ           tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ    
yatra tapaḥ parākramya vratam dhārayati uttaram   ṛtam ca yatra śraddhā ca apaḥ brahma samāhitāḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yasmin bhūmiḥ antarikṣam dyauḥ yasmin adhi āhitā   yatra agniḥ candramāḥ sūryaḥ vātaḥ tiṣṭhanti ārpitāḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yasya trayastriṃśat devāḥ aṅge sarve samāhitāḥ   skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathama jāḥ ṛcaḥ sāma yajuḥ mahī   eka ṛṣiḥ yasmin ārpitaḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yatra amṛtam ca mṛtyuḥ ca puruṣe adhi samāhite   samudraḥ yasya nāḍyaḥ puruṣe adhi samāhitāḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yasya catasraḥ pradiśaḥ nāḍyaḥ tiṣṭhanti prathamāḥ   yajñaḥ yatra parākrāntaḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
ye puruṣe brahma viduḥ te viduḥ parameṣṭhinam   yaḥ veda parameṣṭhinam yaḥ ca veda prajāpatim   jyeṣṭham ye brāhmaṇam viduḥ te skambham anusaṃviduḥ  
yasya śiraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ cakṣuḥ aṅgirasaḥ abhavan   aṅgāni yasya yātavaḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yasya brahma mukham āhuḥ jihvām madhukaśām uta   virājam ūdhar yasya āhuḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
 yasmāt ṛcaḥ apātakṣan yajuḥ yasmāt apākaṣan   sāmāni yasya lomāni atharva aṅgirasaḥ mukham skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ     brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ               katamaḥ svid eva saḥ                       katamaḥ svid eva saḥ                       katamaḥ svid eva saḥ                       katamaḥ svid eva saḥ               katamaḥ svid eva sa
asat cākhām pratiṣṭhantīm paramam iva janāḥ viduḥ   uta u sat manyante avare ye te śākhām upāsate  
yatra ādityāḥ ca rudrāḥ ca vasavaḥ ca samāhitāḥ   bhūtam ca yatra bhavyam ca sarve lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
yasya trayastriṃśat devāḥ nidhim rakṣanti sarvadā   nidhim tam adya kaḥ veda yam devāḥ abhirakṣatha  
yatra devāḥ brahma vidaḥ brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate   yaḥ vai tān vidyāt pratyakṣam sa brahmā veditā syāt  
bṛhantaḥ nāma te devāḥ ye asataḥ pari jajñire   ekam tat aṅgam skambhasya asat āhuḥ paras janāḥ  
yatra skambhaḥ prajanayan purāṇam vyavartayat   ekam tat aṅgam skambhasya purāṇam anusaṃviduḥ 
yasya trayastriṃśat devāḥ aṅge gātrāḥ vibhejire   tān vai trayastriṃśat devān eke braham vidaḥ viduḥ  
hiraṇya garbham paramam anatyudyam janāḥ viduḥ   skambhaḥ tat agre prāsiñcat hiraṇyam loke antarā  
skambhe lokāḥ skambhe tapaḥ skambhe adhi ṛtam āhitam   skambha tvā veda pratyakṣam indre sarvam samāhitam  
indre lokāḥ indre tapaḥ indre adhi ṛtam āhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam   indram tvā veda pratyakṣam skambhe sarvam pratiṣṭh
nāma nāmnā johavīti purā sūryāt purā uṣasaḥ   yat ajaḥ prathamam saṃbabhūva sa ha tat sva rājyam iyāya yasmāt na anyat param asti bhūtam  
yasya bhūmiḥ pramā antarikṣam uta udaram   divam yaḥ cakre mūrdhānam tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ  
yasya sūryaḥ cakṣuḥ candramāḥ ca punarṇavaḥ   agnim yaḥ cakre āsyam tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ  
yasya vātaḥ prāṇa apānau cakṣuḥ aṅgirasaḥ abhavan   diśaḥ yaḥ cakre prajñānīḥ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ  
skambhaḥ dādhāra dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime skambhaḥ dādhāra uru antarikṣam   skambhaḥ dādhāra pradiśaḥ ṣaṭ urvīḥ skambhaḥ idam viśvam bhuvanam ā viveśa  
yaḥ śramāt tapasaḥ jātaḥ lokān sarvān samānaśe   somam yaḥ cakre kevalam tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ  
katham vātaḥ na ilayati katham na ramate manaḥ   kim āpaḥ satyam prepsantīḥ na ilayanti kadā cana  
mahat yakṣam bhuvanasya madhye tapasi krāntam salilasya pṛṣṭhe   tasmin śrayante ye u ke ca devāḥ vṛkṣasya skandhaḥ paritas iva śākhāḥ  
yasmai hastābhyām pādābhyām vācā śrotreṇa cakṣuṣā   yasmai devāḥ sadā balim prayacchanti vimite amitam skambham tam brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
apa tasya hatam tamaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ sa pāpmanā   sarvāṇi tasmin jyotīṃṣi yāni trīṇi prajāpatau  
yaḥ vetasam hiraṇyayam tiṣṭhantam salile veda   sa vai guhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ  
tantram eke yuvatī virūpe abhyākrāmam vayataḥ ṣaṣ mayūkham   pra anyā tantūn tirate dhatte anyā na apa vṛñjāte na gamātaḥ antam  
tayoḥ aham parinṛtyantyoḥ iva na vi jānāmi yatarā parastāt   pumān enat vayati ud gṛṇanti pumān enat vi jabhāra adhi nāke  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
yaḥ bhūtam ca bhavyam ca sarvam yaḥ ca adhitiṣṭhati   su aryasya ca kevalam tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ  
skambhena ime viṣṭabhite dyauḥ ca bhūmiḥ ca tiṣṭhataḥ   skambhaḥ idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat nimiṣat ca yat  
tisraḥ ha prajāḥ atyāyam āyan ni anyāḥ arkam abhitas aviśanta   bṛhan ha tasthau rajasaḥ vimānaḥ haritaḥ hariṇīḥ ā viveśa  
dvādaśa pradhayaḥ cakram ekam trīṇi nabhyāni kaḥ u tat ciketa   tatra āhatāḥ trīṇi śatāni śaṅkavaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ ca khīlāḥ avicācalāḥ ye  
idam savitar vi jānīhi ṣaṭ yamāḥ ekaḥ ekajaḥ   tasmin ha apitvam ichante yaḥ eṣām ekaḥ ekajaḥ  
āvis san nihitam guhā jarat nāma mahat padam   tatra idam sarvam ārpitam ejat prāṇat pratiṣṭhitam  
eka cakram vartate eka nemi sahasra akṣaram pra puras ni paścā   ardhena viśvam bhuvanam jajāna yat asya ardham kva tat babhūva  
pañca vāhī vahati agram eṣām praṣṭayaḥ yuktāḥ anusaṃvahanti   a yātam asya dadṛśe na yātam param nedīyaḥ avaram davīyaḥ  
tiryak bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva budhnaḥ tasmin yaśaḥ nihitam viśva rūpam   tat āsate ṛṣayaḥ sapta sākam ye asya gopāḥ mahataḥ babhūvuḥ  
yā purastāt yujyate yā ca paścāt yā viśvatas yujyate yā ca sarvatas   yayā yajñaḥ prāṅ tāyate tām tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām     tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām       tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām       tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām     tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām     tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām     tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām     tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛcām     tvā pṛcchāmi katamā sā ṛc
yat ejati patati yat ca tiṣṭhati prāṇat a prāṇat nimiṣat ca yat bhuvat   tat dādhāra pṛthivīm viśva rūpam tat saṃbhūya bhavati ekam eva  
anantam vitatam purutra anantam antavat ca ā samante   te nākapālaḥ carati vicinvan vidvān bhūtam uta bhavyam asya  
prajāpatiḥ carati garbhe antar a dṛśyamānaḥ bahudhā vi jāyate   ardhena viśvam bhuvanam jajāna yat asya ardham katamaḥ sa ketuḥ  
ūrdhvam bharantam udakam kumbhena iva udahāryam   paśyanti sarve cakṣuṣā na sarve manasā viduḥ  
dūre pūrṇena vasati dūre ūnena hīyate   mahat yakṣam bhuvanasya madhye tasmai balim rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ bharanti  
yatas sūryaḥ udeti astam yatra ca gacchati   tat eva manye aham jyeṣṭham tat u na ati eti kim cana  
ye arvāk madhye uta vā purāṇam vedam vidvāṃsam abhitas vadanti   ādityam eva te pari vadanti sarve agnim dvitīyam trivṛtam ca haṃsam  
sahasrāhṇyam viyatau asya pakṣau hareḥ haṃsasya patataḥ svargam   sa devān sarvān urasi upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā  
satyena ūrdhvaḥ tapati brahmaṇā arvāṅ vi paśyati   prāṇena tiryaṅ prāṇati yasmin jyeṣṭham adhi śritam  
yaḥ vai te vidyāt araṇī yābhyām nirmathyate vasu   sa vidvān jyeṣṭham manyeta sa vidyāt brāhmaṇam mahat   sa vidvān jyeṣṭham manyeta sa vidyāt brāhmaṇam mahat                                                                                                                                                                  
apād agre sam abhavat saḥ agre svar ābharat   catuṣpād bhūtvā bhogyaḥ sarvam ādatta bhojanam  
bhogyaḥ bhavat atha u annam adat bahu   yaḥ devam uttarāvantam upāsātai sanātanam  
sanātanam enam āhuḥ uta adya syāt punarṇavaḥ   ahar rātre pra jāyete anyaḥ anyasya rūpayoḥ  
śatam sahasram ayutam nyarbudam asaṃkhyeyam svam asmin niviṣṭam   tat asya ghnanti abhipaśyataḥ eva tasmāt devaḥ rocat eṣaḥ etat  
bālāt ekam aṇīyaskam uta ekam na iva dṛśyate   tatas pariṣvajīyasī devatā sā mama priyā  
iyam kalyāṇā ajarā martyasya amṛtā gṛhe   yasmai kṛtā śaye sa yaḥ cakāra jajāra saḥ  
tvam strī tvam pumān asi tvam kumāraḥ uta vā kumārī 
tvam jīrṇaḥ daṇḍena vañcasi tvam jātaḥ bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ 
uta eṣām pitā uta vā putraḥ eṣām uta eṣām jyeṣṭhaḥ uta vā kaniṣṭhaḥ   ekaḥ ha devaḥ manasi praviṣṭaḥ prathamaḥ jātaḥ saḥ u garbhe antar  
pūrṇāt pūrṇam ud acati pūrṇam pūrṇena sicyate   uta u tat adya vidyāma yatas tat pariṣicyate  
eṣā sanatnī sanam eva jātā eṣā purāṇī pari sarvam babhūva   mahī devī uṣasaḥ vibhātī sā ekena ekena miṣatā vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi caṣṭe   vi 
aviḥ vai nāma devatā ṛtena āste parīvṛtā   tasyāḥ rūpeṇa ime vṛkṣāḥ haritāḥ harita srajaḥ  
anti santam na jahāti anti santam na paśyati   devasya paśya kāvyam na mamāra na jīryati  
apūrveṇa iṣitāḥ vācaḥ tāḥ vadanti yathāyatham   vadantīḥ yatra gacchanti tat āhuḥ brāhmaṇam mahat  
yatra devāḥ ca manuṣyāḥ cārāḥ nābhau iva śritāḥ   apām tvā puṣpam pṛchāmi yatra tat māyayā hitam  
yebhiḥ vātaḥ iṣitaḥ pravāti ye dadante pañca diśaḥ sadhrīcīḥ   ye āhutim atyamanyanta devāḥ apām netāraḥ katame te āsan  
imām eṣām pṛthivīm vaste ekaḥ antarikṣam pari ekaḥ babhūva   divam eṣām dadate yaḥ vidhartā viśvāḥ āśāḥ prati rakṣanti eke  
yaḥ vidyāt sūtram vitatam yasmin otāḥ prajāḥ imāḥ   sūtram sūtrasya yaḥ vidyāt sa vidyāt brāhmaṇam mahat  
veda aham sūtram vitatam yasmin otāḥ prajāḥ imāḥ   sūtram sūtrasya aham veda atha u yat brāhmaṇam mahat  
yat antarā dyāvāpṛthivī agniḥ ait pradahan viśvadāvyaḥ   yatra atiṣṭhan eka patnīḥ parastāt kva iva āsīt mātariśvā tadānīm  
apsu āsīt mātariśvā praviṣṭaḥ praviṣṭāḥ devāḥ salilāni āsan 
bṛhan ha tasthau rajasaḥ vimānaḥ pavamānaḥ haritaḥ ā viveśa  
uttareṇa iva gayatrīm amṛte adhi vi cakrame   sāmnā ye sāma saṃviduḥ ajaḥ tat dadṛśe kva  
niveśanaḥ saṃgamanaḥ vasūnām devaḥ iva savitā satya dharmā   indraḥ na tasthau samare dhanānām  
puṇḍarīkam nava dvāram tribhiḥ guṇebhiḥ āvṛtam   tasmin yat yakṣam ātmanvat tat vai brahma vidaḥ viduḥ  
akāmaḥ dhīraḥ amṛtaḥ svayaṃbhuḥ rasena tṛptaḥ na kutas cana ūnaḥ   tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyoḥ ātmānam dhīram ajaram yuvānam   tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyoḥ ātmānam dhīram ajaram yuvānam   tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyoḥ ātmānam dhīram ajaram yuvānam   tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyoḥ ātmānam dhīram ajaram yuvānam   tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyoḥ ātmānam dhīram ajaram yuvānam   tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyo
aghāyatām api nahyā mukhāni sapatneṣu vajram arpaya etam   indreṇa dattā prathamā śata odanā bhrātṛvya ghnī yajamānasya gātuḥ  
vediḥ te carma bhavatu barhiḥ lomāni yāni te   eṣā tvā raśanā agrabhīt grāvā tvā eṣaḥ adhi nṛtyatu  
bālāḥ te prokṣaṇīḥ santu jīhvā sam mārṣṭu aghnye   śuddhā tvam yajñiyā bhūtvā divam prehi śata odane  
yaḥ śata odanām pacati kāmapreṇa sa kalpate   prītāḥ hi asya ṛtvijaḥ sarve yanti yathāyatham  
sa svargam ā rohati yatra adaḥ tridivam divaḥ   apūpa nābhim kṛtvā yaḥ dadāti śata odanām  
sa tān lokān sam āpnoti ye divyāḥ ye ca pārthivāḥ   hiraṇyajyotiṣam kṛtvā yaḥ dadāti śata odanām  
ye te devi śamitāraḥ paktāraḥ ye ca te janāḥ   te tvā sarve gopsyanti mā ebhyaḥ bhaiṣīḥ śata odane  
vasavaḥ tvā dakṣiṇatas uttarāt marutaḥ tvā   ādityāḥ paścāt gopsyanti sā agniṣṭomam ati drava  
devāḥ pitaraḥ manuṣyāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ ca ye  te tvā sarve gopsyanti sā atirātram ati drava  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
ghṛtam prokṣantī subhagā devī devān gamiṣyati   paktāram aghnye mā hiṃsīḥ divam prehi śata odane  
ye devāḥ diviṣadaḥ antarikṣa sadaḥ ca ye ye ca ime bhūmyām adhi   tebhyaḥ tvam dhukṣva sarvadā kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu  
yat te śiraḥ yat te mukham yau karṇau ye ca te hanū   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yau te oṣṭhau ye nāsike ye śṛṅge ye ca te akṣiṇī   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yat te klomāḥ yat dhṛdayam purītat sahakaṇṭhikā   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yat te yakṛt ye matasne yat āntram yāḥ ca te gudāḥ   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yaḥ te plāśiḥ yaḥ vaniṣṭhuḥ yau kukṣī yat ca carma te   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu  
yat te majjā yat asthi yat maṃsam yat ca lohitam   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yau te bāhū ye doṣaṇī yau aṃsau yā ca te kakud   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yāḥ te grīvāḥ ye skandhāḥ yāḥ pṛṣṭīḥ yāḥ ca parśavaḥ   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīra

yat te pucham ye te bālāḥ yat ūdhar ye ca te stanāḥ   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yāḥ te jaṅghāḥ yāḥ kuṣṭhikāḥ ṛcharāḥ ye ca te śaphāḥ   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atho madhu  
yat te carma śata odane yāni lomāni aghnye   āmikṣām duhratām dātre kṣīram sarpiḥ atha u madhu  
kroḍau te stām purodāśau ājyena abhighāritau   tau pakṣau devi kṛtvā sā paktāram divam vaha  
ulūkhale musale yaḥ ca carmaṇi yaḥ vā śūrpe taṇḍulaḥ kaṇaḥ   yam vā vātaḥ mātariśvā pavamānaḥ mamātha agniḥ tat hotā su hutam kṛṇotu  
apaḥ devīḥ madhumatīḥ ghṛtaścutaḥ brahmaṇām hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi   yad kāmaḥ idam abhiṣiñcāmi vaḥ aham tat me sarvam sam padyatām vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām     tad kāmaḥ idam abhiṣiñcāmi vaḥ aham tat me sarvam sam padyatām vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām     tat kāmaḥ idam abhiṣiñcāmi vaḥ aham tat me sarvam sam padyatām vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām     tat kāmaḥ idam abhiṣiñcāmi vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇā
namaḥ te jāyamānāyai jātāyai uta te namaḥ   bālebhyaḥ śaphebhyaḥ rūpāya aghnye te namaḥ  
yaḥ vidyāt sapta pravataḥ sapta vidyāt parāvataḥ   śiraḥ yajñasya yaḥ vidyāt sa vaśām prati gṛhṇīyāt  
veda aham sapta pravataḥ sapta veda parāvataḥ   śiraḥ yajñasya aham veda somam ca asyām vicakṣaṇam  
yayā dyauḥ yayā pṛthivī yayā apaḥ gupitāḥ imāḥ   vaśām sahasra dhārām brahmaṇā āchāvadāmasi  
śatam kaṃsāḥ śatam dogdhāraḥ śatam goptāraḥ adhi pṛṣṭhe asyāḥ   ye devāḥ tasyām prāṇanti te vaśām viduḥ ekadhā  
yajña padīrā akṣīrā svadhā prāṇā mahīlukā   vaśā parjanya patnī devām api eti brahmaṇā  
anu tvā agniḥ prāviśat anu somaḥ vaśe tvā   ūdhar te bhadre parjanyaḥ vidyutaḥ te stanāḥ vaśe  
apaḥ tvam dhukṣe prathamāḥ urvarāḥ aparāḥ vaśe   tṛtīyam rāṣṭram dhukṣe annam kṣīram vaśe tvam  
yat ādityaiḥ hūyamānā upātiṣṭha ṛtavari   indraḥ sahasram pātrān somam tvā apāyayat vaśe  
yat anūcī indram aiḥ āt tvā ṛṣabhaḥ ahvayat   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram kruddhaḥ aharat vaśe   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram kruddhaḥ aharat vaśe   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram kruddhaḥ aharat vaśe   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram kruddhaḥ aharat vaśe   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram kruddhaḥ aharat vaśe   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram kruddhaḥ aharat vaśe   tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīram krud
yat te kruddhaḥ dhanapatiḥ ā kṣīram aharat vaśe   idam tat adya nākaḥ triṣu pātreṣu rakṣati  
triṣu pātreṣu tam somam ā devī aharat vaśā   atharvā yatra dīkṣitaḥ barhiṣi āsta hiraṇyaye  
sam hi somena āgata sam u sarveṇa padvatā   vaśā samudram adhi aṣṭhat gandharvaiḥ kalibhiḥ saha  
sam hi vātena agata sam u sarvaiḥ patatribhiḥ   vaśā samudre prānṛtyat ṛcaḥ sāmāni bibhratī  
sam hi sūryeṇa āgata sam u sarveṇa cakṣuṣā   vaśā samudram ati akhyat bhadrā jyotīṃṣi bibhratī  
abhīvṛtā hiraṇyena yat atiṣṭhaḥ ṛtāvari   aśvaḥ samudraḥ bhūtvā adhi askandat vaśe tvā  
tat bhadrāḥ sam agacchanta vaśā deṣṭrī atho svadhā   atharvā yatra dīkṣitaḥ barhiṣī āsta hiraṇyaye  
vaśā mātā rājanyasya vaśā mātā svadhe tava   vaśāyāḥ yajñe āyudham tatas cittam ajāyata  
ūrdhvaḥ binduḥ ud acarat brahmaṇaḥ kakudāt adhi   tatas tvam jajñiṣe vaśe tatas hotā ajāyata  
āsnaḥ te gāthāḥ abhavan uṣṇihābhyaḥ balam vaśe   pājasyāt jajñe yajñaḥ stanebhyaḥ raśmayaḥ tava                                                                            
īrmābhyām ayanam jātam sakthibhyām ca vaśe tava   āntrebhyaḥ jajñire atrāḥ udarāt adhi vīrudhaḥ  
yat udaram varuṇasya anuprāviśathāḥ vaśe   tatas tvā brahmā ud ahvayat sa hi netram avet tava  
sarve garbhāt avepanta jāyamānāt asūsvaḥ   sasūva hi tām āhu vaśā iti brahmabhiḥ kḷptaḥ sa hi asyāḥ bandhuḥ  
yudhaḥ ekaḥ sam sṛjati yaḥ asyāḥ ekaḥ id vaśī   tarāṃsi yajñāḥ abhavan tarasām cakṣuḥ abhavat vaśā  
vaśā yajñam prati agṛhṇāt vaśā sūryam adhārayat   vaśāyām antar aviśat odanaḥ brahmaṇā saha  
vaśām eva amṛtam āhuḥ vaśām mṛtyum upāsate   vaśā idam sarvam abhavat devāḥ manuṣyāḥ asurāḥ pitaraḥ ṛṣayaḥ  
yaḥ evam vidyāt sa vaśām prati gṛhṇīyāt   tathā hi yajñaḥ sarvapād duhe dātre an apasphuran  
tisraḥ jihvāḥ varuṇasya antar dīdyati āsani   tāsām yā madhye rājati sā vaśā duṣpratigrahā  
caturdhā retaḥ abhavat vaśāyāḥ   āpaḥ turīyam amṛtam turīyam yajñaḥ turīyam paśavaḥ turīyam  
vaśā dyauḥ vaśā pṛthivī vaśā viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ   vaśāyāḥ dugdham apiban sādhyāḥ vasavaḥ ca ye

somam enām eke duhre ghṛtam eke upāsate   ye evam viduṣe vaśām daduḥ te gatāḥ tridivam divaḥ  
brāhmaṇebhyaḥ vaśām dattvā sarvān lokān sam aśnute   ṛtam hi asyām ārpitam api brahma atho tapaḥ

agne jāyasva aditiḥ nāthitā iyam brahmaudanam pacati putra kāmā   sapta ṛṣayaḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ te tvā manthantu prajayā saha iha  
kṛṇuta dhūmam vṛṣaṇaḥ sakhāyaḥ adroghāvitā vācam acha   ayam agniḥ pṛtanāṣāh su vīraḥ yena devāḥ asahanta dasyūn  
agne ajaniṣṭhāḥ mahate vīryāya brahmaudanāya paktave jātavedaḥ   sapta ṛṣayaḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ te tvā ajījanan asyai rayim sarva vīram ni yaccha  
samiddhaḥ agne samidhā sam idhyasva vidvān devān yajñiyān ā iha vakṣaḥ   tebhyaḥ haviḥ śrapayam jātavedaḥ uttamam nākam adhi rohaya imam  
tredhā bhāgaḥ nihitaḥ yaḥ purā vaḥ devānām pitṝṇām martyānām   aṃśām jānīdhvam vi bhajāmi tān vaḥ yaḥ devānām saḥ imām pārayāti  
agne sahasvān abhibhūḥ abhi id asi nīcaḥ ni ubja dviṣataḥ sapatnān   iyam mātrā mīyamānā mitā ca sajātān te bali hṛtaḥ kṛṇotu  
sākam sajātaiḥ payasā saha edhi ud ubja enām mahate vīryāya   ūrdhvaḥ nākasya adhi roha viṣṭapam svargaḥ lokaḥ iti yam vadanti  
iyam mahī prati gṛhṇātu carma pṛthivī devī sumanasyamānā   atha gacchema sukṛtasya lokam  
etau grāvāṇau sayujā yuṅdhi carmaṇi nirbindhi aṃśūn yajamānāya sādhu   avaghnatī ni jahi ye imām pṛtanyavaḥ ūrdhvam prajām udbharanti ud ūha  
gṛhāṇa grāvāṇau sakṛtau vīra haste ā te devāḥ yajñiyāḥ yajñam aguḥ   trayaḥ varāḥ yatamān tvam vṛṇīṣe tāḥ te samṛddhīḥ iha rādhayāmi   trayaḥ varāḥ yatamān tvam vṛṇīṣe tāḥ te samṛddhīḥ iha rādhayāmi   trayaḥ varāḥ yatamān tvam vṛṇīṣe tāḥ te samṛddhīḥ iha rādhayāmi   trayaḥ varāḥ yatamān tvam vṛṇīṣe tāḥ te samṛddhīḥ iha rādhayāmi   trayaḥ varāḥ yatamān tvam vṛṇīṣe tāḥ t
iyam te dhītiḥ idam u te janitram gṛhṇātu tvām aditiḥ śūra putrā   parā punīhi yaḥ imām pṛtanyavaḥ asyai rayim sarva vīram ni yaccha  
upaśvase druvaye sīdata yūyam vi vicyadhvam yajñiyāsaḥ tuṣaiḥ   śriyā samānān ati sarvān syāma adhaspadam dviṣataḥ pādayāmi  
parehi nāri punar ehi kṣipram apām tvā goṣṭhaḥ adhi arukṣat bharāya   tāsām gṛhṇītāt yatamāḥ yajñiyāḥ asan vibhājya dhīrītarāḥ jahītāt  
emāḥ aguḥ yoṣitaḥ śumbhamānāḥ ud tiṣṭha nāri tavasam rabhasva   su patnī patyā prajayā prajāvatī ā tvā agan yajñaḥ prati kumbham gṛbhāya  
ūrjaḥ bhāgaḥ nihitaḥ yaḥ purā vaḥ ṛṣi praśiṣṭā apaḥ ā bhara etāḥ   ayam yajñaḥ gātu vid nātha vid prajā vid ugraḥ paśu vid vīra vid vaḥ astu  
agne caruḥ yajñiyaḥ tvā adhi arukṣat śuciḥ tapiṣṭhaḥ tapasā tapa enam   ārṣeyāḥ daivāḥ abhisaṃgatya bhāgam imam tapiṣṭhāḥ ṛtubhiḥ tapantu  
śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ yoṣitaḥ yajñiyāḥ imāḥ āpaḥ carum ava sarpantu śubhrāḥ   aduḥ prajām bahulām paśūn naḥ paktā odanasya su kṛtām etu lokam  
brahmaṇā śuddhāḥ uta pūtāḥ ghṛtena somasya aṃśavaḥ taṇḍulāḥ yajñiyāḥ ime   apaḥ pra viśata prati gṛhṇātu vaḥ caruḥ imam paktvā su kṛtām eta lokam  
uruḥ prathasva mahatā mahimnā sahasra pṛṣṭhaḥ su kṛtasya loke   pitāmahāḥ pitaraḥ prajā upajā aham paktā pañcadaśaḥ te asmi  
sahasra pṛṣṭhaḥ śata dhāraḥ akṣitaḥ brahmaudanaḥ deva yānaḥ svar gaḥ   amūn te ā dadhāmi prajayā reṣaya enān bali hārāya mṛḍatāt mahyam eva    
udehi vedim prajayā vardhaya enām nudasva rakṣaḥ prataram dhehi enām   śriyā samānān ati sarvān syāma adhaspadam dviṣataḥ pādayāmi  
abhyāvartasva paśubhiḥ saha enām pratyaṅ enām devatābhiḥ saha edhi   mā tvā prāpat śapathaḥ mā abhicāraḥ sve kṣetre anamīvā vi rāja  
ṛtena taṣṭā manasā hitā eṣā brahmaudanasya vihitā vediḥ agre   aṃsadhrīm śuddhām upa dhehi nāri tatra odanam sādaya daivānām  
aditeḥ hastām srucam etām dvitīyām sapta ṛṣayaḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ yām akṛṇvan   sā gātrāṇi viduṣī odanasya darviḥ vedyām adhi enam cinotu  
śṛtam tvā havyam upa sīdantu daivāḥ niḥsṛpya agneḥ punar enān pra sīda   somena pūtaḥ jaṭhare sīda brahmaṇām ārṣeyāḥ te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ  
soma rājan saṃjñānam ā vapa ebhyaḥ subrāhmaṇāḥ yatame tvā upasīdān   ṛṣīn ārṣeyān tapasaḥ adhi jātān brahmaudane su havā johavīmi  
śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ yoṣitaḥ yajñiyāḥ imāḥ brahmaṇām hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi   yad kāmaḥ idam abhiṣiñcāmi vaḥ aham indraḥ marutvān sa dadāt idam me  
idam me jyotiḥ amṛtam hiraṇyam pakvam kṣetrāt kāmadughā me eṣā   idam dhanam ni dadhe brāhmaṇeṣu kṛṇve panthām pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ  
agnau tuṣān ā vapa jātavedasi paras kambūkām apa mṛḍḍhi dūram   etam śuśruma gṛharājasya bhāgam atho vidma nirṛteḥ bhāgadheyam  
śrāmyataḥ pacataḥ viddhi sunvataḥ panthām svargam adhi rohaya enam   yena rohāt param āpadya yat vayaḥ uttamam nākam paramam vyoma                                                                                                                                                                                        
babhreḥ adhvaryo mukham etat vi mṛḍḍhi ājyāya lokam kṛṇuhi pravidvān   ghṛtena gātrāḥ anu sarvā vi mṛḍḍhi kṛṇve panthām pitṛṣu yaḥ svar gaḥ  
babhre rakṣaḥ samadam ā vapa ebhyaḥ a brāhmaṇāḥ yatame tvā upasīdān   purīṣiṇaḥ prathamānāḥ purastāt ārṣeyāḥ te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ  
ārṣeyeṣu ni dadhe odana tvā nānā ārṣeyāṇām api asti atra   agniḥ me goptā marutaḥ ca sarve viśve devāḥ abhi rakṣantu pakvam  
yajñam duhānam sadam id prapīnam pumāṃsam dhenum sadanam rayīṇām   prajā amṛta tvam uta dīrgham āyuḥ rāyaḥ ca poṣaiḥ upa tvā sadema  
vṛṣabhaḥ asi svarge ṛṣīn ārṣeyān gaccha   su kṛtām loke sīda tatra nau saṃskṛtam

yena devāḥ jyotiṣā dyām udāyan brahmaudanam paktvā su kṛtasya lokam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nākam uttamam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nākam uttamam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nākam uttamam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nākam uttamam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nākam uttamam   tena geṣma su kṛtasya lokam svar ārohantaḥ abhi nāk
bhava śarvau mṛḍatam mā abhi yātam bhūtapatī paśupatī namaḥ vām   pratihitām āyatām mā vi srāṣṭam mā naḥ hiṃsiṣṭam dvipadaḥ mā catuṣpadaḥ  
śune kroṣṭre mā śarīrāṇi kartam ali klavebhyaḥ gṛdhrebhyaḥ ye ca kṛṣṇāḥ aviṣyavaḥ   makṣikāḥ te paśupate vayāṃsi te vighase mā vidanta  
krandāya te prāṇāya yāḥ ca te bhava ropayaḥ   namaḥ te rudra kṛṇmaḥ sahasrākṣāya amartya  
purastāt te namaḥ kṛṇmaḥ uttarāt adharāt uta   abhīvargāt divaḥ pari antarikṣāya te namaḥ  
mukhāya te paśupate yāni cakṣūṃṣi te bhava   tvace rūpāya saṃdṛśe pratīcīnāya te namaḥ  
aṅgebhyaḥ te udarāya jihvāyāḥ āsyāya te   dadbhyaḥ gandhāya te namaḥ  
astrā nīla śikhaṇḍena sahasrākṣeṇa vājinā   rudreṇa ardhaka ghātinā tena mā sam arāmahi  
sa naḥ bhavaḥ pari vṛṇaktu viśvatas āpaḥ iva agniḥ pari vṛṇaktu naḥ bhavaḥ   mā naḥ abhi māṃsta namaḥ astu asmai  
catuḥ namaḥ aṣṭa kṛtvas bhavāya daśa kṛtvas paśupate namaḥ te   tava ime pañca paśavaḥ vibhaktāḥ gāvaḥ aśvāḥ puruṣāḥ aja avayaḥ  
tava catasraḥ pradiśaḥ tava dyauḥ tava pṛthivī tava idam ugrā uru antarikṣam   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu   tava idam sarvam ātmanvat yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu  
uruḥ kośaḥ vasu dhānaḥ tava ayam yasmin imā viśvā bhuvanāni antar   sa naḥ mṛḍa paśupate namaḥ te paras kroṣṭāraḥ abhibhāḥ śvānaḥ paras yantu agharudaḥ vikeśyaḥ  
dhanuḥ bibharṣi haritam hiraṇyayam sahasra ghnim śata vadham śikhaṇḍin   rudrasya iṣuḥ carati deva hetiḥ tasyai namaḥ yatamasyām diśi itas  
yaḥ abhiyātaḥ nilayate tvām rudra nicikīrṣati   paścāt anuprayuṅkṣe tam viddhasya padanīḥ iva  
bhava rudrau sayujā saṃvidānau ubhau ugrau carataḥ vīryāya   tābhyām namaḥ yatamasyām diśi itas  
namaḥ te astu āyate namaḥ astu parāyate   namaḥ te rudra tiṣṭhate āsīnāya uta te namaḥ  
namaḥ sāyam namaḥ prātar namaḥ rātryāḥ namaḥ divā   bhavāya ca śarvāya ca ubhābhyām akaram namaḥ  
sahasrākṣam atipaśyam purastāt rudram asyantam bahudhā vipaścitam   mā upārāma jihvayā īyamānam  
śyāva aśvam kṛṣṇam asitam mṛṇantam bhīmam ratham keśinaḥ pādayantam   pūrve pratīmaḥ namaḥ astu asmai  
mā naḥ abhi srāḥ matyam deva hetim mā naḥ krudhaḥ paśupate namaḥ te   anyatra asmat divyām śākhām vi dhūnu  
mā naḥ hiṃsīḥ adhi naḥ brūhi pari naḥ vṛṅdhi mā krudhaḥ   mā tvayā sam arāmahi                                                                                                                                                                                                             
mā naḥ goṣu puruṣeṣu mā gṛdhaḥ naḥ aja aviṣu   anyatra ugra vi vartaya piyārūṇām prajām jahi  
yasya takmā kāsikā hetiḥ ekam aśvasya iva vṛṣaṇaḥ krandaḥ eti   abhipūrvam nirṇayate namaḥ astu asmai  
yaḥ antarikṣe tiṣṭhati viṣṭabhitaḥ a yajvanaḥ pramṛṇan deva pīyūn   tasmai namaḥ daśabhiḥ śakvarībhiḥ  
tubhyam āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ mṛgāḥ vane hitāḥ haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunāḥ vayāṃsi   tava yakṣam paśupate apsu antar tubhyam kṣaranti divyāḥ āpaḥ vṛdhe  
śiṃśumārāḥ ajagarāḥ purīkayā jaṣāḥ matsyāḥ rajasā yebhyaḥ asyasi   na te dūram na pariṣṭhā asti te bhava sadyas sarvām pari paśyasi bhūmim pūrvasmāt dhaṃsi uttarasmin samudre  
mā naḥ rudra takmanā mā viṣeṇa mā naḥ sam srāḥ divyena agninā   anyatra asmat vidyutam pātaya etām  
bhavaḥ divaḥ bhavaḥ īśe pṛthivyāḥ bhavaḥ ā papre uru antarikṣam   tasyai namaḥ yatamasyām diśi itas  
bhava rājan yajamānāya mṛḍa paśūnām hi paśupatiḥ babhūtha   yaḥ śraddadhāti santi devāḥ iti catuṣpade dvipade asya mṛḍa  
mā naḥ mahāntam uta mā naḥ arbhakam mā naḥ vahantam uta mā naḥ vakṣyataḥ   mā naḥ hiṃsīḥ pitaram mātaram ca svām tanvam rudra mā rīriṣaḥ naḥ

tasya odanasya bṛhaspatiḥ śiraḥ brahma mukham

cakṣuḥ musalam kāmaḥ ulūkhalam 
ditiḥ śūrpam aditiḥ śūrpa grāhī vātaḥ apāvinak  
aśvāḥ kaṇāḥ gāvaḥ taṇḍulāḥ maśakāḥ tuṣāḥ 
kabru phalīkaraṇāḥ śaraḥ abhram 
śyāmam ayaḥ asya māṃsāni lohitam asya lohitam 
trapu bhasma haritam varṇaḥ puṣkaram asya gandhaḥ

sītāḥ parśavaḥ sikatāḥ ūbadhyam 
ṛtam hasta avanejanam kulyā upasecanam

odanena yajñavataḥ sarve lokāḥ samāpyāḥ 
yasmin samudraḥ dyauḥ bhūmiḥ trayaḥ avara param śritāḥ  
yasya devāḥ akalpanta ucchiṣṭe ṣaṭ aśītayaḥ 
tam tvā odanasya pṛchāmi yaḥ asya mahimā mahān 
sa yaḥ odanasya mahimānam vidyāt 
na alpaḥ iti brūyāt na anupasecanaḥ iti na idam ca kim ca iti 
yāvat dātā abhimanasyeta tat na ati vadet 
brahma vādinaḥ vadanti parāñcam odanam prāśīḥ pratyañcam iti 
tvam odanam prāśīḥ tvām odana iti 
parāñcam ca enam prāśīḥ prāṇāḥ tvā hāsyanti iti enam āha 
pratyañcam ca enam prāśīḥ apānāḥ tvā hāsyanti iti enam āha 
na eva aham odanam na mām odanaḥ 
odane eva odanam prāśīt                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
tatas ca enam anyena śīrṣṇā prāśīḥ yena ca etam pūrve ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan   jyeṣṭhataḥ te prajā mariṣyati iti enam āha   tam vai aham na arvāñcam na parāñcam na pratyañcam   bṛhaspatinā śīrṣṇā   tena enam prāśiṣam tena enam ajīgamam   eṣa vai odanaḥ sarva aṅgaḥ sarva paruḥ sarva tanūḥ   sarva aṅgaḥ eva sarva paruḥ sarva tanūḥ sam bhavati yaḥ evam veda   yaḥ evam veda   yaḥ evam veda

sa yaḥ evam viduṣaḥ upadraṣṭā bhavati prāṇam ruṇaddhi                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
na ca prāṇam ruṇaddhi sarva jyānim jīyate  
 jyānim jīyate purā enam jarasaḥ prāṇaḥ jahāti                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
prāṇāya namaḥ yasya sarvam idam vaśe   yaḥ bhūtaḥ sarvasya īśvaraḥ yasmin sarvam pratiṣṭhitam  
namaḥ te prāṇa krandāya namaḥ te stanayitnave   namaḥ te prāṇa vidyute namaḥ te prāṇa varṣate  
yat prāṇaḥ stanayitnunā abhikrandati oṣadhīḥ   pra vīyante garbhān dadhate atha u bahvīḥ vi jāyante  
yat prāṇe ṛtau āgate abhikrandati oṣadhīḥ   sarvam tadā pra modate yat kim ca bhūmyām adhi  
yadā prāṇaḥ abhyavarṣīt varṣeṇa pṛthivīm mahīm   paśavaḥ tat pra modante mahaḥ vai naḥ bhaviṣyati  
abhivṛṣṭāḥ oṣadhayaḥ prāṇena sam avādiran   āyuḥ vai naḥ prātītaraḥ sarvā naḥ surabhīḥ akaḥ  
namaḥ te astu āyate namaḥ astu parāyate   namaḥ te prāṇa tiṣṭhate āsīnāya uta te namaḥ  
namaḥ te prāṇa prāṇate namaḥ astu apānate   parācīnāya te namaḥ pratīcīnāya te namaḥ sarvasmai te idam namaḥ  
yā te prāṇa priyā tanūḥ yā u te prāṇa preyasī   atha u yat bheṣajam tava tasya naḥ dhehi jīvase  
prāṇaḥ prajāḥ anu vaste pitā putram iva priyam   prāṇaḥ ha sarvasya īśvaraḥ yat ca prāṇati yat ca na  
prāṇaḥ mṛtyuḥ prāṇaḥ takmā prāṇam devāḥ upāsate   prāṇaḥ ha satya vādinam uttame loke ā dadhat  
prāṇaḥ virāj prāṇaḥ deṣṭrī prāṇam sarve upāsate   prāṇaḥ ha sūryaḥ candramāḥ prāṇam āhuḥ prajāpatim  
prāṇa apānau vrīhi yavau anaḍvān prāṇaḥ ucyate   yave ha prāṇaḥ āhitaḥ apānaḥ vrīhiḥ ucyate  
apānati prāṇati puruṣaḥ garbhe antarā   yadā tvam prāṇa jinvasi atha sa jāyate punar  
prāṇam āhuḥ mātariśvānam vātaḥ ha prāṇaḥ ucyate   prāṇe ha bhūtam bhavyam ca prāṇe sarvam pratiṣṭhitam  
ātharvaṇīḥ āṅgirasīḥ daivīḥ manuṣya jāḥ uta   oṣadhayaḥ pra jāyante yadā tvam prāṇa jinvasi  
yadā prāṇaḥ abhyavarṣīt varṣeṇa pṛthivīm mahīm   oṣadhayaḥ pra jāyante atha u yāḥ kāḥ ca vīrudhaḥ  
yaḥ te prāṇa idam veda yasmin ca asi pratiṣṭhitaḥ   sarve tasmai balim harān amuṣmin loke uttame  
yathā prāṇa bali hṛtaḥ tubhyam sarvāḥ prajāḥ imāḥ   eva tasmai balim harān yaḥ tvā śṛṇavat suśravaḥ

brahmacārīṣṇan carati rodasī ubhe tasmin devāḥ saṃmanasaḥ bhavanti   sa dādhāra pṛthivīm divam ca saḥ ācāryam tapasā piparti  
brahmacāriṇam pitaraḥ deva janāḥ pṛthak devāḥ anusaṃyanti sarve   gandharvāḥ enam anu āyan trayastriṃśat tri śatāḥ ṣaṣ sahasrāḥ sarvān sa devān tapasā piparti  
ācāryaḥ upanayamānaḥ brahmacāriṇam kṛṇute garbham antar   tam rātrīḥ tisraḥ udare bibharti tam jātam draṣṭum abhisaṃyanti devāḥ  
iyam samidh pṛthivī dyauḥ dvitīyā uta antarikṣam samidhā pṛṇāti   brahmacārī samidhā mekhalayā śrameṇa lokān tapasā piparti  
pūrvaḥ jātaḥ brahmaṇaḥ brahmacārī gharmam vasānaḥ tapasā ud atiṣṭhat   tasmāt jātam brāhmaṇam brahma jyeṣṭham devāḥ ca sarve amṛtena sākam  
brahmacārī eti samidhā samiddhaḥ kārṣṇam vasānaḥ dīkṣitaḥ dīrgha śmaśruḥ   sa sadyas eti pūrvasmāt uttaram samudram lokān saṃgṛbhya muhur ācarikrat  
brahmacārī janayan brahma apaḥ lokam prajāpatim parameṣṭhinam virājam   garbhaḥ bhūtvā amṛtasya yonau indraḥ ha bhūtvā asurān tatarha  
ācāryaḥ tatakṣa nabhasī ubhe ime urvī gambhīre pṛthivīm divam ca   te rakṣati tapasā brahmacārī tasmin devāḥ saṃmanasaḥ bhavanti

agnau sūrye candramasi mātariśvan brahmacārī apsu samidham ā dadhāti   tāsām arcīṃṣi pṛthak abhre caranti tāsām ājyam puruṣaḥ varṣam āpaḥ

brahmacārī brahma bhrājat bibharti tasmin devāḥ adhi viśve samotāḥ   prāṇa apānau janayan āt vyānam vācam manaḥ hṛdayam brahma medhām

agnim brūmaḥ vanaspatīn oṣadhīḥ uta vīrudhaḥ   indram bṛhaspatim sūryam te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
brūmaḥ rājānam varuṇam mitram viṣṇum atha u bhagam   aṃśam vivasvantam brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
brūmaḥ devam savitāram dhātāram uta pūṣaṇam   tvaṣṭāram agriyam brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
gandharva apsarasaḥ brūmaḥ aśvinā brahmaṇaspatim   aryamā nāma yaḥ devaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
ahar rātre idam brūmaḥ sūryācandramasau ubhā   viśvān ādityān brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
vātam brūmaḥ parjanyam antarikṣam atha u diśaḥ   āśāḥ ca sarvāḥ brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
muñcantu mā śapathyāt ahar rātre atha u uṣāḥ   somaḥ mā devaḥ muñcatu yam āhuḥ candramāḥ iti  
pārthivāḥ divyāḥ paśavaḥ āraṇyāḥ uta ye mṛgāḥ   śakuntān pakṣiṇaḥ brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
bhava śarvau idam brūmaḥ rudram paśupatiḥ ca yaḥ   iṣūḥ yāḥ eṣām saṃvidma tāḥ naḥ santu sadā śivāḥ  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
sapta ṛṣīn vai idam brūmaḥ apaḥ devīḥ prajāpatim   pitṝn yama śreṣṭhān brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ 
ye devāḥ diviṣadaḥ antarikṣa sadaḥ ca ye   pṛthivyām śakrāḥ ye śritāḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
ādityāḥ rudrāḥ vasavaḥ divi devāḥ atharvāṇaḥ   aṅgirasaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
yajñam brūmaḥ yajamānam ṛcaḥ sāmāni bheṣajā   yajūṃṣi hotrāḥ brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
pañca rājyāni vīrudhām soma śreṣṭhāni brūmaḥ   darbhaḥ bhaṅgaḥ yavaḥ sahaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
arāyān brūmaḥ rakṣāṃsi sarpān puṇyajanān pitṝn   mṛtyūn eka śatam brūmaḥ te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
ṛtūn brūmaḥ ṛtupatīn ārtavān uta hāyanān   samāḥ saṃvatsarān māsān te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
eta devāḥ dakṣiṇatas paścāt prāñcaḥ udeta   purastāt uttarāt śakrāḥ viśve devāḥ sametya te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
viśvān devān idam brūmaḥ satya sandhān ṛtāvṛdhaḥ   viśvābhiḥ patnībhiḥ saha te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
sarvān devān idam brūmaḥ satya sandhān ṛtāvṛdhaḥ   sarvābhiḥ patnībhiḥ saha te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
bhūtam brūmaḥ bhūta patim bhūtānām uta yaḥ vaśī   bhūtāni sarvā saṃgatya te naḥ muñcantu aṃhasaḥ  
yāḥ devīḥ pañca pradiśaḥ ye devāḥ dvādaśa ṛtavaḥ   saṃvatsarasya ye daṃṣṭrāḥ te naḥ santu sadā śivāḥ

ucchiṣṭe nāma rūpam ca ucchiṣṭe loke āhitaḥ   ucchiṣṭaḥ indraḥ ca agniḥ ca viśvam antar samāhitam  
ucchiṣṭe dyāvāpṛthivī viśvam bhūtam samāhitam   āpaḥ samudraḥ ucchiṣṭe candramāḥ vātaḥ āhitaḥ  
san ucchiṣṭe asan ca ubhau mṛtyuḥ vājaḥ prajāpatiḥ   laukyāḥ ucchiṣṭe āyattāḥ vraḥ ca draḥ ca api śrīḥ mayi  
dṛḍhaḥ dṛṃha sthiraḥ nyaḥ brahma viśvasṛjaḥ daśa   nābhim iva sarvatas cakram ucchiṣṭe devatāḥ śritāḥ  
ṛc sāma yajuḥ ucchiṣṭaḥ udgīthaḥ prastutam stutam   hiṅkāraḥ ucchiṣṭe svaraḥ sāmnaḥ meḍiḥ ca tat mayi  
aindrāgnam pāvamānam mahānāmnīḥ mahāvratam   ucchiṣṭe yajñasya aṅgāni antar garbhe iva mātari  
rājasūyam vājapeyam agniṣṭomaḥ tat adhvaraḥ   arka aśvamedhau ucchiṣṭe jīvabarhiḥ madintamaḥ  
agnyādheyam atha u dīkṣā kāmapraḥ chandasā saha   utsannāḥ yajñāḥ satrāṇi ucchiṣṭe adhi samāhitāḥ  
agnihotram ca śraddhā ca vaṣaṭkāraḥ vratam tapaḥ   dakṣiṇeṣṭam pūrtam ca ucchiṣṭe adhi samāhitāḥ  
 eka rātraḥ dvi rātraḥ sadyaḥkrīḥ prakrīḥ ukthyaḥ   otam nihitam ucchiṣṭe yajñasya aṇūni vidyayā                                                                                                            
catur rātraḥ pañca rātraḥ ṣaṣ rātraḥ ca ubhayaḥ saha   ṣoḍaśī sapta rātraḥ ca ucchiṣṭāt jajñire sarve ye yajñāḥ amṛte hitāḥ  
pratīhāraḥ nidhanam viśvajit ca abhijit ca yaḥ   sāhnā atirātrau ucchiṣṭe dvādaśa ahaḥ api tat mayi

nindāḥ ca vai anindāḥ ca yat ca hanta iti na iti ca   śarīram śraddhā dakṣiṇā aśraddhā ca anu prāviśan

ānandāḥ modāḥ pramudaḥ abhīmoda mudaḥ ca ye  hasaḥ nariṣṭāḥ nṛttāni śarīram anu prāviśan 
ālāpāḥ ca pralāpāḥ ca abhīlāpa lapaḥ ca ye  śarīram sarve prāviśan āyujaḥ prayujaḥ yujaḥ  
prāṇa apānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiḥ ca kṣitiḥ ca yā   vyāna udānau vāc manaḥ śarīreṇa te īyante  
āśiṣaḥ ca praśiṣaḥ ca saṃśiṣaḥ viśiṣaḥ ca yāḥ   cittāni sarve saṃkalpāḥ śarīram anu prāviśan  
āsteyīḥ ca vāsteyīḥ ca tvaraṇāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ ca yāḥ   guhyāḥ śukrāḥ sthūlāḥ apaḥ tāḥ bībhatsau asādayan  
asthi kṛtvā samidham tat aṣṭa apaḥ asādayan   retaḥ kṛtvā ājyam devāḥ puruṣam āviśan  
yāḥ āpaḥ yāḥ ca devatāḥ yāḥ virāj brahmaṇā saha   śarīram brahma prāviśat śarīre adhi prajāpatiḥ  
sūryaḥ cakṣuḥ vātaḥ prāṇam puruṣasya vi bhejire   atha asya itaram ātmānam devāḥ prāyacchan agnaye  
tasmāt vai vidvān puruṣam idam brahma iti manyate   sarvāḥ hi asmin devatāḥ gāvaḥ goṣṭhe iva āsate  
prathamena pramāreṇa tredhā viṣvaṅ vi gacchati   adaḥ ekena gacchati adaḥ ekena gacchati iha ekena ni sevate  
apsu stīmāsu vṛddhāsu śarīram antarā hitam   tasmim śavaḥ adhi antarā tasmāt śavaḥ adhi ucyate           
ye bāhavaḥ yāḥ iṣavaḥ dhanvanām vīryāṇi ca   asīn paraśūn āyudham citta ākūtam ca yat hṛdi   sarvam tat arbude tvam amitrebhyaḥ dṛśe kuru udārān ca pra darśaya  
ud tiṣṭhata sam nahyadhvam mitrāḥ deva janāḥ yūyam   saṃdṛṣṭāḥ guptāḥ vaḥ santu yā naḥ mitrāṇi arbude  
ud tiṣṭhatam ā rabhetām ādāna saṃdānābhyām   amitrāṇām senāḥ abhi dhattam arbude  
arbudiḥ nāma yaḥ devaḥ īśānaḥ ca nyarbudiḥ   yābhyām antarikṣam āvṛtam iyam ca pṛthivī mahī   tābhyām indra medibhyām aham jitam anu emi senayā  
ud tiṣṭha tvam deva jana arbude senayā saha   bhañjan amitrāṇām senām bhogebhiḥ pari vāraya  
sapta jātān nyarbudaḥ udārāṇām samīkṣayan   tebhiḥ tvam ājye hute sarvaiḥ ud tiṣṭha senayā  
pratighnāna aśru mukhī kṛdhukarṇī ca krośatu   vikeśī puruṣe hate radite arbude tava  
saṃkarṣantī karūkaram manasā putram ichantī   patim bhrātaram āt svān radite arbude tava  
ali klavāḥ jāṣka madāḥ gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ   dhvāṅkṣāḥ śakunayaḥ tṛpyantu amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava  
atho sarvam śvāpadam makṣikā tṛpyatu krimiḥ   pauruṣeye adhi kuṇape radite arbude tava                                                                                                                             adhi kuṇape radite arbude tava      
ā gṛhṇītam sam bṛhatam prāṇa apānāt nyarbude   nivāśāḥ ghoṣāḥ sam yantu amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava  
ud vepaya sam vijantām bhiyā amitrān sam sṛja   uru grāhaiḥ bāhu aṅkaiḥ vidhya amitrān nyarbude  
muhyantu eṣām bāhavaḥ citta ākūtam ca yat dhṛdi   mā eṣām ud śeṣi kim cana radite arbude tava  
pratighnānāḥ sam dhāvantu uraḥ paṭaurau āghnānāḥ   aghāriṇīḥ vikeśyaḥ rudatyaḥ puruṣe hate radite arbude tava  
śvanvatīḥ apsarasaḥ rūpakāḥ uta arbude   antaḥpātre rerihatīm riśām durṇihita eṣiṇīm   sarvāḥ tāḥ arbude tvam amitrebhyaḥ dṛśe kuru udārān ca pra darśaya  
khaḍūre adhicaṅkramām kharvikām kharva vāsinīm   ye udārāḥ antarhitāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ ca ye   sarpāḥ itarajanāḥ rakṣāṃsi  
catur daṃṣṭrām chyāvadataḥ kumbha muṣkām asṛk mukhān   su abhyasāḥ ye ca udbhyasāḥ  
ud vepaya tvam arbude amitrāṇām amūḥ sicaḥ   jayan ca jiṣṇuḥ ca amitrām jayatām indramedinau  
prablīnaḥ mṛditaḥ śayām hataḥ amitraḥ nyarbude   agni jihvāḥ dhūma śikhāḥ jayantīḥ yantu senayā  
tayā arbude praṇuttānām indraḥ hantu varaṃvaram   amitrāṇām śacīpatiḥ mā amīṣām moci kaḥ cana   amitrāṇām śacīpatiḥ mā amīṣām moci kaḥ cana   amitrāṇām śacīpatiḥ mā amīṣām moci kaḥ cana                                                                                                                                      
ud kasantu hṛdayāni ūrdhvaḥ prāṇaḥ ud īṣatu   śauṣkāsyam anu vartatām amitrān mā uta mitriṇaḥ  
ye ca dhīrāḥ ye ca adhīrāḥ parāñcaḥ badhirāḥ ca ye   tamasā ye ca tūparāḥ atho basta abhivāsinaḥ   sarvān tām arbude tvam amitrebhyaḥ dṛśe kuru udārān ca pra darśaya  
arbudiḥ ca triṣandhiḥ ca amitrān naḥ vi vidhyatām   yathā eṣām indra vṛtrahan hanāma śacīpate amitrāṇām sahasraśas  
vanaspatīn vānaspatyān oṣadhīḥ uta vīrudhaḥ   gandharva apsarasaḥ sarpān devān puṇyajanān pitṝn   sarvān tām arbude tvam amitrebhyaḥ dṛśe kuru udārān ca pra darśaya  
īśām vaḥ marutaḥ devaḥ ādityaḥ brahmaṇaspatiḥ   īśām vaḥ indraḥ ca agniḥ ca dhātā mitraḥ prajāpatiḥ   īśām vaḥ ṛṣayaḥ cakruḥ amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava  
teṣām sarveṣām īśānāḥ ud tiṣṭhata sam nahyadhvam   mitrāḥ deva janāḥ yūyam imam saṃgrāmam saṃjitya yathālokam vi tiṣṭhadhvam                                                                                                                                                                                 
ud tiṣṭhata sam nahyadhvam udārāḥ ketubhiḥ saha   sarpāḥ itarajanāḥ rakṣāṃsi amitrān anu dhāvata  
īśām vaḥ veda rājyam triṣandhe aruṇaiḥ ketubhiḥ saha   ye antarikṣe ye divi pṛthivyām ye ca mānavāḥ   triṣandheḥ te cetasi durṇāmānaḥ upāsatām  
ayaḥ mukhāḥ sūcī mukhāḥ atho vikaṅkatī mukhāḥ   kravya adaḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ ā sajantu amitrān vajreṇa triṣandhinā  
antar dhehi jātavedaḥ āditya kuṇapam bahu   triṣandheḥ iyam senā su hitā astu me vaśe  
ud tiṣṭha tvam deva jana arbude senayā saha   ayam baliḥ vaḥ āhutaḥ triṣandheḥ āhutiḥ priyā  
śitipadī sam dyatu śaravyā iyam catuṣpadī   kṛtye amitrebhyaḥ bhava triṣandheḥ saha senayā  
dhūma akṣī sam patatu kṛdhukarṇī ca krośatu   triṣandheḥ senayā jite aruṇāḥ santu ketavaḥ  
avāyantām pakṣiṇaḥ ye vayāṃsi antarikṣe divi ye caranti   śvāpadaḥ makṣikāḥ sam rabhantām āma adaḥ gṛdhrāḥ kuṇape radantām  
yām indreṇa saṃdhām samadhatthāḥ brahmaṇā ca bṛhaspate   tayā aham indra saṃdhayā sarvān devān iha huve itas jayata mā amutas  
bṛhaspatiḥ āṅgirasaḥ ṛṣayaḥ brahma saṃśitāḥ   asura kṣayaṇam vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣandhim divi āśrayan         vadham triṣand
yena asau guptaḥ ādityaḥ ubhau indraḥ ca tiṣṭhataḥ   triṣandhim devāḥ abhajanta ojase ca balāya ca  
sarvān lokān sam ajayan devāḥ āhutyā anayā   bṛhaspatiḥ āṅgirasaḥ vajram yam asiñcata asura kṣayaṇam vadham  
bṛhaspatiḥ āṅgirasaḥ vajram yam asiñcata asura kṣayaṇam vadham   tena aham amūm senām ni limpāmi bṛhaspate amitrān hanmi ojasā  
sarve devāḥ atyāyanti ye aśnanti vaṣaṭkṛtam   imām juṣadhvam āhutim itas jayata mā amutas  
sarve devāḥ atyāyantu triṣandheḥ āhutiḥ priyā   saṃdhām mahatīm rakṣata yayā agre asurāḥ jitāḥ  
vāyuḥ amitrāṇām iṣu agrāṇi āñcatu   indraḥ eṣām bāhūn prati bhanaktu mā śakan pratidhām iṣum   ādityaḥ eṣām astram vi nāśayatu candramāḥ yutām agatasya panthām  
yadi preyuḥ deva purā brahma varmāṇi cakrire   tanū pānam paripāṇam kṛṇvānāḥ yat upocire sarvam tat arasam kṛdhi  
kravyādā anuvartayat mṛtyunā ca purohitam   triṣandhe prehi senayā jaya amitrān pra padyasva  
triṣandhe tamasā tvam amitrān pari vāraya   pṛṣadājya praṇuttānām mā amīṣām moci kaḥ cana  
śitipadī sam patatu amitrāṇām amūḥ sicaḥ   muhyantu adya amūḥ senāḥ amitrāṇām nyarbude                                                                                                                                                                                                          
mūḍhāḥ amitrāḥ nyarbude jahi eṣām varaṃvaram   anayā jahi senayā  
yaḥ ca kavacī yaḥ ca akavacaḥ amitraḥ yaḥ ca ajmani   jyā pāśaiḥ kavaca pāśaiḥ ajmanā abhihataḥ śayām  
ye varmiṇaḥ ye avarmāṇaḥ amitrāḥ ye ca varmiṇaḥ   sarvān tām arbude hatām śvānaḥ adantu bhūmyām  
ye rathinaḥ ye a rathāḥ asādāḥ ye ca sādinaḥ   sarvān adantu tān hatān gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ  
sahasra kuṇapā śetām āmitrī senā samare vadhānām   vividdhā kakaja ākṛtā  
marmāvidham roruvatam suparṇaiḥ adantu duścitam mṛditam śayānam   yaḥ imām pratīcīm āhutim amitraḥ naḥ yuyutsati  
yām devāḥ anutiṣṭhanti yasyāḥ na asti virādhanam   tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣandhinā     tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣandhinā     tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣandhinā     tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣandhinā     tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣandhinā     tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣandhinā     tayā indraḥ hantu vṛtra hā vajreṇa triṣan
satyam bṛhat ṛtam ugram dīkṣā tapaḥ brahma yajñaḥ pṛthivīm dhārayanti   sā naḥ bhūtasya bhavyasya patnī urum lokam pṛthivī naḥ kṛṇotu  
asaṃbādham madhyataḥ mānavānām yasyāḥ udvataḥ pravataḥ samam bahu   nānā vīryāḥ oṣadhīḥ yā bibharti pṛthivī naḥ prathatām rādhyatām naḥ  
yasyām samudraḥ uta sindhuḥ āpaḥ yasyām annam kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ   yasyām idam jinvati prāṇat ejat sā naḥ bhūmiḥ pūrvapeye dadhātu  
yasyāḥ catasraḥ pradiśaḥ pṛthivyāḥ yasyām annam kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ   yā bibharti bahudhā prāṇat ejat sā naḥ bhūmiḥ goṣu api anne dadhātu  
yasyām pūrve pūrva janāḥ vicakrire yasyām devāḥ asurān abhyavartayan   gavām aśvānām vayasaḥ ca viṣṭhā bhagam varcaḥ pṛthivī naḥ dadhātu  
viśvaṃbharā vasu dhānī pratiṣṭhā hiraṇya vakṣāḥ jagataḥ niveśanī   vaiśvānaram bibhratī bhūmiḥ agnim indra ṛṣabhā draviṇe naḥ dadhātu  
yām rakṣanti asvapnāḥ viśvadānīm devāḥ bhūmim pṛthivīm apramādam   sā naḥ madhu priyam duhām atha u ukṣatu varcasā  
yā arṇave adhi salilam agre āsīt yām māyābhiḥ anvacarat manīṣiṇaḥ   yasyāḥ hṛdayam parame vyoman satyena āvṛtam amṛtam pṛthivyāḥ   sā naḥ bhūmiḥ tviṣim balam rāṣṭre dadhātu uttame  
yasyām āpaḥ paricarāḥ samānīḥ ahar rātre apramādam kṣaranti   sā naḥ bhūmiḥ bhūri dhārā payaḥ duhām atha u ukṣatu varcasā  
 indraḥ yām cakre ātmane anamitrām śacīpatiḥ   sā naḥ bhūmiḥ vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ      vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ     vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ     vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ     vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ     vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ     vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ     vi sṛjatām mātā putrāya me payaḥ                         
girayaḥ te parvatāḥ himavantaḥ araṇyam te pṛthivi syonam astu   babhrum kṛṣṇām rohiṇīm viśva rūpām dhruvām bhūmim pṛthivīm indra guptām   a jītaḥ a hataḥ akṣataḥ adhi aṣṭhām pṛthivīm aham  
yat te madhyam pṛthivi yat ca nabhyam yāḥ te ūrjaḥ tanvaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ   tāsu naḥ dhehi abhi naḥ pavasva mātā bhūmiḥ putraḥ aham pṛthivyāḥ parjanyaḥ pitā saḥ u naḥ pipartu  
yasyām vedim parigṛhṇanti bhūmyām yasyām yajñam tanvate viśvakarmāṇaḥ   yasyām mīyante svaravaḥ pṛthivyām ūrdhvāḥ śukrāḥ āhutyāḥ purastāt   sā naḥ bhūmiḥ vardhayat vardhamānā  
yaḥ naḥ dveṣat pṛthivi yaḥ pṛtanyāt yaḥ abhidāsāt manasā yaḥ vadhena   tam naḥ bhūme randhaya pūrva kṛtvari  
tvat jātāḥ tvayi caranti martyāḥ tvam bibharṣi dvipadaḥ tvam catuṣpadaḥ   tava ime pṛthivi pañca mānavāḥ yebhyaḥ jyotiḥ amṛtam martyebhyaḥ udyan sūryaḥ raśmibhiḥ ātanoti  
tāḥ naḥ prajāḥ sam duhratām samagrāḥ vācaḥ madhu pṛthivi dhehi mahyam 
viśvasvam mātaram oṣadhīnām dhruvām bhūmim pṛthivīm dharmaṇā dhṛtām   śivām syonām anu carema viśvahā  
mahat sadhastham mahatī babhūvitha mahān vegaḥ ejathuḥ vepathuḥ te   mahān tvā indraḥ rakṣati apramādam   sā naḥ bhūme pra rocaya hiraṇyasya iva saṃdṛśi mā naḥ dvikṣata kaḥ cana  
agniḥ bhūmyām oṣadhīṣu agnim āpaḥ bibhrati agniḥ aśmasu   agniḥ antar puruṣeṣu goṣu aśveṣu agnayaḥ  
agniḥ divaḥ ā tapati agneḥ devasya uru antarikṣam   agnim martāsaḥ indhate havyavāham ghṛta priyam   agnim martāsaḥ indhate havyavāham ghṛta priyam   agnim martāsaḥ indhate havyavāham ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam   ghṛta priyam
agni vāsāḥ pṛthivī asitajñūḥ tviṣīmantam saṃśitam mā kṛṇotu  
bhūmyām devebhyaḥ dadati yajñam havyam araṃkṛtam   bhūmyām manuṣyāḥ jīvanti svadhayā annena martyāḥ   sā naḥ bhūmiḥ prāṇam āyuḥ dadhātu jaradaṣṭim mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu  
yaḥ te gandhaḥ pṛthivi saṃbabhūva yam bibhrati oṣadhayaḥ yam āpaḥ   yam gandharvāḥ apsarasaḥ ca bhejire tena mā surabhim kṛṇu mā naḥ dvikṣata kaḥ cana  
yaḥ te gandhaḥ puṣkaram āviveśa yam saṃjabhruḥ sūryāyāḥ vivāhe   amartyāḥ pṛthivi gandham agre tena mā surabhim kṛṇu mā naḥ dvikṣata kaḥ cana  
yaḥ te gandhaḥ puruṣeṣu strīṣu puṃsu bhagaḥ ruciḥ   yaḥ aśveṣu vīreṣu yaḥ mṛgeṣu uta hastiṣu   kanyāyām varcaḥ yat bhūme tena asmān api sam sṛja mā naḥ dvikṣata kaḥ cana  
śilā bhūmiḥ aśmā pāṃsuḥ sā bhūmiḥ saṃdhṛtā dhṛtā   tasyai hiraṇya vakṣase pṛthivyāḥ akaram namaḥ  
yasyām vṛkṣāḥ vānaspatyāḥ dhruvāḥ tiṣṭhanti viśvahā   pṛthivīm viśva dhāyasam dhṛtām achāvadāmasi  
udīrāṇāḥ uta āsīnāḥ tiṣṭhantaḥ prakrāmantaḥ   padbhyām dakṣiṇa savyābhyām mā vyathiṣmahi bhūmyām  
vimṛgvarīm pṛthivīm ā vadāmi kṣamām bhūmim brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānām   ūrjam puṣṭam bibhratīm anna bhāgam ghṛtam tvā abhi ni sīdema bhūme  
 pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛthivi mā ud punāmi   pavitreṇa pṛt
yāḥ te prācīḥ pradiśaḥ yāḥ udīcīḥ yāḥ te bhūme adharāt yāḥ ca paścāt   syonāḥ tāḥ mahyam carate bhavantu mā ni paptam bhuvane śiśriyāṇaḥ  
mā naḥ paścāt mā purastāt nudiṣṭhāḥ mā uttarāt adharāt uta   svasti bhūme naḥ bhava mā vidan paripanthinaḥ varīyaḥ yāvaya vadham  
yāvat te abhi vipaśyāmi bhūme sūryeṇa medinā   tāvat me cakṣuḥ mā mā iṣṭa uttarām uttarām samām  
yat śayānaḥ paryāvarte dakṣiṇam sakhyam abhi bhūme pārśvam uttānāḥ tvā pratīcīm yat pṛṣṭībhiḥ adhiśemahe   mā hiṃsīḥ tatra naḥ bhūme sarvasya pratiśīvari  
yat te bhūme vikhanāmi kṣipram tat api rohatu   mā te marma vimṛgvari mā te hṛdayam arpipam  
grīṣmaḥ te bhūme varṣāṇi śarad dhemantaḥ śiśiraḥ vasantaḥ   ṛtavaḥ te vihitāḥ hāyanīḥ ahar rātre pṛthivi naḥ duhātām  
yā apa sarpam vijamānā vimṛgvarī yasyām āsan agnayaḥ ye apsu antar   parā dasyūn dadatī deva pīyūn indram vṛṇānā pṛthivī na vṛtram śakrāya dadhre vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe  
yasyām sadaḥ havirdhāne yūpaḥ yasyām nimīyate   brahmāṇaḥ yasyām arcanti ṛgbhiḥ sāmnā yajuḥ vidaḥ yujyante yasyām ṛtvijaḥ somam indrāya pātave  
yasyām pūrve bhūta kṛtaḥ ṛṣayaḥ gāḥ udānṛcuḥ   sapta satreṇa vedhasaḥ yajñena tapasā saha  
sā naḥ bhūmiḥ ā diśatu yat dhanam kāmayāmahe   bhagaḥ anuprayuṅktām indraḥ etu purogavaḥ      
yasyām gāyanti nṛtyanti bhūmyām martyāḥ vyailabāḥ   yudhyante yasyām ākrandaḥ yasyām vadati dundubhiḥ   sā naḥ bhūmiḥ pra nudatām sapatnān asapatnam mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu  
yasyām annam vrīhi yavau yasyāḥ imāḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ   bhūmyai parjanya patnyai namaḥ astu varṣamedase  
yasyāḥ puras deva kṛtāḥ kṣetre yasyāḥ vikurvate   prajāpatiḥ pṛthivīm viśva garbhām āśām āśām raṇyām naḥ kṛṇotu  
nidhim bibhratī bahudhā guhā vasu maṇim hiraṇyam pṛthivī dadātu me   vasūni naḥ vasu dāḥ rāsamānā devī dadhātu sumanasyamānā  
janam bibhratī bahudhā vivācasam nānā dharmāṇam pṛthivī yathaukasam   sahasram dhārāḥ draviṇasya me duhām dhruvā iva dhenuḥ an apasphurantī  
yaḥ te sarpaḥ vṛścikaḥ tṛṣṭa daṃśmā hemanta jabdhaḥ bhṛmalaḥ guhā śaye   krimiḥ jinvat pṛthivi yat yat ejati prāvṛṣi tat naḥ sarpat mā upa sṛpat yat śivam tena naḥ mṛḍa  
ye te panthānaḥ bahavaḥ janāyanāḥ rathasya vartmānasaḥ ca yātave   yaiḥ saṃcaranti ubhaye bhadra pāpāḥ tam panthānam jayema anamitram ataskaram yat śivam tena naḥ mṛḍa  
malvam bibhratī guru bhṛt bhadra pāpasya nidhanam titikṣuḥ   varāheṇa pṛthivī saṃvidānā sūkarāya vi jihīte mṛgāya  
ye te āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ mṛgāḥ vane hitāḥ siṃhāḥ vyāghrāḥ puruṣādaḥ caranti   ulam vṛkam pṛthivi duchunām itas ṛkṣīkām rakṣaḥ apa bādhaya asmat  
ye gandharvāḥ apsarasaḥ ye cārāyāḥ kimīdinaḥ   piśācān sarvā rakṣāṃsi tān asmat bhūme yāvaya      
yām dvipādaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanti haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunāḥ vayāṃsi   yasyām vātaḥ mātariśvā īyate rajāṃsi kṛṇvan cyāvayan ca vṛkṣān   vātasya pravām upavām anu vāti arciḥ  
yasyām kṛṣṇam aruṇam ca saṃhite ahar rātre vihite bhūmyām adhi   varṣeṇa bhūmiḥ pṛthivī vṛtā āvṛtā sā naḥ dadhātu bhadrayā priye dhāmani dhāmani  
dyauḥ ca me idam pṛthivī ca antarikṣam ca me vyacaḥ   agniḥ sūryaḥ āpaḥ medhām viśve devāḥ ca sam daduḥ  
aham asmi sahamānaḥ uttaraḥ nāma bhūmyām   abhīṣāh asmi viśvāṣāh āśām āśām viṣāsahiḥ  
adaḥ yat devi prathamānā purastāt devaiḥ uktā vyasarpaḥ mahitvam   ā tvā subhūtam aviśat tadānīm akalpayathāḥ pradiśaḥ catasraḥ  
ye grāmāḥ yat araṇyam yāḥ sabhāḥ adhi bhūmyām   ye saṃgrāmāḥ samitayaḥ teṣu cāru vadema te  
aśvaḥ iva rajaḥ dudhuve vi tān janān yaḥ ākṣiyan pṛthivīm yāt ajāyata   mandrā agretvarī bhuvanasya gopāḥ vanaspatīnām gṛbhiḥ oṣadhīnām  
yat vadāmi madhumat tat vadāmi yat īkṣe tat vananti mā   tviṣīmān asmi jūtimān ava anyān hanmi dodhataḥ  
śantivā surabhiḥ syonā kīlālodhnī payasvatī   bhūmiḥ adhi bravītu me pṛthivī payasā saha  
yām anvaichat dhaviṣā viśvakarmā antar arṇave rajasi praviṣṭām   bhujiṣyam pātram nihitam guhā yat āvis bhoge abhavat mātṛmadbhyaḥ  
tvam asi āvapanī janānām aditiḥ kāmadughā paprathānā   yat te ūnam tat te ā pūrayāti prajāpatiḥ prathama jāḥ ṛtasya  
upasthāḥ te anamīvāḥ a yakṣmāḥ asmabhyam santu pṛthivi prasūtāḥ   dīrgham naḥ āyuḥ pratibudhyamānāḥ vayam tubhyam bali hṛtaḥ syāma  
bhūme mātar ni dhehi mā bhadrayā su pratiṣṭhitam   saṃvidānā divā kave śriyām mā dhehi bhūtyām         divā kave śriyām mā dhehi bhūtyām               divā kave śriyām mā dhehi bhūtyām                                         divā kave śriyām mā dhehi bhūtyām                     divā kave śriyām mā dhehi bhūtyām               divā kave śriyām mā dhehi bhūtyām    
naḍam ā roha na te atra loke idam sīsam bhāgadheyam te ehi   yaḥ goṣu yakṣmaḥ puruṣeṣu yakṣmaḥ tena tvam sākam adharāṅ parehi  
agha śaṃsa duḥśaṃsābhyām kareṇa anukareṇa ca   yakṣmam ca sarvam tena itas mṛtyum ca niḥ ajāmasi  
niḥ itas mṛtyum nirṛtim niḥ arātim ajāmasi   yaḥ naḥ dveṣṭi tam addhi agne akravyād yam u dviṣmaḥ tam u te pra suvāmasi  
yadi agniḥ kravyād yadi vā vyāghraḥ imam goṣṭham praviveśa anyokāḥ   tam māṣa ājyam kṛtvā pra hiṇomi dūram sa gacchatu apsuṣadaḥ api agnīn  
yat tvā kruddhāḥ pracakruḥ manyunā puruṣe mṛte   su kalpam agne tat tvayā punar tvā ud dīpayāmasi  
punar tvā ādityāḥ rudrāḥ vasavaḥ punar brahmā vasu nītiḥ agne   punar tvā brahmaṇaḥ patiḥ ādhāt dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya  
yaḥ agniḥ kravyād praviveśa naḥ gṛham imam paśyan itaram jātavedasam   tam harāmi pitṛ yajñāya dūram sa gharmam indhām parame sadhasthe  
kravya adam agnim pra hiṇomi dūram yama rājñaḥ gacchatu ripra vāhaḥ   iha ayam itaraḥ jātavedāḥ devaḥ devebhyaḥ havyam vahatu prajānan  
kravya adam agnim iṣitaḥ harāmi janān dṛṃhantam vajreṇa mṛtyum   ni tam śāsmi gārhapatyena vidvān pitṝṇām loke api bhāgaḥ astu  
 kravya adam agnim śaśamānam ukthyam pra hiṇomi pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ   mā deva yānaiḥ punar ā gāḥ atra eva edhi pitṛṣu jāgṛhi tvam   tvam   tvam                                                                                                  
sam indhate saṃkasukam svastaye śuddhāḥ bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ   jahāti ripram ati enaḥ eti samiddhaḥ agniḥ supunā punāti  
devaḥ agniḥ saṃkasukaḥ divaḥ pṛṣṭhāni āruhat   mucyamānaḥ niḥ eṇasaḥ amok asmān aśastyāḥ  
asmin vayam saṃkasuke agnau riprāṇi mṛjmahe   abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra naḥ āyūṃṣi tāriṣat  
saṃkasukaḥ vikasukaḥ nirṛthaḥ yaḥ ca nisvaraḥ   te te yakṣmam savedasaḥ dūrāt dūram anīnaśan  
yaḥ naḥ aśveṣu vīreṣu yaḥ naḥ goṣu aja aviṣu   kravya adam niḥ nudāmasi yaḥ agniḥ jana yopanaḥ  
anyebhyaḥ tvā puruṣebhyaḥ gobhyaḥ aśvebhyaḥ tvā   niḥ kravya adam nudāmasi yaḥ agniḥ jīvita yopanaḥ  
yasmin devāḥ amṛjata yasmin manuṣyāḥ uta   tasmin ghṛta stāvaḥ mṛṣṭvā tvam agne divam ruha  
samiddhaḥ agne āhuta sa naḥ mā abhyapakramīḥ   atra eva dīdihi dyavi jyok ca sūryam dṛśe  
sīse mṛḍḍhvam naḍe mṛḍḍhvam agnau saṃkasuke ca yat  atha u avyām rāmāyām śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe 
 avyām asiknyām mṛṣṭvā śuddhāḥ bhavata yajñiyāḥ   avyām asiknyām mṛṣṭvā śuddhāḥ bhavata yajñiyāḥ                                                                                                  
param mṛtyo anu parehi panthām yaḥ te eṣaḥ itaraḥ deva yānāt   cakṣuṣmate śṛṇvate te bravīmi iha ime vīrāḥ bahavaḥ bhavantu  
ime jīvāḥ vi mṛtaiḥ āvavṛtran abhūt bhadrā deva hutiḥ naḥ adya   prāñcaḥ agāma nṛtaye hasāya su vīrāsaḥ vidatham ā vadema  
imam jīvebhyaḥ paridhim dadhāmi mā eṣām nu gāt aparaḥ artham etam   śatam jīvantaḥ śaradaḥ purūcīḥ tiras mṛtyum dadhatām parvatena  
ā rohata āyuḥ jarasam vṛṇānāḥ anupūrvam yatamānāḥ yati stha   tān vaḥ tvaṣṭā su janimā sa joṣāḥ sarvam āyuḥ nayatu jīvanāya  
yathā ahāni anupūrvam bhavanti yathā rtavaḥ ṛtubhiḥ yanti sākam   yathā na pūrvam aparaḥ jahāti eva dhātar āyūṃṣi kalpaya eṣām  
aśmanvatī rīyate sam rabhadhvam vīrayadhvam pra tarata sakhāyaḥ   atrā jahīta ye asan durevāḥ anamīvān ud tarema abhi vājān  
ud tiṣṭhata pra tarata sakhāyaḥ aśmanvatī nadī syandate iyam   atrā jahīta ye asan aśivāḥ śivān syonān ud tarema abhi vājān  
vaiśvadevīm varcasā ā rabhadhvam śuddhāḥ bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ   atikrāmantaḥ duritā padāni śatam himāḥ sarva vīrāḥ madema  
udīcīnaiḥ pathibhiḥ vāyumadbhiḥ atikrāmantaḥ avarān parebhiḥ   tris sapta kṛtvas ṛṣayaḥ paretāḥ mṛtyum prati auhan pada yopanena  
mṛtyoḥ padam yopayantaḥ eta drāghīyaḥ āyuḥ prataram dadhānāḥ   āsīnāḥ mṛtyum nudata sadhasthe atha jīvāsaḥ vidatham ā vadema                                                                                                                                                                                   
imāḥ nārīḥ avidhavāḥ su patnīḥ āñjanena sarpiṣā sam spṛśantām   anaśravaḥ anamīvāḥ su ratnāḥ ā rohantu janayaḥ yonim agre  
vyākaromi haviṣā aham etau tau brahmaṇā vi aham kalpayāmi   svadhām pitṛbhyaḥ ajarām kṛṇomi dīrgheṇa āyuṣā sam imān sṛjāmi  
yaḥ naḥ agniḥ pitaraḥ hṛtsu antar āviveśa amṛtaḥ martyeṣu   mayi aham tam pari gṛhṇāmi devam mā saḥ asmān dvikṣata mā vayam tam  
apāvṛtya gārhapatyāt kravyādā preta dakṣiṇā   priyam pitṛbhyaḥ ātmane brahmabhyaḥ kṛṇuta priyam  
dvi bhāga dhanam ādāya pra kṣiṇāti avartyā   agniḥ putrasya jyeṣṭhasya yaḥ kravyād a nirāhitaḥ  
yat kṛṣate yat vanute yat ca vasnena vindate   sarvam martyasya tat na asti kravyād ced a nirāhitaḥ  
a yajñiyaḥ hata varcāḥ bhavati na enena haviḥ attave   chinatti kṛṣyā goḥ dhanāt yam kravyād anuvartate  
muhur gṛdhyaiḥ pra vadati ārtim martyaḥ nītya   kravya ad yān agniḥ antikāt anuvidvān vitāvati  
grāhyāḥ gṛhāḥ sam sṛjyante striyāḥ yat mriyate patiḥ   brahmā eva vidvān eṣyaḥ yaḥ kravya adam nirādadhat  
 āpaḥ mā tasmāt śumbhantu agneḥ saṃkasukāt ca yat        mā tasmāt śumbhantu agneḥ saṃkasukāt ca yat                                                                                                                                                                                                 
tāḥ adharāt udīcīḥ āvavṛtran prajānaitīḥ pathibhiḥ deva yānaiḥ   parvatasya vṛṣabhasya adhi pṛṣṭhe navāḥ caranti saritaḥ purāṇīḥ  
agne akravyād niḥ kravyādam nuda devayajanam vaha 
imam kravyād ā viveśa ayam kravyādam anu agāt   vyāghrau kṛtvā nānānam tam harāmi śiva aparam  
antardhiḥ devānām paridhiḥ manuṣyāṇām agniḥ gārhapatyaḥ ubhayān antarā śritaḥ 
jīvānām āyuḥ pra tira tvam agne pitṝṇām lokam api gacchantu ye mṛtāḥ   su gārhapatyaḥ vitapan arātim uṣām uṣām śreyasīm dhehi asmai  
sarvān agne sahamānaḥ sapatnān aiṣām ūrjam rayim asmāsu dhehi 
imam indram vahnim paprim anvārabhadhvam sa vaḥ niḥ vakṣat duritāt avadyāt   tena apa hata śarum āpatantam tena rudrasya pari pāta āstām  
anaḍvāham plavam anvārabhadhvam sa vaḥ niḥ vakṣat duritāt avadyāt   ā rohata savituḥ nāvam etām ṣaḍbhiḥ urvībhiḥ amatim tarema  
ahar rātre anu eṣi bibhrat kṣemyaḥ tiṣṭhan prataraṇaḥ su vīraḥ   an āturān sumanasaḥ talpa bibhrat jyok eva naḥ puruṣa gandhiḥ edhi  
 te devebhyaḥ ā vṛścante pāpam jīvanti sarvadā   kravya ad yān agniḥ antikāt aśvaḥ iva anuvapate naḍam                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
ye aśraddhā dhana kāmyā kravyādā samāsate   te vai anyeṣām kumbhīm paryādadhati sarvadā  
pra iva pipatiṣati manasā muhur ā vartate punar   kravya ad yān agniḥ antikāt anuvidvān vitāvati  
aviḥ kṛṣṇā bhāgadheyam paśūnām sīsam kravyād api candram te āhuḥ   māṣāḥ piṣṭāḥ bhāgadheyam te havyam araṇyānyāḥ gahvaram sacasva  
iṣīkām jaratīm iṣṭvā tilpiñjam daṇḍanam naḍam   tam indraḥ idhmam kṛtvā yamasya agnim nirādadhau  
pratyañcam arkam pratyarpayitvā pravidvān panthām vi hi āviveśa   parā amīṣām asūn dideśa dīrgheṇa āyuṣā sam imān sṛjāmi     
pumān puṃsaḥ adhi tiṣṭha carma ihi tatra hvayasva yatamā priyā te   yāvantau agre prathamam sameyathuḥ tat vām vayaḥ yama rājye samānam  
tāvat vām cakṣuḥ tati vīryāṇi tāvat tejaḥ tatidhā vājināni   agniḥ śarīram sacate yadā edhaḥ adha pakvāt mithunā sam bhavāthaḥ  
sam asmin loke sam u deva yāne sam smā sametam yama rājyeṣu   pūtau pavitraiḥ upa tat dhvayethām yat yat retaḥ adhi vām saṃbabhūva  
āpaḥ putrāsaḥ abhi sam viśadhvam imam jīvam jīva dhanyāḥ sametya   tāsām bhajadhvam amṛtam yam āhuḥ odanam pacati vām janitrī  
yam vām pitā pacati yam ca mātā riprāt nirmuktyai śamalāt ca vācaḥ   saḥ odanaḥ śata dhāraḥ svargaḥ ubhe vi āpa nabhasī mahitvā  
ubhe nabhasī ubhayān ca lokān ye yajvanām abhijitāḥ svargāḥ   teṣām jyotiṣmān madhumān yaḥ agre tasmin putraiḥ jarasi sam śrayethām  
prācīm prācīm pradiśam ā rabhethām etam lokam śraddadhānāḥ sacante   yat vām pakvam pariviṣṭam agnau tasya guptaye daṃpatī sam śrayethām  
dakṣiṇām diśam abhi nakṣamāṇau paryāvartethām abhi pātram etat   tasmin vām yamaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ pakvāya śarma bahulam ni yacchāt  
pratīcī diśām iyam id varam yasyām somaḥ adhipāḥ mṛḍitā ca   tasyām śrayethām su kṛtaḥ sacethām adhā pakvāt mithunā sam bhavāthaḥ  
uttaram rāṣṭram prajaya uttarāvat diśām udīcī kṛṇavat naḥ agram   pāṅktam chandaḥ puruṣaḥ babhūva viśvaiḥ viśva aṅgaiḥ saha sam bhavema   pāṅktam chandaḥ puruṣaḥ babhūva viśvaiḥ viśva aṅgaiḥ saha sam bhavema   pāṅktam chandaḥ puruṣaḥ babhūva viśvaiḥ viśva aṅgaiḥ saha sam bhavema   pāṅktam chandaḥ puruṣaḥ babhūva viśvaiḥ viśva aṅgaiḥ saha sam bhavema   pāṅktam chandaḥ puruṣaḥ babhūva viśvaiḥ viśva 
dhruvā iyam virāj namaḥ astu asyai śivā putrebhyaḥ uta mahyam astu   sā naḥ devī adite viśva vāraḥ iryaḥ iva gopāḥ abhi rakṣa pakvam  
pitā iva putrān abhi sam svajasva naḥ śivāḥ naḥ vātāḥ iha vāntu bhūmau   yam odanam pacataḥ devate iha tam naḥ tapaḥ uta satyam ca vettu  
yat yat kṛṣṇaḥ śakunaḥ ā iha gatvā tsaran viṣaktam bile āsasāda   yat vā dāsī ārdra hastā samaṅkte ulūkhalam musalam śumbhata apaḥ  
ayam grāvā pṛthu budhnaḥ vayodhāḥ pūtaḥ pavitraiḥ apa hantu rakṣaḥ   ā roha carma mahi śarma yaccha mā daṃpatī pautram agham ni gātām  
vanaspatiḥ saha devaiḥ naḥ āgan rakṣaḥ piśācām apabādhamānaḥ   saḥ ud śrayātai pra vadāti vācam tena lokām abhi sarvān jayema  
sapta medhān paśavaḥ pari agṛhṇan yaḥ eṣām jyotiṣmān uta yaḥ cakarśa   trayastriṃśat devatāḥ tān sacante sa naḥ svargam abhi neṣa lokam  
svargam lokam abhi naḥ nayāsi sam jāyayā saha putraiḥ syāma   gṛhṇāmi hastam anu mā aitu atra mā naḥ tārīt nirṛtiḥ mā u arātiḥ  
grāhim pāpmānam ati tām ayāma tamaḥ vi asya pra vadāsi valgu   vānaspatyaḥ udyataḥ mā jihiṃsīḥ mā taṇḍulam vi śarīḥ devayantam  
viśva vyacāḥ ghṛta pṛṣṭhaḥ bhaviṣyan sayoniḥ lokam upa yāhi etam   varṣa vṛddham upa yaccha śūrpam tuṣam palāvān apa tat vinaktu  
trayaḥ lokāḥ saṃmitāḥ brāhmaṇena dyauḥ eva asau pṛthivī antarikṣam   aṃśūn gṛbhītvā anvārabhethām ā pyāyantām punar ā yantu śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   śūrpam   
pṛthak rūpāṇi bahudhā paśūnām eka rūpaḥ bhavasi sam samṛddhyā   etām tvacam lohinīm tām nudasva grāvā śumbhāti malagaḥ iva vastrā  
pṛthivīm tvā pṛthivyām ā veśayāmi tanūḥ samānī vikṛtā te eṣā   yat yat dyuttam likhitam arpaṇena tena mā susroḥ brahmaṇā api tat vapāmi  
janitrī iva prati haryā asi sūnum sam tvā dadhāmi pṛthivīm pṛthivyā   ukhā kumbhī vedyām mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ yajñāyudhaiḥ ājyena atiṣaktā  
agniḥ pacan rakṣatu tvā purastāt indraḥ rakṣatu dakṣiṇatas marutvān   varuṇaḥ tvā dṛṃhāt dharuṇe pratīcyāḥ uttarāt tvā somaḥ sam dadātai  
pūtāḥ pavitraiḥ pavante abhrāt divam ca yanti pṛthivīm ca lokān   tāḥ jīvalāḥ jīva dhanyāḥ pratiṣṭhāḥ pātre āsiktāḥ pari agniḥ indhām  
ā yanti divaḥ pṛthivīm sacante bhūmyāḥ sacante adhi antarikṣam   śuddhāḥ satīḥ tāḥ u śumbhantaḥ eva tāḥ naḥ svargam abhi lokam nayantu  
uta iva prabhvīḥ uta saṃmitāsaḥ uta śukrāḥ śucayaḥ ca amṛtāsaḥ   tāḥ odanam daṃpatibhyām praśiṣṭāḥ āpaḥ śikṣantīḥ pacata sunāthāḥ  
saṃkhyātāḥ stokāḥ pṛthivīm sacante prāṇa apānaiḥ saṃmitāḥ oṣadhībhiḥ   asaṃkhyātāḥ opyamānāḥ suvarṇāḥ sarvam vyāpuḥ śucayaḥ śuci tvam  
ud yodhanti abhi valganti taptāḥ phenam asyanti bahulān ca bindūn   yoṣā iva dṛṣṭvā patim ṛtviyāya etaiḥ taṇḍulaiḥ bhavata sam āpaḥ  
ud thāpaya sīdataḥ budhne enān adbhiḥ ātmānam abhi sam spṛśantām   amāsi pātraiḥ udakam yat etat mitāḥ taṇḍulāḥ pradiśaḥ yadi imāḥ     
pra yaccha parśum tvarayā harausam a hiṃsantaḥ oṣadhīḥ dāntu parvan   vāsām somaḥ pari rājyam babhūva amanyutā naḥ vīrudhaḥ bhavantu  
navam barhiḥ odanāya stṛṇīta priyam hṛdaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ valgu astu   tasmin devāḥ saha daivīḥ viśantu imam prāśnantu ṛtubhiḥ niṣadya  
vanaspate stīrṇam ā sīda barhiḥ agniṣṭobhaiḥ saṃmitaḥ devatābhiḥ   tvaṣṭrā iva rūpam su kṛtam svadhityā enāḥ ā ihāḥ pari pātre dadṛśrām  
ṣaṣṭyām śaratsu nidhi pāḥ abhīchāt svar pakvena abhi aśnavātai   upa enam jīvān pitaraḥ ca putrāḥ etam svargam gamaya antam agneḥ  
dhartā dhriyasva dharuṇe pṛthivyāḥ acyutam tvā devatāḥ cyāvayantu   tam tvā daṃpatī jīvantau jīva putrau ud vāsayātaḥ pari agnidhānāt  
sarvān samāgāḥ abhijitya lokān yāvantaḥ kāmāḥ sam atītṛpaḥ tān   vi gāhethām āyavanam ca darviḥ ekasmin pātre adhi ud hara enam  
upa stṛṇīhi prathaya purastāt ghṛtena pātram abhi ghāraya etat   vāśrā iva usrā taruṇam stanasyum imam devāsaḥ abhihiṅkṛṇota  
upa astarīḥ akaraḥ lokam etam uruḥ prathatām asamaḥ svargaḥ   tasmim chrayātai mahiṣaḥ suparṇaḥ devāḥ enam devatābhyaḥ pra yacchān  
yat yat jāyā pacati tvat paraḥ paraḥ patiḥ vā jāye tvat tiras   sam tat sṛjethām saha vām tat astu saṃpādayantau saha lokam ekam  
yāvantaḥ asyāḥ pṛthivīm sacante asmat putrāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ   sarvān tām upa pātre hvayethām nābhim jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān   sarvān tām upa pātre hvayethām nābhim jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān   sarvān tām upa pātre hvayethām nābhim jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān   sarvān tām upa pātre hvayethām nābhim jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān   sarvān tām upa pātre hvayethām nābhim jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān   sarvān tām upa
vasoḥ yāḥ dhārāḥ madhunā prapīnāḥ ghṛtena miśrāḥ amṛtasya nābhayaḥ   sarvāḥ tāḥ ava rundhe svargaḥ ṣaṣṭyām śaratsu nidhi pāḥ abhīchāt  
nidhim nidhi pāḥ abhi enam ichāt anīśvarāḥ abhitas santu ye anye   asmābhiḥ dattaḥ nihitaḥ svargaḥ tribhiḥ kāṇḍaiḥ trīn svargān arukṣat  
agniḥ rakṣaḥ tapatu yat videvam kravyād piśācaḥ iha mā pra pāsta   nudāmaḥ enam apa rudhmaḥ asmat ādityāḥ enam aṅgirasaḥ sacantām  
ādityebhyaḥ aṅgirobhyaḥ madhu idam ghṛtena miśram prati vedayāmi   śuddha hastau brāhmaṇasya a nihatya etam svargam su kṛtau a pītam  
idam prāpam uttamam kāṇḍam asya yasmāt lokāt parameṣṭhī samāpa   ā siñca sarpiḥ ghṛtavat sam aṅgdhi eṣa bhāgaḥ aṅgirasaḥ naḥ atra  
satyāya ca tapase devatābhyaḥ nidhim śevadhim pari dadmaḥ etam   mā naḥ dyūte ava gāt mā samityām mā sma anyasmai ud sṛjata purā mat

priyam priyāṇām kṛṇavāma tamaḥ te yantu yatame dviṣanti   dhenuḥ anaḍvān vayaḥ vayaḥ āyat eva pauruṣeyam apa mṛtyum nudantu  
 sam agnayaḥ viduḥ anyaḥ anyam yaḥ oṣadhīḥ sacate yaḥ ca sindhūn   yāvantaḥ devāḥ divi ātapanti hiraṇyam jyotiḥ pacataḥ babhūva   yāvantaḥ devāḥ divi ātapanti hiraṇyam jyotiḥ pacataḥ babhūva     tapanti hiraṇyam jyotiḥ pacataḥ babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti babhūva     tapanti ba
eṣā tvacām puruṣe sam babhūva anagnāḥ sarve paśavaḥ ye anye   kṣatreṇa ātmānam pari dhāpayāthaḥ amotam vāsaḥ mukham odanasya  
yat akṣeṣu vadāḥ yat samityām yat vā vadāḥ anṛtam vitta kāmyā   samānam tantum abhi samvasānau tasmin sarvam śamalam sādayāthaḥ  
varṣam vanuṣva api gaccha devān tvacaḥ dhūmam pari ud pātayāsi   viśva vyacāḥ ghṛta pṛṣṭhaḥ bhaviṣyan sa yoniḥ lokam upa yāhi etam  
tanvam svargaḥ bahudhā vi cakre yathā vidaḥ ātman anya varṇām   apājait kṛṣṇām ruśatīm punānaḥ yā lohinī tām te agnau juhomi  
prācyai tvā diśe agnaye adhipataye asitāya rakṣitre ādityāya iṣumate   etam pari dadmaḥ tam naḥ gopāyata asmākam aitoḥ   diṣṭam naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema  
dakṣiṇāyai tvā diśaḥ indrāya adhipataye tiraścirājaye rakṣitre yamāya iṣumate   etam pari dadmaḥ tam naḥ gopāyata asmākam aitoḥ   diṣṭam naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema  
pratīcyai tvā diśe varuṇāya adhipataye pṛdākave rakṣitre annāya iṣumate   etam pari dadmaḥ tam naḥ gopāyata asmākam aitoḥ   diṣṭam naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema  
udīcyai tvā diśe somāya adhipataye svajāya rakṣitre aśanyāḥ iṣumatyai   etam pari dadmaḥ tam naḥ gopāyata asmākam aitoḥ   diṣṭam naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema  
dhruvāyai tvā diśe viṣṇave adhipataye kalmāṣa grīvāya rakṣitre oṣadhībhyaḥ iṣumatībhyaḥ   etam pari dadmaḥ tam naḥ gopāyata asmākam aitoḥ   diṣṭam naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema  
ūrdhvāyai tvā diśe bṛhaspataye adhipataye śvitrāya rakṣitre varṣāya iṣumate   etam pari dadmaḥ tam naḥ gopāyata asmākam aitoḥ   diṣṭam naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema     tat sam bhavema     tat naḥ atra jarase ni neṣat jarā mṛtyave pari naḥ dadātu atha pakvena saha sam bhavema     tat saha sam bhavema  
dadāmi iti eva brūyāt anu ca enām abhutsata   vaśām brahmabhyaḥ yācadbhyaḥ tat prajāvat apatyavat  
prajayā sa vi krīṇīte paśubhiḥ ca upa dasyati   yaḥ ārṣeyebhyaḥ yācadbhyaḥ devānām gām na ditsati  
kūṭayā asya sam śīryante śloṇayā kāṭam ardati   baṇḍayā dahyante gṛhāḥ kāṇayā dīyate svam  
vilohitaḥ adhiṣṭhānāt śaknaḥ vindati gopatim   tathā vaśāyāḥ saṃvidyam duradabhnā hi ucyase  
padoḥ asyāḥ adhiṣṭhānāt viklinduḥ nāma vindati   anāmanāt sam śīryante yāḥ mukhena upajighrati  
yaḥ asyāḥ karṇau āskunoti ā sa deveṣu vṛścate   lakṣma kurve iti manyate kanīyaḥ kṛṇute svam  
yat asyāḥ kasmai cit bhogāya bālān kaḥ cit prakṛntati   tatas kiśorāḥ mriyante vatsān ca ghātukaḥ vṛkaḥ  
yat asyāḥ gopatau satyāḥ loma dhvāṅkṣaḥ ajīhiḍat   tatas kumārāḥ mriyante yakṣmaḥ vindati anāmanāt  
yat asyāḥ palpūlanam śakṛt dāsī samasyati   tatas aparūpam jāyate tasmāt a vyeṣyat enasaḥ  
jāyamānā abhi jāyate devān sa brāhmaṇān vaśā   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya gopanam   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya gopanam   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya gopanam   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya gopanam   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya gopanam   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya gopanam   tasmāt brahmabhyaḥ deyā eṣā tat āhuḥ svasya go
ye enām vanim āyanti teṣām deva kṛtā vaśā   brahmajyeyam tat abruvan yaḥ enām nipriyāyate  
yaḥ ārṣeyebhyaḥ yācadbhyaḥ devānām gām na ditsati   ā sa deveṣu vṛścate brāhmaṇānām ca manyave  
yaḥ asya syāt vaśā bhogaḥ anyām icheta tarhi saḥ   hiṃste a dattā puruṣam yācitām ca na ditsati  
yathā śevadhiḥ nihitaḥ brāhmaṇānām tathā vaśā   tām etat achāyanti yasmin kasmin ca jāyate  
svam etat achāyanti yat vaśām brāhmaṇāḥ abhi   yathā enān anyasmin jinīyāt eva asyāḥ nirodhanam  
caret eva traihāyaṇāt a vijñāta gadā satī   vaśām ca vidyāt nārada brāhmaṇāḥ tarhi eṣyāḥ  
yaḥ enām avaśām āha devānām nihitam nidhim   ubhau tasmai bhavāśarvau parikramya iṣum asyataḥ  
yaḥ asyāḥ ūdhaḥ na veda atha u asyāḥ stanān uta   ubhayena eva asmai duhe dātum ced aśakat vaśām  
duradabhnā enam ā śaye yācitām ca na ditsati   na asmai kāmāḥ sam ṛdhyante yām a dattvā cikīrṣati  
devāḥ vaśām ayācat mukham kṛtvā brāhmaṇam   teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ   teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ     teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ     teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ     teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ     teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ     teṣām sarveṣām adadat heḍam ni eti mānuṣaḥ     teṣām s
heḍam paśūnām ni eti brāhmaṇebhyaḥ adadat vaśām   devānām nihitam bhāgam martyaḥ ced nipriyāyate  
yat anye śatam yāceyuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ go patim vaśām   atha enām devāḥ abruvan evam ha viduṣaḥ vaśā  
yaḥ evam viduṣe a dattvā atha anyebhyaḥ dadat vaśām   durgā tasmai adhiṣṭhāne pṛthivī sahadevatā  
devāḥ vaśām ayācan yasmin agre ajāyata   tām etām vidyāt nāradaḥ saha devaiḥ ud ājata  
anapatyam alpa paśum vaśā kṛṇoti pūruṣam   brāhmaṇaiḥ ca yācitām atha enām nipriyāyate  
agnīṣomābhyām kāmāya mitrāya varuṇāya ca   tebhyaḥ yācanti brāhmaṇāḥ teṣu ā vṛścate adadat  
yāvat asyāḥ go patiḥ na upaśṛṇuyāt ṛcaḥ svayam   caret asya tāvat goṣu na asya śrutvā gṛhe vaset  
yaḥ asyāḥ ṛcaḥ upaśrutya atha goṣu acīcarat   āyuḥ ca tasya bhūtim ca devāḥ vṛścanti hīḍitāḥ  
vaśā carantī bahudhā devānām nihitaḥ nidhiḥ   āvis kṛṇuṣva rūpāṇi yadā sthāma jighāṃsati  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
manasā sam kalpayati tat devām api gacchati   tatas ha brahmāṇaḥ vaśām upaprayanti yācitum  
svadhākāreṇa pitṛbhyaḥ yajñena devatābhyaḥ   dānena rājanyaḥ vaśāyāḥ mātuḥ heḍam na gacchati  
vaśā mātā rājanyasya tathā saṃbhūtam agraśas   tasyāḥ āhuḥ anarpaṇam yat brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate  
yathā ājyam pragṛhītam ālumpet srucaḥ agnaye   eva ha brahmabhyaḥ vaśām agnaye ā vṛścate adadat  
puroḍāśa vatsā su dughā loke asmai upa tiṣṭhati   sā asmai sarvān kāmān vaśā pradaduṣe duhe  
sarvān kāmān yama rājye vaśā pradaduṣe duhe   atha āhuḥ nārakam lokam nirundhānasya yācitām  
pravīyamānā carati kruddhā gopataye vaśā   vehatam mā manyamānaḥ mṛtyoḥ pāśeṣu badhyatām  
yaḥ vehatam manyamānaḥ amā ca pacate vaśām   api asya putrān pautrān ca yācayate bṛhaspatiḥ  
mahat eṣā ava tapati carantī goṣu gauḥ api   atha u ha gopataye vaśādaduṣe viṣam duhe

yāḥ vaśāḥ udakalpayan devāḥ yajñāt udetya   tāsām viliptyam bhīmām udākuruta nāradaḥ  
tām devāḥ amīmāṃsanta vaśeyam avaśā iti   tām abravīt nāradaḥ eṣā vaśānām vaśatamā iti  
kati nu vaśāḥ nārada yāḥ tvam vettha manuṣya jāḥ   tāḥ tvā pṛchāmi vidvāṃsam kasyāḥ na aśnīyāt a brāhmaṇaḥ  
viliptyā bṛhaspate yā ca sūta vaśā vaśā   tasyāḥ na aśnīyāt a brāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ āśaṃseta bhūtyām  
namaḥ te astu nārada anuṣṭhu viduṣe vaśā   katamāsām bhīmatamā yām a dattvā parābhavet  
viliptī yā bṛhaspate atho sūta vaśā vaśā   tasyāḥ na aśnīyāt a brāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ āśaṃseta bhūtyām  
trīṇi vai vaśā jātāni viliptī sūta vaśā vaśā   tāḥ pra yacchet brahmabhyaḥ saḥ anāvraskaḥ prajāpatau  
etat vaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ haviḥ iti manvīta yācitaḥ   vaśām ced enam yāceyuḥ yāḥ bhīma ādaduṣaḥ gṛhe  
devāḥ vaśām pari avadat na naḥ adāt iti hīḍitāḥ   etābhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ bhedam tasmāt vai sa parābhavat  
uta enām bhedaḥ na adadāt vaśām indreṇa yācitaḥ   tasmāt tam devāḥ āgasaḥ avṛścan aham uttare

avartiḥ aśyamānā nirṛtiḥ aśitā 
aśitā lokāt chinatti brahmagavī brahmajyam asmāt ca amuṣmāt ca         
tasyāḥ āhananam kṛtyā meniḥ āśasanam valagaḥ ūbadhyam  
asvagatā parihṇu tā 
agniḥ kravyād bhūtvā brahmagavī brahmajyam praviśya atti 
sarvā asya aṅgā parvā mūlāni vṛścati 
chinatti asya pitṛ bandhu parā bhāvayati mātṛ bandhu
