svāvṛt devasya amṛtam yadī goḥ atas jātāsaḥ dhārayantaḥ urvī   viśve devāḥ anu tat te yajuḥ guḥ duhe yat enī divyam ghṛtam vār  
kim svid naḥ rājā jagṛhe kad asya ati vratam cakṛma kaḥ vi veda   mitraḥ cit hi ṣmā juhurāṇaḥ devām ślokaḥ na yātām api vājaḥ asti  
durmantu atra amṛtasya nāma sa lakṣmā yat viṣurūpā bhavāti   yamasya yaḥ manavate sumantu agne tam ṛṣva pāhi a prayuchan  
yasmin devāḥ vidathe mādayante vivasvataḥ sadane dhārayante   sūrye jyotiḥ adadhuḥ māsi aktūn pari dyotanim carataḥ ajasrā  
yasmin devāḥ manmani saṃcaranti apīcye na vayam asya vidma   mitraḥ naḥ atra aditiḥ anāgān savitā devaḥ varuṇāya vocat  
sakhāyaḥ ā śiṣāmahe brahma indrāya vajriṇe   stuṣe u su nṛtamāya dhṛṣṇave  
śavasā hi asi śrutaḥ vṛtra hatyena vṛtra hā   maghaiḥ maghonaḥ ati śūra dāśasi  
stegaḥ na kṣām ati eṣi pṛthivīm mahī naḥ vātāḥ iha vāntu bhūmau   mitraḥ naḥ atra varuṇaḥ yujamānaḥ agniḥ vane na vi asṛṣṭa śokam  
stuhi śrutam garta sadam janānām rājānam bhīmam upahatnum ugram   mṛḍā jaritre rudra stavānaḥ anyam asmat te ni vapantu senyam                    jaritre rudra stavānaḥ anyam asmat te ni vapantu senyam      
sarasvatīm devayantaḥ havante sarasvatīm adhvare tāyamāne   sarasvatīm su kṛtaḥ havante sarasvatī dāśuṣe vāryam dāt  
sarasvatīm pitaraḥ havante dakṣinā yajñam abhinakṣamāṇāḥ   āsadya asmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam anamīvāḥ iṣaḥ ā dhehi asme  
sarasvati yā sa ratham yayātha ukthaiḥ svadhābhiḥ devi pitṛbhiḥ madantī   sahasra argham iḍaḥ atra bhāgam rāyaḥ poṣam yajamānāya dhehi  
ud īratām avaraḥ ud parāsaḥ ud madhyamāḥ pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ   asum ye īyuḥ avṛkāḥ ṛta jñāḥ te naḥ avantu pitaraḥ haveṣu  
ā aham pitṝn suvidatrām avitsi napātam ca vikramaṇam ca viṣṇoḥ   barhiṣadaḥ ye svadhayā sutasya bhajanta pitvaḥ te iha āgamiṣṭhāḥ  
idam pitṛbhyaḥ namaḥ astu adya ye pūrvāsaḥ ye aparāsaḥ īyuḥ   ye pārthive rajasi ā niṣaktāḥ ye vā nūnam suvṛjanāsu dikṣu  
mātalī kavyaiḥ yamaḥ aṅgirobhiḥ bṛhaspatiḥ ṛkvabhiḥ vāvṛdhānaḥ   yān ca devāḥ vāvṛdhuḥ ye ca devān te naḥ avantu pitaraḥ haveṣu  
svāduḥ kila ayam madhumān uta ayam tīvraḥ kila ayam rasavān uta ayam   uta u nu asya papivāṃsam indram na kaḥ cana sahate āhaveṣu  
pareyivāṃsam pravataḥ mahīḥ iti bahubhyaḥ panthām an upaspaśānam   vaivasvatam saṃgamanam janānām yamam rājānam haviṣā saparyata  
yamaḥ naḥ gātum prathamaḥ viveda na eṣā gavyūtiḥ apabhartavai u  yatra naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ enāḥ jajñānāḥ pathyāḥ anu svāḥ   yatra naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ enāḥ jajñānāḥ pathyāḥ anu svāḥ   yatra naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ enāḥ jajñānāḥ pathyāḥ anu svāḥ   yatra naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ enāḥ jajñānāḥ pathyāḥ anu svāḥ   yatra naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ enāḥ jajñānāḥ pathyāḥ anu
barhiṣadaḥ pitaraḥ ūti arvāk imā vaḥ havyā cakṛma juṣadhvam   te ā gatāvasā śaṃtamena adhāḥ naḥ śam yos arapaḥ dadhāta  
ācyā jānu dakṣiṇatas niṣadya idam naḥ haviḥ abhi gṛṇantu viśve   mā hiṃsiṣṭa pitaraḥ kena cit naḥ yat vaḥ āgaḥ puruṣa tā karāma  
tvaṣṭā duhitre vahatum kṛṇoti tena idam viśvam bhuvanam sam eti   yamasya mātā paryuhyamānā mahaḥ jāyā vivasvataḥ nanāśa  
prehi prehi pathibhiḥ pūryāṇaiḥ yena te pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ   ubhā rājānau svadhayā madantau yamam paśyāsi varuṇam ca devam  
apeta vīta vi ca sarpata atas asmai etam pitaraḥ lokam akran   ahobhiḥ adbhiḥ aktubhiḥ vyaktam yamaḥ dadāti avasānam asmai  
uśantaḥ tvā idhīmahi uśantaḥ sam idhīmahi   uśan uśataḥ ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave  
dyumantaḥ tvā idhīmahi dyumantaḥ sam idhīmahi   dyumān dyumataḥ ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave  
aṅgirasaḥ naḥ pitaraḥ navagvāḥ atharvāṇaḥ bhṛgavaḥ somyāsaḥ   teṣām vayam sumatau yajñiyānām api bhadre saumanase syāma  
aṅgirobhiḥ yajñiyaiḥ ā gahi iha yama vairūpaiḥ iha mādayasva   vivasvantam huve yaḥ pitā te asmin barhiṣi ā niṣadya  
imam yama prastaram ā hi roha aṅgirobhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ   ā tvā mantrāḥ kavi śastāḥ vahantu enāḥ rājan haviṣaḥ mādayasva  
                                                                                                                  
yamāya somaḥ pavate yamāya kriyate haviḥ   yamam ha yajñaḥ gacchati agni dūtaḥ araṃkṛtaḥ  
yamāya madhumattamam juhota pra ca tiṣṭhata   idam namaḥ ṛṣibhyaḥ pūrvajebhyaḥ pūrvebhyaḥ pathikṛdbhyaḥ  
yamāya ghṛtavat payaḥ rājñe haviḥ juhotana   sa naḥ jīveṣu ā yamet dīrgham āyuḥ pra jīvase  
mā enam agne vi dahaḥ mā abhi śūśucaḥ mā asya tvacam cikṣipaḥ mā śarīram   śṛtam yadā karasi jātavedaḥ atha īm enam pra hiṇutāt pitṝn upa  
yadā śṛtam kṛṇavaḥ jātavedaḥ atha imam enam pari dattāt pitṛbhyaḥ   yadā u gacchāti asu nītim etām atha devānām vaśanīḥ bhavāti  
trikadrukebhiḥ pavate ṣaṭ urvīḥ ekam id bṛhat   triṣṭubh gāyatrī chandāṃsi sarvā tāḥ yamaḥ ārpitā  
sūryam cakṣuṣā gaccha vātam ātmanā divam ca gaccha pṛthivīm ca dharmabhiḥ   apaḥ vā gaccha yadi tatra te hitam oṣadhīṣu prati tiṣṭha śarīraiḥ  
ajaḥ bhāgaḥ tapasaḥ tam tapasva tam te śociḥ tapatu tam te arciḥ   yāḥ te śivāḥ tanvaḥ jātavedaḥ tābhiḥ vaha enam su kṛtām u lokam  
yāḥ te śocayaḥ raṃhayaḥ jātavedaḥ yābhiḥ āpṛṇāsi divam antarikṣam   ajam yantam anu tāḥ sam ṛṇvatām atha itarābhiḥ śivatamābhiḥ śṛtam kṛdhi  
ava sṛja punar agne pitṛbhyaḥ yaḥ te āhutaḥ carati svadhāvān   āyuḥ vasānaḥ upa yātu śeṣaḥ sam gacchatām tanvā su varcāḥ                                                                                                                                                                                    
ati drava śvānau sārameyau catur akṣau śabalau sādhunā pathā   adha pitṝn suvidatrām apīhi yamena ye sadhamādam madanti  
yau te śvānau yama rakṣitārau catur akṣau pathiṣadī nṛ cakṣasā   tābhyām rājan pari dhehi enam svasti asmai anamīvam ca dhehi  
urūṇasau asutṛpau udumbalau yamasya dūtau carataḥ janām anu   tau asmabhyam dṛśaye sūryāya punar dātām asum adya iha bhadram  
somaḥ ekebhyaḥ pavate ghṛtam ekaḥ upāsate   yebhyaḥ madhu pradhāvati tān cit eva api gacchatāt  
ye cit pūrve ṛta sātāḥ ṛta jātāḥ ṛtāvṛdhaḥ   ṛṣīn tapasvataḥ yama tapaḥ jām api gacchatāt  
tapasā ye anādhṛṣyāḥ tapasā ye svar yayuḥ   tapaḥ ye cakrire mahaḥ tān cit eva api gacchatāt  
ye yudhyante pradhaneṣu śūrāsaḥ ye svar tanūtyajaḥ   ye vā sahasra dakṣiṇāḥ tām cit eva api gacchatāt  
sahasraṇīthāḥ kavayaḥ ye gopāyanti sūryam   ṛṣīn tapasvataḥ yama tapaḥ jām api gacchatāt  
syonāḥ asmai bhava pṛthivī anṛkṣarā niveśanī   yaccha asmai śarma saprathāḥ  
asaṃbādhe pṛthivyāḥ urau loke ni dhīyasva   svadhā yāḥ cakṛṣe jīvan tāḥ te santu madhuścutaḥ               svadhā yāḥ cakṛṣe jīvan tāḥ te santu madhuścutaḥ                                                                                                                                                        
hvayāmi te manasā manaḥ iha imān gṛhām upa jujuṣāṇaḥ ehi   sam gacchasva pitṛbhiḥ sam yamena syonāḥ tvā vātāḥ upa vāntu śagmāḥ  
ud tvā vahantu marutaḥ udavāhāḥ udaprutaḥ   ajena kṛṇvantaḥ śītam varṣeṇa ukṣantu bāl iti  
ud ahvam āyuḥ āyuṣe kratve dakṣāya jīvase   svān gacchatu te manaḥ adha pitṝn upa drava  
mā te manaḥ māsoḥ mā aṅgānām mā rasasya te   mā te hāsta tanvaḥ kim cana iha  
mā tvā vṛkṣaḥ sam bādhiṣṭa mā devī pṛthivī mahī   lokam pitṛṣu vittvā edhasva yama rājasu  
yat te aṅgam atihitam parācais apānaḥ prāṇaḥ yaḥ u vā te paretaḥ   tat te saṃgatya pitaraḥ sanīḍāḥ ghāsāt ghāsam punar ā veśayantu  
apa imam jīvāḥ arudhan gṛhebhyaḥ tam niḥ vahata pari grāmāt itas   mṛtyuḥ yamasya āsīt dūtaḥ pracetāḥ asūn pitṛbhyaḥ gamayām cakāra  
ye dasyavaḥ pitṛṣu praviṣṭāḥ jñāti mukhāḥ a huta adaḥ caranti   parāpuraḥ nipuraḥ ye bharanti agniḥ tān asmāt pra dhamāti yajñāt  
sam viśantu iha pitaraḥ svā naḥ syonam kṛṇvantaḥ pratirante āyuḥ   tebhyaḥ śakema haviṣā nakṣamāṇāḥ jyok jīvantaḥ śaradaḥ purūcīḥ  
yām te dhenum nipṛṇāmi yam u kṣīre odanam   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat ajīvanaḥ   tena janasyāsaḥ bhartā yaḥ atra asat a
aśvāvatīm pra tara yā su śevā rkṣākam vā prataram navīyaḥ   yaḥ tvā jaghāna vadhyaḥ saḥ astu mā saḥ anyat vidata bhāgadheyam  
yamaḥ paraḥ avaraḥ vivasvān tatas param na ati paśyāmi kim cana   yame adhvaraḥ adhi me niviṣṭaḥ bhuvaḥ vivasvān anvātatāna  
apāgūhan amṛtām martyebhyaḥ kṛtvā savarṇām adadhuḥ vivasvate   uta aśvinau abharat yat tat āsīt ajahāt u dvā mithunā saraṇyūḥ  
ye nikhātāḥ ye paroptāḥ ye dagdhāḥ ye ca uddhitāḥ   sarvān tān agne ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave  
ye agni dagdhāḥ ye an agni dagdhāḥ madhye divaḥ svadhayā mādayante   tvam tān vettha yadi te jātavedaḥ svadhayā yajñam svadhitim juṣantām  
śam tapa mā ati tapaḥ agne mā tanvam tapaḥ   vaṇeṣu śuṣmaḥ astu te pṛthivyām astu yat dharaḥ 
dadāmi asmai avasānam etat yaḥ eṣaḥ āgan mama ced abhūt iha   yamaḥ cikitvān prati etat āha mama eṣa rāyaḥ upa tiṣṭhatām iha  
imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā  
pra imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā  
apaḥ imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā   śate śaratsu naḥ
vi imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu na u purā  
niḥ imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu na u purā  
ud imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā  
sam imām mātrām mimīmahe yathā aparam na māsātai   śate śaratsu naḥ u purā  
amāsi mātrām svar agām āyuṣmān bhūyāsam   yathā aparam na māsātai śate śaratsu na u purā  
prāṇaḥ apānaḥ vyānaḥ āyuḥ cakṣuḥ dṛśaye sūryāya   a paripareṇa pathā yama rājñaḥ pitṝn gaccha  
ye agravaḥ śaśamānāḥ pareyuḥ hitvā dveṣāṃsi anapatyavantaḥ   te dyām uditya avidanta lokam nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi dīdhyānāḥ  
udanvatī dyauḥ avamā pīlumatī iti madhyamā   tṛtīyā ha pradyauḥ iti yasyām pitaraḥ āsate  
ye na pituḥ pitaraḥ ye pitāmahāḥ ye āviviśuḥ uru antarikṣam   ye ākṣiyanti pṛthivīm uta dyām tebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ namasā vidhema  
idam id vai u na aparam divi paśyasi sūryam   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi             
idam id vai u na aparam jarasi anyat itas aparam   jāyā patim iva vāsasā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi  
abhi tvā ūrṇomi pṛthivyāḥ mātuḥ vastreṇa bhadrayā   jīveṣu bhadram tat mayi svadhā pitṛṣu sā tvayi  
agnīṣomā pathikṛtā syonam devebhyaḥ ratnam dadhathuḥ vi lokam   upa preṣyantam pūṣaṇam yaḥ vahāti añjoyānaiḥ pathibhiḥ tatra gacchatam  
pūṣā tvā itas cyāvayatu pra vidvān an aṣṭa paśuḥ bhuvanasya gopāḥ   sa tvā etebhyaḥ pari dadat pitṛbhyaḥ agniḥ devebhyaḥ suvi datriyebhyaḥ  
āyuḥ viśvāyuḥ pari pātu tvā pūṣā tvā pātu prapathe purastāt   yatra āsate su kṛtaḥ yatra te īyuḥ tatra tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu  
imau yunajmi te vahnī asunītāya voḍhave   tābhyām yamasya sādanam samitiḥ ca ava gacchatāt  
etat tvā vāsaḥ prathamam nu āgan apa etat ūha yat iha ābibhar purā   iṣṭāpūrtam anusaṃkrāma vidvān yatra te dattam bahudhā vibandhuṣu  
agneḥ varma pari gobhiḥ vyayasva sam prorṇuṣva medasā pīvasā ca   na id tvā dhṛṣṇuḥ harasā jarhṛṣāṇaḥ dadhṛṣāṇaḥ vidhakṣan parīṅkhayātai  
daṇḍam hastāt ādadānaḥ gatāsoḥ saha śrotreṇa varcasā balena   atra eva tvam iha vayam su vīrāḥ viśvāḥ mṛdhaḥ abhimātīḥ jayema  
dhanuḥ hastāt ādadānaḥ mṛtasya saha kṣatreṇa varcasā balena   samāgṛbhāya vasu bhūri puṣṭam arvāṅ tvam ehi upa jīva lokam     vasu bhūri puṣṭam arvāṅ tvam ehi upa jīva lokam                                                                                                                                                     
iyam nārī pati lokam vṛṇānā ni padyate upa tvā martya pretam   dharmam purāṇam anupālayantī tasyai prajām draviṇam ca iha dhehi  
ud īrṣva nārī abhi jīva lokam gatāsum etam upa śeṣaḥ ehi   hasta grābhasya dadhiṣoḥ tava idam patyuḥ janitvam abhi sam babhūtha  
apaśyam yuvatim nīyamānām jīvām mṛtebhyaḥ pariṇīyamānām   andhena yat tamasā prāvṛtā āsīt prāktaḥ apācīm anayam tat enām  
prajānati aghnye jīva lokam devānām panthām anusaṃcarantī   ayam te gopatiḥ tam juṣasva svargam lokam adhi rohaya enam  
upa dyām upa vetasam avattaraḥ nadīnām   agne pittam apām asi  
yam tvam agne samadahaḥ tam u niḥ vāpaya punar   kyāmbūḥ atra rohatu śāṇḍadūrvā vyalkaśā  
idam te ekam puras u te ekam tṛtīyena jyotiṣā sam viśasva   saṃveśane tanvā cāruḥ edhi priyaḥ devānām parame sadhasthe  
ud tiṣṭha prehi pra dravaukaḥ kṛṇuṣva salile sadhasthe   tatra tvam pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ sam somena madasva sam svadhābhiḥ  
pra cyavasva tanvam sam bharasva mā te gātrā vi hāyi mā u śarīram   manaḥ niviṣṭam anusaṃviśasva yatra bhūmeḥ juṣase tatra gaccha  
varcasā mām pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ añjantu devāḥ madhunā ghṛtena   cakṣuṣe mā prataram tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tārayantaḥ jarase mā jaradaṣṭim vardhantu     tār
varcasā mām sam anaktu agniḥ medhām me viṣṇuḥ ni anaktu āsan   rayim me viśve ni yacchantu devāḥ syonāḥ māpaḥ pavanaiḥ punantu  
mitrāvaruṇā pari mām adhātām ādityāḥ mā svaravaḥ vardhayantu   varcaḥ me indraḥ ni anaktu hastayoḥ jaradaṣṭim mā savitā kṛṇotu  
yaḥ mamāra prathamaḥ martyānām yaḥ preyāya prathamaḥ lokam etam   vaivasvatam saṃgamanam janānām yamam rājānam haviṣā saparyata  
parā yāta pitaraḥ ā ca yāta ayam vaḥ yajñaḥ madhunā samaktaḥ   dattaḥ asmabhyam draviṇā iha bhadram rayim ca naḥ sarva vīram dadhāta  
kaṇvaḥ kakṣīvān purumīḍhaḥ agastyaḥ śyāvāśvaḥ sobharī arcanānāḥ   viśvāmitraḥ ayam jamadagniḥ atriḥ avantu naḥ kaśyapaḥ vāmadevaḥ  
viśvāmitra jamadagne vasiṣṭha bharadvāja gotama vāmadeva   śardiḥ naḥ atriḥ agrabhīt namobhiḥ su saṃśāsaḥ pitaraḥ mṛḍata naḥ  
kasye mṛjānāḥ ati yanti ripram āyuḥ dadhānāḥ prataram navīyaḥ   āpyāyamānāḥ prajayā dhanena adha syāma surabhayaḥ gṛheṣu  
añjate vi añjate sam añjate kratum rihanti madhunā abhi añjate   sindhoḥ ucchvāse patayantam ukṣaṇam hiraṇya pāvāḥ paśum āsu gṛhnate  
yat vaḥ mudram pitaraḥ somyam ca tena u sacadhvam sva yaśasaḥ hi bhūta   te arvāṇaḥ kavayaḥ ā śṛṇota suvidatrāḥ vidathe huyamānāḥ  
ye atrayaḥ aṅgirasaḥ navagvāḥ iṣṭāvantaḥ rātiṣācaḥ dadhānāḥ   dakṣiṇāvantaḥ su kṛtaḥ ye u sthāsadya asmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam   dakṣiṇāvantaḥ su kṛtaḥ ye u sthāsadya asmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam                                                                                                                                   
adhā yathā naḥ pitaraḥ parāsaḥ pratnāsaḥ agne ṛtam āśaśānāḥ   śuci id ayan dīdhyataḥ ukthaśasaḥ kṣāmāḥ bhindantaḥ aruṇīḥ apa vran  
su karmānaḥ su rucaḥ devayantaḥ ayaḥ na devāḥ janimā dhamantaḥ   śucantaḥ agnim vāvṛdhantaḥ indram urvīm gavyām pariṣadam naḥ akran  
ā yūthā iva kṣumati paśvaḥ akhyat devānām janimānti ugraḥ   martāsaḥ cit urvaśīḥ akṛpran vṛdhe cit aryaḥ uparasya āyoḥ  
akarma te su apasaḥ abhūmaḥ ṛtam avasran uṣasaḥ vibhātīḥ   viśvam tat bhadram yat avanti devāḥ bṛhat vadema vidathe su vīrāḥ  
indraḥ mā marutvān prācyāḥ diśaḥ pātu bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
dhātā mā nirṛtyāḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ pātu bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
aditiḥ mā ādityaiḥ pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ pātu bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
somaḥ mā viśvaiḥ devaiḥ udīcyāḥ diśaḥ pātu bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
dhartā ha tvā dharuṇaḥ dhārayātai ūrdhvam bhānum savitā dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
prācyām tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
dakṣiṇāyām tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
pratīcyām tvā diśi purā saṃvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
udīcyām tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
dhruvāyām tvā diśi purā saṃvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
ūrdhvāyām tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhu cyutā pṛthivī dyām iva upari   loka kṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ yajāmahe ye devānām huta bhāgāḥ iha stha  
dhartā asi dharunaḥ asi vaṃsa gaḥ asi  
uda pūḥ asi madhu pūḥ asi vāta pūḥ asi  
itas ca mā amutas ca avatām yame iva yatamāne yat ā etam   pra vām bharan mānuṣāḥ devayantaḥ ā sīdatām svam u lokam vidāne  
svāsasthe bhavatam indave naḥ yuje vām brahma pūrvyam namobhiḥ   vi ślokaḥ eti pathyā iva sūriḥ śṛṇvantu viśve amṛtāsaḥ etat  
trīṇi padāni rupaḥ anu arohat catuṣpadīm anu etat vratena   akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhau abhi sam punāti   akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhau abhi sam punāti   akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhau abhi sam punāti   akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhau abhi sam punāti   akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhau abhi sam punāti   akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhau abhi sam punāti   akṣareṇa pr
devebhyaḥ kam avṛṇīta mṛtyum prajāyai kim amṛtam na avṛṇīta   bṛhaspatiḥ yajñam atanuta ṛṣiḥ priyām yamaḥ tanvam ā rireca  
tvam agne īḍitaḥ jātavedaḥ avāṭ havyāni surabhīṇi kṛtvā   prādāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhayā te akṣan addhi tvam deva prayatā havīṃṣi  
āsīnāsaḥ aruṇīnām upasthe rayim dhatta dāśuṣe martyāya   putrebhyaḥ pitaraḥ tasya vasvaḥ pra yacchata te iha ūrjam dadhāta  
agniṣvāttāḥ pitaraḥ ā iha gacchata sadaḥsadaḥ sadata su praṇītayaḥ   attaḥ havīṃṣi prayatāni barhiṣi rayim ca naḥ sarva vīram dadhāta  
upahūtāḥ naḥ pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ barhiṣyeṣu nidhiṣu priyeṣu   te ā gamantu te iha śruvantu adhi bruvantu te avantu asmān  
ye naḥ pituḥ pitaraḥ ye pitāmahāḥ anūjahire soma pītham vasiṣṭhāḥ   tebhiḥ yamaḥ samrarāṇaḥ havīṃṣi uśan uśadbhiḥ pratikāmam attu  
ye tātṛṣuḥ devatrā jehamānāḥ hotrāvidaḥ stoma taṣṭāsaḥ arkaiḥ   ā agne yāhi sahasram deva vandaiḥ satyaiḥ kavibhiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ gharma sadbhiḥ  
ye satyāsaḥ haviḥ adaḥ haviṣpāḥ indreṇa devaiḥ sa ratham tureṇa   ā agne yāhi suvidatrebhiḥ arvāṅ paraiḥ pūrvaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ gharma sadbhiḥ  
upa sarpa mātaram bhūmim etām uru vyacasam pṛthivīm su śevām   ūrṇamradāḥ pṛthivī dakṣiṇāvataḥ eṣā tvā pātu prapathe purastāt  
ud śvañcasva pṛthivi mā ni bādhathāḥ su upāyanā asmai bhava su upasarpaṇā   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram yathā sicā abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi   mātā putram 
ucchvañcamānā pṛthivī su tiṣṭhatu sahasram mite upa hi śrayantām   te gṛhāsaḥ ghṛtaścutaḥ syonāḥ viśvāhā asmai śaraṇāḥ santu atra  
ud te stabhnāmi pṛthivīm tvat pari imam logam nidadhan mā u aham riṣam   etām sthūṇām pitaraḥ dhārayanti te tatra yamaḥ sādanā te kṛṇotu  
imam agne camasam mā vi jihvaraḥ priyaḥ devānām uta somyānām   ayam yaḥ camasaḥ deva pānaḥ tasmin devāḥ amṛtāḥ mādayantām  
atharvā pūrṇam camasam yam indrāya abibhar vājinīvate   tasmin kṛṇoti su kṛtasya bhakṣam tasmin induḥ pavate viśvadānim  
yat te kṛṣṇaḥ śakunaḥ ātutoda pipīlaḥ sarpaḥ uta vā śvāpadaḥ   agniḥ tat viśvāt agadam kṛṇotu somaḥ ca yaḥ brāhmaṇām āviveśa  
payasvatīḥ oṣadhayaḥ payasvat māmakam payaḥ   apām payasaḥ yat payaḥ tena mā saha śumbhatu  
imāḥ nārīḥ avidhavāḥ su patnīḥ āñjanena sarpiṣā sam spṛśantām   anaśravaḥ anamīvāḥ su ratnāḥ ā rohantu janayaḥ yonim agre  
sam gacchasva pitṛbhiḥ sam yamena iṣṭāpūrtena parame vyoman   hitvā avadyam punar astam ehi sam gacchatām tanvā su varcāḥ  
ye naḥ pituḥ pitaraḥ ye pitāmahāḥ ye āviviśuḥ uru antarikṣam   tebhyaḥ svarāt asunītiḥ naḥ adya vatha avaśam tanvaḥ kalpayāti  
śītike śītikāvati hlādike hlādikāvati   maṇḍūkī apsu śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śītike śītikāvati śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ imam su agnim śamaya   śamaya   śam bhuvaḥ im
vivasvān naḥ abhayam kṛṇotu yaḥ sutrāmā jīra dānuḥ sudānuḥ   iha ime vīrāḥ bahavaḥ bhavantu gomat aśvavat mayi astu puṣṭam  
vivasvān naḥ amṛta tve dadhātu paraitu mṛtyuḥ amṛtam naḥ aitu   imān rakṣatu puruṣān ā jarimṇaḥ mā u su eṣām asavaḥ yamam guḥ  
yaḥ dadhre antarikṣe na mahnā pitṝṇām kaviḥ pramatiḥ matīnām   tam arcata viśvamitrāḥ havirbhiḥ sa naḥ yamaḥ prataram jīvase dhāt  
ā rohata divam uttamām ṛṣayaḥ mā bibhītana   soma pāḥ soma pāyinaḥ idam vaḥ kriyate haviḥ aganma jvotiḥ uttamam  
pra ketunā bṛhatā bhāti agniḥ ā rodasī vṛṣabhaḥ roravīti   divaḥ cit antāt upamām ud ānaṭ apām upasthe mahiṣaḥ vavardha  
nāke suparṇam upa yat patantam hrdā venantaḥ abhyacakṣata tvā   hiraṇya pakṣam varuṇasya dūtam yamasya yonau śakunam bhuranyum  
indra kratum naḥ ā bhara pitā putrebhyaḥ yathā   śikṣa naḥ asmin puruhūta yāmani jīvāḥ jyotiḥ aśīmahi  
apūpa apihitān kumbhān yān te devāḥ adhārayan   te te santu svadhāvantaḥ madhumantaḥ ghṛtaścutaḥ  
yāḥ te dhānāḥ anukirāmi tila miśrā svadhāvatīḥ   tāḥ te santu vibhvīḥ prabhvīḥ tāḥ te yamaḥ rājā anu manyatām  
punar dehi vanaspate yaḥ eṣa nihitaḥ tvayi   yathā yamasya sādane āsātau vidathāḥ vadan  
ā rabhasva jātavedaḥ tejasvat dharaḥ astu te   śarīram asya sam dahātha enam dehi su kṛtām u loke  
ye te pūrve parāgatāḥ apare pitaraḥ ca ye  tebhyaḥ ghṛtasya kulyā etu śata dhārā vyundatī  
etat ā roha vayaḥ unmṛjānaḥ svāḥ iha bṛhat u dīdayante   abhi prehi madhyataḥ mā apa hāsthāḥ pitṝnām lokam prathamaḥ yaḥ atra       abhi prehi madhyataḥ mā apa hāsthāḥ pitṝnām lokam prathamaḥ yaḥ atra       tvā iha bṛhat u dīdayante   abhi prehi madhyataḥ mā apa hāsthāḥ pitṝnām lokam prathamaḥ yaḥ atra       tvā iha bṛhat u dīdayante   abhi prehi madhyataḥ mā apa hāsthāḥ pitṝnām lokam prathamaḥ yaḥ atra    
ā rohata janitrīm jātavedasaḥ pitṛ yānaiḥ sam vaḥ ā rohayāmi   avāṭ havya iṣitaḥ havyavāhaḥ ījānam yuktāḥ su kṛtām dhatta loke  
devāḥ yajñam ṛtavaḥ kalpayanti haviḥ puroḍāśam srucaḥ yajñāyudhāni   tebhiḥ yāhi pathibhiḥ deva yānaiḥ yaiḥ ījānāḥ svargam yanti lokam  
ṛtasya panthām anu paśya sādhu aṅgirasaḥ su kṛtaḥ yena yanti   tebhiḥ yāhi pathibhiḥ svargam yatra ādityāḥ madhu bhakṣayanti tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva  
trayaḥ suparṇāḥ uparasya māyū nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi viṣṭapi śritāḥ   svargāḥ lokāḥ amṛtena viṣṭhāḥ iṣam ūrjam yajamānāya duhrām  
juhūḥ dādhāra dyām upabhṛt antarikṣam dhruvā dādhāra pṛthivīm pratiṣṭhām   prati imām lokāḥ ghṛta pṛṣṭhāḥ svargāḥ kāmaṃkāmam yajamānāya duhrām  
dhruvaḥ ā roha pṛthivīm viśva bhojasam antarikṣam upabhṛt ā kramasva   juhu dyām gaccha yajamānena sākam sruveṇa vatsena diśaḥ prapīnāḥ sarvāḥ dhukṣva a hṛṇyamānaḥ  
tīrthaiḥ taranti pravataḥ mahīḥ iti yajña kṛtaḥ su kṛtaḥ yena yanti   atra adadhuḥ yajamānāya lokam diśaḥ bhūtāni yat akalpayanta  
aṅgirasām ayanam pūrvaḥ agniḥ ādityānām ayanam gārhapatyaḥ dakṣiṇānām ayanam dakṣiṇāgniḥ   mahimānam agneḥ vihitasya brahmaṇā samaṅgaḥ sarvaḥ upa yāhi śagmaḥ  
pūrvaḥ agniḥ tvā tapatu śam purastāt śam paścāt tapatu gārhapatyaḥ   dakṣiṇāgniḥ te tapatu śarma varma uttaratas madhyatas antarikṣāt diśaḥ diśaḥ agne pari pāhi ghorāt  
yūyam agne śaṃtamābhiḥ tanūbhiḥ ījānam abhi lokam svargam   aśvāḥ bhūtvā pṛṣṭi vāhaḥ vahātha yatra devaiḥ sadhamādam madanti                                                                                                                                                                                  
śam agne paścāt tapa śam purastāt śam uttarāt śam adharāt tapa enam   ekaḥ tredhā vihitaḥ jātavedaḥ samyak enam dhehi su kṛtām u loke  
śam agnayaḥ samiddhāḥ ā rabhantām prājāpatyam medhyam jātavedasaḥ   śṛtam kṛṇvantaḥ iha mā ava cikṣipan  
yajñaḥ eti vitataḥ kalpamānaḥ ījānam abhi lokam svargam   tam agnayaḥ sarva hutam juṣantām prājāpatyam medhyam jātavedasaḥ  
ījānaḥ citam ārukṣat agnim nākasya pṛṣṭhāt divam utpatiṣyan   tasmai pra bhāti nabhasaḥ jyotiṣīmān svargaḥ panthāḥ su kṛte deva yānaḥ  
agniḥ hotā adhvaryuḥ te bṛhaspatiḥ indraḥ brahmā dakṣiṇatas te astu   hutaḥ ayam saṃsthitaḥ yajñaḥ eti yatra pūrvam ayanam hutānām

etat te devaḥ savitā vāsaḥ dadāti bhartave   tat tvam yamasya rājye vasānaḥ tārpyam cara  
dhānā dhenuḥ abhavat vatsaḥ asyāḥ tilaḥ abhavat   tām vai yamasya rājye akṣitām upa jīvati  
etāḥ te asau dhenavaḥ kāmadughāḥ bhavantu   enīḥ śyenīḥ sarūpāḥ virūpāḥ tila vatsāḥ upa tiṣṭhantu tvā atra  
enīḥ dhānāḥ hariṇīḥ śyenīḥ asya kṛṣṇāḥ dhānāḥ rohiṇīḥ dhenavaḥ te   tila vatsāḥ ūrjam asmai duhānāḥ viśvāhā santu an apasphurantīḥ  
vaiśvānare haviḥ idam juhomi sāhasram śata dhāram utsam   sa bibharti pitaram pitāmahān prapitāmahān bibharti pinvamānaḥ  
sahasra dhāram śata dhāram utsam akṣitam vyacyamānam salilasya pṛṣṭhe   ūrjam duhānam an apasphurantam upāsate pitaraḥ svadhābhiḥ  
idam kasāmbu cayanena citam tat sajātāḥ ava paśyateta   martyaḥ ayam amṛta tvam eti tasmai gṛhān kṛṇuta yāvatsabandhu  
iha eva edhi dhana saniḥ iha cittaḥ ihakratuḥ   iha edhi vīryavattaraḥ vayodhāḥ aparāhataḥ

yam te mantham yam odananam yat māṃsam nipṛṇāmi te   te te santu svadhāvantaḥ madhumantaḥ ghṛtaścutaḥ  
yāḥ te dhānāḥ anukirāmi tila miśrāḥ svadhāvatīḥ   tāḥ te santu udbhvīḥ prabhvīḥ tāḥ te yamaḥ rājā anu manyatām  
idam pūrvam aparam niyānam yena te pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ   purogavāḥ ye abhisācaḥ asya te tvā vahanti su kṛtām u lokam  
sarasvatīm devayantaḥ havante sarasvatīm adhvare tāyamāne   sarasvatīm su kṛtaḥ havante sarasvatī dāśuṣe vāryam dāt  
sarasvatīm pitaraḥ havante dakṣiṇāḥ yajñam abhinakṣamāṇāḥ   āsadya asmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam anamīvāḥ iṣaḥ ā dhehi asme  
sarasvati yā sa ratham yayātha ukthaiḥ svadhābhiḥ devi pitṛbhiḥ madantī   sahasra argham iḍaḥ atra bhāgam rāyaḥ poṣam yajamānāya dhehi  
pṛthivīm tvā pṛthivyām ā veśayāmi devaḥ naḥ dhātā pra tirāti āyuḥ   parāparā etā vasu vid vaḥ astu adhā mṛtāḥ pitṛṣu sam bhavantu  
ā pra cyavethām apa tat mṛjethām yat vām abhibhāḥ atra ūcuḥ   asmāt etam aghnyau tat vaśīyaḥ dātuḥ pitṛṣu ihabhojanau mama  
dakṣiṇā bhadrataḥ naḥ anena dattā su dughā vayodhāḥ   yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhyaḥ upasaṃparāṇayāt imān   yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhyaḥ upasaṃparāṇayāt imān   yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhyaḥ upasaṃparāṇayāt imān   yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhyaḥ upasaṃparāṇayāt imān   yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhyaḥ upasaṃparāṇayāt imān   yauvane jīvān upapṛñcat
idam pitṛbhyaḥ pra bharāmi barhiḥ jīvam devebhyaḥ uttaram stṛṇāmi   tat ā roha puruṣa medhyaḥ bhavan prati tvā jānantu pitaraḥ paretam  
prati tvā jānantu pitaraḥ paretam   yathā aparu tanvam sam bharasva gātrāṇi te brahmaṇā kalpayāmi  
parṇaḥ rājā apidhānam carūṇām ūrjaḥ balam sahaḥ ojaḥ naḥ āgan   āyuḥ jīvebhyaḥ vidadhat dīrgha āyu tvāya śata śāradāya  
ūrjaḥ bhāgaḥ yaḥ imam jajāna aśma annānām ādhipatyam jagāma   tam arcata viśvamitrāḥ havirbhiḥ sa naḥ yamaḥ prataram jīvase dhāt  
yathā yamāya harmyam avapan pañca mānavāḥ   eva ā vapāmi harmyam yathā me bhūrayaḥ asata  
idam hiraṇyam bibhṛhi yat te pitā abibhar purā   svargam yataḥ pituḥ hastam niḥ mṛḍḍhi dakṣiṇam  
ye ca jīvāḥ ye ca mṛtāḥ ye jātāḥ ye ca yajñiyāḥ   tebhyaḥ ghṛtasya kulyā etu madhu dhārā vyundatī  
vṛṣā matīnām pavate vicakṣaṇaḥ sūraḥ ahnām pratarītā uṣasām divaḥ   prāṇaḥ sindhūnām kalaśām acikradat indrasya hārdim āviśat manīṣayā  
tveṣaḥ te dhūmaḥ ūrṇotu divi sam śukraḥ ātataḥ   sūraḥ na hi dyutā tvam kṛpā pāvaka rocase  
 pra vai eti induḥ indrasya niṣkṛtim sakhā sakhyuḥ na pra mināti saṃgiraḥ   maryaḥ iva yoṣāḥ sam arṣase somaḥ kalaśe śata yāmanā pathā                                                                                                 
akṣan amīmadanta hi ava priyām adhūṣata   astoṣata sva bhānavaḥ viprāḥ yaviṣṭhāḥ īmahe  
ā yāta pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ   āyuḥ asmabhyam dadhataḥ prajām ca rāyaḥ ca poṣaiḥ abhi naḥ sacadhvam  
parā yāta pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pūryāṇaiḥ   adhā māsi punar ā yāta naḥ gṛhān haviḥ attum suprajasaḥ su vīrāḥ  
yat vaḥ agniḥ ajahāt ekam aṅgam pitṛ lokam gamayam jātavedāḥ   tat vaḥ etat punar ā pyāyayāmi sa aṅgāḥ svarge pitaraḥ mādayadhvam  
abhūt dūtaḥ prahitaḥ jātavedāḥ sāyam nyahnaḥ upavandyaḥ nṛbhiḥ   prādāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhayā te akṣan addhi tvam deva prayatā havīṃṣi  
asau hā iha te manaḥ kakutsalam iva jāmayaḥ   abhi enam bhūme ūrṇuhi  
śumbhantām lokāḥ pitṛṣadanāḥ pitṛṣadane tvā loke ā sādayāmi 
ye asmākam pitaraḥ teṣām barhiḥ asi 
ud uttamam varuṇa pāśam asmat ava adhamam śrathāya   adha vayam āditya vrate tava anāgasaḥ aditaye syāma  
pra asmat pāśān varuṇa muñca sarvān yaiḥ samāme badhyate yaiḥ vyāme   adhā jīvema śaradam śatāni tvayā rājan gupitāḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ   adhā jīvema śaradam śatāni tvayā rājan gupitāḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ   adhā jīvema śaradam śatāni tvayā rājan gupitāḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ   adhā jīvema śaradam śatāni tvayā rājan gupitāḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ   adhā jīvema śaradam śatāni tvayā rājan gupitāḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ   tvayā rājan gupitāḥ ra
agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā namaḥ 
somāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ 
pitṛbhyaḥ somavadbhyaḥ svadhā namaḥ 
yamāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ 
etat te pratatāmaha svadhā ye ca tvām anu 
etat te tatāmaha svadhā ye ca tvām anu 
etat te tata svadhā 
svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthiviṣadbhyaḥ  
svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ antarikṣa sadbhyaḥ 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ ūrje namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ rasāya  
namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ bhāmāya namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ manyave 
namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ yat ghoram tasmai namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ yat krūram tasmai 
namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ yat śivam tasmai namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ yat syonam tasmai 
namaḥ vaḥ pitaraḥ svadhā vaḥ pitaraḥ 
ye atra pitaraḥ pitaraḥ ye atra yūyam stha yuṣmān te anu yūyam teṣām śreṣṭhāḥ bhūyāstha 
ye iha pitaraḥ jīvāḥ iha vayam smaḥ   asmān te anu vayam teṣām śreṣṭhāḥ bhūyāsma  
ā tvā agne idhīmahi dyumantam deva ajaram   yat gha sā te panīyasī samidh dīdayati dyavi   iṣam stotṛbhyaḥ ā bhara  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
saṃsam sravantu nadyaḥ sam vātāḥ sam patatriṇaḥ   yajñam imam vardhayata giraḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi  
imam homāḥ yajñam avata imam saṃsrāvaṇāḥ uta yajñam imam vardhayata giraḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi 
rūpam rūpam vayaḥ vayaḥ saṃrabhya enam pari svaje   yajñam imam catasraḥ pradiśaḥ vardhayantu saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi  
śam te āpaḥ haimavatīḥ śam u te santu utsyāḥ   śam te saniṣyadāḥ āpaḥ śam u te santu varṣyāḥ  
śam te āpaḥ dhanvanyāḥ śam te santu anūpyāḥ   śam te khanitrimāḥ āpaḥ śam yāḥ kumbhebhiḥ ābhṛtāḥ  
anabhrayaḥ khanamānāḥ viprāḥ gambhīre apasaḥ   bhiṣagbhyaḥ bhiṣaktarāḥ āpaḥ achā vadāmasi  
apām aha divyānām apām srotasyānām   apām aha praṇejane aśvāḥ bhavatha vājinaḥ  
tāḥ apaḥ śivāḥ apaḥ a yakṣmaṃkaraṇīḥ apaḥ   yathā eva tṛpyate mayaḥ tāḥ te ā datta bhesajīḥ  
divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pari antarikṣāt vanaspatibhyaḥ adhi oṣadhībhyaḥ   yatra yatra vibhṛtaḥ jātavedāḥ tatas stutaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ naḥ ehi  
yaḥ te apsu mahimā yaḥ vaneṣu yaḥ oṣadhīṣu paśuṣu apsu antar   agne sarvāḥ tanvaḥ sam rabhasva tābhiḥ naḥ ehi draviṇaḥ dāḥ ajasraḥ  
yaḥ te deveṣu mahimā svargaḥ yā te tanuḥ pitṛṣu āviveśa   puṣṭiḥ yā te manuṣyeṣu paprathe agne tayā rayim asmāsu dhehi  
śrutkarṇāya kavaye vedyāya vacobhiḥ vākaiḥ upa yāmi rātim   yatas bhayam abhayam tat naḥ astu ava devānām yaja heḍaḥ agne  
yām āhutim prathamām atharvā yā jātā yā havyam akṛṇot jātavedāḥ   tām te etām prathamaḥ johavīmi tābhiḥ tuptaḥ vahatu havyam agniḥ agnaye svāhā  
ākūtim devīm subhagām puras dadhe cittasya mātā su havā naḥ astu   yām āśām emi kevalī sā me astu videyam enām manasi praviṣṭām  
ākūtyā naḥ bṛhaspate ākūtyā naḥ upa ā gahi   atha u bhagasya naḥ dhehi atha u naḥ su havaḥ bhava  
bṛhaspatiḥ me ākūtim āṅgirasaḥ prati jānātu vācam etām   yasya devāḥ devatāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ sa su praṇītāḥ kāmaḥ anu etu asmān  
indraḥ rājā jagataḥ carṣaṇīnām adhi kṣami viṣurūpam yat asti   tatas dadāti dāśuṣe vasūni codat rādhaḥ upastutaḥ cit arvāk  
sahasra bāhuḥ puruṣaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ sahasrapād   sa bhūmim viśvatas vṛtvā ati atiṣṭhat daśa aṅgulam  
tribhiḥ padbhiḥ dyām arohat pād asya iha bhavat punar   tathā vi akrāmat viṣvaṅ aśanān aśane anu  
tāvantaḥ asya mahimānaḥ tatas jyāyān ca pūruṣaḥ   pādaḥ asya viśvā bhūtāni tripād asya amṛtam divi  
puruṣaḥ eva idam sarvam yat bhūtam yat ca bhāvyam   uta amṛta tvasya īśvaraḥ yat anyena abhavat saha  
yat puruṣam vi adadhuḥ katidhā vi akalpayan   mukham kim asya kim bāhū kim ūrū pādau ucyate  
brāhmaṇaḥ asya mukham āsīt bāhūḥ rājanyaḥ abhavat   madhyam tat asya yat vaiśyaḥ padbhyām śūdraḥ ajāyata  
candramāḥ manasaḥ jātaḥ cakṣoḥ sūryaḥ ajāyata   mukhāt indraḥ ca agniḥ ca prāṇāt vāyuḥ ajāyata  
nābhyāḥ āsīt antarikṣam śīrṣṇaḥ dyauḥ sam avartata   padbhyām bhūmiḥ diśaḥ śrotrāt tathā lokām akalpayan  
virāj agre sam abhavat virājaḥ adhi pūruṣaḥ   sa jātaḥ ati aricyata paścāt bhūmim atho puras  
yat puruṣeṇa haviṣā devāḥ yajñam atanvata   vasantaḥ asya āsīt ājyam grīṣmaḥ idhmaḥ śarad haviḥ  
tam yajñam prāvṛṣā praukṣan puruṣam jātam agraśas   tena devāḥ ayajanta sādhyāḥ vasavaḥ ca ye  
tasmāt aśvāḥ ajāyanta ye ca ke ca ubhayāt atas   gāvaḥ ha jajñire tasmāt tasmāt jātāḥ aja avayaḥ  
tasmāt yajñāt sarva huta ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire   chandaḥ ha jajñire tasmāt yajuḥ tasmāt ajāyata  
tasmāt yajñāt sarva hutaḥ saṃbhṛtam pṛṣadājyam   paśūn tān cakre vāyavyān āraṇyāḥ grāmyāḥ ca ye  
sapta asya āsan paridhayaḥ tris sapta samidhaḥ kṛtāḥ   devāḥ yat yajñam tanvānāḥ abadhnan puruṣam paśum  
mūrdhnaḥ devasya bṛhataḥ aṃśavaḥ sapta saptatīḥ   rājñaḥ somasya ajāyanta jātasya puruṣāt adhi  
citrāṇi sākam divi rocanāni sarīsṛpāṇi bhuvane javāni   turmiśam sumatim ichamānaḥ ahāni gīrbhiḥ saparyāmi nākam  
su havam agne kṛttikā rohiṇī ca astu bhadram mṛgaśiraḥ śam ārdrā   punarvasū sūnṛtā cāru puṣyaḥ bhānuḥ āśleṣāḥ ayanam maghā me  
puṇyam pūrvā phalgunyau ca atra hastaḥ citrā śivā svāti sukhaḥ me astu   rādhe viśākhe su havā anurādhā jyeṣṭhā su nakṣatram ariṣṭa mūlam  
annam pūrvā rāsatām me aṣādhāḥ ūrjam devī uttarāḥ ā vahantu   abhijit me rāsatām puṇyam eva śravaṇaḥ śraviṣṭhāḥ kurvatām su puṣṭim  
ā me mahat śatabhiṣaj varīyaḥ ā me dvayā proṣṭhapadā su śarma   ā revatī ca aśvayujau bhagam me ā me rayim bharaṇyaḥ ā vahantu  
yāni nakṣatrāṇi divi antarikṣe apsu bhūmau yāni nageṣu dikṣu   prakalpayan candramāḥ yāni eti sarvāṇi mama etāni śivāni santu  
aṣṭāviṃśāni śivāni śagmāni saha yogam bhajantu me   yogam pra padye kṣemam ca kṣemam pra padye yogam ca namaḥ ahar rātrābhyām astu  
svastitam me su prātar su sāyam su divam su mṛgam su śakunam me astu   su havam agne svasti amartyam gatvā punar āya abhinandan  
anuhavam parihavam parivādam parikṣavam   sarvaiḥ me rikta kumbhān parā tān savitar suva  
apapāpam parikṣavam puṇyam bhakṣīmahi kṣavam   śivā te pāpa nāsikām puṇya gaḥ ca abhi mehatām  
imāḥ yāḥ brahmaṇaḥ pate viṣucīḥ vāte īrate   sadhrīcīḥ indra tāḥ kṛtvā mahyam śivatamāḥ kṛdhi  
svasti naḥ astu abhayam naḥ astu namaḥ ahar uratrābhyām astu 
śāntā dyauḥ śāntā pṛthivī śāntam idam uru antarikṣam   śāntāḥ udanvatīḥ āpaḥ śāntāḥ naḥ santu oṣadhīḥ  
śāntāni pūrvarūpāṇi śāntam naḥ astu kṛta akṛtam   śāntam bhūtam ca bhavyam ca sarvam eva śam astu naḥ  
iyam yā parameṣṭhinī vāc devī brahma saṃśitā   yayā eva sasṛje ghoram tayā eva śāntiḥ astu naḥ  
idam yat parameṣṭhinam manaḥ vām brahma saṃśitam   yena eva sasṛje ghoram tena eva śāntiḥ astu naḥ  
imāni yāni pañca indriyāni manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni me hṛdi brahmaṇā saṃśitāni   yaiḥ eva sasṛje ghoram taiḥ eva śāntiḥ astu naḥ  
śam naḥ mitraḥ śam varuṇaḥ śam viṣṇuḥ śam prajāpatiḥ   śam naḥ indraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ śam naḥ bhavatu aryamā  
śam naḥ mitraḥ śam varuṇaḥ śam vivasvān cham antakaḥ   utpātāḥ pārthiva antarikṣāḥ śam naḥ divicarāḥ grahāḥ  
śam naḥ bhūmiḥ vepyamānā śam ulkā nirhatam ca yat   śam gāvaḥ lohita kṣīrāḥ śam bhūmiḥ ava tīryatīḥ  
nakṣatram ulkā abhihatam śam astu naḥ śam naḥ abhicārāḥ śam u santu kṛtyāḥ   śam naḥ nikhātāḥ valgāḥ śam ulkāḥ deśa upasargāḥ śam u naḥ bhavantu  
śam naḥ grahāḥ cāndramasāḥ śam ādityaḥ ca rāhuṇā   śam naḥ mṛtyuḥ dhūmaketuḥ śam rudrāḥ tigma tejasaḥ  
śam rudrāḥ śam vasavaḥ śam ādityāḥ śam agnayaḥ   śam naḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ devāḥ śam devāḥ śam bṛhaspatiḥ  
brahma prajāpatiḥ dhātā lokāḥ vedāḥ sapta ṛṣayaḥ agnayaḥ   taiḥ me kṛtam svastyayanam indraḥ me śarma yacchatu brahmā me śarma yacchatu   viśve me devāḥ śarma yacchantu sarve me devāḥ śarma yacchantu  
yāni kāni cit śāntāni loke sapta ṛṣayaḥ viduḥ   sarvāṇi śam bhavantu me śam me astu abhayam me astu  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               
śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntibhiḥ 
yat iha ghoram yat iha krūram yat iha pāpam tat śāntam tat śivam sarvam eva śam astu naḥ 
śam naḥ indra agnī bhavatām avobhiḥ śam naḥ indrāvaruṇā rāta havyā   śam indrāsomā suvitāya śam yoḥ śam naḥ indrāpūṣaṇā vājasātau  
śam naḥ bhagaḥ śam u naḥ śaṃsaḥ astu śam naḥ puraṃdhiḥ śam u santu rāyaḥ   śam naḥ satyasya suyamasya śaṃsaḥ śam naḥ aryamā puru jātaḥ astu  
śam naḥ dhātā śam u dhartā naḥ astu śam naḥ urūcī bhavatu svadhābhiḥ   śam rodasī bṛhatī śam naḥ adriḥ śam naḥ devānām su havāni santu  
śam naḥ agniḥ jyotiḥ anīkaḥ astu śam naḥ mitrāvaruṇau aśvinā śam   śam naḥ su kṛtām su kṛtāni santu śam naḥ iṣiraḥ abhi vātu vātaḥ  
śam naḥ dyāvāpṛthivī pūrva hūtau śam antarikṣam dṛśaye naḥ astu   śam naḥ oṣadhīḥ vaninaḥ bhavantu śam naḥ rajasaḥ patiḥ astu jiṣṇuḥ  
śam naḥ indraḥ vasubhiḥ devaḥ astu śam ādityebhiḥ varuṇaḥ su śaṃsaḥ   śam naḥ rudraḥ rudrebhiḥ jalāṣaḥ śam naḥ tvaṣṭā gnābhiḥ iha śṛṇotu  
śam naḥ somaḥ bhavatu brahma śam naḥ śam naḥ grāvāṇaḥ śam u santu yajñāḥ   śam naḥ svarūnām mitayaḥ bhavantu śam naḥ prasvaḥ śam u astu vediḥ  
śam naḥ sūryaḥ uru cakṣāḥ ud etu śam naḥ bhavantu pradiśaḥ catasraḥ   śam naḥ parvatāḥ dhruvayaḥ bhavantu śam naḥ sindhavaḥ śam u santu āpaḥ  
śam naḥ aditiḥ bhavatu vratebhiḥ śam naḥ bhavantu marutaḥ su arkāḥ   śam naḥ viṣṇuḥ śam u pūṣā naḥ astu śam naḥ bhavitram śam u astu vāyuḥ  
śam naḥ devaḥ savitā trāyamāṇaḥ śam naḥ bhavantu uṣasaḥ vibhātīḥ   śam naḥ parjanyaḥ bhavatu prajābhyaḥ śam naḥ kṣetrasya patiḥ astu śaṃbhuḥ  
śam naḥ satyasya patayaḥ bhavantu śam naḥ arvantaḥ śam u santu gāvaḥ   śam naḥ ṛbhavaḥ su kṛtaḥ su hastāḥ śam naḥ bhavatu pitaraḥ haveṣu  
śam naḥ devāḥ viśva devāḥ bhavantu śam sarasvatī saha dhībhiḥ astu   śam abhiṣācaḥ śam u rātiṣācaḥ śam naḥ divyāḥ pārthivāḥ śam naḥ apyāḥ  
śam naḥ ajaḥ ekapād devaḥ astu śam ahiḥ budhnyaḥ śam samudraḥ   śam naḥ apām napāt peruḥ astu śam naḥ pṛṣṇiḥ bhavatu deva gopā  
ādityāḥ rudrāḥ vasavaḥ juṣantām idam brahma kriyamāṇam navīyaḥ   sṛṇvantu naḥ divyāḥ pārthivāsaḥ go jātāḥ uta ye yajñiyāsaḥ  
ye devānām ṛtvijaḥ yajñiyāsaḥ manoḥ yajatrāḥ amṛtāḥ ṛta jñāḥ   te naḥ rāsantām uru gāyam adya yūyam pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ  
tat astu mitrāvaruṇā tat agne śam yos asmabhyam idam astu śastam   aśīmahi gādham uta pratiṣṭhām namaḥ dive bṛhate sādanāya  
uṣāḥ apa svasuḥ tamaḥ sam vartayati vartanim su jāta tā   ayā vājam deva hitam sanema madema śata himāḥ su vīrāḥ  
indrasya bāhū sthavirau vṛṣāṇau citrāḥ imāḥ vṛṣabhau pārayiṣṇū   tau yokṣe prathamaḥ yogaḥ āgate yābhyām jitam asurāṇām svar yat  
āśuḥ śiśānaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ na bhīmaḥ ghanāghanaḥ kṣobhaṇaḥ carṣaṇīnām   saṃkrandanaḥ animiṣaḥ eka vīraḥ śatam senāḥ ajayat sākam indraḥ  
saṃkrandanena animiṣeṇa jiṣṇunā āyodhyena duścyavanena dhṛṣṇunā   tat indreṇa jayata tat sahadhvam yudhaḥ naraḥ iṣu hastena vṛṣṇā  
saḥ iṣu hastaiḥ sa niṣaṅgibhiḥ vaśī saṃsraṣṭā sa yudhaḥ indraḥ gaṇena   saṃsṛṣṭa jit soma pāḥ bāhu śardhī ugra dhanvā pratihitābhiḥ astā  
bala vijñāyaḥ sthaviraḥ pravīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamānaḥ ugraḥ   abhivīraḥ abhiṣatvā sahaḥ jit jaitram indra ratham ā tiṣṭha go vidam  
imam vīram anu harṣadhvam ugram indram sakhāyaḥ anu sam rabhadhvam   grāma jitam go jitam vajra bāhum jayantam ajma pramṛṇantam ojasā  
abhi gotrāṇi sahasā gāhamānaḥ adāyaḥ ugraḥ śatamanyuḥ indraḥ   duścyavanaḥ pṛtanāṣāh ayodhyaḥ asmākam senāḥ avatu pra yutsu  
bṛhaspate pari dīya rathena rakṣaḥ hā amitrām apabādhamānaḥ   prabhañjam śatrūn pramṛṇan amitrān asmākam edhi avitā tanūnām  
indraḥ eṣām netā bṛhaspatiḥ dakṣiṇā yajñaḥ puras etu somaḥ   deva senānām abhibhañjatīnām jayantīnām marutaḥ yantu madhye  
indrasya vṛṣṇaḥ varuṇasya rājñaḥ ādityānām marutām śardhaḥ ugram   mahāmanasām bhuvana cyavānām ghoṣaḥ devānām jayatām ud asthāt  
asmākam indraḥ samṛteṣu dhvajeṣu asmākam yāḥ iṣavaḥ tāḥ jayantu   asmākam vīrāḥ uttare bhavantu asmān devāsaḥ avata haveṣu  
idam ucchreyaḥ avasānam āgām śive me dyāvāpṛthivī abhūtām   asapatnāḥ pradiśaḥ me bhavantu na vai tvā dviṣmaḥ abhayam naḥ astu  
yatas indra bhayāmahe tatas naḥ abhayam kṛdhi   maghavam chagdhi tava tvam naḥ ūtibhiḥ vi dviṣaḥ vi mṛdhaḥ jahi  
indram vayam anūrādham havāmahe anu rādhyāsma dvipadā catuṣpadā   mā naḥ senāḥ araruṣīḥ upa guḥ viṣūciḥ indra druhaḥ vi nāśaya  
indraḥ trātā uta vṛtra hā para sphānaḥ vareṇyaḥ   sa rakṣitā caramatas sa madhyatas sa paścāt sa purastāt naḥ astu  
urum naḥ lokam anu neṣi vidvān svar yat jyotiḥ abhayam svasti   ugrā te indra sthavirasya bāhū upa kṣayema śaraṇā bṛhantā  
abhayam naḥ karati antarikṣam abhayam dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime   abhayam paścāt abhayam purastāt uttarāt adharāt abhayam naḥ astu  
abhayam mitrāt abhayam amitrāt abhayam jñātāt abhayam puras yaḥ   abhayam naktam abhayam divā naḥ sarvāḥ āśāḥ mama mitram bhavantu  
asapatnam purastāt paścāt naḥ abhayam kṛtam   savitā mā dakṣiṇatas uttarāt mā śacīpatiḥ  
divaḥ me ādityāḥ rakṣatu bhūmyāḥ rakṣantu agnayaḥ   indra agnī rakṣatām mā purastāt aśvinau abhitas śarma yacchatām   tiraścīn aghnyā rakṣatu jātavedāḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ me sarvatas santu varma  
agniḥ mā pātu vasubhiḥ purastāt tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
vāyuḥ mā antarikṣeṇa etasyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
somaḥ mā rudraiḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
varuṇaḥ mā ādityaiḥ etasyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
sūryaḥ mā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
āpaḥ mā oṣadhīmatīḥ etasyāḥ diśaḥ pāntu tāsu krame tāsu śraye tām puram praimi   tāḥ mā rakṣantu tāḥ mā gopāyantu tābhyaḥ ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
viśvakarmā mā sapta ṛṣibhiḥ udīcyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
indraḥ mā marutvān etasyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
prajāpatiḥ mā prajananavān saha pratiṣṭhayā dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
bṛhaspatiḥ mā viśvaiḥ devaiḥ ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmim śraye tām puram praimi   sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmai ātmānam pari dade svāhā  
agnim te vasuvantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ prācyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
vāyum te antarikṣavantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ etasyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
somam te rudravantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
varuṇam te ādityavantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ etasyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
sūryam te dyāvāpṛthivīvantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyava pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
apaḥ te oṣadhīmatīḥ ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ etasyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
viśvakarmāṇam te sapta ṛṣivantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ udīcyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
indram te marutvantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ etasyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
prajāpatim te prajananavantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
bṛhaspatim te viśvadevavantam ṛchantu   ye māghāyavaḥ ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ abhidāsān  
mitraḥ pṛthivyāḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
vāyuḥ antarikṣeṇa ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
sūryaḥ divā ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
candramāḥ nakṣatraiḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
somaḥ oṣadhībhiḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
yajñaḥ dakṣiṇābhiḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
samudraḥ nadībhiḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
brahma brahmacāribhiḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
indraḥ vīryeṇa ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
devāḥ amṛtena ud akrāman tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
prajāpatiḥ prajābhiḥ ud akrāmat tām puram pra nayāmi vaḥ   tām ā viśata tām pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yacchatu  
apa nyadhuḥ pauruṣeyam vadham yam indra agnī dhātā savitā bṛhaspatiḥ   somaḥ rājā varuṇaḥ aśvinā yamaḥ pūṣā asmān pari pātu mṛtyoḥ  
yāni cakāra bhuvanasya yaḥ patiḥ prajāpatiḥ mātariśvā prajābhyaḥ   pradiśaḥ yāni vasate diśaḥ ca tāni me varmāṇi bahulāni santu  
yat te tanūṣu anahyanta devāḥ dyurājayaḥ dehinaḥ   indraḥ yat cakre varma tat asmān pātu viśvatas  
varma me dyāvāpṛthivī varma ahar varma sūryaḥ   varma me viśve devāḥ kran mā mā prāpat pratīcikā  
gāyatrī uṣṇih anuṣṭubh bṛhatī paṅktiḥ triṣṭubh jagatyai 
āṅgirasānām ādyaiḥ pañca anuvākaiḥ svāhā 
ṣaṣṭhāya svāhā 
saptama aṣṭamābhyām svāhā 
nīla nakhebhyaḥ svāhā 
haritebhyaḥ svāhā 
kṣudrebhyaḥ svāhā 
paryāyikebhyaḥ svāhā 
prathamebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā 
dvitīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā 
tṛtīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā 
upottamebhyaḥ svāhā 
uttamebhyaḥ svāhā 
uttarebhyaḥ svāhā 
ṛṣibhyaḥ svāhā 
śikhibhyaḥ svāhā 
gaṇebhyaḥ svāhā 
mahā gaṇebhyaḥ svāhā 
sarvebhyaḥ aṅgirobhyaḥ vida gaṇebhyaḥ svāhā 
pṛthak sahasrābhyām svāhā 
brahmaṇe svāhā 
brahma jyeṣṭhā sambhṛtā viryāṇi brahma agre jyeṣṭham divam ā tatāna   bhūtānām brahmā prathamā uta jajñe tena arhati brahmaṇā spardhitum kaḥ  
ātharvaṇānām catur ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
pañca ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
ṣaṣ ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
sapta ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
aṣṭa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
nava ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
daśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
ekādaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
dvādaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
trayodaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
caturdaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
pañcadaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
ṣoḍaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
saptadaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
aṣṭādaśa ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
ekonaviṃśatiḥ svāhā 
viṃśatiḥ svāhā 
mahatkāṇḍāya svāhā 
tṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
eka ṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
kṣudrebhyaḥ svāhā 
eka anṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
rohitebhyaḥ svāhā 
sūryābhyām svāhā 
vrātyābhyām svāhā 
prājāpatyābhyām svāhā 
viṣāsahyai svāhā 
maṅgalikebhyaḥ svāhā 
brahmaṇe svāhā 
brahma jyeṣṭhā saṃbhṛtā vīryāṇi brahma agre jyeṣṭham divam ā tatāna   bhūtānām brahmā prathamā uta jajñe tena arhati brahmaṇā spardhitum kaḥ  
yena devam savitāram pari devāḥ adhārayan   tena imam brahmaṇas pate pari rāṣṭrāya dhattana  
pari imam indram āyuṣe mahe kṣatrāya dhattana   yathā enam jarase nayāt jyok kṣatre adhi jāgarat  
pari imam indram āyuṣe mahe śrotrāya dhattana   yathā enam jarase nayāt jyok śrotre adhi jāgarat  
pari dhatta dhatta naḥ varcasā imam jarā mṛtyum kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ   bṛhaspatiḥ prāyacchat vāsaḥ etat somāya rājñe paridhātavai u 
jarām su gaccha pari dhatsva vāsaḥ bhava gṛṣṭīnām abhiśasti pāḥ u  śatam ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcī rāyaḥ ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva  
pari idam vāsaḥ adhithāḥ svastaye abhūḥ vāpīnām abhiśasti pāḥ u  śatam ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcīḥ vasūni cāruḥ vi bhajāsi jīvan  
yoge yoge tavastaram vājevāje havāmahe   sakhāyaḥ indram ūtaye  
hiraṇya varṇaḥ ajaraḥ su vīraḥ jarā mṛtyuḥ prajayā sam viśasva   tat agniḥ āha tat u somaḥ āha bṛhaspatiḥ savitā tat indraḥ  
a śrāntasya tvā manasā yunajmi prathamasya ca   utkūlam udvahaḥ bhava uduhya prati dhāvatāt  
agneḥ prajātam pari yat hiraṇyam amṛtam dadhre adhi martyeṣu   yaḥ enat veda saḥ id enam arhati jarā mṛtyuḥ bhavati yaḥ bibharti  
yat dhiraṇyam sūryeṇa suvarṇam prajāvantaḥ manavaḥ pūrve īṣire   tat tvā candram varcasā sam sṛjati āyuṣmān bhavati yaḥ bibharti  
āyuṣe tvā varcase tvā ojase ca balāya ca   yathā hiraṇya tejasā vibhāsāsi janān anu  
yat veda rājā varuṇaḥ veda devaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ   indraḥ yat vṛtra hā veda tat te āyuṣyam bhuvat tat te varcasyam bhuvat  
gobhiḥ tvā pātu ṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣā tvā pātu vājibhiḥ   vāyuḥ tvā brahmaṇā pātu indraḥ tvā pātu indriyaiḥ  
somaḥ tvā pātu oṣadhībhiḥ nakṣatraiḥ pātu sūryaḥ   mādbhyaḥ tvā candraḥ vṛtra hā vātaḥ prāṇena rakṣatu  
tisraḥ divaḥ tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ trīṇi antarikṣāṇi caturaḥ samudrān   trivṛtam stomam trivṛtaḥ āpaḥ āhuḥ tāḥ tvā rakṣantu trivṛtā trivṛdbhiḥ  
trīn nākān trīn samudrān trīn bradhnān trīn vaiṣṭapān   trīn mātariśvanaḥ trīn sūryān goptṝn kalpayāmi te  
ghṛtena tvā sam ukṣāmi agne ājyena vardhayan   agneḥ candrasya sūryasya mā prāṇam māyinaḥ dabhan  
mā vaḥ prāṇam mā vaḥ apānam mā haraḥ māyinaḥ dabhan   bhrājantaḥ viśva vedasaḥ devāḥ daivyena dhāvata  
prāṇena agnim sam sṛjati vātaḥ prāṇena saṃhitaḥ   prāṇena viśvatomukham sūryam devāḥ ajanayan  
āyuṣā āyuḥ kṛtām jīva āyuṣmān jīva mā mṛthāḥ   prāṇena ātmanvatām jīva mā mṛtyoḥ ud agāḥ vaśam  
devānām nihitam nidhim yam indraḥ anvavindat pathibhiḥ deva yānaiḥ   āpaḥ hiraṇyam jugupuḥ trivṛdbhiḥ tāḥ tvā rakṣantu trivṛtā trivṛdbhiḥ  
trayastriṃśat devatāḥ trīṇi ca vīryāṇi priyāyamāṇāḥ jugupuḥ apsu antar   asmin candre adhi yat hiraṇyam tena ayam kṛṇavat vīryāṇi  
ye devāḥ divi ekādaśa stha te devāsaḥ haviḥ idam juṣadhvam 
ye devāḥ antarikṣe ekādaśa stha te devāsaḥ haviḥ idam juṣadhvam 
ye devā pṛthivyām ekādaśa stha te devāsaḥ haviḥ idam juṣadhvam 
asapatnam purastāt paścāt naḥ abhayam kṛtam   savitā mā dakṣiṇatas uttarāt mā śacīpatiḥ  
divaḥ me ādityāḥ rakṣantu bhūmyāḥ rakṣantu agnayaḥ   indra agnī rakṣatām mā purastāt aśvinau abhitas śarma yacchatām   tiraścīn aghnyā rakṣatu jātavedāḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ me sarvatas santu varma  
imam badhnāmi te maṇim dīrgha āyu tvāya tejase   darbham sapatna dambhanam dviṣataḥ tapanam hṛdaḥ  
dviṣataḥ tāpayan hṛdaḥ śatrūṇām tāpayan manaḥ   durhārdaḥ sarvān tvam darbha gharmaḥ iva abhīn saṃtāpayan  
gharmaḥ iva abhitapan darbha dviṣataḥ nitapan maṇe   hṛdaḥ sapatnānām bhinddhi indraḥ iva virujam balam  
bhinddhi darbha sapatnānām hṛdayam dviṣatām maṇe   udyan tvacam iva bhūmyāḥ śiraḥ eṣām vi pātaya  
bhinddhi darbha sapatnān me bhinddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ   bhinddhi me sarvān durhārdaḥ bhinddhi me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
chinddhi darbha sapatnān me chinddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ   chinddhi me sarvān durhārdaḥ chinddhi me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
vṛśca darbha sapatnān me vṛśca me pṛtanāyataḥ   vṛśca me sarvān durhārdaḥ vṛśca me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
kṛnta darbha sapatnān me kṛnta me pṛtanāyataḥ   kṛnta me sarvān durhārdaḥ kṛnta me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
piṃśa darbha sapatnān me piṃśa me pṛtanāyataḥ   piṃśa me sarvān durhārdaḥ piṃśa me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
vidhya darbha sapatnān me vidhya me pṛtanāyataḥ   vidhya me sarvān durhārdaḥ vidhya me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
nikṣa darbha sapatnān me nikṣa me pṛtanāyataḥ   nikṣa me sarvān durhārdaḥ nikṣa me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
tṛnddhi darbha sapatnān me tṛnddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ   tṛnddhi me sarvān durhārdaḥ tṛnddhi me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
runddhi darbha sapatnān me runddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ   runddhi me sarvān durhārdaḥ runddhi me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
mṛṇa darbha sapatnān me mṛṇa me pṛtanāyataḥ   mṛṇa me sarvān durhārdaḥ mṛṇa me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
mantha darbha sapatnān me mantha me pṛtanāyataḥ   mantha me sarvān durhārdaḥ mantha me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
piṇḍḍhi darbha sapatnān me piṇḍḍhi me pṛtanāyataḥ   piṇḍḍhi me sarvān durhārdaḥ piṇḍḍhi me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
oṣa darbha sapatnān me oṣa me pṛtanāyataḥ   oṣa me sarvān durhārdaḥ oṣa me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
daha darbha sapatnān me daha me pṛtanāyataḥ   daha me sarvān durhārdaḥ daha me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
jahi darbha sapatnān me jahi me pṛtanāyataḥ   jahi me sarvān durhārdaḥ jahi me dviṣataḥ maṇe  
yat te darbha jarā mṛtyu śatam varmasu varma te   tena imam varmiṇam kṛtvā sapatnām jahi vīryaiḥ  
śatam te darbha varmāṇi sahasram vīryāṇi te   tam asmai viśve tvām devāḥ jarase bhartavai aduḥ  
tvām āhuḥ deva varma tvām darbha brahmaṇaḥ patim   tvām indrasya āhuḥ varma tvam rāṣṭrāṇi rakṣasi  
sapatna kṣayaṇam darbha dviṣataḥ tapanam hṛdaḥ   maṇim kṣatrasya vardhanam tanū pānam kṛṇomi te  
yat samudraḥ abhyakrandat parjanyaḥ vidyutā saha   tatas hiranyayaḥ binduḥ tatas darbhaḥ ajāyata  
audumbareṇa maṇinā puṣṭi kāmāya vedhasā   paśūṇām sarveṣām sphātim goṣṭhe me savitā karat  
yaḥ naḥ agniḥ gārhapatyaḥ paśūnām adhipāḥ asat   audumbaraḥ vṛṣā maṇiḥ sam mā sṛjatu puṣṭyā  
karīṣiṇīm phalavatīm svadhām irām ca naḥ gṛhe   audumbarasya tejasā dhātā puṣṭim dadhātu me  
yat dvipād ca catuṣpād ca yāni annāni ye rasāḥ   gṛhṇe aham tu eṣām bhūmānam bibhrat audumbaram maṇim  
puṣṭim paśūnām pari jagrabha aham catuṣpadām dvipadām yat ca dhānyam   payaḥ paśūnām rasam oṣadhīnām bṛhaspatiḥ savitā me ni yacchāt  
aham paśūnām adhipāḥ asāni mayi puṣṭam puṣṭa patiḥ dadhātu   mahyam audumbaraḥ maṇiḥ draviṇāni ni yacchatu  
upa mā audumbaraḥ maṇiḥ prajayā ca dhanena ca   indreṇa jinvitaḥ maṇiḥ ā mā agan saha varcasā  
devaḥ maṇiḥ sapatna hā dhana sāḥ dhana sātaye   paśoḥ annasya bhūmānam gavām sphātim ni yacchatu  
yathā agre tvam vanaspate puṣṭhyā saha jajñiṣe   eva dhanasya me sphātim ā dadhātu sarasvatī  
ā me dhanam sarasvatī paya sphātim ca dhānyam   sinīvālī upa ā vahāt ayam ca audumbaraḥ maṇiḥ  
tvam maṇīṇām adhipāḥ vṛṣā asi tvayi puṣṭam puṣṭa patiḥ jajāna   tvayi ime vājāḥ draviṇāni sarva audumbaraḥ sa tvam asmat sahasva ārāt ārāt arātim amatim kṣudham ca  
grāmaṇīḥ asi grāmaṇīḥ utthāya abhiṣiktaḥ abhi mā siñca varcasā   tejaḥ asi tejaḥ mayi dhāraya adhi rayiḥ asi rayim me dhehi  
puṣṭiḥ asi puṣṭyāḥ mā sam aṅgdhi gṛhamedhī gṛhapatim mā kṛṇu   audumbaraḥ sa tvam asmāsu dhehi rayim ca naḥ sarva vīram ni yaccha rāyaḥ poṣāya prati muñce aham tvām  
ayam audumbaraḥ maṇiḥ vīraḥ vīrāya badhyate   sa naḥ sanim madhumatīm kṛṇotu rayim ca naḥ sarva vīram ni yacchāt  
śata kāṇḍaḥ duścyavanaḥ sahasra parṇaḥ uttiraḥ   darbhaḥ yaḥ ugraḥ oṣadhiḥ tam te badhnāmi āyuṣe  
na asya keśān pra vapanti na urasi tāḍam ā ghnate   yasmai a chinna parṇena darbhena śarma yacchati  
divi te tūlam oṣadhe pṛthivyām asi niṣṭhitaḥ   tvayā sahasra kāṇḍena āyuḥ pra vardhayāmahe  
tisraḥ divaḥ ati atṛṇat tisraḥ imāḥ pṛthivīḥ uta   tvayā aham durhārdaḥ jihvām ni tṛṇadmi vacāṃsi  
tvam asi sahamānaḥ aham asmi sahasvān   ubhau sahasvantau bhūtvā sapatnān sahiṣīvahi  
sahasva naḥ abhimātim sahasva pṛtanāyataḥ   sahasva sarvān durhārdaḥ suhārdaḥ me bahūn kṛdhi  
darbheṇa deva jātena divi ṣṭambhena śaśvat id   tena aham śaśvataḥ janām asanam sanavāni ca  
priyam mā darbha kṛṇu brahmarājanyābhyām śūdrāya ca āryāya ca   yasmai ca kāmayāmahe sarvasmai ca vipaśyate  
yaḥ jāyamānaḥ pṛthivīm adṛṃhat yaḥ astabhnāt antarikṣam divam ca   yam bibhratam nanu pāpmā viveda sa naḥ ayam darbhaḥ varuṇaḥ divā kaḥ  
sapatna hā śata kāṇḍaḥ sahasvān oṣadhīnām prathamaḥ sam babhūva   sa naḥ ayam darbhaḥ pari pātu viśvatas tena sākṣīya pṛtanāḥ pṛtanyataḥ  
sahasra arghaḥ śata kāṇḍaḥ payasvān apām agniḥ vīrudhām rājasūyam   sa naḥ ayam darbhaḥ pari pātu viśvatas devaḥ maṇiḥ āyuṣā sam sṛjāti naḥ  
ghṛtāt ulluptaḥ madhumān payasvān bhūmi dṛṃhaḥ acyutaḥ cyāvayiṣṇuḥ   nudan sapatnān adharān ca kṛṇvan darbhāḥ roha mahatām indriyeṇa  
tvam bhūmim ati eṣi ojasā tvam vedyām sīdasi cāruḥ adhvare   tvām pavitram ṛṣayaḥ abharanta tvam punīhi duritāni asmat  
tīkṣṇaḥ rājā viṣāsahī rakṣaḥ hā viśvacarṣaṇiḥ   ojaḥ devānām balam ugram etat tam te badhnāmi jarase svastaye  
darbheṇa tvam kṛṇavat vīryāṇi darbham bibhrat ātmanā mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ   atiṣṭhāya varcasā adhānyān sūryaḥ iva ā bhāhi pradiśaḥ catasraḥ  
jāṅgiḍaḥ asi jaṅgiḍaḥ rakṣitā asi jaṅgidaḥ   dvipād catuṣpād asmākam sarvam rakṣatu jaṅgidaḥ  
yāḥ gṛtsyaḥ tri pañca āśīḥ śatam kṛtyā kṛtaḥ ca ye  sarvān vinaktu tejasaḥ arasām jaṅgidaḥ karat  
arasam kṛtrimam nādam arasāḥ sapta visrasaḥ   apetaḥ jaṅgiḍāmatim iṣum astā iva śātaya  
kṛtyā dūṣaṇaḥ eva ayam atha u arāti dūṣaṇaḥ   atha u sahasvān jaṅgiḍaḥ pra naḥ āyumṣi tāriṣat  
sa jaṅgiḍasya mahimā pari naḥ pātu viśvatas   viṣkandham yena sāsaha saṃskandham ojaḥ ojasā  
tris tvā devāḥ ajanayat niṣṭhitam bhūmyām adhi   tam u tvā aṅgirāḥ iti brāhmaṇāḥ pūrvyāḥ viduḥ  
na tvā pūrvāḥ oṣadhayaḥ na tvā taranti yāḥ navāḥ   vibādhaḥ ugraḥ jaṅgiḍaḥ paripāṇaḥ su maṅgalaḥ  
atha upadāna bhagavaḥ jāṅgiḍa amita vīrya   purā te ugrā grasataḥ upendraḥ vīryam dadau 
ugraḥ id te vanaspate indraḥ ojmānam ā dadhau  amīvāḥ sarvāḥ cātayam jahi rakṣāṃsi oṣadhe 
āśarīkam viśarīkam balāsam pṛṣṭyāmayam   takmānam viśva śāradam arasām jaṅgiḍaḥ karat  
indrasya nāma gṛhṇantaḥ ṛsayaḥ jaṅgidam daduḥ   devāḥ yam cakruḥ bheṣajam agre viṣkandha dūṣaṇam  
sa naḥ rakṣatu jaṅgiḍaḥ dhana pālaḥ dhanā iva   devāḥ yam cakruḥ brāhmaṇāḥ paripāṇam arāti ham  
durhārdaḥ saṃghoram cakṣuḥ pāpa kṛtvānam āgamam   tān tvam sahasracakṣo pratībodhena nāśaya paripāṇaḥ asi jaṅgiḍaḥ  
pari mā divaḥ pari mā pṛthivyāḥ pari antarikṣāt pari mā vīrudbhyaḥ   pari mā bhūtāt pari mā uta bhavyāt diśaḥ diśaḥ jaṅgiḍaḥ pātu asmān  
yaḥ ṛṣṇavaḥ deva kṛtāḥ yaḥ uta u vavṛte anyaḥ   sarvān stān viśva bheṣajaḥ arasām jaṅgiḍaḥ karat  
śata vāraḥ anīnaśat yakṣmān rakṣāṃsi tejasā   ārohan varcasā saha maṇiḥ durṇāma cātanaḥ  
śṛṅgābhyām rakṣaḥ nudate mūlena yātudhānyaḥ   madhyena yakṣmam bādhate na enam pāpmā ati tatrati  
ye yakṣmāsaḥ arbhakāḥ mahāntaḥ ye ca śabdinaḥ   sarvām durṇāmahāḥ maṇiḥ śata vāraḥ anīnaśat  
śatam vīrān ajanayat śatam yakṣmān apāvapat   durṇāmnaḥ sarvān hatvā ava rakṣāṃsi dhūnute  
hiraṇya śṛṅgaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ śāta vāraḥ ayam maṇiḥ   durṇāmnaḥ sarvān tṛdhvā ava rakṣāṃsi akramīt  
śatam aham durṇāmnīnām gandharva apsarasām śatam   śatam śaśvanvatīnām śata vāreṇa vāraye  
idam varcaḥ agninā dattam āgan bhargaḥ yaśaḥ sahaḥ ojaḥ vayaḥ balam   trayastriṃśat yāni ca vīryāṇi tāni agniḥ pra dadātu me  
varcaḥ ā dhehi me tanvām sahaḥ ojaḥ vayaḥ balam   indriyāya tvā karmaṇe vīryāya prati gṛhṇāmi śata śāradāya  
ūrje tvā balāya tvā ojase sahase tvā   abhibhūyāya tvā rāṣṭra bhṛtyāya pari ūhāmi śata śāradāya  
ṛtubhyaḥ tvā ārtavebhyaḥ mādbhyaḥ saṃvatsarebhyaḥ   dhātre vidhātre samṛdhe bhūtasya pataye yaje  
na tam yakṣmāḥ arundhate na enam śapathaḥ aśnute   yam bheṣajasya gulguloḥ surabhiḥ gandhaḥ aśnute  
viṣvañcaḥ tasmāt yakṣmāḥ mṛgāḥ aśvāḥ iva īrate   yat gulgulu saindhavam yat vā api asi samudriyam  
ubhayoḥ agrabham nāma asmai ariṣṭatātaye 
aitu devaḥ trāyamāṇaḥ kuṣṭhaḥ himavataḥ pari   takmānam sarvam nāśaya sarvāḥ ca yātudhānyaḥ  
trīṇi te kuṣṭha nāmāni nadyamāraḥ nadyāḥ ariṣaḥ   nadyāḥ ayam puruṣaḥ riṣat   yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā  
jīvalā nāma te mātā jīvantaḥ nāma te pitā   nadyāḥ ayam puruṣaḥ riṣat   yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyam prātar atho divā  
uttamaḥ asi oṣadhīnām anaḍvān jagatām iva vyāghraḥ śvapadām iva   nadyāḥ ayam puruṣaḥ riṣat   yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyam prātar atho divā  
tris śāmbubhyaḥ aṅgirebhyaḥ tris ādityebhyaḥ pari   tris jātaḥ viśva devebhyaḥ   sa kuṣṭhaḥ viśva bheṣajaḥ sākam somena tiṣṭhati   aśvatthaḥ deva sadanaḥ tṛtīyasyām itas divi   tatra amṛtasya cakṣaṇam tatas kuṣṭhaḥ ajāyata   sa kuṣṭhaḥ viśva bheṣajaḥ sākam somena tiṣṭhati   hiraṇyayī nauḥ acarat hiraṇya bandhanā divi   tatra amṛtasya cakṣaṇam tatas kuṣṭhaḥ ajāyata   sa kuṣṭhaḥ viśva bheṣajaḥ sāka
śīrṣa śokam tṛtīyakam sa daṃdiḥ yaḥ ca hāyanaḥ   takmānam viśvadhā vīrya adharāñcam parā suva  
yat me chidram manasaḥ yat ca vācaḥ sarasvatī manyumantam jagāma   viśvaiḥ tat devaiḥ saha saṃvidānaḥ sam dadhātu bṛhaspatiḥ  
mā naḥ āpaḥ medhām mā brahma pra mathiṣṭana   suṣyadā yūyam syandadhvam upahūtaḥ aham sumedhāḥ varcasvī  
mā naḥ medhām mā naḥ dīkṣām mā naḥ hiṃsiṣṭam yat tapaḥ   śivāḥ naḥ śam santu āyuṣe śivāḥ bhavantu mātaraḥ  
yā naḥ pīparat aśvinā jyotiṣmatī tamaḥ tiras   tām asme rāsatām iṣam  
bhadram ichantaḥ ṛṣayaḥ svar vidaḥ tapaḥ dīkṣām upaniṣeduḥ agre   tatas rāṣṭram balam ojaḥ ca jātam tat asmai devāḥ upasaṃnamantu  
brahma hotā brahma yajñāḥ brahmaṇā svaravaḥ mitāḥ   adhvaryuḥ brahmaṇaḥ jātaḥ brahmaṇaḥ antarhitam haviḥ  
brahma srucaḥ ghṛtavatīḥ brahmaṇā vediḥ uddhitā   brahma yajñasya tattvam ca ṛtvijaḥ ye haviṣkṛtaḥ   śamitāya svāhā  
aṃhaḥ muce pra bhare manīṣām ā sutrāvṇe sumatim āvṛṇānaḥ   imam indra prati havyam gṛbhāya satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmāḥ  
aṃhaḥ mucam vrṣabham yajñiyānām virājantam prathamam adhvarāṇam   apām napātam aśvinā huve dhiyaḥ indriyeṇa te indriyam dattam ojaḥ  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   agniḥ mā tatra nayatu agniḥ medhā dadhātu me   agnaye svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   vāyuḥ mā tatra nayatu vāyuḥ praṇān dadhātu me vāyave svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   sūryaḥ mā tatra nayatu cakṣuḥ sūryaḥ dadhātu me   sūryāya svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   candraḥ mā tatra nayatu manaḥ candraḥ dadhātu me   candrāya svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   somaḥ mā tatra nayatu payaḥ somaḥ dadhātu me   somāya svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   indraḥ mā tatra nayatu balam indraḥ dadhātu me   indrāya svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   āpaḥ mā tatra nayatu amṛtam mā upa tiṣṭhatu   adbhyaḥ svāhā  
yatra brahma vidaḥ yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha   brahmā mā tatra nayatu brahmā brahma dadhātu me   brahmaṇe svāhā  
āyuṣaḥ asi prataraṇam vipram bheṣajam ucyase   tat āñjana tvam śaṃtāte śam āpaḥ abhayam kṛtam  
yaḥ harimā jāyānyaḥ aṅgabhedaḥ viṣalpakaḥ   sarvam te yakṣmam aṅgebhyaḥ bahis niḥ hantu āñjanam  
āñjanam pṛthivyām jātam bhadram puruṣa jīvanam   kṛṇotu apramāyukam ratha jūtim anāgasam  
prāṇa prāṇam trāyasva asave mṛḍa   nirṛte nirṛtyā naḥ pāśebhyaḥ muñca  
sindhoḥ garbhaḥ asi vidyutām puṣpam   vātaḥ prāṇaḥ sūryaḥ cakṣuḥ divaḥ payaḥ  
devāñjana traikakuda pari mā pāhi viśvatas   na tvā taranti oṣadhayaḥ bāhyāḥ parvatīyāḥ uta  
vi idam madhyam avāsṛpat rakṣaḥ hā amīva cātanaḥ   amīvāḥ sarvāḥ cātayat nāśayat abhibhāḥ itas  
bahu idam rājan varuṇa anṛtam āha pūruṣaḥ   tasmāt sahasra vīrya muñca naḥ pari aṃhasaḥ  
yat āpaḥ aghnyāḥ iti varuṇa iti yat ūcima   tasmāt sahasra vīrya muñca naḥ pari aṃhasaḥ  
mitraḥ ca tvā varuṇaḥ ca anupreyatuḥ āñjana   tau tvā anugatya dūram bhogāya punar ohatuḥ  
ṛṇāt ṛṇam iva sam naya kṛtyām kṛtyā kṛtaḥ gṛham   cakṣuḥ mantrasya durhārdaḥ pṛṣṭīḥ api śṛṇāñjana  
yat asmāsu duṣvapnyam yat goṣu yat ca naḥ gṛhe   anāmagaḥ tam ca durhārdaḥ priyaḥ prati muñcatām  
apām ūrjaḥ ojasaḥ vāvṛdhānam agneḥ jātam adhi jātavedasaḥ   catur vīram parvatīyam yat āñjanam diśaḥ pradiśaḥ karat id śivāḥ te  
catur vīram badhyate āñjanam te sarvāḥ diśaḥ abhayāḥ te bhavantu   dhruvaḥ tiṣṭhāsi savitā iva cāryaḥ imāḥ viśaḥ abhi harantu te balim  
ākṣva ekam maṇim ekam krṇuṣva snāhi ekena piba ekam eṣām   catur vīram nairṛtebhyaḥ caturbhyaḥ grāhyā bandhebhyaḥ pari pātu asmān  
agniḥ mā agninā avatu prāṇāya apānāya āyuṣe varcase ojase   tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā  
indraḥ mā indriyeṇa avatu prāṇāya apānāya āyuṣe varcase ojase   tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā  
somaḥ mā saumyena avatu prāṇāya apānāya āyuṣe varcase ojase   tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā  
bhagaḥ ma bhagena avatu prāṇāya apānāya āyuṣe varcase ojase   tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā  
marutaḥ mā gaṇaiḥ avantu prāṇāya apāna āyuṣe varcase ojase tejase   svastaye subhūtaye svāhā  
prajāpatiḥ tvā badhnāt prathamam a stṛtam vīryāya kam   tat te badhnāmi āyuṣe varcase ojase ca balāya ca astṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
ūrdhvaḥ tiṣṭhatu rakṣan apramādam astṛta imam mā tvā dabhan paṇayaḥ yātudhānāḥ   indraḥ iva dasyūn ava dhūnuṣva pṛtanyataḥ sarvām chatrūn vi sahasva astṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
śatam ca na praharantaḥ nighnantaḥ na tastire   tasmin indraḥ pari adatta cakṣuḥ prāṇam atho balam a stṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
indrasya tvā varmaṇā pari dhāpayāmaḥ yaḥ devānām adhirājaḥ babhūva   punar tvā devāḥ pra nayantu sarve a stṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
asmin maṇau eka śatam vīryāṇi sahasram prāṇāḥ asmin astṛte   vyāghraḥ śatrūn abhi tiṣṭha sarvān yaḥ tvā pṛtanyāt adharaḥ saḥ astu astṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
ghṛtāt ulluptaḥ madhumān payasvān sahasra prāṇaḥ śata yoniḥ vayodhāḥ   śambhūḥ ca mayobhūḥ ca ūrjasvān ca payasvān ca āstṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
yathā tvam uttaraḥ asaḥ asapatnaḥ sapatna hā   sajātānām asat vaśī tathā tvā savitā karat astṛtaḥ tvā abhi rakṣatu  
ā rātri pārthivam rajaḥ pituḥ aprāyi dhāmabhiḥ   divaḥ sadāṃsi bṛhatī vi tiṣṭhase ā tveṣam vartate tamaḥ  
na yasyāḥ pāram dadṛśe na yoyuvat viśvam asyām ni viśate yat ejati   ariṣṭāsaḥ te urvi tamasvati rātri pāram aśīmahi bhadre pāram aśīmahi  
ye te rātri nṛ cakṣasaḥ draṣṭāraḥ navatiḥ nava   aśītiḥ santi aṣṭa uta u te sapta saptatiḥ  
ṣaṣṭiḥ ca ṣaṭ ca revati pañcāśat pañca sumnayi   catvāraḥ catvāriṃśat ca trayaḥ triṃśat ca vājini  
dvau ca te viṃśatiḥ ca te rātri ekādaśa avamāḥ   tebhiḥ naḥ adya pāyubhiḥ nu pāhi duhitar divaḥ  
rakṣā mākir naḥ agha śaṃsaḥ īśata mā naḥ duḥśaṃsaḥ īśata   mā naḥ adya gavām stenaḥ māvīnām vṛkaḥ īśata  
mā aśvānām bhadre taskaraḥ mā nṛṇām yātudhānyaḥ   paramebhiḥ pathibhiḥ stenaḥ dhāvatu taskaraḥ   pareṇa datvatī rajjuḥ pareṇa aghāyuḥ arṣatu  
adha rātri tṛṣṭa dhūmam a śīrṣāṇam ahim kṛṇu   hanū vṛkasya jambhayā stenam drupade jahi  
tvayi rātri vasāmasi svapiṣyāmasi jāgṛhi   gobhyaḥ naḥ śarma yaccha aśvebhyaḥ puruṣebhyaḥ  
atha u yāni ca yasmā ha yāni ca antar parīṇahi   tāni te pari dadmasi  
rātri mātar uṣase naḥ pari dehi   uṣāḥ naḥ ahne pari dadātu ahar tubhyam vibhāvari  
yat kim ca idam patayati yat kim ca idam sarīsṛpam   yat kim ca parvata ayāsa tvam tasmāt tvam rātri pāhi naḥ  
sā paścāt pāhi sā puras sā uttarāt adharāt uta   gopāya naḥ vibhāvari stotāraḥ te iha smasi  
ye rātrim anutiṣṭhanti ye ca bhūteṣu jāgrati   paśūn ye sarvān rakṣanti te naḥ ātmasu jāgrati te naḥ paśuṣu jāgrati  
veda vai rātri te nāma ghṛtācī nāma vai asi   tām tvām bharadvājaḥ veda sā naḥ vitte adhi jāgrati  
iṣirā yoṣā yuvatiḥ damūnā rātrī devasya savituḥ bhagasya   aśva kṣabhā su havā saṃbhṛta śrīḥ ā paprau dyāvāpṛthivī mahitvā  
ati viśvāni aruhat gambhiraḥ varṣiṣṭham aruhanta śraviṣṭhāḥ   uśatī rātri anu sā bhadrā abhi tiṣṭhate mitraḥ iva svadhābhiḥ  
varye vande subhage sujāte ājagan rātri sumanāḥ iha syām   asmān trāyasva naryāṇi jātāḥ atho yāni gavyāni puṣṭyā  
siṃhasya rātri uśatī pīṃṣasya vyāghrasya dvīpinaḥ varcaḥ ā dade   aśvasya bradhnam puruṣasya māyum puru rūpāṇi kṛṇuṣe vibhātī  
śivām rātrim anusūryam ca himasya mātā su havā naḥ astu   asya stomasya subhage ni bodha yena tvā vande viśvāsu dikṣu  
stomasya naḥ vibhāvari rātri rājā iva joṣase   asāma sarva vīrāḥ bhavāma sarva vedasaḥ vyuchantīḥ anūṣasaḥ  
śamyā ha nāma dadhiṣe mama dipsanti ye dhanā   rātrīhi tān asutapāḥ yaḥ stenaḥ na vidyate yat punar na vidyate  
bhadrā asi rātri camasaḥ na viṣṭaḥ viṣvaṅ go rūpam yuvatiḥ bibharṣi   cakṣuṣmatī me uśatī vapūmṣi prati tvam divyā na kṣām amukthāḥ  
yaḥ adya stenaḥ āyati aghāyuḥ martyaḥ ripuḥ   rātrī tasya pratītya pra grīvāḥ pra śiraḥ hanat  
pra pādau na yathāyati pra hastau na yathā āśiṣat   yaḥ malimluḥ upāyati sa saṃpiṣṭaḥ apāyati   apāyati su apāyati śuṣke sthāṇau apāyati  
adha rātri tṛṣṭa dhūmam a śīrṣāṇam ahim kṛṇu   akṣau vṛkasya niḥ jahyāḥ tena tam drupade jahi  
ye te rātri anaḍvāhaḥ tīkṣṇa śṛṅgāḥ su āśavaḥ   tebhiḥ naḥ adya pārayāti durgāṇi viśvahā  
rātrim rātrim ariṣyantaḥ tarema tanvā vayam   gambhīram aplavāḥ iva na tareyuḥ arātayaḥ  
yathā śāmyākaḥ prapatan apavān na anuvidyate   eva rātri pra pātaya yaḥ asmām abhyaghāyati  
apa stenam vāsayaḥ go ajam uta taskaram   atha u yaḥ arvataḥ śiraḥ abhidhāya ninīṣati  
yat adya rātri subhage vibhajanti ayaḥ vasu   yat etat asmān bhojaya yathā id anyān upāyasi  
uṣase naḥ pari dehi sarvān rātri anāgasaḥ   uṣāḥ naḥ ahne ā bhajāt ahar tubhyam vibhāvari  
ayutaḥ aham ayutaḥ me ātmā ayutam me cakṣuḥ ayutam me śrotram   ayutaḥ me prāṇaḥ ayutaḥ me apānaḥ ayutaḥ me vyānaḥ ayutaḥ aham sarvaḥ  
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinoḥ bāhubhyām pūṣṇaḥ hastābhyām prasūtaḥ ā rabhe 
kāmaḥ tat agre sam avartata manasaḥ retaḥ prathamam yat āsīt   sa kāma kāmena bṛhatā sayonī rāyaḥ poṣam yajamānāya dhehi  
tvam kāma sahasā asi pratiṣṭhitaḥ vibhuḥ vibhāvā sakhaḥ ā sakhīyate   tvam ugraḥ pṛtanāsu sasahiḥ sahaḥ ojaḥ yajamānāya dhehi  
dūrāt cakamānāya pratipāṇāya akṣaye   ā asmai aśṛṇvan āśāḥ kāmena ajanayan svar  
kāmena mā kāmaḥ āgan hṛdayāt dhṛdayam pari   yat amīṣām adaḥ manaḥ tat aitu upa mām iha  
yat kāma kāmayamānāḥ idam kṛṇmasi te haviḥ   tat naḥ sarvam sam ṛdhyatām atha etasya haviṣaḥ vīhi svāhā  
kālaḥ aśvaḥ vahati sapta raśmiḥ sahasra akṣaḥ ajaraḥ bhūri retāḥ   tam ā rohanti kavayaḥ vipaścitaḥ tasya cakrā bhuvanāni viśvā  
sapta cakrān vahati kālaḥ eṣa sapta asya nābhīḥ amṛtam nu akṣaḥ   saḥ imā viśvā bhuvanāni añjat kālaḥ saḥ īyate prathamaḥ nu devaḥ  
pūrṇaḥ kumbhaḥ adhi kāle āhitaḥ tam vai paśyāmaḥ bahudhā nu santam   saḥ imā viśvā bhuvanāni pratyaṅ kālam tam āhuḥ parame vyoman  
saḥ eva sam bhuvanāni ābharat saḥ eva sam bhuvanāni pari ait   pitā san abhavat putraḥ eṣām tasmāt vai na anyat param asti tejaḥ  
kālaḥ amūm divam ajanayat kālaḥ imāḥ pṛthivīḥ uta   kāle ha bhūtam bhavyam ceṣitam ha vi tiṣṭhate  
kālaḥ bhūtim asṛjata kāle tapati sūryaḥ   kāle ha viśvā bhūtāni kāle cakṣuḥ vi paśyati  
kāle manaḥ kāle prāṇaḥ kāle nāma samāhitam   kālena sarvāḥ nandanti āgatena prajāḥ imāḥ  
kāle tapaḥ kāle jyeṣṭham kāle brahma samāhitam   kālaḥ ha sarvasya īśvaraḥ yaḥ pitā āsīt prajāpateḥ  
tena iṣitam tena jātam tat u tasmin pratiṣṭhitam   kālaḥ ha brahma bhūtvā bibharti parameṣṭhinam  
kālaḥ prajāḥ asṛjata kālaḥ agre prajāpatim   svayaṃbhūḥ kaśyapaḥ kālāt tapaḥ kālāt ajāyata  
kālāt āpaḥ sam abhavan kālāt brahma tapaḥ diśaḥ   kālena ud eti sūryaḥ kāle ni viśate punar  
kālena vātaḥ pavate kālena pṛthivī mahī   dyauḥ mahī kāle āhitā  
kālaḥ ha bhūtam bhavyam ca putraḥ ajanayat purā   kālāt ṛcaḥ sam abhavan yajuḥ kālāt ajāyata  
kālaḥ yajñam sam airayat devebhyaḥ bhāgam akṣitam   kāle gandharva apsarasaḥ kāle lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ  
kāle ayam aṅgirāḥ devaḥ atharvā ca adhi tiṣṭhataḥ   imam ca lokam paramam ca lokam puṇyān ca lokān vidhṛtīḥ ca puṇyāḥ   sarvān lokān abhijitya brahmaṇā kālaḥ saḥ īyate paramaḥ nu devaḥ  
rātrim rātrim a prayātam bharantaḥ aśvāya iva tiṣṭhate ghāsam asmai   rāyaḥ poṣeṇa sam iṣā madantaḥ mā te agne prativeśāḥ riṣāma  
yā te vasoḥ vātaḥ iṣuḥ sā te eṣā tayā naḥ mṛḍa   rāyaḥ poṣeṇa sam iṣā madantaḥ mā te agne prativeśāḥ riṣāma  
sāyam sāyam gṛhapatiḥ naḥ agniḥ prātar prātar saumanasasya dātā   vasoḥ vasoḥ vasu dānaḥ edhi vayam tvā indhānāḥ tanvam puṣema  
prātar prātar gṛhapatiḥ naḥ agniḥ sāyaṃsāyam saumanasasya dātā   vasoḥ vasoḥ vasu dānaḥ edhi indhānāḥ tvā śataṃhimāḥ ṛdhema  
a paścā dagdha annasya bhūyāsam   anna ādāya annapataye rudrāya namaḥ agnaye   sabhyaḥ sabhām me pāhi ye ca sabhyāḥ sabhāsadaḥ  
tvām indra puruhūta viśvam āyuḥ vi aśnavan   aharahar balim id te harantaḥ aśvāya iva tiṣṭhate ghāsam agne  
yamasya lokāt adhi ā babhūvitha pramadāḥ martyān pra yunakṣi dhīraḥ   ekākinā sa ratham yāsi vidvān svapnam mimānaḥ asurasya yonau  
bandhaḥ tvā agre viśva cayāḥ apaśyat purā rātryāḥ janitoḥ eke ahni   tatas svapna idam adhi ā babhūvitha bhiṣagbhyaḥ rūpam apagūhamānaḥ  
bṛhat gāvāsurebhyaḥ adhi devān upāvartata mahimānam ichan   tasmai svapnāya dadhuḥ ādhipatyam trayastriṃśāsaḥ svar ānaśānāḥ  
na etām viduḥ pitaraḥ na uta devāḥ yeṣām jalpiḥ carati antarā idam   trite svapnam adadhuḥ āptye naraḥ ādityāsaḥ varuṇena anuśiṣṭāḥ  
yasya krūram abhajanta duṣkṛtaḥ asvapnena sukṛtaḥ puṇyam āyuḥ   svar madasi parameṇa bandhunā tapyamānasya manasaḥ adhi jajñiṣe  
vidma te sarvāḥ parijāḥ purastāt vidma svapna yaḥ adhipāḥ iha te   yaśaśvinaḥ naḥ yaśasā iha pāhi ārāt dviṣebhiḥ apa yāhi dūram  
yathā kalām yathā śapham yathā ṛṇam samnayanti   eva duṣvapnyam sarvam apriye sam nayāmasi  
sam rājānaḥ aguḥ sam ṛṇāmi aguḥ sam kuṣṭhāḥ aguḥ sam kalāḥ aguḥ   sam asmāsu yat duṣvapnyam niḥ dviṣate duṣvapnyam suvāma  
devānām patnīnām garbha yamasya kara yaḥ bhadraḥ svapna   sa mama yaḥ pāpaḥ tat dviṣate pra hiṇmaḥ   mā tṛṣṭānām asi kṛṣṇa śakuneḥ mukham  
tam tvā svapna tathā sam vidma sa tvam svapna aśvaḥ iva kāyam aśvaḥ iva nīnāham   anā asmākam deva pīyum piyārum vapa yat asmāsu duṣvapnyam yat goṣu yat ca naḥ gṛhe  
anā asmākaḥ tat deva pīyuḥ piyāruḥ niṣkam iva prati muñcatām   nava aratnīn apamayāḥ asmākam tatas pari   duṣvapnyam sarvam dviṣate niḥ dayāmasi  
ghṛtasya jūtiḥ samanā sa devā saṃvatsaram haviṣā vardhayantī   śrotram cakṣuḥ prāṇaḥ achinnaḥ naḥ astu achinnāḥ vayam āyuṣaḥ varcasaḥ  
upa asmān prāṇaḥ hvayatām upa prāṇam havāmahe   varcaḥ jagrāha pṛthivī antarikṣam varcaḥ somaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ vidhattā  
varcasaḥ dyāvāpṛthivī saṃgrahaṇī babhūvathuḥ varcaḥ gṛhītvā pṛthivīm anu sam carema   yaśasam gāvaḥ gopatim upa tiṣṭhanti āyatīḥ yaśaḥ gṛhītvā pṛthivīm anu sam carema  
vrajam kṛṇudhvam sa hi vaḥ nṛpāṇaḥ varma ā sīvyadhvam bahulā pṛthūni   puraḥ kṛṇudhvam āyasīḥ a dhṛṣṭāḥ mā vaḥ susrot camasaḥ dṛṃhata tam  
yajñasya cakṣuḥ prabhṛtiḥ mukham ca vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi   imam yajñam vitatam viśvakarmaṇā devāḥ yantu sumanasyamānāḥ  
ye devānām ṛtvijaḥ ye ca yajñiyāḥ yebhyaḥ havyam kriyate bhāgadheyam   imam yajñam saha patnībhiḥ etya yāvantaḥ devāḥ taviṣā mādayantām  
tvam agne vrata pāḥ asi devaḥ ā martyeṣu ā   tvam yajñeṣu īḍyaḥ  
yat vaḥ vayam pramināma vratāni viduṣām devāḥ aviduṣṭarāsaḥ   agniḥ tat viśvāt ā pṛṇātu vidvān somasya yaḥ brāhmaṇām āviveśa  
ā devānām api panthām aganma yat śaknavāma tat anupravoḍhum   agniḥ vidvān sa yajāt saḥ id hotā saḥ adhvarān saḥ ṛtūn kalpayāti  
vāc me āsan nasoḥ prāṇaḥ cakṣuḥ akṣṇoḥ śrotram karṇayoḥ   a palitāḥ keśāḥ a śoṇāḥ dantāḥ bahu bāhvoḥ balam  
ūrvoḥ ojaḥ jaṅghayoḥ javaḥ pādayoḥ   pratiṣṭhā ariṣṭāni me sarvātmā anibhṛṣṭaḥ  
tanūḥ tanvā me sahe dataḥ sarvam āyuḥ aśīya   syonam me sīda puruḥ pṛṇasva pavamānaḥ svarge  
priyam mā kṛṇu deveṣu priyam rājasu mā kṛṇu   priyam sarvasya paśyataḥ uta śūdraḥ uta ārye  
ud tiṣṭha brahmaṇas pate devān yajñena bodhaya   āyuḥ prāṇam prajām paśūn kīrtim yajamānam ca vardhaya  
agne samidham āhārṣam bṛhate jātavedase   sa me śraddhām ca medhām ca jātavedāḥ pra yacchatu  
idhmena tvā jātavedaḥ samidhā vardhayāmasi   tathā tvam asmān vardhaya prajayā ca dhanena ca  
yat agne yāni kāni cit ā te dārūṇi dadhmasi   sarvam tat astu me śivam tat juṣasva yaviṣṭhya  
etāḥ te agne samidhaḥ tvam iddhaḥ samidh bhava   āyuḥ asmāsu dhehi amṛta tvam ācāryāya  
hariḥ suparṇaḥ divam āruhaḥ arciṣā ye tvā dipsanti divam utpatantam   ava tām jahi harasā jātavedaḥ a bibhyat ugraḥ arciṣā divam ā roha sūrya  
ayaḥ jālāḥ asurāḥ māyinaḥ ayasmayaiḥ pāśaiḥ aṅkinaḥ ye caranti   tān te randhayāmi harasā jātavedaḥ sahasra ṛṣṭiḥ sapatnān pramṛṇan pāhi vajraḥ  
paśyema śaradaḥ śatam 
jīvema śaradaḥ śatam 
budhyema śaradaḥ śatam 
rohema śaradaḥ śatam 
pūṣā ima śaradaḥ śatam 
bhavema śaradaḥ śatam 
bhūṣema śaradaḥ śatam 
bhūyasīḥ śaradaḥ śatam 
avyasaḥ ca vyacasaḥ ca bilam vi syāmi māyayā   tābhyām uddhṛtya vedam atha karmāṇi kṛṇmahe  
jīvā stha jīvyāsam sarvam āyuḥ jīvyāsam  
upajīvā stha upa jīvyāsam sarvam āyuḥ jīvyāsam  
saṃjīvāḥ stha sam jīvyāsam sarvam āyuḥ jīvyāsam  
jīvalā stha jīvyāsam sarvam āyuḥ jīvyāsam  
indra jīva sūrya jīva devāḥ jīvāḥ jīvyāsam aham  sarvam āyuḥ jīvyāsam  
stutā mayā vara dā veda mātā pra codayantām pāvamānī dvijānām   āyuḥ prāṇam prajām paśum kīrtim draviṇam brahmavarcasam   mahyam dattvā vrajata brahma lokam  
yasmāt kośāt udabharāma vedam tasmin antar ava dadhmaḥ enam   kṛtam iṣṭam brahmaṇaḥ vīryeṇa tena mā devāḥ tapasā avata iha  
indra tvā vṛṣabham vayam sute some havāmahe   sa pāhi madhvaḥ andhasaḥ  
marutaḥ yasya hi kṣaye pāthāḥ divaḥ vimahasaḥ   sa sugopātamaḥ janaḥ  
ukṣa annāya vaśā annāya soma pṛṣṭhāya vedhase   stomaiḥ vidhema agnaye  
marutaḥ potrāt suṣṭubhaḥ su arkāt ṛtunā somam pibantu  
agniḥ āgnīdhrāt suṣṭubhaḥ su arkāt ṛtunā somam pibatu 
indraḥ brahmā brāhmaṇāt suṣṭubhaḥ su arkāt ṛtunā somam pibatu 
devaḥ draviṇaḥ dāḥ potrāt suṣṭubhaḥ su arkāt ṛtunā somam pibatu 
ā yāhi suṣuma hi te indra somam pibā imam   ā idam barhiḥ sadaḥ mama  
ā tvā brahma yujā harī vahatām indra keśinā   upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu  
brahmāṇaḥ tvā vayam yujā soma pām indra sominaḥ   sutāvantaḥ havāmahe  
ā naḥ yāhi sutāvataḥ asmākam suṣṭutīḥ upa   pibā su śiprin andhasaḥ  
ā te siñcāmi kukṣyoḥ anu gātrā vi dhāvatu   gṛbhāya jihvayā madhu  
svāduḥ te astu saṃsude madhumān tanve tava   somaḥ śam astu te hṛde  
ayam u tvā vicarṣaṇe janīḥ iva abhi saṃvṛtaḥ   pra somaḥ indra sarpatu  
tuvi grīvaḥ vapodaraḥ su bāhuḥ andhasaḥ sade   indraḥ vṛtrāṇi jighnate  
indra prehi puras tvam viśvasya īśānaḥ ojasā   vṛtrāṇi vṛtraham jahi  
dīrghaḥ te astu aṅkuśaḥ yena vasu prayacchasi   yajamānāya sunvate  
ayam te indra somaḥ nipūtaḥ adhi barhiṣi   ehi īm asya drava piba  
śāci go śāci pūjana ayam raṇāya te sutaḥ   ākhaṇḍala pra hūyase  
yaḥ te śṛṅga vṛṣaḥ napāt praṇapāt kuṇḍapāyyaḥ   ni asmin dadhre ā manaḥ  
indra tvā vṛṣabham vayam sute some havāmahe   sa pāhi madhvaḥ andhasaḥ  
indra kratu vidam sutam somam harya puruṣṭuta   pibā vṛṣasva tātṛpim  
indra pra naḥ dhitāvānam yajñam viśvebhiḥ devebhiḥ   tira stavāna viśpate  
indra somāḥ sutāḥ ime tava pra yanti satpate   kṣayam candrāsaḥ indavaḥ  
dadhiṣva jaṭhare sutam somam indra vareṇyam   tava dyukṣāsaḥ indavaḥ  
girvaṇaḥ pāhi naḥ sutam madhoḥ dhārābhiḥ ajyase   indra tvā adātam id yaśaḥ  
abhi dyumnāni vaninaḥ indram sacante akṣitā   pītvī somasya vāvṛdhe  
arvāvataḥ naḥ ā gahi parāvataḥ ca vṛtrahan   imā juṣasva naḥ giraḥ  
yat antarā parāvatam arvāvatam ca hūyase   indra iha tatas ā gahi  
ud gha id abhi śrutāmagham vṛṣabham narya apasam   astāram eṣi sūrya  
nava yaḥ navatim puras bibheda bāhu ojasā   ahim ca vṛtrahā avadhīt  
sa naḥ indraḥ śivaḥ sakhā aśvāvat gomat yavamat   uru dhārā iva dohate  
indra kratu vidam sutam somam harya puruṣṭuta   pibā vṛṣasva tātṛpim  
eva pāhi pratnathā mandatu tvā śrudhi brahma vāvṛdhasva uta gīrbhiḥ   āvis sūryam kṛṇuhi pīpihi iṣaḥ jahi śatrūṃr abhi gāḥ indra tṛndhi  
arvāṅ ehi soma kāmam tvā āhuḥ ayam sutaḥ tasya pibā madāya   uru vyacāḥ jaṭhare ā vṛṣasva pitā iva naḥ śṛṇuhi hūyamānaḥ  
āpūrṇaḥ asya kalaśaḥ svāhā sektā iva kośam siṣice pibadhyai   sam u priyāḥ āvavṛtran madāya pradakṣiṇit abhi somāsaḥ indram  
tam vaḥ dasmam ṛtīṣaham vasoḥ mandānam andhasaḥ   abhi vatsam na svasareṣu dhenavaḥ indram gīrbhiḥ navāmahe  
dyukṣam sudānum taviṣībhiḥ āvṛtam girim na puru bhojasam   kṣumantam vājam śatinam sahasriṇam makṣū gomantam īmahe  
tat tvā yāmi su vīryam tat brahma pūrvacittaye   yena yatibhyaḥ bhṛgave dhane hite yena praskaṇvam āvitha  
yena samudram asṛjaḥ mahīḥ apaḥ tat indra vṛṣṇi te śavaḥ   sadyas saḥ asya mahimā na saṃnaśe yam kṣoṇīḥ anucakrade
