ud u te madhumattamāḥ giraḥ stomāsaḥ īrate   satrājitaḥ dhanasāḥ akṣita ūtayaḥ vājayantaḥ rathāḥ iva  
kaṇvāḥ iva bhṛgavaḥ sūryāḥ iva viśvam id dhītam ānaśuḥ   indram stomebhiḥ mahayantaḥ āyavaḥ priyamedhāsaḥ asvaran  
indraḥ pūrbhid ātirat dāsam arkaiḥ vidat vasuḥ dayamānaḥ vi śatrūn   brahma jūtaḥ tanvā vāvṛdhānaḥ bhūri dātraḥ āpṛṇat rodasī ubhe  
makhasya te taviṣasya pra jūtim iyarmi vācam amṛtāya bhūṣan   indra kṣitīnām asi mānuṣīṇām viśām daivīnām uta pūrva yāvā  
indraḥ vṛtram avṛṇot śardhanītiḥ pra māyinām amināt varpaṇītiḥ   ahan vyaṃsam uśadhak vaneṣu āvis dhenāḥ akṛṇot rāmyāṇām  
indraḥ svarṣā janayan ahāni jigāya uśigbhiḥ pṛtanāḥ abhiṣṭiḥ   prārocayat manave ketum ahnām avindat jyotiḥ bṛhate raṇāya  
indraḥ tujaḥ barhaṇāḥ ā viveśa nṛvat dadhānaḥ naryā purūṇi   acetayat dhiyaḥ imā jaritre pra imam varṇam atirat śukram āsām  
mahaḥ mahāni panayanti asya indrasya karma su kṛtā purūṇi   vṛjanena vṛjinān sam pipeṣa māyābhiḥ dasyūṃr abhibhūti ojāḥ  
yudhā indraḥ mahnā varivaḥ cakāra devebhyaḥ sat patiḥ carṣaṇiprāḥ   vivasvataḥ sadane asya tāni viprāḥ ukthebhiḥ kavayaḥ gṛṇanti  
satrāsāham vareṇyam sahaḥ dām sasavāṃsam svar apaḥ ca devīḥ   sasāna yaḥ pṛthivīm dyām uta imām indram madanti anu dhīraṇāsaḥ  
sasāna atyām uta sūryam sasāna indraḥ sasāna puru bhojasam gām   hiraṇyayam uta bhogam sasāna hatvī dasyūn prāryam varṇam āvat  
indraḥ oṣadhīḥ asanot ahāni vanaspatīn asanot antarikṣam   bibheda balam nunude vivācaḥ atha abhavat damitā abhikratūnām  
śunam huvema maghavānam indram asmin bhare nṛtamam vājasātau   śṛṇvantam ugram ūtaye samatsu ghnantam vṛtrāṇi saṃjitam dhanānām  
ud u brahmāṇi airata śravasya indram samarye mahayā vasiṣṭha   ā yaḥ viśvāni śavasā tatāna upaśrotā me īvataḥ vacāṃsi  
ayāmi ghoṣaḥ indra deva jāmiḥ irajyanta yat śurudhaḥ vivāci   nahi svam āyuḥ cikite janeṣu tāni id aṃhāṃsi ati parṣi asmān  
yuje ratham gaveṣaṇam haribhyām upa brahmāṇi jujuṣāṇam asthuḥ   vi bādhiṣṭa sya rodasī mahitvā indraḥ vṛtrāṇi apratī jaghanvān  
āpaḥ cit pipyuḥ staryaḥ na gāvaḥ nakṣan ṛtam jaritāraḥ te indra   yāhi vāyuḥ na niyutaḥ naḥ achā tvam hi dhībhiḥ dayase vi vājān  
te tvā madāḥ indra mādayantu śuṣmiṇam tuvi rādhasam jaritre   ekaḥ devatrā dayase hi martān asmin śūra savane mādayasva  
eva id indram vṛṣaṇam vajra bāhum vasiṣṭhāsaḥ abhi arcanti arkaiḥ   sa naḥ stutaḥ vīravat dhātu gomat yūyam pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ  
ṛjīṣī vajrī vṛṣabhaḥ turāṣāh chuṣmī rājā vṛtra hā soma pāvā   yuktvā haribhyām upa yāsat arvāk mādhyaṃdine savane matsat indraḥ  
indraḥ ca somam pibatam bṛhaspate asmin yajñe mandasānāḥ vṛṣaṇvasū   ā vām viśantu indavaḥ svābhuvaḥ asme rayim sarva vīram ni yacchatam  
ā vaḥ vahantu saptayaḥ raghuṣyadaḥ raghu patvānaḥ pra jigāta bāhubhiḥ   sīdata barhiḥ uru vaḥ sadaḥ kṛtam mādayadhvam marutaḥ madhvaḥ andhasaḥ  
imam stomam arhate jātavedase ratham iva sam mahema manīṣayā   bhadrā hi naḥ pramatiḥ asya saṃsadi agne sakhye mā riṣāma vayam tava  
a ebhiḥ agne sa ratham yāhi arvāk nānā ratham vā vibhavaḥ hi aśvāḥ   patnīvataḥ triṃśatam trīn ca devān anuṣvadham ā vaha mādayasva  
vayam u tvām apūrvya sthūram na kad cit bharantaḥ avasyavaḥ   vāje citram havāmahe   vāje citram havāmahe  
upa tvā karman ūtaye sa naḥ yuvā ugraḥ cakrāma yaḥ dhṛṣat   tvām id hi avitāram vavṛmahe sakhāyaḥ indra sānasim  
yaḥ naḥ idam idam purā pra vasyaḥ ānināya tam u vaḥ stuṣe   sakhāyaḥ indram ūtaye  
haryaśvam sat patim carṣaṇīsaham sa hi sma yaḥ amandata   ā tu naḥ sa vayati gavyam aśvyam stotṛbhyaḥ maghavā śatam  
pra maṃhiṣṭhāya bṛhate bṛhadraye satya śuṣmāya tavase matim bhare   apām iva pravaṇe yasya durdharam rādhaḥ viśvāyu śavase apāvṛtam  
adha te viśvam anu hāsat iṣṭayaḥ āpaḥ nimnā iva savanā haviṣmataḥ   yat parvate na samaśīta haryataḥ indrasya vajraḥ śnathitā hiraṇyayaḥ  
asmai bhīmāya namasā sam adhvaraḥ uṣaḥ na śubhraḥ ā bhara panīyase   yasya dhāma śravase nāma indriyam jyotiḥ akāri haritaḥ nāyase  
ime te indra te vayam puruṣṭuta ye tvā ārabhya carāmasi prabhūvaso   nahi tvat anyaḥ girvaṇaḥ giraḥ sadhat kṣoṇīḥ iva prati naḥ harya tat vacaḥ  
bhūri te indra vīryam tava smasi asya stotuḥ maghavan kāmam ā pṛṇa   anu te dyauḥ bṛhatī vīryam mama iyam ca te pṛthivī neme ojase  
tvam tam indra parvatam mahām urum vajreṇa vajrin parvaśas cakartitha   avāsṛjaḥ nivṛtāḥ sartavai apaḥ satrā viśvam dadhiṣe kevalam sahaḥ  
udaprutaḥ na vayaḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ vāvadataḥ abhriyasya iva ghoṣāḥ   giri bhrajaḥ na ūrmayaḥ madantaḥ bṛhaspatim abhi arkāḥ anāvan  
sam gobhiḥ aṅgirasaḥ nakṣamāṇaḥ bhagaḥ iva id aryamaṇam nināya   jane mitraḥ na dampatī anakti bṛhaspate vājayāśūṃr iva ājau  
sādhvaryāḥ atithinīḥ iṣirā spārhāḥ suvarṇāḥ anavadya rūpāḥ   bṛhaspatiḥ parvatebhyaḥ vitūryāḥ niḥ gāḥ ūpe yavam iva sthivibhyaḥ  
āpruṣāyat madhunā ṛtasya yonim avakṣipan arkaḥ ulkām iva dyoḥ   bṛhaspatiḥ uddharan aśmanaḥ gāḥ bhūmyāḥ udnā iva vi tvacam bibheda  
apa jyotiṣā tamaḥ antarikṣat udnaḥ śīpālam iva vātaḥ ājat   bṛhaspatiḥ anumṛśyā valasyā abhram iva vātaḥ ā cakre ā gāḥ  
yadā valasya pīyataḥ jasum bhet bṛhaspatiḥ agni tapobhiḥ arkaiḥ   dadbhiḥ na jihvā pariviṣṭam ādat āvis nidhīṃr akṛṇot usriyāṇām  
bṛhaspatiḥ amata hi tyad āsām nāma svarīṇām sadane guhā yat   āṇḍā iva bhitvā śakunasya garbham ud usriyāḥ parvatasya tmanā ajat  
aśnā apinaddham madhu pari apaśyat matsyam na dīnaḥ udani kṣiyantam   niḥ tat jabhāra camasam na vṛkṣāt bṛhaspatiḥ viraveṇa vikṛtya  
sa uṣām avindat sa svar saḥ agnim saḥ arkeṇa vi babādhe tamāṃsi   bṛhaspatiḥ go vapuṣaḥ valasya niḥ majjānam na parvaṇaḥ jabhāra  
himā iva parṇā muṣitā vanāni bṛhaspatinā akṛpayat valaḥ gāḥ   anānukṛtyam apunar cakāra yāt sūryāmāsā mithas uccarātaḥ  
abhi śyāvam na kṛśanebhiḥ aśvam nakṣatrebhiḥ pitaraḥ dyām apiṃśan   rātryām tamaḥ adadhuḥ jyotiḥ ahan bṛhaspatiḥ bhinat adrim vidat gāḥ  
idam akarma namaḥ abhriyāya yaḥ pūrvīḥ anu ānonavīti   bṛhaspatiḥ sa hi gobhiḥ saḥ aśvaiḥ sa vīrebhiḥ sa nṛbhiḥ naḥ vayaḥ dhāt  
achā me indram matayaḥ svarvidaḥ sadhrīcīḥ viśvāḥ uśatīḥ anūṣata   pari svajante janayaḥ yathā patim maryam na śundhyum maghavānam ūtaye  
na ghā tvadrik apa veti me manaḥ tve id kāmam puruhūta śiśraya   rājā iva dasma ni sadaḥ adhi barhiṣi asmin su some avapānam astu te  
viṣūvṛt indraḥ amuteḥ uta kṣudhaḥ saḥ id rāyaḥ maghavā vasvaḥ īśate   tasya id ime pravaṇe sapta sindhavaḥ vayaḥ vardhanti vṛṣabhasya śuṣmiṇaḥ  
vayaḥ na vṛkṣam su palāśam āsadan somāsaḥ indram mandinaḥ camūṣadaḥ   pra eṣām anīkam śavasā davidyutat vidat svar manave jyotiḥ āryam  
kṛtam na śvaghnī vi cinoti devane saṃvargam yat maghavā sūryam jayat   na tat te anyaḥ anu vīryam śakat na purāṇaḥ maghavan na uta nūtanaḥ  
viśam viśam maghavā pari aśāyata janānām dhenāḥ avacākaśat vṛṣā   yasya aha śakraḥ savaneṣu raṇyati sa tīvraiḥ somaiḥ sahate pṛtanyataḥ  
āpaḥ na sindhum abhi yat samakṣaran somāsaḥ indram kulyāḥ iva hradam   vardhanti viprāḥ mahaḥ asya sādane yavam na vṛṣṭiḥ divyena dānunā  
vṛṣā na kruddhaḥ patayat rajaḥsu ā yaḥ arya patnīḥ akṛṇot imāḥ apaḥ   sa sunvate maghavā jīra dānave avindat jyotiḥ manave haviṣmate  
ud jāyatām paraśu jyotiṣā saha bhūyāḥ ṛtasya su dughā purāṇavat   vi rocatām aruṣaḥ bhānunā śuciḥ svar na śukram śuśucīta satpatiḥ  
gobhiḥ tarema amatim durevām yavena kṣudham puruhūta viśvām   vayam rājabhiḥ prathamā dhanāni asmākena vṛjanena jayema  
bṛhaspatiḥ naḥ pari pātu paścāt uta uttarasmāt adharāt aghāyoḥ   indraḥ purastāt uta madhyataḥ naḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ varivaḥ kṛṇotu  
bṛhaspate yuvam indraḥ ca vasvaḥ divyasya īśāthe uta pārthivasya   dhattam rayim stuvate kīraye cit yūyam pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ  
vayam u tvā taditarthāḥ indra tvāyantaḥ sakhāyaḥ   kaṇvāḥ ukthebhiḥ jarante  
na gha īm anyat ā papana vajrin apasaḥ naviṣṭau   tava id u stomam ciketa  
ichanti devāḥ sunvantam na svapnāya spṛhayanti   yanti pramādam atandrāḥ  
vayam indra tvāyavaḥ abhi pra nonumaḥ vṛṣan   viddhi tu asya naḥ vaso  
mā naḥ nide ca vaktave aryaḥ randhīḥ arāvne   tve api kratuḥ mama  
tvam varmā asi saprathaḥ puroyodhaḥ ca vṛtrahan   tvayā prati bruve yujā  
vārtrahatyāya śavase pṛtanāṣāhyāya ca   indra tvā vartayāmasi  
arvācīnam su te manaḥ uta cakṣuḥ śatakrato   indra kṛṇvantu vāghataḥ  
nāmāni te śatakrato viśvābhiḥ gīrbhiḥ īmahe   indra abhimātiṣāhye  
puruṣṭutasya dhāmabhiḥ śatena mahayāmasi   indrasya carṣaṇī dhṛtaḥ  
indram vṛtrāya hantave puruhūtam upa bruve   bhareṣu vājasātaye  
vājeṣu sāsahiḥ bhava tvām īmahe śatakrato   indra vṛtrāya hantave  
dyumneṣu pṛtanājye pṛtsutūrṣu śravaḥsu ca   indra sākṣva abhimātiṣu  
śuṣmintamam naḥ ūtaye dyumninam pāhi jāgṛvim   indra somam śatakrato  
indriyāṇi śatakrato yā te janeṣu pañcasu   indra tāni te ā vṛṇe  
agan indra śravaḥ bṛhat dyumnam dadhiṣva duṣṭaram   ud te śuṣmam tirāmasi  
arvāvataḥ naḥ ā gahi atha u śakra parāvataḥ   u lokaḥ yaḥ te adrivas indra iha tatas ā gahi  
indraḥ aṅgam mahat bhayam abhi sat apa cucyavat   sa hi sthiraḥ vicarṣaṇiḥ  
indraḥ ca mṛlayāti naḥ na naḥ paścāt agham naśat   bhadram bhavāti naḥ puras  
indraḥ āśābhyaḥ pari sarvābhyaḥ abhayam karat  jetā śatrūn vicarṣaṇiḥ 
ni u su vācam pra mahe bharāmahe giraḥ indrāya sadane vivasvataḥ   nu cit hi ratnam sasatām iva avidat na duṣṭutiḥ draviṇaḥ deṣu śasyate  
duraḥ aśvasya duraḥ indra goḥ asi duraḥ yavasya vasunaḥ inaḥ patiḥ   śikṣānaraḥ pradivaḥ akāma karśanaḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ tam idam gṛṇīmasi  
śacīvas indra puru kṛt dyumattama tava id idam abhitas cekite vasu   atas saṃgṛbhya abhibhūtaḥ ā bhara mā tvāyataḥ jarituḥ kāmam ūnayīḥ  
ebhiḥ dyubhiḥ sumanāḥ ebhiḥ indubhiḥ nirundhānaḥ amatim gobhiḥ aśvinā   indreṇa dasyum darayantaḥ indubhiḥ yuta dveṣasaḥ sam iṣā rabhemahi  
sam indra rāyā sam iṣā rabhemahi sam vājebhiḥ puru ścandraiḥ abhidyubhiḥ   sam devyā pramatyā vīra śuṣmayā go agrayā aśvāvatyā rabhemahi  
te tvā madāḥ amadan tāni vṛṣṇyā te somāsaḥ vṛtra hatyeṣu satpate   yat kārave daśa vṛtrāṇi aprati barhiṣmate ni sahasrāṇi barhayaḥ  
yudhā yudham upa gha id eṣi dhṛṣṇuyā purā puram sam idam haṃsi ojasā   namyā yat indra sakhyā parāvati nibarhayaḥ namucim nāma māyinam  
tvam karañjam uta parṇayam vadhīḥ tejiṣṭhayā atithigvasya vartanī   tvam śatā vaṅgṛdasya abhinat puraḥ anānudaḥ pariṣūtāḥ ṛjiśvanā  
tvam etām jana rājñaḥ dvis daśā bandhunā suśravasā upajagmuṣaḥ   ṣaṣṭim sahasrā navatim nava śrutaḥ ni cakreṇa rathyā duṣpadā avṛṇak  
tvam āvitha suśravasam tava ūtibhiḥ tava trāmabhiḥ indra tūrvayāṇam   tva asmai kutsam atithigvam āyum mahe rājñe yūne arandhanāyaḥ  
yaḥ udṛci indra deva gopāḥ sakhāyaḥ te śivatamāḥ asāma   tvām stoṣāma tvayā su vīrāḥ drāghīyaḥ āyuḥ prataram dadhānāḥ  
abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sute sutam sṛjāmi pītaye   tṛmpā vi aśnuhi madam  
mā tvā mūrāḥ aviṣyavaḥ mā upahasvānaḥ ā dabhan  mākīm brahma dviṣaḥ vanaḥ 
iha tvā goparīṇasā mahe mandantu rādhase   saraḥ gauraḥ yathā piba  
abhi pra gopatim girā indram arca yathā vide   sūnum satyasya satpatim  
ā harayaḥ sasṛjrire aruṣīḥ adhi barhiṣi   yatra abhi saṃnavāmahe  
indrāya gāvaḥ āśiram duduhre vajriṇe madhu   yat sīm upahvare vidat  
ā tū naḥ indra madryak ghuvānaḥ soma pītaye   haribhyām yāhi adrivas  
sattaḥ hotā naḥ ṛtviyaḥ tistire barhiḥ ānuṣak   ayujran prātar adrayaḥ  
imāḥ brahma brahma vāhaḥ kriyante ā barhiḥ sīda   vīhi śūra purolāśam  
rārandhi savaneṣu naḥ eṣu stomeṣu vṛtrahan   uktheṣu indra girvaṇaḥ  
matayaḥ soma pām urum rihanti śavasaḥ patim   indram vatsam na mātaraḥ  
sa mandasva hi andhasaḥ rādhase tanvā mahe   na stotāram nide karaḥ  
vayam indra tvāyavaḥ haviṣmantaḥ jarāmahe   uta tvam asmayuḥ vaso  
māre asmat vi mumucaḥ hari priya arvāṅ yāhi   indra svadhāvas matsva iha  
arvāñcam tvā sukhe rathe vahatām indra keśinā   ghṛtasnū barhiḥ āsade  
upa naḥ sutam ā gahi somam indra gavāśiram   haribhyām yaḥ te asmayuḥ  
tam indra madam ā gahi barhiṣṭhām grāvabhiḥ sutam   kuvid nu asya tṛpṇavaḥ  
indram itthā giraḥ mama achāguḥ iṣitāḥ itas   āvṛte soma pītaye  
indram somasya pītaye stomaiḥ iha havāmahe   ukthebhiḥ kuvid āgamat  
indra somāḥ sutāḥ ime tān dadhiṣva śatakrato   jathare vājinīvaso  
vidma hi tvā dhanaṃjayam vājeṣu dadhṛṣam kave   adha te sumnam īmahe  
imam indra gavāśiram yavāśiram ca naḥ piba   āgatyā vṛṣabhiḥ sutam  
tubhyaḥ id indra sve okye somam codāmi pītaye   eṣa rārantu te hṛdi  
tvām sutasya pītaye pratnam indra havāmahe   kuśikāsaḥ avasyavaḥ  
aśvāvati prathamaḥ goṣu gacchati suprāvīḥ indra martyaḥ tava ūtibhiḥ   tam id pṛṇakṣi vasunā bhavīyasā sindhum āpaḥ yathā abhitas vicetasaḥ  
āpaḥ na devīḥ upa yanti hotriyam avaḥ paśyanti vitatam yathā rajaḥ   prācais devāsaḥ pra nayanti devayum brahma priyam joṣayante varāḥ iva  
adhi dvayoḥ adadhāḥ ukthyam vacaḥ yata srucā mithunā yā saparyataḥ   a saṃyattaḥ vrate te kṣeti puṣyati bhadrā śaktiḥ yajamānāya sunvate  
āt aṅgirāḥ prathamam dadhire vayaḥ iddha agnayaḥ śamyāḥ ye su kṛtyayā   sarvam paṇeḥ sam avindanta bhojanam aśvāvantam gomantam ā paśum naraḥ  
yajñaiḥ atharvā prathamaḥ pathaḥ tate tatas sūryaḥ vrata pāḥ venaḥ ājani   ā gāḥ ājat uśanā kāvyaḥ sacā yamasya jātam amṛtam yajāmahe  
barhiḥ vā yat su apatyāya vṛjyate arkaḥ vā ślokam āghoṣate divi   grāvā yatra vadati karuḥ ukthyaḥ tasya id indraḥ abhipitveṣu raṇyati  
pra ugrām pītim vṛṣṇe iyarmi satyām prayai sutasya haryaśva tubhyam   indra dhenābhiḥ iha mādayasva dhībhiḥ viśvābhiḥ śacyā gṛṇānaḥ  
yoge yoge tavastaram vājevāje havāmahe   sakhāyaḥ indram ūtaye  
ā gha gamat yadi śravat sahasriṇībhiḥ ūtibhiḥ   vājebhiḥ upa naḥ havam  
anu pratnasya okasaḥ huve tuvi pratim naram   yam te pūrvam pitā huve  
yuñjanti bradhnam aruṣam carantam pari tasthuṣaḥ   rocante rocanā divi  
yuñjanti asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe   śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛ vāhasā  
ketum kṛṇvan aketave peśaḥ maryāḥ apeśase   sam uṣadbhiḥ ajāyathāḥ  
yat indra aham yathā tvam īśīya vasvaḥ ekaḥ id   stotā me goṣakhā syāt  
śikṣeyam asmai ditseyam śacīpate manīṣiṇe   yat aham gopatiḥ syām  
dhenuḥ te indra sūnṛtā yajamānāya sunvate   gām aśvam pipyuṣī duhe  
na te vartā asti rādhasaḥ indra devaḥ na martyaḥ   yat ditsasi stutaḥ magham  
yajñaḥ indram avardhayat yat bhūmim vi avartayat   cakrāṇaḥ opaśam divi  
vāvṛdhānasya te vayam viśvā dhanāni jigyuṣaḥ   ūtim indraḥ ā vṛṇīmahe  
vi antarikṣam atirat made somasya rocanā   indraḥ yat abhinat valam  
ud gāḥ ājat aṅgirobhyaḥ āvis krṇvan guhā satīḥ   arvāñcam nunude valam  
indreṇa rocanā divaḥ dṛlhāni dṛṃhitāni ca   sthirāṇi na parāṇude  
apām ūrmiḥ madan iva stomaḥ indra ajirāyate   vi te madāḥ arājiṣuḥ  
tvam hi stoma vardhanaḥ indra asi uktha vardhanaḥ   stotṝṇām uta bhadra kṛt  
indram id keśinā harī soma peyāya vakṣataḥ   upa yajñam su rādhasam  
apām phenena namuceḥ śiraḥ indra ud avartayaḥ   viśvā yat ajaya spṛdhaḥ  
māyābhiḥ utsisṛpsataḥ indra dyām ārurukṣataḥ   ava dasyūṃr adhūnuthāḥ  
asunvām indra saṃsadam viṣūcīm vi anāśayaḥ   soma pāḥ uttaraḥ bhavan  
pra te mahe vidathe śaṃsiṣam harī pra te vanve vanuṣaḥ haryatam madam   ghṛtam na yaḥ haribhiḥ cāru secate ā tvā viśantu hari varpasam giraḥ  
harim hi yonim abhi ye samasvaran hinvantaḥ harī divyam yathā sadaḥ   ā yam pṛṇanti haribhiḥ na dhenavaḥ indrāya śūśam harivantam arcata  
saḥ asya vajraḥ haritaḥ yaḥ āyasaḥ hariḥ nikāmaḥ hariḥ ā gabhastyoḥ   dyumnī su śipraḥ hari manyu sāyakaḥ indre ni rūpā haritā mimikṣire  
divi na ketuḥ adhi dhāyi haryataḥ vivyacat vajraḥ haritaḥ na raṃhyā   tudat ahim hari śipraḥ yaḥ āyasaḥ sahasra śokāḥ abhavat harimbharaḥ  
tvaṃtvam aharyathāḥ upastutaḥ pūrvebhiḥ indra hari keśa yajvabhiḥ   tvam haryasi tava viśvam ukthyam asāmi rādhaḥ hari jāta haryatam  
tā vajriṇam mandinam stomyam made indram rathe vahataḥ haryatā harī   purūṇi asmai savanāni haryate indrāya somāḥ harayaḥ dadhanvire  
aram kāmāya harayaḥ dadhamire sthirāya hinvan harayaḥ harī turā   arvadbhiḥ yaḥ haribhiḥ joṣam īyate saḥ asya kāmam harivantam ānaśe  
hari śmaśāruḥ hari keśaḥ āyasaḥ turaspeye yaḥ hari pāḥ avardhata   arvadbhiḥ yaḥ haribhiḥ vājinīvasuḥ ati viśvā duritā pāriṣat dharī  
śruvā iva yasya hariṇī vipetatuḥ śipre vājāya hariṇī davidhvataḥ   pra yat kṛte camase marmṛjat dharī pītvā madasya haryatasya andhasaḥ  
uta sma sadna haryatasya pastyoḥ atyaḥ na vājam harivān acikradat   mahī cit hi dhiṣaṇā aharyat ojasā bṛhat vayaḥ dadhiṣe haryataḥ cit ā  
ā rodasī haryamāṇaḥ mahitvā navyam navyam haryasi manma nu priyam   pra pastyam asura haryatam goḥ āvis kṛdhi haraye sūryāya  
ā tvā haryantam prayujaḥ janānām rathe vahantu hari śipram indra   pibā yathā pratibhṛtasya madhvaḥ haryan yajñam sadhamāde daśoṇim  
apāḥ pūrveṣām harivas sutānām atha u idam savanam kevalam te   mamaddhi somam madhumantam indra satrā vṛṣam jathare ā vṛṣasva  
apsu dhūtasya harivas piba iha nṛbhiḥ sutasya jaṭharam pṛṇasva   mimikṣuḥ yam adrayaḥ indra tubhyam tebhiḥ vardhasva madam uktha vāhaḥ  
pra ugrām pītim vṛṣṇe iyarmi satyām prayai sutasya haryaśva tubhyam   indra dhenābhiḥ iha mādayasva dhībhiḥ viśvābhiḥ śacyā gṛṇānaḥ  
ūtī śacīvas tava vīryeṇa vayaḥ dadhānāḥ uśijaḥ ṛta jñāḥ   prajāvat indra maṃsaḥ duroṇe tasthuḥ gṛṇantaḥ sadhamādyāsaḥ  
yaḥ jātaḥ eva prathamaḥ manasvān devaḥ devān kratunā paryamūṣat   yasya śuṣmāt rodasī abhyasetām nṛmṇasya mahnā sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ pṛthivīm vyathamānām adṛṃhat yaḥ parvatān prakupitām aramṇāt   yaḥ antarikṣam vimame varīyaḥ yaḥ dyām astabhnāt sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ hatvā ahim ariṇāt sapta sindhūn yaḥ gāḥ udājat apadhā valasya   yaḥ aśmanoḥ antar agnim jajāna saṃvṛk samatsu sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yena imā viśvā cyavanā kṛtāni yaḥ dāsam varṇam adharam guhākaḥ   śvaghnī iva yaḥ jigīvām lakṣam ādat aryaḥ puṣṭāni sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yam sma pṛchanti kuha sa iti ghoram uta īm āhuḥ na eṣaḥ asti iti enam   saḥ aryaḥ puṣṭīḥ vijaḥ iva ā mināti śrath asmai dhatta sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ radhrasya coditā yaḥ kṛśasya yaḥ brahmaṇaḥ nādhamānasya kīreḥ   yukta grāvṇaḥ yaḥ avitā su śipraḥ suta somasya sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yasya aśvāsaḥ pradiśi yasya gāvaḥ yasya grāmāḥ yasya viśve rathāsaḥ   yaḥ sūryam yaḥ uṣasam jajāna yaḥ apām netā sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yam krandasī saṃyatī vihvayete pare avare ubhayāḥ amitrāḥ   samānam cit ratham ātasthivāṃsā nānā havete sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yasmāt naḥ ṛte vijayante janāsaḥ yam yudhyamānāḥ avase havante   yaḥ viśvasya pratimānam babhūva yaḥ acyuta cyut sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ śasvataḥ mahi enaḥ dadhānān a manyamānām śarvā jaghāna   yaḥ śardhate na anudadāti śṛdhyām yaḥ dasyoḥ hantā sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ śambharam parvateṣu kṣiyantam catvāriṃśyām śaradi anvavindat   ojāyamānam yaḥ ahim jaghāna dānum śayānam sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ śambharam paryatarat kasībhiḥ yaḥ acāru kāsnā apibat sutasya   antar girau yajamānam bahum janam yasmin āmūrchat sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ sapta raśmiḥ vṛṣabhaḥ tuviṣmān avāsṛjat sartave sapta sindhūn   yaḥ rauhiṇam asphurat vajra bāhuḥ dyām ārohantam sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
dyāvā cit asmai pṛthivī mamete śuṣmāt cit asya parvatāḥ bhayante   yaḥ soma pāḥ nicitaḥ vajra bāhuḥ yaḥ vajra hastaḥ sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ sunvantam avati yaḥ pacantam yaḥ śaṃsantam yaḥ śaśamānam ūtī   yasya brahma vardhanam yasya somaḥ yasya idam rādhaḥ sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
jātaḥ vi akhyat pitroḥ upasthe bhuvaḥ na veda janituḥ parasya   staviṣyamāṇaḥ naḥ yaḥ asmat vratā devānām sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ soma kāmaḥ haryaśvaḥ sūriḥ yasmāt rejante bhuvanāni viśvā   yaḥ jaghāna śambaram yaḥ ca śuṣṇam yaḥ eka vīraḥ sa janāsaḥ indraḥ  
yaḥ sunvate pacate dudhre ā cit vājam dardarṣi sa kila asi satyaḥ   vayam te indra viśvaha priyāsaḥ su vīrāsaḥ vidatham ā vadema  
asmai id u pra tavase turāya prayaḥ na harmi stomam māhināya   ṛcīṣamāya adhrigave oham indrāya brahmāṇi rātatamā  
asmai id u prayaḥ iva pra yaṃsi bharāmi āngūṣam bādhe suvṛkti   indrāya hṛdā manasā manīṣā pratnāya patye dhiyaḥ marjayanta  
asmai id u tyam upamam svarṣām bharāmi āṅgūṣam āsyena   maṃhiṣṭham achoktibhiḥ matīnām suvṛktibhiḥ sūrim vāvṛdhadhyai  
asmai id u stomam sam hinomi ratham na taṣṭā iva tatsināya   giraḥ ca gir vāhase suvṛkti indrāya viśvaminvam medhirāya  
asmai id u saptim iva śravasya indrāya arkam juhvā sam añje   vīram dānaukasam vandadhyai purām gūrta śravasam darmāṇam  
asmai id u tvaṣṭā takṣat vajram su apastamam svaryam raṇāya   vṛtrasya cit vidat yena marma tujan īśānaḥ tujatā kiyedhāḥ  
asya id u mātuḥ savaneṣu sadyas mahaḥ pitum papivām cāru annā   muṣāyat viṣṇuḥ pacatam sahīyān vidhyat varāham tiras adrim astā  
asmai id u gnāḥ cit deva patnīḥ indrāya arkam ahi hatye ūvuḥ   pari dyāvāpṛthivī jabhre urvī na asya te mahimānam pari staḥ  
asya id eva pra ririce mahitvam divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ pari antarikṣāt   svarāt indraḥ damaḥ ā viśva gūrtaḥ svariḥ amatraḥ vavakṣe raṇāya  
asya id eva śavasā śuśantam vi vṛścat vajreṇa vṛtram indraḥ   gāḥ na vrāṇāḥ avanīḥ amuñcat abhi śravaḥ dāvane sacetāḥ  
asya id u tveṣasā ranta sindhavaḥ pari yat vajreṇa sīm ayacchat   īśāna kṛt dāśuṣe daśasyan turvītaye gādham turvaṇiḥ kaḥ  
asmai id u pra bhara tūtujānaḥ vṛtrāya vajram īśānaḥ kiyedhāḥ   goḥ na parva vi radā tiraśceṣyan arṇāṃsi apām caradhyai  
asya id u pra brūhi pūrvyāṇi turasya karmāṇi navyaḥ ukthaiḥ   yudhe yat iṣṇānaḥ āyudhāni ṛghāyamāṇaḥ niriṇāti śatrūn  
asya id u bhiyā girayaḥ ca dṛlhāḥ dyāvā ca bhūmā januṣaḥ tujete   upa u venasya joguvānaḥ oṇim sadyas bhuvat vīryāya nodhāḥ  
asmai id u tyad anu dāyi eṣām ekaḥ yat vavne bhūreḥ īśānaḥ   pra etaśam sūrye paspṛdhānam sauvaśvye suṣvim āvat indraḥ  
eva te hāriyojanā suvṛktī indra brahmāṇi gotamāsaḥ akran   ā eṣu viśva peśasam dhiyam dhāḥ prātar makṣū dhiyāvasuḥ jagamyāt  
yaḥ ekaḥ id dhavyaḥ carṣaṇīnām indram tam gīrbhiḥ abhi arcaḥ ābhiḥ   yaḥ patyate vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣṇyāvān satyaḥ satvā puru māyaḥ sahasvān   yaḥ patyate vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣṇyāvān satyaḥ satvā puru māyaḥ sahasvān   yaḥ patyate vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣṇyāvān satyaḥ satvā puru māyaḥ sahasvān   yaḥ patyate vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣṇyāvān satyaḥ satvā puru māyaḥ sahasvān   yaḥ patyate vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣṇyāvān satyaḥ satv
tam u naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ navagvāḥ sapta viprāsaḥ abhi vājayantaḥ   nakṣat dābham taturim parvateṣṭhām adrogha vācam matibhiḥ śaviṣṭham  
tam īmahe indram asya rāyaḥ puru vīrasya nṛvataḥ purukṣoḥ   yaḥ aṣkṛdhoyuḥ ajaraḥ svarvān tam ā bhara harivas mādayadhyai  
tat naḥ vi vocaḥ yadi te purā cit jaritāraḥ ānaśuḥ sumnam indra   kaḥ te bhāgaḥ kim vayaḥ dudhra khiduḥ puruhūta purūvaso asura ghnaḥ  
tam pṛchantī vajra hastam ratheṣṭhām indram vepī vakvarī yasya nu gīḥ   tuvi grābham tuvi kūrmim rabhodām gātum iṣe nakṣate tumram acha  
ayā ha tyam māyayā vāvṛdhānam manaḥ juvā svatavaḥ parvatena   acyutā cit vīlitā su ojaḥ rujaḥ vi dṛlhā dhṛṣatā virapśin  
tam vaḥ dhiyā navyasya śaviṣṭham pratnam pratnavat paritaṃsayadhyai   sa naḥ vakṣat animānaḥ suvahnā indraḥ viśvāni ati durgahāṇi  
ā janāya druhvaṇe pārthivāni divyāni dīpayaḥ antarikṣā   tapa vṛṣan viśvatas śociṣā tān brahma dviṣe śocaya kṣām apaḥ ca  
bhuvaḥ janasya divyasya rājā pārthivasya jagataḥ tveṣa saṃdṛś   dhiṣva vajram dakṣiṇe indra haste viśvāḥ ajurya dayase vi māyāḥ  
ā saṃyatam indra naḥ svastim śatru tūryāya bṛhatīm amṛdhrām   yayā dāsāni āryāṇi vṛtrā karaḥ vajrin sutukā nāhuṣāṇi  
sa naḥ niyudbhiḥ puruhūta vedhaḥ viśva vārābhiḥ ā gahi prayajyo   na yāḥ adevaḥ varate na devaḥ ābhiḥ yāhi tūyam ā madrī adrik  
yaḥ tigma śṛṅgaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ na bhīmaḥ ekaḥ kṛṣṭīḥ cyavayati pra viśvāḥ   yaḥ śaśvataḥ adāśuṣaḥ gayasya prayantāsi suṣvitarāya vedaḥ  
tvam ha tyad indra kutsam āvaḥ śuśrūṣamāṇaḥ tanvā samarye   dāsam yat śuṣṇam kuyavam ni asmai arandhayaḥ ārjuneyāya śikṣan  
tvam dhṛṣṇo dhṛṣatā vītahavyam pra āvaḥ viśvābhiḥ ūtibhiḥ sudāsam   pra paurukutsim trasadasyum āvaḥ kṣetrasātā vṛtra hatyeṣu pūrum  
tvam nṛbhiḥ nṛmaṇaḥ deva vītau bhūrīṇi vṛtrā haryaśva haṃsi   tvam ni dasyum cumurim dhunim cāsvāpayaḥ dabhītaye su hantu  
tava cyautnāni vajrahasta tāni nava yat puras navatim ca sadyas   niveśane śatatamā aviveṣīḥ aham ca vṛtram namucim uta ahan  
sanā tā te indra bhojanāni rātahavyāya dāśuṣe sudāse   vṛṣṇe te harī vṛṣaṇā yunajmi vyantu brahmāṇi puru śāka vājam  
mā te asyām sahasāvan pariṣṭau aghāya bhūma harivas parādau   trāyasva naḥ avṛkebhiḥ varūthaiḥ tava priyāsaḥ sūriṣu syāma  
priyāsaḥ id te maghavan abhiṣṭau naraḥ madema śaraṇe sakhāyaḥ   ni turvaśam ni yādvam śiśīhi atithigvāya śaṃsyam kariṣyan  
sadyas cit nu te maghavan abhiṣṭau naraḥ śaṃsanti uktha śāsaḥ ukthā   ye te havebhiḥ vi paṇīn adāśan asmān vṛṇīṣva yujyāya tasmai  
ete stomāḥ narām nṛtama tubhyam asmadryañcaḥ dadataḥ maghāni   teṣām indra vṛtra hatye śivaḥ bhūḥ sakhā ca śūraḥ avitā ca nṛṇām  
nu indra śūra stavamānaḥ ūtī brahma jūtaḥ tanvā vāvṛdhasva   upa naḥ vājān mimīhi upa stīn yuyam pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ  
ā yāhi suṣuma hi te indra somam pibā imam   ā idam barhiḥ sadaḥ mama  
ā tvā brahma yujā harī vahatām indra keśinā   upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu  
brahmāṇaḥ tvā vayam yujā soma pām indra sominaḥ   sutāvantaḥ havāmahe  
indram id gāthinaḥ bṛhat indram arkebhiḥ arkiṇaḥ   indram vāṇīḥ anūṣata  
indraḥ id dharyoḥ sacā saṃmiślaḥ ā vacaḥ yujā   indraḥ vajrī hiraṇyayaḥ  
indraḥ dīrghāya cakṣase ā sūryam rohayat divi   vi gobhiḥ adrim airayat  
indram vaḥ viśvatas pari havāmahe janebhyaḥ  asmākam astu kevalaḥ 
vi antarikṣam atirat made somasya rocanā   indraḥ yat abhinat valam  
ud gāḥ ājat aṅgirobhyaḥ āvis kṛṇvan guhā satīḥ   arvāñcam nunude valam  
indreṇa rocanā divaḥ dṛlhāni dṛṃhitāni ca   sthirāṇi na parāṇude  
apām ūrmiḥ madan iva stomaḥ indra ajirāyate   vi te madāḥ arājiṣuḥ  
indreṇa sam hi dṛkṣase saṃjagmānaḥ abibhyuṣā   mandū samāna varcasā  
anavadyaiḥ abhidyubhiḥ makhaḥ sahasvat arcati   gaṇaiḥ indrasya kāmyaiḥ  
āt aha svadhām anu punar garbha tvam erire   dadhānāḥ nāma yajñiyam  
indraḥ dadhīcaḥ asthabhiḥ vṛtrāṇi apratiṣkutaḥ   jaghāna navatīḥ nava  
ichan aśvasya yat śiraḥ parvateṣu apaśritam   tat vidat śaryaṇāvati  
atra āha goḥ amanvata nāma tvaṣṭuḥ apīcyam   itthā candramasaḥ gṛhe  
vācam aṣṭāpadīm aham nava sraktim ṛta spṛśam   indrāt pari tanvam mame  
anu tvā rodasī ubhe krakṣamāṇam akṛpetām   indra yat dasyu hā abhavaḥ  
uttiṣṭhan ojasā saha pītvī śipre avepayaḥ   somam indra camū sutam  
bhindhi viśvāḥ apa dviṣaḥ bādhaḥ jahī mṛdhaḥ   vasu spārham tat ā bhara  
yat vīlau indra yat sthire yat parśāne parābhṛtam   vasu spārham tat ā bhara  
yasya te viśva mānuṣaḥ bhūreḥ dattasya vedati   vasu spārham tat ā bhara  
pra samrājam carṣaṇīnām indram stotā navyam gīrbhiḥ   naram nṛṣāham maṃhiṣṭham  
yasmin ukthāni raṇyanti viśvāni ca śravasya   apām avaḥ na samudre  
tam suṣṭutyā vivāse jyeṣṭha rājam bhare kṛtnum   mahaḥ vājinam sanibhyaḥ  
ayam u te sam atasi kapotaḥ iva garbhadhim  vacaḥ tat cit naḥ ohase 
stotram rādhānām pate girvāhaḥ vīra yasya te   vibhūtiḥ astu sūnṛtā  
ūrdhvaḥ tiṣṭha naḥ ūtaye asmin vāje śatakrato   sam anyeṣu bravāvahai  
praṇetāram vasyaḥ achā kartāram jyotiḥ samatsu   sāsahvāṃsam yudhāmitrān  
sa naḥ papriḥ pārayāti svasti nāvā puruhūtaḥ   indraḥ viśvāḥ ati dviṣaḥ  
sa tvam naḥ indra vājobhiḥ daśasyā ca gātuyā ca   achā ca naḥ sumnam neṣi  
tam indram vājayāmasi mahe vṛtrāya hantave   sa vṛṣā vṛṣabhaḥ bhuvat  
indraḥ sa dāmane kṛtaḥ ojiṣṭhaḥ sa made hitaḥ   dyumnī ślokī sa somyaḥ  
girā vajraḥ na saṃbhṛtaḥ sabalaḥ anapacyutaḥ   vavakṣa ṛṣvaḥ astṛtaḥ  
indram id gāthinaḥ bṛhat indram arkebhiḥ arkiṇaḥ   indram vāṇīḥ anūṣata  
indraḥ id dharyoḥ sacā saṃmiślaḥ ā vacaḥ yujā   indraḥ vajrī hiraṇyayaḥ  
indraḥ dīrghāya cakṣase ā sūryam rohayat divi   vi gobhiḥ adrim airayat  
ā yāhi suṣuma hi te indra somam pibā imam   ā idam barhiḥ sadaḥ mama  
ā tvā brahma yujā harī vahatām indra keśinā   upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu  
brahmāṇaḥ tvā vayam yujā soma pām indra sominaḥ   sutāvantaḥ havāmahe  
yuñjanti bradhnam aruṣam carantam pari tasthuṣaḥ   rocante rocanā divi  
yuñjanti asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe   śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛ vāhasā  
ketum kṛṇvan aketave peśaḥ maryāḥ apeśase   sam uṣadbhiḥ ajāyathāḥ  
ud u tyam jātavedasam devam vahanti ketavaḥ   dṛśe viśvāya sūryam  
apa tye tāyavaḥ yathā nakṣatrāḥ yanti aktubhiḥ   sūrāya viśva cakṣase  
adṛśran asya ketavaḥ vi raśmayaḥ janām anu  bhrājantaḥ agnayaḥ yathā  
taraṇiḥ viśva darśataḥ jyotiṣkṛt asi sūrya   viśvam ā bhāsi rocana  
pratyaṅ devānām viśaḥ pratyaṅ ud eṣi mānuṣīḥ   pratyaṅ viśvam svar dṛśe  
yena pāvaka cakṣasā bhuraṇyantam janām anu   tvam varuṇa paśyasi  
vi dyām eṣi rajaḥ pṛthu ahar mimānaḥ aktubhiḥ   paśyam janmāni sūrya  
sapta tvā haritaḥ rathe vahanti deva sūrya   śociṣkeśam vicakṣaṇam  
ayukta sapta śundhyuvaḥ sūraḥ rathasya naptyaḥ   tābhiḥ yāti sva yuktibhiḥ  
abhi tvā varcasā giraḥ siñcanti ā caraṇyuvaḥ   abhi vatsam na dhenavaḥ  
tāḥ arṣanti śubhriyaḥ pṛñcatīḥ varcasā payaḥ   jātam janiḥ yathā hṛdā  
vajra apavasādhyaḥ kīrtiḥ mriyamāṇam āvahan   mahyam āyuḥ ghṛtam payaḥ  
ā ayam gauḥ pṛśniḥ akramīt asadat mātaram puras   pitaram ca prayan svar  
antar carati rocanā asya prāṇāt apānataḥ   vi akhyat mahiṣaḥ svar  
triṃśat dhāmā vi rājati vāc pataṅgaḥ aśiśriyat   prati vastoḥ ahar dyubhiḥ  
yat śakrāḥ vācam āruhan antarikṣam siṣāsathaḥ   sam devāḥ amadan vṛṣā  
śakraḥ vācam a dhṛṣṭa āyoḥ uvācaḥ a dhṛṣṇuhi   maṃhiṣṭhaḥ ā madardivi  
śakraḥ vācam a dhṛṣṇuhi dhāma dharman vi rājati   vimadan barhiḥ āsaran  
tam vaḥ dasmam ṛtīṣaham vasoḥ mandānam andhasaḥ   abhi vatsam na svasareṣu dhenavaḥ indram gīrbhiḥ navāmahe  
dyukṣam sudānum taviṣībhiḥ āvṛtam girim na puru bhojasam   kṣumantam vājam śatinam sahasriṇam makṣū gomantam īmahe  
tat tvā yāmi su vīryam tat brahma pūrvacittaye   yena yatibhyaḥ bhṛgave dhane hite yena praskaṇvam āvitha  
yena samudram asṛjaḥ mahīḥ apaḥ tat indra vṛṣṇi te śavaḥ   sadyas saḥ asya mahimā na saṃnaśe yam kṣoṇīḥ anucakrade  
kat navyaḥ atasīnām turaḥ gṛṇīta martyaḥ   nahi nu asya mahimānam indriyam svar gṛṇantaḥ ānaśuḥ  
kad u stuvantaḥ ṛtayanta devataḥ ṛṣiḥ kaḥ vipraḥ ohate   kadā havam maghavan indra sunvataḥ kad u stuvataḥ ā gamaḥ  
abhi pra vaḥ su rādhasam indram arca yathā vide   yaḥ jaritṛbhyaḥ maghavā purūvasuḥ sahasreṇa iva śikṣati  
śata anīkā iva pra jigāti dhṛṣṇuyā hanti vṛtrāṇi dāśuṣe   gireḥ iva pra rasāḥ asya pinvire datrāṇi puru bhojasaḥ  
pra su śrutam su rādhasam arcā śakram abhiṣṭaye   yaḥ sunvate stuvate kāmyam vasu sahasreṇa iva maṃhate  
śata anīkāḥ hetayaḥ asya duṣṭarāḥ indrasya samiṣaḥ mahīḥ   giriḥ na bhujmā maghatsu pinvate yat īm sutāḥ amandiṣuḥ  
vayam gha tvā sutāvantaḥ āpaḥ na vṛkta barhiṣaḥ   pavitrasya prasravaṇeṣu vṛtrahan pari stotāraḥ āsate  
svaranti tvā sute naraḥ vaso nireke ukthinaḥ   kadā sutam tṛṣāṇaḥ oke ā gamaḥ indra svabdī iva vaṃsagaḥ  
kaṇvebhiḥ dhṛṣṇo ā dhṛsat vājam darṣi sahasriṇam   piśaṅga rūpam maghavan vicarṣaṇe makṣū gomantam īmahe  
kaḥ īm veda sute sacā pibantam kad vayaḥ dadhe   ayam yaḥ puras vibhinatti ojasā mandānaḥ śiprī andhasaḥ  
dānā mṛgaḥ na vāraṇaḥ purutrā caratham dadhe   nakir tvā ni yamat ā sute gamaḥ mahāḥ carasi ojasā  
yaḥ ugraḥ san a niṣṭṛta sthiraḥ raṇāya saṃskṛtaḥ   yadi stotuḥ maghavā śṛṇavat dhavam na indraḥ yoṣatī ā gamat  
viśvāḥ pṛtanāḥ abhibhūtaram naram sajūs tatakṣuḥ indram jajanuḥ ca rājase   kratvā variṣṭham vare āmurim uta ugram ojiṣṭham tavasam tarasvinam  
sam īm rebhāsaḥ asvaran indram somasya pītaye   svar patim yat īm vṛdhe dhṛta vrataḥ hi ojasā sam ūtibhiḥ  
nemim namanti cakṣasā meṣam viprāḥ abhisvarā   su dītayaḥ vaḥ adruhaḥ api karṇe tarasvinaḥ sam ṛkvabhiḥ  
tam indram johavīmi maghavānam ugram satrā dadhānam a pratiṣkutam śavāṃsi   maṃhiṣṭhaḥ gīrbhiḥ ā ca yajñiyaḥ vavartat rāye naḥ viśvā su pathā kṛṇotu vajrī  
yāḥ indra bhujaḥ ābharaḥ svarvān asurebhyaḥ   stotāram id maghavan asya vardhaya ye ca tve vṛkta barhiṣaḥ  
yam indra dadhiṣe tvam aśvam gām bhāgam avyayam   yajamāne sunvati dakṣiṇāvati tasmin tam dhehi mā paṇau  
indraḥ madāya vāvṛdhe śavase vṛtrahā nṛbhiḥ   tam id mahatsu ājiṣūta īm arbhe havāmahe sa vājeṣu pra naḥ aviṣat  
asi hi vīra senyaḥ asi bhūri parādadiḥ   asi dabhrasya cit vṛdhaḥ yajamānāya śikṣasi sunvate bhūri te vasu  
yat udīrate ājayaḥ dhṛṣṇave dhīyate dhanā   yukṣvā mada cyutā harī kam hanaḥ kam vasau dadhaḥ asmān indra vasau dadhaḥ  
mademade hi naḥ dadiḥ yūthā gavām ṛjukratuḥ   sam gṛbhāya puru śata ubhayā hastyā vasu śiśīhi rāyaḥ ā bhara  
mādayasva sute sacā śavase śūra rādhase   vidma hi tvā purūvasum upa kāmān sasṛjmahe athā naḥ avitā bhava  
ete te indra jantavaḥ viśvam puṣyanti vāryam   antar hi khyaḥ janānām aryaḥ vedaḥ a dāśuṣām teṣām naḥ vedaḥ ā bhara  
surūpa kṛtnum ūtaye su dughām iva go duhe   juhūmasi dyavidyavi  
upa naḥ savanā gahi somasya soma pāḥ piba   go dāḥ id revataḥ madaḥ  
atha te antamānām vidyāma sumatīnām   mā naḥ ati khye ā gahi  
śuṣmintamam naḥ ūtaye dyumninam pāhi jāgṛvim   indra somam śatakrato  
indriyāṇi śatakrato yā te janeṣu pañcasu   indra tāni te ā vṛṇe  
agan indra śravaḥ bṛhat dyumnam dadhiṣva duṣṭaram   ud te śuṣmam tirāmasi  
arvāvataḥ naḥ ā gahi atha u śakra parāvataḥ   u lokaḥ yaḥ te adrivas indra iha tatas ā gahi  
indraḥ aṅga mahat bhayam abhi sat apa cucyavat   sa hi sthiraḥ vicarṣaniḥ  
indraḥ ca mṛlayāti naḥ na naḥ paścāt agham naśat   bhadram bhavāti naḥ puras  
indraḥ āśābhyaḥ pari sarvābhyaḥ abhayam karat  jetā śatrūn vicarṣaṇiḥ 
kaḥ īm veda sute sacā pibantam kad vayaḥ dadhe   ayam yaḥ puras vibhinatti ojasā mandānaḥ śiprī andhasaḥ  
dānā mṛgaḥ na vāraṇaḥ purutrā caratham dadhe   nakir tvā ni yamat ā sute gamaḥ mahān carasi ojasā  
yaḥ ugraḥ san a niṣṭṛta sthiraḥ raṇāya saṃskṛtaḥ   yadi stotuḥ maghavā śṛṇavat dhavam na indraḥ yoṣatī ā gamat  
vayam gha tvā sutāvantaḥ āpaḥ na vṛkta barhiṣaḥ   pavitrasya prasravaṇeṣu vṛtrahan pari stotāraḥ āsate  
svaranti tvā sute naraḥ vaso nireke ukthinaḥ   kadā sutam tṛṣāṇaḥ oke ā gamaḥ indra svabdī iva vaṃsagaḥ  
kaṇvebhiḥ dhṛṣṇo ā dhṛṣat vājam darṣi sahasriṇam   piśaṅga rūpam maghavan vicarṣaṇe makṣū gomantam īmahe  
śrāyante iva sūryam viśvā id indrasya bhakṣata   vasūni jāte janamāne ojasā prati bhāgam na dīdhima  
anarśarātim vasudām upa stuhi bhadrāḥ indrasya rātayaḥ   saḥ asya kāmam vidhataḥ na roṣati manaḥ dānāya codayan  
baṭ mahām asi sūrya baṭ āditya mahām asi   mahaḥ te sataḥ mahimā panasyate addhā deva mahām asi  
baṭ sūrya śravasā mahām asi satrā deva mahāṃ asi   mahnā devānām asuryaḥ purohitaḥ vibhu jyotiḥ adābhyam  
ud u tye madhu mattamāḥ giraḥ stomāsaḥ īrate   satrājitaḥ dhanasāḥ akṣita ūtayaḥ vājayantaḥ rathāḥ iva  
kaṇvāḥ iva bhṛgavaḥ sūrye iva viśvam id dhītam ānaśuḥ   indram stomebhiḥ mahayantaḥ āyavaḥ priyamedhāsaḥ asvaran  
ud id nu asya ricyate aṃśaḥ dhanam na jigyusaḥ   yaḥ indraḥ harivān na dabhanti tam ripaḥ dakṣam dadhāti somini  
mantram akharvam sudhitam supeśasam dadhāta yajñiyeṣu ā   pūrvīḥ cana prasitayaḥ taranti tam ye indre karmaṇā bhuvat 
eva hi asi vīrayuḥ eva śūraḥ uta sthiraḥ   eva te rādhyam manaḥ  
eva rātiḥ tuvīmagha viśvebhiḥ dhāyi dhātṛbhiḥ   aghā cit indra me sacā  
mā u su brahmā iva tandrayuḥ bhuvaḥ vājānām pate   matsva sutasya gomataḥ  
eva hi asya sūnṛtā virapśī gomatī mahī   pakvā śākhā na dāśuṣe  
eva hi te vibhūtayaḥ ūtayaḥ indra māvate   sadyas cit santi dāśuṣe  
eva hi asya kāmyā stomaḥ uktham ca śaṃsyā   indrāya soma pītaye  
tam te madam gṛṇīmasi vṛṣaṇam pṛtsu sāsahim   u loka kṛtnum adrivas hari śriyam  
yena jyotīmṣi āyave manave ca viveditha   mandānaḥ asya barhiṣaḥ vi rājasi  
tat adya cit te ukthinaḥ anu stuvanti pūrvathā   vṛṣa patnīḥ apaḥ jaya divedive  
tam u abhi pra gāyata puruhūtam puruṣṭutam   indram gīrbhiḥ taviṣam ā vivāsata  
yasya dvibarhasaḥ bṛhat sahaḥ dādhāra rodasī   girīn ajrān apaḥ svar vṛṣatvanā  
sa rājasi puruṣṭutam ekaḥ vṛtrāṇi jighnase   indra jaitrā śravasya ca yantave  
vayam u tvām apūrvya sthūram na kad cit bharantaḥ avasyavaḥ   vāje citram havāmahe   vāje citram havāmahe  
upa tvā karman ūtaye sa naḥ yuvā ugraḥ cakrāma yaḥ dhṛṣat   tvām id hi avitāram vavṛmahe sakhāyaḥ indra sānasim  
yaḥ naḥ idam idam purā pra vasyaḥ ānināya tam u vaḥ stuṣe   sakhāyaḥ indram ūtaye  
haryaśvam sat patim carṣaṇīsaham sa hi sma yaḥ amandata   ā tu naḥ sa vayati gavyam aśvyam stotṛbhyaḥ maghavā śatam  
indrāya sāma gāyata viprāya bṛhate bṛhat   dharma kṛte vipaścite panasyave  
tvam indra abhibhūḥ asi tvam sūryam arocayaḥ   viśvakarmā viśvadevaḥ mahān asi  
vibhrājam jyotiṣā svar agacchaḥ rocanam divaḥ   devāḥ te indra sakhyāya yemire  
tam u abhi pra gāyata puruhūtam puruṣṭutam   indram gīrbhiḥ taviṣam ā vivāsata  
yasya dvibarhasaḥ bṛhat sahaḥ dādhāra rodasī   girīn ajrān apaḥ svar vṛṣatvanā  
sa rājasi puruṣṭutam ekaḥ vṛtrāṇi jighnase   indra jaitra śravasya ca yantave  
imā nu kam bhuvanā sīṣadhāma indraḥ ca viśve ca devāḥ   yajñam ca naḥ tanvam ca prajām ca ādityaiḥ indraḥ saha cīkḷpāti  
ādityaiḥ indraḥ sa gaṇaḥ marudbhiḥ asmākam bhūtu avitā tanūnām   hatvāya devāḥ asurān yat āyan devāḥ deva tvam abhirakṣamāṇāḥ  
pratyañcam arkam anayam śacībhiḥ āt id svadhām iṣirām pari apaśyan   ayā vājam deva hitam sanema madema śata himāḥ su vīrāḥ  
yaḥ ekaḥ id vidayate vasu martāya dāśuṣe   īśānaḥ apratiṣkutaḥ indraḥ aṅga  
kadā martam arādhasam padā kṣumpam iva sphurat   kadā naḥ śuśravat giraḥ indraḥ aṅga  
yaḥ cit hi tvā bahubhyaḥ ā sutāvān āvivāsati   ugram tat patyate śavaḥ indraḥ aṅga  
yaḥ indra soma pātamaḥ madaḥ śaviṣṭha cetati   yena haṃsi ni attriṇam tam īmahe  
yena daśagvam adhrigum vepayantam svarṇaram   yena samudram āvitha tam īmahe  
yena sindhum mahīḥ apaḥ rathān iva pracodayaḥ   panthām ṛtasya yātave tam īmahe  
ā indra naḥ gadhi priyaḥ satrājit agohyaḥ   giriḥ na viśvatas pṛthuḥ patiḥ divaḥ  
abhi hi satya soma pāḥ ubhe babhūtha rodasī   indra asi sunvataḥ vṛdhaḥ patiḥ divaḥ  
tvam hi śaśvatīnām indra dartā purām asi   hantā dasyoḥ manoḥ vṛdhaḥ patiḥ divaḥ  
eva id u madhvaḥ madintaram siñca vai adhvaryo andhasaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ   eva hi 
indra sthātar harīṇām nakir te pūrvya stutim   ud ānaṃśa śavasā na bhandanā  
tam vaḥ vājānām patim ahūmahi śravasyavaḥ   aprāyubhiḥ yajñebhiḥ vāvṛdhenyam  
etaḥ nu indram stavāma sakhāyaḥ stomyam naram   kuṣṭīḥ yaḥ viśvāḥ abhi asti ekaḥ id  
agorudhāya gaviṣe dyukṣāya dasmyam vacaḥ   ghṛtāt svādīyaḥ madhunaḥ ca vocata  
yasya amitāni vīryā na rādhaḥ paryetave   jyotiḥ na viśvam abhi asti dakṣiṇā  
stuhi indram vyaśvavat anūrmim vājinam yamam   aryaḥ gayam maṃhamānam vi dāśuṣe  
eva nūnam upa stuhi vaiyaśva daśamam navam   suvidvāṃsam carkṛtyam caraṇīnām  
vettha hi nirṛtīnām vajrahasta parivṛjam   aharahar śundhyuḥ paripadām iva  
vanoti hi sunvan kṣayam parīṇasaḥ sunvānaḥ hi sma yajati ava dviṣaḥ devānām ava dviṣaḥ   sunvānaḥ id siṣāsati sahasrā vājī avṛtaḥ   sunvānāya indraḥ dadāti ābhuvam rayim dadāti ābhuvam  
mā u su vaḥ asmat abhi tāni pauṃsyā sanā bhūvan dyumnāni mā uta jāriṣuḥ asmat purā uta jāriṣuḥ   yat vaḥ citram yugeyuge navyam ghoṣāt amartyam   asmāsu tat marutaḥ yat ca duṣṭaram didhṛtāḥ yat ca duṣṭaram  
agnim hotāram manye dāsvantam vasum sūnum sahasaḥ jātavedasam vipram na jātavedasam   yaḥ ūrdhvayā su adhvaraḥ devaḥ devācyā kṛpā   ghṛtasya vibhrāṣṭim anu vaṣṭi śociṣā ājuhvānasya sarpiṣaḥ  
yajñaiḥ saṃmiślāḥ pṛṣatībhiḥ ṛṣṭibhiḥ yāmam chubhrāsaḥ añjiṣu priyāḥ uta   āsadyāḥ barhiḥ bharatasya sūnavaḥ potrāt ā somam pibata divaḥ naraḥ  
ā vakṣi devān iha vipra yakṣi ca uśan hotar ni sadā yoniṣu triṣu   prati vīhi prasthitam somyam madhu piba āgnīdhrāt tava bhāgasya tṛsṇuhi  
eṣa sya te tanvaḥ nṛmṇa vardhanaḥ sahaḥ ojaḥ pradivi bāhvoḥ hitaḥ   tubhyam sutaḥ maghavan tubhyam ābhṛtaḥ tvam asya brāhmaṇāt ā tṛpat piba  
yam u pūrvam a huve tam idam huve sa id u havyaḥ dadiḥ yaḥ nāma patyate   adhvaryubhiḥ prasthitam somyam madhu potrāt somam draviṇaḥ daḥ piba ṛtubhiḥ  
surūpa kṛtnum ūtaye su dughām iva go duhe   juhūmasi dyavidyavi  
upa naḥ savanā gahi somasya soma pāḥ piba   go dāḥ id revataḥ madaḥ  
atha te antamānām vidyāma sumatīnām   mā naḥ ati khye ā gahi  
parehi vigram astṛtam indram pṛchā vipaścitam   yaḥ te sakhibhyaḥ ā varam  
uta bruvantu naḥ nidaḥ niḥ anyatas cit ārata   dadhānāḥ indraḥ id duvaḥ  
uta naḥ subhagām ariḥ voceyuḥ dasma kṛṣṭayaḥ   syāma id indrasya śarmaṇi  
ā īm āśum āśave bhara yajña śriyam nṛ mādanam   patayan mandayat sakham  
asya pītvā śatakrato ghanaḥ vṛtrāṇām abhavaḥ   prāvaḥ vājeṣu vājinam  
tam tvā vājeṣu vājinam vājayāmaḥ śatakrato   dhanānām indra sātaye  
yaḥ rāyaḥ avaniḥ mahān su pāraḥ sunvataḥ sakhā   tasmai indrāya gāyata  
ā tu etā ni sīdata indram abhi pra gāyata   sakhāyaḥ stoma vāhasaḥ  
purūtamam purūṇām īśānam vāryāṇām   indram some sacā sute  
sa gha naḥ yoge ā bhuvat sa rāye sa puraṃdhyām   gamat vājebhiḥ ā sa naḥ  
yasya saṃsthe na vṛṇvate harī samatsu śatravaḥ   tasmai indrāya gāyata  
suta pāvne sutāḥ ime śucayaḥ yanti vītaye   somāsaḥ dadhi āśiraḥ  
tvam sutasya pītaye sadyas vṛddhaḥ ajāyathāḥ   indra jyaiṣṭhyāya sukrato  
ā tvā viśantu āśavaḥ somāsaḥ indra girvaṇaḥ   śam te santu pracetase  
tvām stomāḥ avīvṛdhan tvām ukthā śatakrato   tvām vardhantu naḥ giraḥ  
akṣita ūtiḥ sanet imam vājam indraḥ sahasriṇam   yasmin viśvāni pauṃsyā  
mā naḥ martāḥ abhi druhan tanūnām indra girvaṇaḥ   īśānaḥ yavaya vadham  
yuñjanti bradhnam aruṣam carantam pari tasthuṣaḥ   rocante rocanā divi  
yuñjanti asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe   śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛ vāhasā  
ketum kṛṇvan aketave peśaḥ maryāḥ apeśase   sam uṣadbhiḥ ajāyathāḥ  
āt aha svadhām anu punar garbha tvam erire   dadhānāḥ nāma yajñiyam  
vīlu cit ārujatnubhiḥ guhā cit indra vahnibhiḥ   avindaḥ usriyāḥ anu  
devayantaḥ yathā matim achā vidat vasum giraḥ   mahām anūṣata śrutam  
indreṇa sam hi dṛkṣase saṃjagmānaḥ abibhyuṣā   mandū samāna varcasā  
anavadyaiḥ abhidyubhiḥ makhaḥ sahasvat arcati   gaṇaiḥ indrasya kāmyaiḥ  
atas parijman ā gahi divaḥ vā rocanāt adhi   sam asmin ṛñjate giraḥ  
itas vā sātim īmahe divaḥ vā pārthivāt adhi   indram mahaḥ vā rajasaḥ  
indram id gathinaḥ bṛhat indram arkebhiḥ arkiṇaḥ   indram vāṇīḥ anūṣata  
indraḥ id dharyoḥ sacā saṃmiślaḥ ā vacaḥ yujā   indraḥ vajrī hiraṇyayaḥ  
indraḥ dīrghāya cakṣase ā sūryam rohayat divi   vi gobhiḥ indram airayat  
indra vājeṣu naḥ ava sahasra pradhaneṣu ca   ugraḥ ugrābhiḥ ūtibhiḥ  
indram vayam mahādhane indram arbhe havāmahe   yujam vṛtreṣu vajriṇam  
sa naḥ vṛṣan amum carum satrā adāvan apa vṛdhi   asmabhyam a pratiṣkutaḥ  
tuñjetuñje ye uttare stomāḥ indrasya vajriṇaḥ   na vindhe asya suṣṭutim  
vṛṣā yūthā iva vaṃsagaḥ kṛṣṭīḥ iyarti ojasā   īśānaḥ a pratiṣkutaḥ  
yaḥ ekaḥ carṣaṇīnām vasūnām irajyati   indraḥ pañca kṣitīnām  
indram vaḥ viśvatas pari havāmahe janebhyaḥ  asmākam astu kevalaḥ 
ā indra sānasim rayim sa jitvānam sadāsaham   varṣiṣṭham ūtaye bhara  
ni yena muṣṭi hatyayā ni vṛtrā ruṇadhāmahai   tvotāsaḥ ni arvatā  
indra tvotāsaḥ ā vayam vajram ghanā dadīmahi   jayema sam yudhi spṛdhaḥ  
vayam śūrebhiḥ astṛbhiḥ indra tvayā yujā vayam   sāsahyāma pṛtanyataḥ  
mahān indraḥ paras ca nu mahitvam astu vajriṇe   dyauḥ na prathinā śavaḥ  
samohe vā ye āśata naraḥ tokasya sanitau   viprāsaḥ vā dhiyāyavaḥ  
yaḥ kukṣiḥ soma pātamaḥ samudre iva pinvate   urvīḥ āpaḥ na kākudaḥ  
eva hi asya sūnṛtā virapśī gomatī mahī   pakvā śākhā na dāśuṣe  
eva hi te vibhūtayaḥ ūtayaḥ indra māvate   sadyas cit santi dāśuṣe  
eva hi asya kāmyā stomaḥ uktham ca śaṃsyā   indrāya soma pītaye  
indra ihi matsi andhasaḥ viśvebhiḥ soma parvabhiḥ   mahān abhiṣṭiḥ ojasā  
ā īm enam sṛjata sute mandim indrāya mandine   cakrim viśvāni cakraye  
matsva su śipra mandibhiḥ stomebhiḥ viśvacarṣaṇe   sacā eṣu savaneṣu ā  
asṛgram indra te giraḥ prati tvām ud ahāsata   ajoṣāḥ vṛṣabham patim  
sam codaya citram arvāk rādhaḥ indra vareṇyam   asat id te vibhu prabhu  
asmān su tatra codaya indra rāye rabhasvataḥ   tuvi dyumna yaśasvataḥ  
sam gomat indra vājavat asme pṛthu śravaḥ bṛhat  viśvāyuḥ dhehi akṣitam  
asme dhehi śravaḥ bṛhat dyumnam sahasra sātamam   indra tāḥ rathinīḥ iṣaḥ  
vasoḥ indram vasu patim gīrbhiḥ gṛṇantaḥ ṛgmiyam   homa gantāram ūtaye  
sutesute nyokase bṛhat bṛhataḥ ā id ariḥ   indrāya śūṣam arcati  
viśveṣu hi tvā savaneṣu tuñjate samānam ekam vṛṣamaṇyavaḥ pṛthak svar saniṣyavaḥ pṛthak   tam tvā nāvam na parṣaṇim śūṣasya dhuri dhīmahi   indram na yajñaiḥ catayantaḥ āyavaḥ stomebhiḥ indram āyavaḥ  
vi tvā tatasre mithunāḥ avasyavaḥ vrajasya sātā gavyasya niḥsṛjaḥ sakṣantaḥ indra niḥsṛjaḥ   yat gavyantā dvā janā svar yantā samūhasi   āvis karikrat vṛṣaṇam sacābhuvam vajram indra sacābhuvam  
uta u naḥ asyāḥ uṣasaḥ juṣeta hi arkasya bodhi haviṣaḥ havīmabhiḥ svarṣātā havīmabhiḥ   yat indra hantave mṛghaḥ vṛṣā vajrim ciketasi   ā me asya vedhasaḥ navīyasaḥ manma śrudhi navīyasaḥ  
tubhya id imā savanā śūra viśvā tubhyam brahmāṇi vardhanā kṛṇomi   tvam nṛbhiḥ havyaḥ viśvadhā asi  
nu cit nu te manyamānasya dasmaḥ ud aśnuvanti mahimānam ugra   na vīryam indra te na rādhaḥ  
pra vaḥ mahe mahivṛdhe bharadhvam pracetase pra sumatim kṛṇudhvam   viśaḥ pūrvīḥ pra cara carṣaṇiprāḥ  
yadā vajram hiraṇyam id athā ratham harī yamasya vahataḥ vi sūribhiḥ   ā tiṣṭhati maghavā sanaśrutaḥ indraḥ vājasya dīrghaśravasaḥ patiḥ  
so cit nu vṛṣṭiḥ yūthyā svā sacām indraḥ śmaśrūṇi haritā abhi pruṣṇute   ava veti su kṣayam sute madhu ud id dhūṇoti vātaḥ yathā vanam  
yaḥ vācā vivācaḥ mṛdhra vācaḥ purū sahasra aśivā jaghāna   tat tat id asya pauṃsyam gṛṇīmasi pitā iva yaḥ taviṣīm vāvṛdhe śavaḥ  
yat cit hi satya soma pāḥ anāśastāḥ iva smasi   ā tū naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
śiprin vājānām pate śacīvas tava daṃsanā   ā tu naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
ni svāpayā mithūdṛśā sastām a budhyamāne   ā tū naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
sasantu tyāḥ arātayaḥ bodhantu śūra rātayaḥ   ā tū naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
sam indra gardabham mṛṇa nuvantam papaya amuyā   ā tu naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
patāti kuṇḍṛṇācyā dūram vātaḥ vanāt adhi   ā tū naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
sarvam parikrośam jahi jambhayā kṛkadāśvam   ā tū naḥ indra śaṃsaya goṣu aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha  
vi tvā tatasre mithunāḥ avasyavaḥ vrajasya sātā gavyasya niḥsṛjaḥ sakṣantaḥ indra niḥsṛjaḥ   yat gavyanta dvā janā svar yantā samūhasi   āvis karikrat vṛṣaṇam sacābhuvam vajram indra sacābhuvam  
viduḥ te asya vīryasya pūravaḥ puraḥ yat indra śāradīḥ avātiraḥ sāsahānaḥ avātiraḥ   śāsaḥ tam indra martyam ayajum śavasaḥ pate   mahīm amuṣṇāḥ pṛthivīm imāḥ apaḥ mandasānaḥ imāḥ apaḥ  
āt id te asya vīryasya carkiran madeṣu vṛṣan uśijaḥ yat āvitha sakhīyataḥ yat āvitha   cakartha kāram ebhyaḥ pṛtanāsu pravantave   te anyām anyām nadyam saniṣṇata śravasyantaḥ saniṣṇata  
vane na vā yaḥ ni adhāyi cākram chuciḥ vām stomaḥ bhuraṇau ajīgaḥ   yasya id indraḥ puru dineṣu hotā nṛṇām narvaḥ nṛtamaḥ kṣapāvān  
pra te asyāḥ uṣasaḥ pra aparasyāḥ nṛtau syāma nṛtam asya nṛṇām   anu triśokaḥ śatam āvahat nṝn kutsena rathaḥ yaḥ asat sasavān  
kaḥ te madaḥ indra rantyaḥ bhūt duraḥ giraḥ abhi ugraḥ vi dhāva   kad vāho arvāk upa mā manīṣāḥ ā tvā śakyām upamam rādhaḥ annaiḥ  
kad u dyumnam indra tvāvataḥ nṝn kayā dhiyā karase kad naḥ āgan   mitraḥ na satyaḥ urugāya bhṛtyāḥ anne samasya yat asat manīṣāḥ  
preraya sūraḥ artham na pāram ye asya kāmam janidhāḥ iva gman   giraḥ ca ye te tuvi jāta pūrvīḥ naraḥ indra pratiśikṣanti annaiḥ  
mātre nu te sumite indra pūrvī dyauḥ majmanā pṛthivī kāvyena   varāya te ghṛtavantaḥ sutāsaḥ svādnan bhavantu pītaye madhūni  
ā madhvaḥ asmai asican amatram indrāya pūrṇam sa hi satya rādhāḥ   sa vāvṛdhe variman ā pṛthivyāḥ abhi kratvā naryaḥ pauṃsyaiḥ ca  
vi ānaḷ indraḥ pṛtanāḥ svojāḥ ā asmai yatante sakhyāya pūrvīḥ   ā smā ratham na pṛtanāsu tiṣṭha yam bhadrayā sumatyā codayāse  
ā satyaḥ yātu maghavā ṛjīṣī dravantu asya harayaḥ upa naḥ   tasmai id andhaḥ suṣuma su dakṣam iha abhipitvam karate gṛṇānaḥ  
ava sya śūra adhvanaḥ na ante asmin naḥ adya savane mandadhyai   śaṃsāti uktham uśanā iva vedhāḥ cikituṣe asuryāya manma  
kaviḥ na niṇyam vidathāni sādhan vṛṣā yat sekam vipipānaḥ arcāt   divaḥ itthā jījanat sapta kārūn ahnā cit cakruḥ vayunā gṛṇantaḥ  
svar yat vedi su dṛśīkam arkaiḥ mahi jyotīḥ rurucuḥ yat ha vastoḥ   andhā tamāṃsi dudhitā vicakṣe nṛbhyaḥ cakāra nṛtamaḥ abhiṣṭau  
vavakṣe indraḥ amitam ṛjiṣi ubhe ā paprau rodasī mahitvā   atas cit asya mahimā vi reci abhi yaḥ viśvā bhuvanā babhūva  
viśvāni śakraḥ naryāṇi vidvān apaḥ rireca sakhibhiḥ nikāmaiḥ   aśmānam cit ye bibhiduḥ vacobhiḥ vrajam gomantam uśijaḥ vi vavruḥ  
apaḥ vṛtram vavrivāṃsam parāhan prāvat te vajram pṛthivī sacetāḥ   pra arṇāṃsi samudriyāṇi ainoḥ patiḥ bhavam śavasā śūra dhṛṣṇo  
apaḥ yat adrim puruhūta dardar āvis bhuvat saramā pūrvyam te   sa naḥ netā vājam ā darṣi bhūrim gotrā rujan aṅgirobhiḥ gṛṇānaḥ  
tat vaḥ gāya sute sacā puruhūtāya satvane   śam yat gave na śākine  
na ghā vasuḥ ni yamate dānam vājasya gomataḥ   yat sīm upa śravat giraḥ  
kuvitsasya pra hi vrajam gomantam dasyu hā gamat  śacībhiḥ apa naḥ varat 
indra kratum naḥ ā bhara pitā putrebhyaḥ yathā   śikṣa naḥ asmin puruhūta yāmani jīvāḥ jyotiḥ aśīmahi  
mā naḥ ajñātāḥ vṛjanāḥ durādhyaḥ mā aśivāsaḥ ava kramuḥ   tvayā vayam pravataḥ śaśvatīḥ apaḥ ati śūra tarāmasi  
indra jyeṣṭham naḥ ā bharam ojiṣṭham papuri śravaḥ   yena ime citra vajrahasta rodasī ā ubhe su śipra prāḥ  
tvām ugram avase carṣaṇīsaham rājan deveṣu hūmahe   viśvā su naḥ vithurā pibdanā vaso amitrān suṣahān kṛdhi  
yat dyāvaḥ indra te śatam śatam bhūmiḥ uta syuḥ   na tvā vajrin sahasram sūryāḥ anu na jātam aṣṭa rodasī  
ā paprātha mahinā kṛṣṇyā vṛṣan viśvā śaviṣṭha śavasā   asmān ava maghavan gomati vraje vajrim citrābhiḥ ūtibhiḥ  
yat indra yāvataḥ tvam etāvat aham īśīya   stotāram id didhiṣeya radāvaso na pāpa tvāya rāsīya  
śikṣeyam id mahayate divedive rāyaḥ ā kuhacid vide   nahi tvat anyat maghavan naḥ āpyam vasyaḥ asti pitā cana  
indra tri dhātu śaraṇam tri varūtham svastimat   chardiḥ yaccha maghavadbhyaḥ ca mahyam ca yāvaya didyum ebhyaḥ  
ye gavyatā manasā śatrum ādabhuḥ abhipraghnanti dhṛṣṇuyā   agha smā naḥ maghavan indra girvaṇaḥ tanū pāḥ antamaḥ bhava  
indra ā yāhi citra bhāno sutāḥ ime tvāyavaḥ   aṇvībhiḥ tanā pūtāsaḥ  
indra ā yāhi dhiyā iṣitaḥ vipra jutaḥ sutāvataḥ   upa brahmāṇi vāghataḥ  
indra ā yāhi tūtujānaḥ upa brahmāṇi harivas   sute dadhiṣva naḥ canaḥ  
mā cit anyat vi śaṃsata sakhāyaḥ mā riṣaṇyata   indram id stotā vṛṣaṇam sacā sute muhur ukthā ca śaṃsata  
avakrakṣiṇam vṛṣabham yathā ajuram gām na carṣaṇīsaham   vidveṣaṇam saṃvanana ubhayaṃkaram maṃhiṣṭham ubhayāvinam  
yat cit hi tvā janāḥ ime nānā havante ūtaye   asmākam brahmā idam indra bhūtu te ahā viśvā ca vardhanam  
vi tartūryante maghavan vipaścitaḥ aryaḥ vipaḥ janānām   upa kramasva puru rūpam ā bhara vājam nediṣṭham ūtaye  
brahmaṇā te brahma yujā yunajmi harī sakhāyā sadhamādaḥ āśū   sthiram ratham sukham indra adhitiṣṭhan prajānan vidvāṃ upa yāhi somam  
adhvaryavaḥ aruṇam dugdham aṃśum juhotana vṛṣabhāya kṣitīnām   gaurāt vedīyām avapānam indraḥ viśvāhā id yāti suta somam ichan  
yat dadhiṣe pradivi cāru annam divedive pītim id asya vakṣi   uta hṛdā uta manasā juṣāṇaḥ uśan indra prasthitān pāhi somān  
jajñānaḥ somam sahase papātha pra te mātā mahimānam uvāca   ā indra paprātha uru antarikṣam yudhā devebhyaḥ varivaḥ cakartha  
yat yodhaya mahataḥ manyamānān sākṣāma tān bāhubhiḥ śāśadānān   yat vā nṛbhiḥ vṛtaḥ indra abhiyudhyāḥ tam tvayā ājim sauśravasam jayema  
pra indrasya vocam prathamā kṛtāni pra nūtanā maghavā yā cakāra   yadā id adevīḥ asahiṣṭa māyāḥ atha abhavat kevalaḥ somaḥ asya  
tava idam viśvam abhitas paśavyam yat paśyasi cakṣasā sūryasya   gavām asi gopatiḥ ekaḥ indra bhakṣīmahi te prayatasya vasvaḥ  
bṛhaspate yuvam indraḥ ca vasvaḥ divyasya īśāthe uta pārthivasya   dhattam rayim stuvate kīraye cit yūyam pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ  
yaḥ tastambha sahasā vi jmaḥ antān bṛhaspatiḥ triṣadhasthaḥ raveṇa   tam pratnāsaḥ ṛṣayaḥ dīdhyānāḥ puras viprāḥ dadhire mandra jihvam  
dhunetayaḥ supraketam madantaḥ bṛhaspate abhi ye naḥ tatasre   pṛṣantam sṛpram adabdham ūrvam bṛhaspate rakṣatāt asya yonim  
bṛhaspate yā paramā parāvat atas ā te ṛta spṛśaḥ ni seduḥ   tubhyam khātāḥ avatāḥ adri dugdhāḥ madhvaḥ ścotanti abhitas virapśam  
bṛhaspatiḥ prathamam jāyamānaḥ mahaḥ jyotiṣaḥ parame vyoman   sapta āsyaḥ tuvi jātaḥ raveṇa vi sapta raśmiḥ adhamat tamāṃsi  
sa suṣṭubhā saḥ ṛkvatā gaṇena valam ruroja phaligam ravena   bṛhaspatiḥ usriyā havya sūdaḥ kanikradat vāvaśatīḥ ud ājat  
eva pitre viśvadevāya vṛṣṇe yajñaiḥ vidhema namasā havirbhiḥ   bṛhaspate su prajāḥ vīravantaḥ vayam syāma patayaḥ rayīṇām  
astā iva su prataram lāyam asyan bhūṣan iva pra bhara stomam asmai   vācā viprāḥ tarata vācam aryaḥ ni rāmaya jaritaḥ somaḥ indram  
dohena gām upa śikṣa sakhāyam pra bodhaya jaritar jāram indram   kośam na pūrṇam vasunā nyṛṣṭam ā cyāvaya magha deyāya śūram  
kim aṅga tvā maghavan bhojam āhuḥ śiśīhi mā śiśayam tvā śṛṇomi   apnasvatī mama dhīḥ astu śakra vasu vidam bhagam indra ā bhara naḥ  
tvām janāḥ mamasatyeṣu indra saṃtasthānāḥ vi hvayante samīke   atrā yujam kṛṇute yaḥ haviṣmān na a sunvatā sakhyam vaṣṭi śūraḥ  
dhanam naḥ spandram bahulam yaḥ asmai tīvrān somān āsunoti prayasvān   tasmai śatrūn sutukān prātar ahnaḥ ni svaṣṭrān yuvati hanti vṛtram  
yasmin vayam dadhima śaṃsam indre yaḥ śiśrāya maghavā kāmam asme   ārāt cit san bhayatām asya śatruḥ ni asmai dyumnā janyā namantām  
ārāt śatrum apa bādhasva dūram ugraḥ yaḥ śambaḥ puruhūta tena   asme dhehi yavamat gomat indra kṛdhī dhiyam jaritre vāja ratnām  
pra yam antar vṛṣa savāsaḥ ajman tīvrāḥ somāḥ bahulāntāsaḥ indram   na aha dāmānam maghavā ni yaṃsan ni sunvate vahati bhūri vāmam  
uta prahām atidīvā jayati kṛtam iva śvaghnī vi cinoti kāle   yaḥ deva kāmaḥ na dhanam ruṇaddhi sam id tam rāyaḥ sṛjati svadhābhiḥ  
gobhiḥ tarema amatim durevām yavena vā kṣudham puruhūta viśve   vayam rājasu prathamā dhanāni ariṣṭāsaḥ vṛjanībhiḥ jayema  
bṛhaspatiḥ naḥ pari pātu paścāt uta uttarasmāt adharāt aghayoḥ   indraḥ purastāt uta madhyataḥ naḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ varīyaḥ kṛṇotu  
yaḥ adribhid prathama jāḥ ṛtāvā bṛhaspatiḥ āṅgirasaḥ haviṣmān   dvibarhajmā prāgharmasat pitā naḥ ā rodasī vṛṣabhaḥ roravīti  
janāya cit yaḥ īvate u lokam bṛhaspatiḥ deva hūtau cakāra   ghnan vṛtrāṇi vi puraḥ dardarīti jayam śatrūṃr amitrān pṛtsu sāhan  
bṛhaspatiḥ sam ajayat vasūni mahaḥ vrajān gomate devaḥ eṣaḥ   apaḥ siṣāsan svar a pratītaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ hanti amitram arkaiḥ  
imām dhiyam sapta śīrṣṇīm pitā naḥ ṛta prajātām bṛhatīm avindat   turīyam svid janayat viśvajanyaḥ ayāsyaḥ uktham indrāya śaṃsan  
ṛtam śaṃsantaḥ ṛju dīdhyānāḥ divaḥ putrāsaḥ asurasya vīrāḥ   vipram padam aṅgirasaḥ dadhānāḥ yajñasya dhāma prathamam mananta  
haṃsaiḥ iva sakhibhiḥ vāvadadbhiḥ aśman mayāni nahanā vyasyan   bṛhaspatiḥ abhikanikradat gāḥ uta prāstaut ud ca vidvām agāyat  
avas dvābhyām paras ekayā gāḥ guhā tiṣṭhantīḥ anṛtasya setau   bṛhaspatiḥ tamasi jyotiḥ ichan ud usrāḥ ākaḥ vi hi tisraḥ āvaḥ  
vibhidya īm apācīm niḥ trīṇi sākam udadheḥ akṛntat   bṛhaspatiḥ uṣasam sūryam gām arkam viveda stanayan iva dyauḥ  
indraḥ valam rakṣitāram dughānām kareṇa iva vi cakarta raveṇa   sveda añjibhiḥ āśiram ichamānaḥ arodayat paṇim ā gāḥ amuṣṇāt  
saḥ īm satyebhiḥ sakhibhiḥ śucadbhiḥ godhāyasam vi dhanasaiḥ adardaḥ   brahmaṇaḥ patiḥ vṛṣabhiḥ varāhaiḥ gharma svedebhiḥ draviṇam vi ānaṭ  
te satyena manasā go patim gāḥ iyānāsaḥ iṣaṇayanta dhībhiḥ   bṛhaspatiḥ mithoavadyapebhiḥ ud usriyāḥ asṛjata sva yugbhiḥ  
tam vardhayantaḥ matibhiḥ śivābhiḥ siṃham iva nānadatam sadhasthe   bṛhaspatim vṛṣaṇam śūrasātau bharebhare anu madema jiṣṇum  
yadā vājam asanat viśva rūpam ā dyām arukṣat uttarāṇi sadma   bṛhaspatim vṛṣaṇam vardhayantaḥ nānā santaḥ bibhrataḥ jyotiḥ āsā  
satyam āśiṣam kṛṇuta vayodhai kīrim cit hi avatha svebhiḥ evaiḥ   paścā mṛdhaḥ apa bhavantu viśvāḥ tat rodasī śṛṇutam viśvaminve  
indraḥ mahnā mahataḥ arṇavasya vi mūrdhānam abhinat arbudasya   ahan ahim ariṇāt sapta sindhūn devaiḥ dyāvāpṛthivī prāvatam naḥ  
abhi pra gopatim girā indram arca yathā vide   sūtum satyasya satpatim  
ā harayaḥ sasṛjrire aruṣīḥ adhi barhiṣi   yatra abhi saṃnavāmahe  
indrāya gāvaḥ āśiram duduhre vajriṇe madhu   yat sīm upahvare vidat  
ud yat bradhnasya viṣṭapam gṛham indraḥ ca ganvahi   madhvaḥ pītvā sacevahi tris sapta sakhyuḥ pade  
arcata prārcata priyamedhāsaḥ arcata   arcantu putrakāḥ uta puram na dhṛṣṇu arcata  
ava svarāti gargaraḥ godhā pari saniṣvaṇat   piṅgā pari caniṣkadat indrāya brahma udyatam  
ā yat patanti enyaḥ su dughāḥ an apasphuraḥ   apasphuram gṛbhāyata somam indrāya pātave  
apāt indraḥ apāt agniḥ viśve devāḥ amatsata   varuṇaḥ id iha kṣayat tam āpaḥ abhī anūṣata vatsam saṃśiśvarīḥ iva  
sudevaḥ asi varuṇa yasya te sapta sindhavaḥ   anukṣaranti kākudam sūryam suṣirām iva  
yaḥ vyatīn aphāṇayat su yuktām upa dāśuṣe   takvaḥ netā tat id vapuḥ upamā yaḥ amucyata  
ati id u śakraḥ ohate indraḥ viśvāḥ ati dviṣaḥ   bhinat kanīnaḥ odanam pacyamānam paras girā  
arbhakaḥ na kumārakaḥ adhi tiṣṭhan avam ratham   sa pakṣan mahiṣam mṛgam pitre mātre vibhukratum  
ā tū su śipra daṃpate ratham tiṣṭha hiraṇyayam   adha dyukṣam sacevahi sahasra pādam aruṣam svasti gām anehasam  
tam gha īm itthā namasvinaḥ upa svarājam āsate   artham cit asya sudhitam yat etave āvartayanti dāvane  
anu pratnasya okasaḥ priyamedhāsaḥ eṣām   pūrvām anu prayatim vṛkta barhiṣaḥ hita prayasaḥ āśata  
yaḥ rājā carṣaṇīnām yātā rathebhiḥ adhriguḥ   viśvāsām tarutā pṛtanānām jyeṣṭhaḥ yaḥ vṛtra hā gṛṇe  
indram tam śumbha puru hanman avase yasya dvitā vidhartari   hastāya vajraḥ prati dhāyi darśataḥ mahaḥ dive na sūryaḥ  
nakir tam karmaṇā naśat yaḥ cakāra sadāvṛdham   indram na yajñaiḥ viśva gūrtam ṛbhvasam adhṛṣṭam dhṛṣṇu ojasam  
aṣālham ugram pṛtanāsu sāsahim yasmin mahīḥ uru jrayaḥ   sam dhenavaḥ jāyamāne anonavuḥ dyāvaḥ kṣāmaḥ anonavuḥ  
yat dyāvaḥ indra te śatam śatam bhūmīḥ uta syuḥ   na tvā vajrin sahasram sūryāḥ anu na jātam aṣṭa rodasī  
ā paprātha mahinā vṛṣṇyā vṛṣan viśvā śaviṣṭha śavasā   asmān ava maghavan gomati vraje vajrim citrābhiḥ ūtibhiḥ  
ud tvā mandantu stomāḥ kṛṇuṣva rādhaḥ adrivas   ava brahma dviṣaḥ jahi  
padā paṇīn arādhasaḥ ni bādhasva mahān asi   nahi tvā kaḥ cana prati  
tvam īśiṣe sutānām indra tvam asutānām   tvam rājā janānām  
īṅkhayantīḥ apasyuvaḥ indram jātam upāsate   bhejānāsaḥ su vīryam  
tvam indra balāt adhi sahasaḥ jātaḥ ojasaḥ   tvam vṛṣan vṛṣā id asi  
tvam indra asi vṛtrahā vi antarikṣam atiraḥ   ud dyām astabhnāḥ ojasā  
tvam indra sajoṣasam arkam bibharṣi bāhvoḥ   vajram śiśānaḥ ojasā  
tvam indra abhibhuḥ asi viśvā jātāni ojasā   sa viśvā bhuvaḥ ābhavaḥ  
ā yātu indraḥ sva patiḥ madāya yaḥ dharmaṇā tūtujānaḥ tuviṣmān   pratvakṣāṇaḥ ati viśvā sahāṃsi apāreṇa mahatā vṛṣṇyena  
suṣṭhāmā rathaḥ suyamā harī te mimyakṣa vajraḥ nṛpate gabhastau   śībham rājan su pathā yāhi arvāṅ vardhāma te papusaḥ vṛṣṇyāni  
indra vāhaḥ nṛpatim vajra bāhum ugram ugrāsaḥ taviṣāsaḥ enam   pratvakṣasam vṛṣabham satya śuṣmam ā īm asmatrā sadhamādaḥ vahantu  
eva patim droṇasācam sacetasam ūrjaḥ skambham dharuṇaḥ ā vṛṣāyase   ojaḥ kṛṣva sam gṛbhāya tve api asaḥ yathā kenipānām inaḥ vṛdhe  
gaman asme vasūni ā hi śaṃsiṣam su āśiṣam bharam ā yāhi sominaḥ   tvam īśiṣe sā asmin ā satsi barhiṣi anādhṛṣyā tava pātrāṇi dharmaṇā  
pṛthak prāyan prathamāḥ deva hūtayaḥ akṛṇvata śravasyāni duṣṭarā   na ye śekuḥ yajñiyām nāvam āruham irmā eva te ni aviśanta kepayaḥ  
eva eva apāk apare santu dūdhyaḥ aśvāḥ yeṣām duryuge āyuyujre   itthā ye prāk upare santi dāvane purūṇi yatra vayunāni bhojanā  
girīn ajrān rejamānām adhārayat dyauḥ krandat antarikṣāṇi kopayat   samīcīne dhiṣaṇe vi skabhāyati vṛṣṇaḥ pītvā made ukthāni śaṃsati  
imam bibharmi su kṛtam te aṅkuśam yena ārujāsi maghavam chaphārujaḥ   asmin su te savane astu oktyam sutaḥ iṣṭau maghavan bodhi ābhagaḥ  
gobhiḥ tarema amatim durevām yavena kṣudham puruhūta viśvām   vayam rājabhiḥ prathamā dhanāni asmākena vṛjanena jayema  
bṛhaspatiḥ naḥ pari pātu paścāt uta uttarasmāt adharāt aghayoḥ   indraḥ purastāt uta madhyataḥ naḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ varivaḥ kṛṇotu  
trikadrukeṣu mahiṣaḥ yava āśiram tuvi śuṣmaḥ tṛpat somam apibat viṣṇunā sutam yathā avaśat   saḥ īm mamāda mahi karma kartave mahām urum sā enam saścat devaḥ devam satyam indram satyaḥ induḥ  
pra u su asmai puroratham indrāya śūṣam arcata   abhīke cit u loka kṛt saṃge samatsu vṛtrahā asmākam bodhi coditāḥ nabhantām anyakeṣām jyākāḥ adhi dhanvasu  
tvam sindhūṃr avāsṛjaḥ adharācaḥ ahan ahim   a śatruḥ indra jajñiṣe viśvam puṣyasi vāryam tam tvā pari svajāmahe nabhantām anyakeṣām jyākāḥ adhi dhanvasu  
vi su viśvāḥ arātayaḥ aryaḥ naśanta naḥ dhiyaḥ   astāsi śatrave vadham yaḥ naḥ indra jighāṃsati yā te rātiḥ dadiḥ vasu   nabhantām anyakeṣām jyakāḥ adhi dhanvasu  
tīvrasya abhivayasaḥ asya pāhi sarva rathā vi harī iha muñca   indra mā tvā yajamānāsaḥ anye ni rīraman tubhyam ime sutāsaḥ  
tubhyam sutāḥ tubhyam u sotvāsaḥ tvām giraḥ śvātryāḥ ā hvayanti   indra idam adya savanam juṣāṇaḥ viśvasya vidvāṃ iha pāhi somam  
yaḥ uśatā manasā somam asmai sarva hṛdā deva kāmaḥ sunoti   na gāḥ indraḥ tasya parā dadāti praśastam id cārum asmai kṛṇoti  
anuspaṣṭaḥ bhavati eṣaḥ asya yaḥ asmai revān na sunoti somam   niḥ aratnau maghavā tam dadhāti brahma dviṣaḥ hanti anānudiṣṭaḥ  
aśvāyantaḥ gavyantaḥ vājayantaḥ havāmahe tvā upagantavai u  ābhūṣantaḥ te sumatau navāyām vayam indra tvā śunam huvema  
muñcāmi tvā haviṣā jīvanāya kam ajñāta yakṣmāt uta rāja yakṣmāt   grāhiḥ jagrāha yadi etat tasyāḥ indra agnī pra mumuktam enam  
yadi kṣita āyuḥ yadi vā paretaḥ yadi mṛtyoḥ antikam nītaḥ eva   tam ā harāmi nirṛteḥ upasthāt a spārśam enam śata śāradāya  
sahasra akṣeṇa śata vīryeṇa śata āyuṣā haviṣā ahārṣam enam   indraḥ yathā enam śaradaḥ nayāti ati viśvasya duritasya pāram  
śatam jīva śaradaḥ vardhamānaḥ śatam hemantān śatam u vasantān   śatam te indraḥ agniḥ savitā bṛhaspatiḥ śata āyuṣā haviṣā ahārṣam enam  
āhārṣam avidam tvā punar āgāḥ punarṇavaḥ   sarva aṅga sarvam te cakṣuḥ sarvam āyuḥ ca te avidam  
brahmaṇā agniḥ samvidānaḥ rakṣaḥ hā bādhatām itas   amīvā yaḥ te garbham durṇāmāḥ yonim āśaye  
yaḥ te garbham amīvā durṇāmā yonim āśaye   agniḥ tam brahmaṇā saha niḥ kravya adam anīnaśat  
yaḥ te hanti patayantam niṣatsnum yaḥ sarīsṛpam   jātam yaḥ te jighāṃsati tam itas nāśayāmasi  
yaḥ te ūrū viharati antarā dampatī śaye   yonim yaḥ antar ārelhi tam itas nāśayāmasi  
yaḥ tvā bhrātā patiḥ bhūtvā jāraḥ bhūtvā nipadyate   prajām yaḥ te jighāṃsati tam itas nāśayāmasi  
yaḥ tvā svapnena tamasā mohayitvā nipadyate   prajām yaḥ te jighāṃsati tam itas nāśayāmasi  
akṣībhyām te nāsikābhyām karṇābhyām chubukāt adhi   yakṣmam śīrṣaṇyam mastiṣkāt jihvāyāḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
grīvābhyaḥ te uṣṇihābhyaḥ kīkasābhyaḥ anūkyāt   yakṣmam doṣaṇyam aṃsābhyām bāhubhyām vi vṛhāmi te  
hṛdayāt te pari klomnaḥ halīkṣṇāt pārśvābhyām   yakṣmam matasnābhyām plīhnaḥ yaknaḥ te vi vṛhāmasi  
āntrebhyaḥ te gudābhyaḥ vaniṣṭhoḥ udarāt adhi   yakṣmam kukṣibhyām plāśeḥ nābhyāḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
ūrubhyām te aṣṭhīvadbhyām pārṣṇibhyām prapadābhyām   yakṣmam bhasadyam śroṇibhyām bhāsadam bhāṃsasaḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
mehanāt vanaṃkaraṇāt lomabhyaḥ te nakhebhyaḥ   yakṣmam sarvasmāt ātmanaḥ tam idam vi vṛhāmi te  
asthibhyaḥ te majjabhyaḥ snāvabhyaḥ dhamanibhyaḥ   yakṣmam pāṇibhyām aṅgulibhyaḥ nakhebhyaḥ vi vṛhāmi te  
aṅge aṅge lomni lomni yaḥ te parvaṇi parvaṇi   yakṣam tvacasyam te vayam kaśyapasya vībarheṇa viṣvañcam vi vṛhāmasi  
apehi manasas pate apa kāma paras cara   paras nirṛtyāḥ ā cakṣva bahudhā jīvataḥ manaḥ  
vayam enam idā hyopīpema iha vajriṇam   tasmai u adya samanā sutam bhara nūnam bhūṣata śrute  
vṛkaḥ cit asya vāraṇaḥ urāmathiḥ ā vayuneṣu bhūṣati   sa imam naḥ stomam jujuṣāṇaḥ ā gahi indra pra citrayā dhiyā  
kad u nu asya akṛtam indrasya asti pauṃsyam   kena u nu kam śromatena na śuśruve januṣaḥ pari vṛtrahā  
tvām id hi havāmahe sātā vājasya kāravaḥ   tvām vṛtreṣu indra satpatim naraḥ tvām kāṣṭhāsu arvataḥ  
sa tvam naḥ citra vajrahasta dhṛṣṇuyāḥ mahaḥ stavānaḥ adrivas   gām aśvam rathyam indra sam kira satrā vājam na jigyuṣe  
abhi tvā pūrva pītaye indra stomebhiḥ āyavaḥ   samīcīnāsaḥ ṛbhavaḥ sam asvaran rudrāḥ gṛṇanta pūrvyam  
asya id indraḥ vāvṛdhe vṛṣṇyam śavaḥ made sutasya viṣṇavi   adya tam asya mahimānam āyavaḥ anu stuvanti pūrvathā  
adhā hi indra girvaṇaḥ upa tvā kāmān mahaḥ sasṛjmahe   udeva yantaḥ udabhiḥ  
vār na tvā yavyābhiḥ vardhanti śūra brahmāṇi   vār na tvā yavyābhiḥ vardhanti śūra brahmāṇi   vāvṛdhvāṃsam cit adrivas divedive  
yuñjanti harī iṣirasya gāthayā urau rathe uru yuge   indra vāhā vacaḥ yujā  
agnim dūtam vṛṇīmahe hotāram viśva vedasam   asya yajñasya sukratum   asya yajñasya sukratum  
agnim agnim havīmabhiḥ sadā havanta viśpatim   havyavāham puru priyam  
agne devān iha ā vaha jajñānaḥ vṛkta barhiṣe   asi hotā naḥ īḍyaḥ  
īlenyaḥ namasyaḥ tiras tamāṃsi darśataḥ   sam agniḥ idhyate vṛṣā  
vṛṣaḥ agniḥ sam idhyate aśvaḥ na deva vāhanaḥ   tam haviṣmantaḥ īlate  
vṛṣaṇam tvā vayam vṛṣan vṛṣaṇaḥ sam idhīmahi   agne dīdyatam bṛhat  
agnim īliṣva avase gāthābhiḥ śīra śociṣam   agnim rāye purumīlha śrutam naraḥ agnim su dītaye chardiḥ  
agne ā yāhi agnibhiḥ hotāram tvā vṛṇīmahe   ā tvām anaktu prayatā haviṣmatī yajiṣṭham barhiḥ āsade  
acha hi tvā sahasaḥ sūno aṅgiraḥ srucaḥ caranti adhvare   ūrjaḥ napātam ghṛta keśam īmahe agnim yajñeṣu pūrvyam  
imāḥ u tvā purūvaso giraḥ vardhantu yāḥ mama   pāvaka varṇāḥ śucayaḥ vipaścitaḥ abhi stomaiḥ anūṣata  
ayam sahasram ṛṣibhiḥ sahaskṛtaḥ samudraḥ iva paprathe   satyaḥ saḥ asya mahimā gṛne śavaḥ yajñeṣu vipra rājye  
ā naḥ viśvāsu havyaḥ indraḥ samatsu bhūṣatu   upa brahmāṇi savanāni vṛtra hā parama jyāḥ ṛcīṣamaḥ  
tvam dātā prathamaḥ rāghasām asi asi satyaḥ īśāna kṛt   tuvi dyumnasya yujyā vṛṇīmahe putrasya śavasaḥ mahaḥ  
tvam indra pratūrtiṣu abhi viśvāḥ asi spṛdhaḥ   aśasti hā janitā viśvatūr asi tvam tūrya taruṣyataḥ  
anu te śuṣmam turayantam īyatuḥ kṣoṇī śiśum na mātarā   viśvāḥ te spṛdhaḥ śnathayanta manyave vṛtram yat indra tūrvasi  
itas ūtī vaḥ ajaram prahetāram aprahitam   āśum jetāram hetāram rathītamam atūrtam tugryāvṛdham  
yaḥ rājā carṣaṇīnām yātā rathebhiḥ adhriguḥ   viśvāsām tarutā pṛtanānām jyeṣṭhaḥ yaḥ vṛtra hā gṛṇe  
indram tam śumbha puru hanman avase yasya dvitā vidhartari   hastāya vajraḥ prati dhāyi darśataḥ mahaḥ dive na sūryaḥ  
tava tyad indriyam bṛhat tava śuṣmam uta kratum   vajram śiśāti dhiṣaṇā vareṇyam  
tava dyauḥ indra pauṃsyam pṛthivī vardhati śravaḥ   tvām āpaḥ parvatāsaḥ ca hinvire  
tvām viṣṇuḥ bṛhan kṣayaḥ mitraḥ gṛṇāti varuṇaḥ   tvām śardhaḥ madati anu mārutam  
sam asya manyave viśaḥ viśvā namanta kuṣṭayaḥ   samudrāya iva sindhavaḥ  
ojaḥ tat asya titviṣaḥ ubhe yat samavartayat   indraḥ carmā iva rodasī  
vi cit vṛtrasya dodhataḥ vajreṇa śata parvaṇā   śiraḥ bibhet vṛṣṇinā  
tat id āsa bhuvaneṣu jyeṣṭham yatas jajñe ugraḥ tveṣa nṛmṇaḥ   sadyas jajñānaḥ ni riṇāti śatrūn anu yat enam madanti viśve ūmāḥ  
vāvṛdhānaḥ śavasā bhūri ojāḥ śatruḥ dāsāya bhiyasam dadhāti   avyanat ca vyanat ca sasni sam te navanta prabhṛtāḥ madeṣu  
tve kratum api pṛñcanti bhūri dvis yat ete tris bhavanti ūmāḥ   svādoḥ svādīyaḥ svādunā sṛja sam adaḥ su madhu madhunā abhi yodhīḥ  
yadi cit nu tvā dhanā jayantam raṇeraṇe anumadanti viprāḥ   ojīyaḥ śuṣmin sthiram ā tanuṣva mā tvā dabhan durevāsaḥ kaśokāḥ  
tvayā vayam śāśadmahe raṇeṣu prapaśyantaḥ yudhenyāni bhūri   codayāmi te āyudhā vacobhiḥ sam te śiśāmi brahmaṇā vayāṃsi  
ni tat dadhiṣe avare pare ca yasmin āvitha avasā duroṇe   ā sthāpayata mātaram jigatnum atas invata karvarāṇi bhūri  
stuṣva varṣman puru vartmānam sam ṛbhvāṇam inatamam āptam āptyānām   ā darśati śavasā bhūri ojāḥ pra sakṣati pratimānam pṛthivyāḥ  
imā brahma bṛhaddivaḥ kṛṇavat indrāya śūṣam agniyaḥ svarṣāḥ   mahaḥ gotrasya kṣayati svarājā turaḥ cit viśvam arṇavat tapasvān  
eva mahān bṛhaddivaḥ atharvā avocat svām tanvam indram eva   svasārau mātaribhvarī aripre hinvanti ca ene śavasā vardhayanti ca  
citram devānām ketuḥ anīkam jyotiṣmān pradiśaḥ sūryaḥ udyan   divākaraḥ ati dyumnaiḥ tamāṃsi viśvātārīt duritāni śukraḥ  
citram devānām ud agāt anīkam cakṣuḥ mitrasya varuṇasya agneḥ   āprāt dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣam sūryaḥ ātmā jagataḥ tasthuṣaḥ ca  
sūryaḥ devīm uṣasam rocamānām maryaḥ na yoṣām abhī eti paścāt   yatra naraḥ devayantaḥ yugāni vitanvate prati bhadrāya bhadram  
tvam naḥ indra ā bharam ojaḥ nṛmṇam śatakrato vicarṣaṇe   ā vīram pṛtanāṣaham  
tvam hi naḥ pitā vaso tvam mātā śatakrato babhūvitha   adhā te sumnam īmahe  
tvām śuṣmin puruhūta vājayantam upa bruve śatakrato   sa naḥ rāsva su vīryam  
svādoḥ itthā viṣuvataḥ madhvaḥ pibanti gauryaḥ   yāḥ indreṇa sa yāvarīḥ vṛṣṇā madanti śobhase vasvīḥ anu sva rājyam  
tāḥ asya pṛśanāyuvaḥ somam śrīṇanti pṛśnayaḥ   priyāḥ indrasya dhenavaḥ vajram hinvanti sāyakam vasvīḥ anu sva rājyam  
tāḥ asya namasā sahaḥ saparyanti pracetasaḥ   vratāni asya saścire purūṇi pūrvacittaye vasvīḥ anu sva rājyam  
indrāya madūne sutam pari stobhantu naḥ giraḥ   arkam arcantu kāravaḥ  
yasmin viśvāḥ adhi śriyaḥ raṇanti sapta saṃsadaḥ   indram sute havāmahe  
trikadrukeṣu cetanam devāsaḥ yajñam atnata   tam id vardhantu naḥ giraḥ  
yat somam indra viṣṇavi yat vā gha trita āptye   yat vā marutsu mandase sam indubhiḥ  
yat vā śakra parāvati samudre adhi mandase   asmākam id sute raṇā sam indubhiḥ  
yat vā asi sunvataḥ vṛdhaḥ yajamānasya satpate   ukthe vā yasya raṇyasi sam indubhiḥ  
yat adya kac ca vṛtrahan udagāḥ abhi sūrya   sarvam tat indra te vaśe 
yat vā pravṛddha satpate na marāḥ iti manyase   uta u tat satyam id tava  
ye somāsaḥ parāvati ye arvāvati sunvire   sarvān tām indra gacchasi  
ubhayam śṛṇavat ca naḥ indraḥ arvāk idam vacaḥ   satrācyā maghavā soma pītaye dhiyā śaviṣṭhaḥ ā gamat  
tam hi sva rājam vṛṣabham tam ojase dhiṣaṇe niṣṭatakṣatuḥ   uta upamānām prathamaḥ ni sīdasi soma kāmam hi te manaḥ  
abhrātṛvyaḥ aanā tvam anāpiḥ indra januṣā sanāt asi   yudhā id āpi tvam ichase  
nakī revantam sakhyāya vindase pīyanti te surāśvaḥ   yadā kṛṇoṣi nadanum sam ūhasi āt id pitā iva hūyase  
aham id hi pituḥ pari medhām ṛtasya jagrabha   aham sūryaḥ iva ajani  
aham pratnena manmanā giraḥ śumbhāmi kaṇva vat  yena indraḥ śuṣmam id dadhe 
ye tvām indra na tuṣṭuvuḥ ṛṣayaḥ ye ca tuṣṭuvuḥ   mama id vardhasva suṣṭutaḥ  
mā bhūma niṣṭyāḥ iva indra tvat araṇāḥ iva   vanāni ni prajahitāni adrivas duroṣāsaḥ amanmahi  
amanmahi id anāśavaḥ anugrāsaḥ ca vṛtrahan   su kṛt su te mahatā śūra rādhasā anu stomam mudīmahi  
pibā somam indra mandatu tvā yam te suṣāva haryaśva adriḥ   sotuḥ bāhubhyām su yataḥ na arvā  
yaḥ te madaḥ yujaḥ cāruḥ asti yena vṛtrāṇi haryaśva haṃsi   sa tvām indra prabhūvaso mamattu  
bodha su me maghavan vācam ā imām yām te vasiṣṭhaḥ arcati praśastim   imā brahma sadhamāde juṣasva  
śagdhi u su śacīpate indra viśvābhiḥ ūtibhiḥ   bhagam na hi tvā yaśasam vasu vidam anu śūra carāmasi  
pauraḥ aśvasya puru kṛt gavām asi utsaḥ deva hiraṇyayaḥ   nakir hi dānam parimardhiṣat tve yat yat yāmi tat ā bhara  
indram id devatātaye indram prayati adhvare   indram samīke vaninaḥ havāmahe indram dhanasya sātaye  
indraḥ mahnā rodasī paprathat śavaḥ indraḥ sūryam arocayat   indre ha viśvā bhuvanāni yemire indre suvānāsaḥ indavaḥ  
astāvi manma pūrvyam brahma indrāya vocata   pūrvīḥ ṛtasya bṛhatīḥ anūṣata stotuḥ meghāḥ asṛkṣata  
turaṇyavaḥ madhumantam ghṛtaścutam viprāsaḥ arkam ānṛcuḥ   asme rayiḥ paprathe vṛṣṇyam śavaḥ asme suvānāsaḥ indavaḥ  
yat indra prāk apāk udak nyak vā hūyase nṛbhiḥ   simā purū nṛṣūtaḥ asi ānave asi praśardha turvaśe  
yat vā rume ruśame śyāvake kṛpe indra mādayase sacā   kaṇvāsaḥ tvā brahmabhiḥ stoma vāhasaḥ indra ā yacchanti ā gahi  
abhi tvā śūra nonumaḥ a dugdhāḥ iva dhenavaḥ   īśānam asya jagataḥ svar dṛśam īśānam indra tasthuṣaḥ  
na tvāvām anyaḥ divyaḥ na pārthivaḥ na jātaḥ na janiṣyate   aśvāyantaḥ maghavan indra vājinaḥ gavyantaḥ tvā havāmahe  
revatīḥ naḥ sadhamāde indre santu tuvi vājāḥ   kṣumantaḥ yābhiḥ madema  
ā gha tvāvān tmanā āpta stotṛbhyaḥ dhṛṣṇo iyānaḥ   ṛṇoḥ akṣam na cakrayoḥ  
ā yat duvaḥ śatakrato ā kāmam jaritṝṇām   ṛṇoḥ akṣam na śacībhiḥ  
tat sūryasya deva tvam tat mahitvam madhyā kartoḥ vitatam sam jabhāra   yadā id ayukta haritaḥ sadhasthāt āt rātrī vāsaḥ tanute simasmai  
tat mitrasya varuṇasya abhicakṣe sūryaḥ rūpam kṛṇute dyoḥ upasthe   anantam anyat ruśat asya prājaḥ kṛṣṇam anyat haritaḥ sam bharanti  
kayā naḥ citraḥ ā bhuvat ūtī sadāvṛdhaḥ sakhā   kayā śaciṣṭhayā vṛtā  
kaḥ tvā satyaḥ madānām maṃhiṣṭhaḥ matsat andhasaḥ   dṛlhā cit āruje vasu  
abhi su naḥ sakhīnām avitā jaritṝṇām   śatam bhavāsi ūtibhiḥ  
imā nu kam bhuvanā sīṣadhāma indraḥ ca viśve ca devāḥ   yajñam ca naḥ tanvam ca prajām ca ādityaiḥ indraḥ saha cīkḷpāti  
ādityaiḥ indraḥ sa gaṇaḥ marudbhiḥ asmākam bhūtu avitā tanūnām   hatvāya devāḥ asurān yat āyan devāḥ deva tvam abhirakṣamāṇāḥ  
pratyañcam arkam anayam śacībhiḥ āt id svadhām iṣirām pari apaśyan   ayā vājam deva hitam sanema madema śata himāḥ su vīrāḥ  
apa indra prācaḥ maghavan amitrān apa apācaḥ abhibhūte nudasva   apa udīcaḥ apa śūra adharācaḥ urau yathā tava śarman madema  
kuvid aṅga yavamantaḥ yavam cit yathā dānti anupūrvam viyūya   iha iha eṣām kṛṇuhi bhojanāni ye barhiṣaḥ namaḥ vṛktim na jagmuḥ  
nahi sthūrī ṛtuthā yātam asti na uta śravaḥ vivide saṃgameṣu   gavyantaḥ indram sakhyāya viprāḥ aśvāyantaḥ vṛṣaṇam vājayantaḥ  
yuvam surāmam aśvinā namucau āsure sacā   vipipānā śubhaḥ patī indram karmasu āvatam  
putram iva pitarau aśvinā ubhā indra āvathuḥ kāvyaiḥ daṃsanābhiḥ   yat surāmam vi apibaḥ śacībhiḥ sarasvatī tvā maghavan abhiṣṇak  
indraḥ sutrāmā svavām avobhiḥ su mṛḍīkaḥ bhavatu viśva vedāḥ   bādhatām dveṣaḥ abhayam naḥ kṛṇotu su vīryasya patayaḥ syāma  
sa sutrāmā svavān indraḥ asmat ārāt cit dveṣaḥ sanutar yuyotu   tasya vayam sumatau yajñiyasya api bhadre saumanase syāma  
vi hi sotoḥ asṛkṣata na indram devam amaṃsata   yatra amadat vṛṣākapiḥ aryaḥ puṣṭeṣu mad sakhā viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
parā hi indra dhāvasi vṛṣākapeḥ ati vyathiḥ   naḥ aha pra vindasi anyatra soma pītaye viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
kim ayam tvām vṛṣākapiḥ cakāra haritaḥ mṛgaḥ   yasmai irasyasi id u nu aryaḥ vā puṣṭimat vasu viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
yam imam tvam vṛṣākapim priyam indra abhirakṣasi   śvā nu asya jambhiṣat api karṇe varāhayuḥ viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
priyā taṣṭāni me kapiḥ vyaktā vi adūduṣat   śiraḥ nu asya rāviṣam na sugam duṣkṛte bhuvam viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
na mat strī subhasattarā na suyāśutarā bhuvat   na mat praticyavīyasī na sakthi udyamīyasī viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
uve amba sulābhike yathā iva aṅgam bhaviṣyati   bhasat me amba sakthi me śiraḥ me vi iva hṛṣyati viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
kim su bāho su aṅgure pṛthuṣṭo pṛthu jāghane   kim śūra patni naḥ tvam abhi amīṣi vṛṣākapim viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
a vīrām iva mām ayam śarāruḥ abhi manyate   uta aham asmi vīriṇī indra patnī marut sakhā viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
saṃhotram sma purā nārī samanam vāva gacchati   vedhāḥ ṛtasya vīriṇī indra patnī mahīyate viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
indrāṇīm āsu nāriṣu subhagām aham aśravam   nahi asyāḥ aparam cana jarasā marate patiḥ viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
na aham indrāṇi rāraṇa sakhyuḥ vṛṣākapeḥ ṛte   yasya idam apyam haviḥ priyam deveṣu gacchati viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
vṛsākapāyi revati su putraḥ āt u su snuṣe   ghasat te indraḥ ukṣaṇaḥ priyam kācid karam haviḥ viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
ukṣṇaḥ hi me pañcadaśa sākam pacanti viṃsatim   uta aham admi pīvaḥ id ubhā kukṣī pṛṇanti me viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
vṛṣabhaḥ na tigma śṛṅgaḥ antar yūtheṣu roruvat   manthaḥ te indra śam hṛde yam te sunoti bhāvayuḥ viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
na sa īśe yasya rambate antarā sakthyā kapṛt   sedi īśe yasya romaśam niṣeduṣaḥ vijṛmbhate viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
na sa īśe yasya romaśam niṣeduṣaḥ vijṛmbhate   sedi īśe yasya rambate antarā sakthyā kapṛth viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
ayam indra vṛṣākapiḥ parasvantam hatam vidat   asim sūnām navam carum āt edhasyānaḥ ācitam viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
ayam emi vicākaśat vicinvan dāsam āryam   pibāmi pāka sutvanaḥ abhi dhīram acākaśam viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
dhanva ca yat kṛntatram ca kati svid tā vi yojanā   nedīyasaḥ vṛṣākape astam ehi gṛhān upa viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
punar ehi vṛṣākape suvitā kalpayāvahai   yaḥ eṣa svapna naṃśanaḥ astam eṣi pathā punar viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
yat udañcaḥ vṛṣākape gṛham indra ajagantana   kva sya pulvaghaḥ mṛgaḥ kam agam jana yopanaḥ viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
parśuḥ ha nāma mānavī sākam sasūva viṃśatim   bhadram bhala tyasyāḥ abhūt yasyāḥ udaram āmayat viśvasmāt indraḥ uttaraḥ  
idam janāḥ upa śruta narāśaṃsaḥ staviṣyate   ṣaṣṭim sahasrā navatim ca kauramaḥ ā ruśameṣu dadmahe  
uṣṭrāḥ yasya pravāhaṇaḥ vadhūmantaḥ dvis daśa   varṣmā rathasya ni jihīḍate divaḥ īṣamāṇāḥ upaspṛśaḥ  
eṣaḥ iṣāya māmahe śatam niṣkān daśa srajaḥ   trīṇi śatāni arvatām sahasrā daśa gonām  
vacyasva rebha vacyasva vṛkṣe na pakve śakunaḥ   naṣṭe jihvā carcarī iti kṣuraḥ na bhurijoḥ iva  
pra rebhāsaḥ manīṣāḥ vṛṣā gāvaḥ iva īrate   amota putrakāḥ eṣām amota gāḥ iva āsate  
pra rebha dhīm bharasva go vidam vasu vidam   devatrā imām vācam srīṇīhi iṣuḥ na avīra stāram  
rājñaḥ viśvajanīnasya yaḥ devaḥ martyām ati   vaiśvānarasya suṣṭutim ā sunota parikṣitaḥ  
parichinnaḥ kṣemam akarot tamaḥ āsanam ācaran   kulāyan kṛṇvan kauravyaḥ patiḥ vadati jāyayā  
katarat te ā harāṇi dadhi manthām pari śrutam   jāyāḥ patim vi pṛchati rāṣṭre rājñaḥ parikṣitaḥ  
abhīvasvaḥ pra jihīte yavaḥ pakvaḥ pathaḥ bilam   janaḥ sa bhadram edhati rāṣṭre rājñaḥ parikṣitaḥ  
indraḥ kārum abūbudhat uttiṣṭha vi cara janam   mama id ugrasya carkṛdhi sarvaḥ id te pṛṇāt ariḥ  
iha gāvaḥ pra jāyadhvam iha aśvāḥ iha pūruṣāḥ   iha u sahasra dakṣiṇaḥ pi pūṣā ni sīdati  
na imāḥ indra gāvaḥ riṣan mā u āsām gopa rīriṣat   mā āsām amitra yuḥ janaḥ indra mā stenaḥ īśata  
upa naḥ na ramasi sūktena vacasā vayam bhadreṇa vacasā vayam   vanāt adhidhvanaḥ giraḥ na riṣyema kadā cana  
yaḥ sabheyaḥ vidathyaḥ sutvā yajvā atha pūruṣaḥ   sūryam ca amuḥ riśādasaḥ tat devāḥ prāk akalpayan  
yaḥ jāmyāḥ aprathayaḥ tat yat sakhāyam dudhūrṣati   jyeṣṭhaḥ yat apracetāḥ tat āhuḥ adharāk iti  
yat bhadrasya puruṣasya putraḥ bhavati dādhṛṣiḥ   tat vipraḥ abravīt u tat gandharvaḥ kāmyam vacaḥ  
yaḥ ca paṇi raghujiṣṭhyaḥ yaḥ ca devām adāśuriḥ   dhīrāṇām śaśvatām aham tat apāk iti śuśruma  
ye ca devāḥ ayajanta atho ye ca parādadiḥ   sūryaḥ divam iva gatvāya maghavā naḥ vi rapśate  
yaḥ an ākta akṣaḥ an abhyaktaḥ a maṇivaḥ a hiraṇyavaḥ   a brahmā brahmaṇaḥ putra stotā kalpeṣu saṃmitā  
yaḥ ākta akṣaḥ subhyaktaḥ su maṇiḥ su hiraṇyavaḥ   subrahmā brahmaṇaḥ putra stotā kalpeṣu saṃmitā  
aprapāṇā ca veśantā revām apratidiśyayaḥ   ayabhyā kanyā kalyāṇī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā  
suprapāṇā ca veśantā revān supratidiśyayaḥ   suyabhyā kanyā kalyāṇī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā  
parivṛktā ca mahiṣī svastyā ca yudhim gamaḥ   anāśuraḥ ca āyāmī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā  
vāvātā ca mahiṣī svastyā ca yudhim gamaḥ   śvāśuraḥ ca āyāmī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā  
yat indra ādaḥ dāśa rājñe mānuṣam vi gāhathāḥ   virūpaḥ sarvasmai āsīt saha yakṣāya kalpate  
tvam vṛṣā akṣum maghavan amram maryākaraḥ raviḥ   tvam rauhiṇam vyāsyaḥ vi vṛtrasya abhinat śiraḥ  
yaḥ parvatān vyadadhāt yaḥ apaḥ vyagāhathāḥ   indraḥ yaḥ vṛtra hā anmaham tasmāt indra namaḥ astu te  
pṛṣṭham dhāvantam haryoḥ auccais śravasam abruvan   svastyaśva jaitrāya indram ā vaha susrajam  
ye tvā śvetāḥ ajaiśravasaḥ hāryaḥ yuñjanti dakṣiṇam   pūrvā namasya devānām bibhrat indra mahīyate  
etāḥ aśvāḥ ā plavante 
pratīpam prāti sutvanam 
tāsām ekā hariknikā 
hariknike kim icchāsi 
sādhum putram hiraṇyayam 
kva āhatam parāsyaḥ 
yatra amūḥ tisraḥ śiṃśapāḥ 
pari trayaḥ 
pṛdākavaḥ 
śṛṅgam dhamantaḥ āsate 
ayat mahā te arvāhaḥ 
saḥ ichakam sa ghāghate 
sa ghāghate gomīdyāḥ go gatīḥ iti 
pumām kuste nimicchasi 
palpa baddha vayaḥ iti 
baddha vaḥ aghā iti 
ajāgāra kevikā 
aśvasya vāraḥ gośapadyake 
śyenīpatī sā 
anāmayā upajihvikā 
kaḥ arya bahulimā iṣūni 
kaḥ asidyāḥ payaḥ 
kaḥ arjunyāḥ payaḥ 
kaḥ kārṣṇyāḥ payaḥ 
etam pṛcha kuham pṛcha  
kuhākam pakvakam pṛcha 
yavānaḥ yatiṣvabhiḥ kubhiḥ 
akupyantaḥ kupāyakuḥ 
āmaṇakaḥ maṇatsakaḥ 
deva tva pratisūrya  
enaścipaṅktikā haviḥ 
pradudrudaḥ maghā prati 
śṛṅga utpanna 
mā tvā abhi sakhā naḥ vidan 
vaśāyāḥ putram ā yanti 
irāvaḥ idum ayam data 
atha u iyan iyan iti 
atha u iyan iti 
atha u śvā asthiraḥ bhavan 
uyam yaka aṃśa lokakā 
āminon iti bhadyate 
tasya anu nibhañjanam 
varuṇaḥ yāti vasvabhiḥ 
śatam vā bhāratī śavaḥ 
śatam āśvāḥ hiraṇyayāḥ   śatam rathyāḥ hiraṇyayāḥ   śatam kuthāḥ hiraṇyayāḥ   ahula kuśa vartaka  
śaphena iva ohate 
āya vanenatī janī 
vaniṣṭhāḥ na ava gṛhyanti 
idam mahyam madūḥ iti 
te vṛkṣāḥ saha tiṣṭhati 
pāka baliḥ 
śaka baliḥ 
aśvattha khadiraḥ dhavaḥ 
arat uparama  
śayaḥ hataḥ iva 
vyāpa pūruṣaḥ 
adūham ityām pūṣakam 
atyardharca parasvataḥ
